# 3.25 Physical Downlink Control Channel Management

## 3.25.0-3 Physical Downlink Control Channel Management Document Owner Deputy Marilyn Ma; Sankha Bhattacharya; Oleksandr Andryeyev (ID: 11168288)

## 3.25.1 PDCCH Resource Management

### 3.25.1.0-1 PDCCH Resource Management Document Owner Oleksandr Andryeyev; Marilyn Ma;  Sankha Bhattacharya (ID: 11168299)

### 3.25.1.1 Control Resource Set (CORESET)

#### 3.25.1.1.0-1 Control Resource Set (CORESET) Document Owner Oleksandr Andryeyev (ID: 11168310)

#### 3.25.1.1.1 Determination of the Coreset

##### 3.25.1.1.1.0-1 Determination of the Coreset Overview (ID: 11168319)

**3.25.1.1.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11168325`)

Determination of the Coreset When 5G-L2-PS shall grants a DCI to a UE, it shall determine the Coreset as per following section:

Search spaces can be used by 5G-L2-PS to grant DCIs, please refer to 5G_UP_ALG_3937_replaced([11168480](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktv_nfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

The determination of Coreset, please refer to 5G_UP_ALG_3944_replaced([11168331](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktvYhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

##### 3.25.1.1.1.0-2 Determination of the Coreset Determination of Coreset (ID: 11168331)

**3.25.1.1.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11168333`)

Determination of the Coreset Acquisition of a Coreset configuration

---

**3.25.1.1.1.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11168338`)

Determination of the Coreset For each UE configured BWP 5G-L2-PS receives UE dedicated BWP ID from PdcchConfig of PsUser_UserSetupReq, and obtains cellBwpId, see 5G_UP_ALG_17939_replaced([11110885](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpIlUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). From PdcchConfig (see 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2185_replaced([11308908](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TrFkS_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), L2-PS obtains search space configuration that is associated with this BWP. Also, in the search space configuration, L2-PS obtains the CORESET ID (associatedCoresetId) that is associated with the search space. From associatedCoresetId, L2-PS obtains the CORESET configurations in PdcchConfig, see also 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2185_replaced([11308908](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TrFkS_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). 5G-L2-PS uses this Coreset of the UE current active BWP to grant all DCI format 0_1, and all DCI format 1_1.

If in a MAC CE message the coreset ID of the UE-Specific Search Space has to be filled, it is the one of the current UE active BWP

---

**3.25.1.1.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11168343`)

Determination of the Coreset Initialization of Coreset by L2-PS at the cell setup

---

**3.25.1.1.1.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11168347`)

Determination of the Coreset At the cell setup, the 5G-L2-PS defines a set of data about the PDCCH from the PsCell_CellSetupReq message:

 All combinations of the Control Resource Set duration.

 The capability to split the CCEs of the UE-Specific Search Spaces between the uplink and downlink in a given CORESET occurrence.

 A double buffering system for 20ms PDCCH slot pattern aligned on even radio frame. This pattern provides schedulers with all information needed to identify the PDCCH constraints.

---

##### 3.25.1.1.1.0-3 Determination of the Coreset Dedicated coreset on DSS cells with DL PRB sharing in subframe 0/5/9 (ID: 11168352)

**3.25.1.1.1.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `12590734`)

Determination of the Coreset When the DSS DL PRB sharing in subframe 0/5/9 is enabled (rrmLteDLPrbSharing=TRUE 5G_UP_ALG_4722_replaced([11172097](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuJoPfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

only dedicated coreset (other than coreset0) configured with cceToRegMapping=nonInterleaved otpion shall be used in subframe 5/9 [CB007372-M] on symbol #2 if this coreset overlaps LTE shared area [End CB007372-M]. The size of dedicated coreset in these subframes shall be aligned to consider only CCE assigned to NR according to values received in EN DSS DL CELL RESOURCE AREA ALLOCATION REQUEST ([11172253: Handling of DL CELL RESOURCE AREA ALLOCATION REQUEST](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuK2VPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) [CB007372-M] and for NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true also CCEs in NR dedicated area. ([12620260: Resource sharing in asymmetric DSS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_NsAEcDfZEfCYiuaHdt7wgQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). [End CB007372-M]

If L2PS will detect that dedicated coreset defined for slot 5/9 is configured with not recommended interleaved option it should output error log indicating improper configuration of coreset. [CB007372-M] For NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true only coreset used in symbol#2 shall be validated and only if this coreset overlaps the LTE shared area (see [12658544: CCE split for asymmetric DSS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_vqrj8UqyEfC0Ye3M8ARUWQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). [End CB007372-M] 

L2PS should not schedule any UE in the slots 5/9 if improper configuration is detected.

Note:

Coreset0 is always interleaved, therefore its usage in slots shared with LTE would not be efficient.

Coresets other than coreset0 might be configured with nonInterleaved or Interleaved option

Scheduling NR PDCCH in the area where LTE is transmitting some data might cause interference.

The coreset definition has to be ensured at the NIDD level by proper configuration.

[CB007372-M] Note2: For NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true the coreset used in symbol #2 may be not overlapping the LTE shared area. In such case all CCEs are available regardless of resources assigned in EN DSS DL CELL RESOURCE AREA ALLOCATION REQUEST. [End CB007372-M]

---

#### 3.25.1.1.2 Control Resource Set duration pattern

##### 3.25.1.1.2.0-1 Control Resource Set duration pattern Control Resource Set duration pattern construction principle (ID: 11168409)

**3.25.1.1.2.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `12632523`)

Control Resource Set duration pattern 12632523: Control Resource Set duration pattern With the PDCCH data received [Before CB014330-F] in the PsCell_CellSetupReq [CB014330-F] during cell setup or cell reconfiguration [End CB014330-F], the 5G-L2-PS builds all combinations with the different Control Resource Set(s) duration allowed for the UE-Specific Search Spaces and per bandwidth part whatever the frequency domain defined for each search space. Each pattern is defined for one slot and is fulfilled from the symbol 0 or 7 with one or several pdcch occasions without any free symbol between pdcch occasions per area (one area at the front of slot and the second area is starting from symbol 7).

All Patterns must have at least one PDCCH occasion starting from the symbol 0 **(if symbols are not reserved for other technology).**

If the cell is a cell shared with LTE [CB007372-A] and NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false [End CB007372-A] first two symbols (0,1) are reserved by LTE thus PDCCH occasion will start from symbol 2.

These CORESETs duration patterns are used to lay out the PDCCH per slot.

The 5G-L2-PS creates the Control Resource Set duration pattern as follow.

The reference CORESET selection is detailed hereafter, to build the Control Resource Set pattern with CCE split:

 Select the CORESET(s) for UE-Specific search space(s) with the lowest start symbol.

 If several CORESETs have same lowest start symbol then choose the one with lowest duration.

 If several CORESETs have the same lowest start symbol and the same duration then choose one with highest number of Resource Blocks.

 If several CORESETs have the same lowest start symbol, same duration and same (highest) number of RB then choose the one with smallest coreset IDentifier.

According to the configuration of search spaces, the 5G-L2-PS builds the control resource set duration patterns without CCE split, if possible. Then, if the CCE split is activated in the cell or if it is not possible to build the CORESET duration patterns without CCE split (only one occurrence of CORESET(s) in the front of the slot with a cell configured with DL and UL shared channels), the 5G-L2-PS tries to build the the control resource set duration pattern with CCE split if at least each BWP contains CORESET with CCE split capability.

If **NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is set to perBWP,** then the CCE split procedure in 5G_UP_ALG_19753_replaced([11168454](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktv_mPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is applicable for multiple dedicated BWPs. Otherwise, the CCE split procedure detailed in 5G_UP_ALG_14850_replaced([11168434](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktv_lfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is applicable for multiple dedicated BWPs.****

[image-0][image_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating the process of constructing a Control Resource Set (CORESET) duration pattern. The flowchart starts with a "Control Resource Set duration pattern construction start" node. From this starting point, the process branches into two main paths: one for CORESET duration patterns without CCE split and another for patterns with CCE split. **Path 1: CORESET duration pattern (no CCE split)** This path involves building all combinations of CORESET duration patterns for each half of the slot. \- If DSS is not present, patterns start from symbol 0. \- If DSS is present, patterns start at each position of CORESETS. \- The process then builds all allowed start symbols according to search space monitoring symbols within the slot. \- For each CORESET starting at the same symbol, the duration of the CORESET is selected. \- All CORESETs fully included in the same duration (even with different start symbols) are listed. \- All search spaces configured for these CORESETs and valid for each included CORESET are listed. \- A CORESET duration pattern is created for this combination. \- A decision is made on whether the CORESET duration pattern could be extended. If yes, a CORESET duration is appended to the previous pattern. If no, the process ends. **Path 2: CORESET duration pattern (with CCE split)** This path begins with a check if only cell Bwpld 0 and 1 are configured in the cell. \- If yes, it proceeds to select a CORESET reference (CORESETref) associated with UE-Specific search space(s) based on criteria like CCE split capability, smallest start symbol, smallest duration, largest number of RB, and smallest CORESET identifier. \- Then, it identifies both split CCE sets of the CORESETref. \- A new CORESET is added with the same or higher duration ending on the start symbol of the CORESETref. \- An interaction check is performed between both CORESETs. \- A decision is made on whether at most one set is impacted by CCEs of the additional CORESET. \- If yes, both CORESETs are allowed. \- If no, the additional CORESET is removed, and the process ends. \- If both CORESETs are allowed, a check is made if other CORESET splits are allowed (Type 1/3). \- If yes, it identifies both split CCE sets of the additional CORESET and checks interaction between both CORESETs. \- A decision is made on whether at most one set of the additional CORESET is impacted by CCEs of the CORESETref. \- If yes, the additional CORESET split is allowed. The set of both CORESETs which are overlapping or between the first CRB of each set with the same direction is considered, and the process ends. \- If no, the additional CORESET has always the direction of the CORESETref split CCE set overlapped or the closest, and the process ends. \- If no (other CORESET split not allowed), the additional CORESET has always the direction of the CORESETref split CCE set overlapped or the closest, and the process ends. \- If the initial check (Only cell Bwpld 0 and 1 configured in cell?) is no, it proceeds to identify both split CCE sets of CORESETref. \- Then, a CORESET is added with the same duration as CORESETref or higher duration ending on the start symbol of the CORESETref. \- An interaction check is performed between both CORESETs. \- A decision is made on whether at most one set is impacted by CCEs of the additional CORESET. \- If yes, both CORESETs are allowed. \- If no, the additional CORESET is removed, and the process ends. \- If both CORESETs are allowed, a check is made if other CORESET splits are allowed (Type 1/3). \- If yes, it identifies both split CCE sets of the additional CORESET and checks interaction between both CORESETs. \- A decision is made on whether at most one set of the additional CORESET is impacted by CCEs of the CORESETref. \- If yes, the additional CORESET split is allowed. The set of both CORESETs which are overlapping or between the first CRB of each set with the same direction is considered, and the process ends. \- If no, the additional CORESET has always the direction of the CORESETref split CCE set overlapped or the closest, and the process ends. \- If no (other CORESET split not allowed), the additional CORESET has always the direction of the CORESETref split CCE set overlapped or the closest, and the process ends. The flowchart uses standard flowchart symbols: rectangles for process steps, diamonds for decisions, and rounded rectangles for start/end points. Arrows indicate the flow of the process. There are also numbered markers (1 and 2) that seem to indicate continuation points between different sections of the diagram.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/img-07311749.png[/image_path][/image-0]

Folder: [3 L2RT Algorithms](https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:f:/r/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/Drawings%20and%20diagrams%20for%205G/User%20Plane/5G%20UP%20Algorithms/3%20L2RT%20Algorithms?csf=1&web=1&e=SYlMbm)

##### 3.25.1.1.2.0-2 Control Resource Set duration pattern Control Resource Set Duration Pattern in Case of Multiple Dedicated BWPs (ID: 11168434)

**3.25.1.1.2.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `13398547`)

Control Resource Set duration pattern 13398547: Control Resource Set duration pattern When more than one dedicated BWP is configured, the 5G-L2-PS builds all control resource set duration patterns according to all dedicated BWP configurations. Then, the 5G-L2-PS builds the CORESET duration pattern for the CCE split as detailed hereafter:

 For each BWP, select the reference CORESETRef,Bwp as detailed in the below flow diagram.

 Sort the reference CORESETRef,Bwp of all BWPs in increasing order of :

 The first CRB Index of the CCE split index of the reference CORESET.

 The CRB index of the reference CORESET.

 The cell BWP idx of the reference CORESET.

 [CB007372-E]   
If the cell is a cell shared with LTE and NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true and if any dedicated CORESET>0 overlaps the LTE shared area (see [12620260: Resource sharing in asymmetric DSS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_NsAEcDfZEfCYiuaHdt7wgQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) then CCE split is allowed on the symbol #2. For multiple dedicated BWP it is enough to check if the dedicated CORESET of the largest BWP overlaps the LTE shared area.  
When more than one dedicated BWP is configured the CCE split index shall be selected for the dedicated CORESET of the largest BWP. Dedicated CORESET(s) from smaller BWP(s) may have the CCE split or not depending on the CRB split index of the dedicated CORESET of the largest BWP. 

Note 1: In cells with asymmetric DSS there is(are) PDCCH occasion(s) without CCE split in slots 0&1  
Note 2: CCE split in symbol#2 is present if both UL and DL Grants are needed in given slot. Otherwise, there is no PDCCH on symbol#2 and only symbols 0&1 are used for PDCCH. For example, such situation may happen in SSB slots when numPdschPrbInSsbSlots=0 or in TRS slots when numPdschPrbInTrsSlots=0.  
[End CB007372-E]

 If the CORESETRef,Bwp in list doesn't overlap the CRB index of a CCE split index of another refererence CORESET of another BWP, then the 5G-L2-PS checks the CORESETRef,Bwp 2 by 2 to verify the interaction between both and detect whether it is possible or not to keep the CCE split. If it is the case, the 5G-L2-PS defines a DL-UL pattern allocation in reference with the one which will be applied to the first CORESetRef,Bwp in the list.

 Then one of the two CORESetRef,Bwp selected and the 5G-L2-PS adds the next CORESETRef,Bwp to check the interaction between 2 CORESETs and the DL-UL pattern. The condition to apply the same UL-DL pattern between CORESETs split is to have the same CRB split index when CORESETs are not interleaved or the overlapped CCEs of CORESETs must be in the same CCE split set.

 After the last check with the last CORESETRef,Bwp,the L2-PS check the interaction with the CORESET(0) if it is not linked to a UE-Specific search space..

[image-0][image_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a process related to CORESET (Control Resource Set) configurations in a cellular network, likely 5G NR. The flowchart starts with a step to select CORESET parameters for each cell based on UE-specific search spaces. It then proceeds to order these CORESETs and checks for overlapping CCE (Control Channel Element) split sets. The flowchart details several decision points and actions: 1\. **Initial Selection and Ordering:** For each cell, it selects CORESETs based on criteria like CCE split capability, start symbol, duration, number of RBs, and identifier. These are then ordered based on CRB index, start CRB index, and cell BWP index. 2\. **Overlap Check:** It checks if any CCE split set of a CORESET overlaps with a different CRB index of a CCE split. If there's an overlap, it indicates that CCE split is not supported in the cell, leading to an "End" state. 3\. **First CORESET Processing:** If no overlap is detected, it selects the first CORESET and identifies its split CCE sets. The DL/UL allocation for this CORESET is then referenced. 4\. **Iterative Processing:** The flowchart then iteratively adds the next CORESET, identifies its split CCE sets, and checks for interactions between the current and next CORESETs. 5\. **Interaction Checks:** * It checks if a CCE set of the current CORESET is impacted by CCEs of the next CORESET with a different CRB index for the CCE split, or if the CRB index is the same and both CORESETs are non-interleaved. * It further checks for the same CRB index for the CCE split or overlapping CCEs within the same CCE split set. * Based on these checks, it determines whether the DL and UL allocation is the same or opposite for the next CORESET. 6\. **Duration Pattern and Availability:** The duration pattern of the next CORESET is added to the current CORESET's duration pattern for CCE split. It then checks if another CORESET is available. 7\. **CRB Index Check and Configuration Update:** If another CORESET is available, it checks for the same CRB index for the CCE split. If not, it proceeds to check if CORESET(0) is used in a UE-specific search space. If it is, the process ends. If not, it checks if CORESET(0) overlaps a CRB index of the current CORESET. If it overlaps, CORESET(0) is not added, leading to an "End" state. If it doesn't overlap, it checks the bandwidth of CORESET(0) within consecutive CRB indexes of the CCE split. 8\. **Configuration Update and Final Decision:** Based on the checks, the CORESET with the highest CRB end and its DL/UL allocation becomes the current configuration for the check with the next CORESET. If CORESET(0) has only one direction defined by the overlapping CORESET, it leads to an "End" state. Otherwise, it identifies the CORESET with the largest overlap with CORESET(0) or the closest one if there's no overlap, and proceeds to a subsequent step labeled "2". The flowchart uses standard flowchart symbols: rectangles for processes, diamonds for decisions, and rounded rectangles for start/end points. Arrows indicate the flow of control.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_11832.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

##### 3.25.1.1.2.0-3 Control Resource Set duration pattern Control Resource Set Duration Pattern in Case of Multiple Dedicated BWPs in TDD FR1 (ID: 11168454)

**3.25.1.1.2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `12734387`)

Control Resource Set duration pattern 12734387: Control Resource Set duration pattern If **NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is set to perBWP,** then CCE split procedure in below flow diagram shall be followed for multiple dedicated BWPs. The main differences of this flow diagram compared to 5G_UP_ALG_14850_replaced([11168434](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktv_lfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are highlighted in red.**** For each BWP, selecting and sorting the reference CORESET (CORESETRef,Bwp) is similar to 5G_UP_ALG_14850_replaced([11168434](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktv_lfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). * Then the L2PS selects the first CORESET in the sorted list and denote this as current CORESET (CORESETRef,Bwp,c). The interaction of this CORESET is checked with each overlapping CORESET in the list. If CORESETRef,Bwp,c and another CORESET satisfies one of the three conditions below, CCE split is not supported for CORESETRef,Bwp,c. * Overlap between CRB index of the CCE split of CORESETRef,Bwp,c with a CCE split set of another CORESETRef,Bwp or * CORESETRef,Bwp,c/CORESETRef,Bwp is interleaved and same CRB index for the CCE split with another CORESET or * CORESETRef,Bwp,c/CORESETRef,Bwp is interleaved and the CORESETs have an overlap of # of REGs => REG bundle size * If CCE split is not supported for CORESETRef,Bwp,c, DL or UL DCIs shall be allocated to symbol 0 based on even or odd slot index, and CORESetRef,Bwp,c in symbol 1 will support the opposit direction. If CCE spllit is supported for this CORESetRef,Bwp,c, the 5G-L2-PS defines a DL-UL pattern allocation to CORESetRef,Bwp,c in symbol 0. One of the split set in symbol 0 will have UL or DL direction and the other split set will have the opposite direction based on even or odd slot index. In both cases (CCE split supported or not), the UL/DL direction of this CORESETRef,Bwp,c will be the reference for other CORESETs (dlUlSlotRef). Then the next CORESET (CORESETRef,Bwp,n) from the list is selected and L2PS checks the interaction of this CORESET with each overlapping CORESET in the list (CORESETRef,Bwp). Then the above three conditions are checked to decide whether to enable or disable CCE split for CORESETRef,Bwp,n. If CCE split is supported for CORESETRef,Bwp,n, then the L2PS applies CCE split to this CORESET (if not CORESETRef,Bwp,n is placed in two symbols), and allocates UL/DL direction based on dlUlSlotRef and selects the next CORESET from the list (CORESETRef,Bwp,n), assigns a new CORESET to CORESETRef,Bwp,c for dlUlSlotRef as in the flow diagram and follows the same procedure until all CORESETs in the list are considered. * After the last check with the last CORESETRef,Bwp,the L2-PS checks the interaction with the CORESET(0) if it is not linked to a UE-Specific search space similar to 5G_UP_ALG_14850_replaced([11168434](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktv_lfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [image-0][image_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a process related to CORESET (Control Resource Set) configuration in a cellular network, likely 5G NR. The flowchart starts with a step to select CORESETs based on specific UE-specific search space configurations. ### 3.25.1.2 Search Spaces

#### 3.25.1.2.0-1 Search Spaces Document Owner Oleksandr Andryeyev (ID: 11168471)

#### 3.25.1.2.1 Search Space for DCI grants

##### 3.25.1.2.1.0-1 Search Space for DCI grants Search spaces used by 5G-L2-PS to grant DCIs (ID: 11168480)

**3.25.1.2.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `13343087`)

Search Space for DCI grants The search spaces can be used by 5G-L2-PS to grant DCIs:

 RA-SearchSpace : the RA-SearchSpace allows to send DCI address to RA-RNTI /TC-RNTI or C-RNTI (if no Type3 and no UE-Specific search space are configuredyet in the UE (5G_UP_ALG_17940_replaced([11153286](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kslh8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). In NSA, such DCIs correspond to Msg2 and to Msg3 HARQ retransmission in Contention Based Random Access.

 A Common Search Space (Type3-PDCCH): An additional Common Search Space to schedule PUSCH with a DCI 0_0 address to UE C-RNTI. It is only used to schedule the Msg3 HARQ retransmission in Contention Free Random Access.

When MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/lteNrDssMode > 1 and cell is configured for SA mode or for Concurrent SA and NSA operation (NRBTS/NRCELL/cellDepType is set as SA or both), Common Search Space for DCI Format 1_0 shall be used for all DL transmissions starting from the call setup and until the configuration of the LTE Cell-RS rate matching parameters in the UE (DSS transient phase defined in 5G_L2_142_replaced([11143994](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_233KLvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The modification of parameters in the UE leading modification in the gNB too, could be decided by the C-Plane itself ("User modification request") or requested towards the C-Plane by the U-Plane ("User Reconfiguration Required"). For this last case, the C-Plane decides if a "User modification request" procedure needs to be triggered or not.

According to the the procedures applied to modify and activate the new settings in the gNB and the UE, the U-Plane uses: 

 When no specific handling is request by the C-Plane, the Type1 (no Type3 and no UE-Specific search spaces are configured in the UE) and Type3 (if configured) search spaces are used until the completion of the procedure hilighted by the C-Plane. During this phase the DCI Format 1_0 and 0_0 are used.

 When the C-Plane requests a specific handling of the parameters modification (5G_UP_ALG_17940_replaced([11153286](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kslh8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the Type1 (no UE-Specific search spaces is configured yet in the UE) or UE-Specific search spaces and associated PDSCH transmisisons are used to deliver the RRC message or after the completion of the procedure (when the delivery to the UE is done at the mac layer, the UL scheduling is blocked until the UE is expected to be able to answer to UL DCI with the new configuration delivered by the U-Plane. Therefore, when RRC message processing is expected to be completed in the UE, the U-Plane uses DCI Format 0_0 if no UE_Specific search space is configured in the UE, otherwise it uses the DCI Format 0_1

 An UE Specific Search Space: This UE Specific Search Space allows to schedule PDSCH/PUSCH with a DCI Format 1_1 and 0_1 address to UE C-RNTI. It is used in all the other cases. [CB015279-A] In addition to the above formats, if the Scell belongs to a different TAG than the Pcell, gNB-DU shall use UE-Specific Search spaces to transmit DCI 1_0 for initiating PDCCH order for achieving UL timing alignment. [End CB015279-A]

 Paging-SearchSpace is used by 5G-L2-PS to grant DCIs. Paging-SearchSpace allows to send DCI address to P-RNTI for paging message and/or short message to highlight a system information and/or CMAS/ETWS modification.

 SI-SearchSpaces are used by 5G-L2-PS to grant DCIs. SI-SearchSpace allows to send DCI address to SI-RNTI to broadcast system information (SIB1 and SI-Msg(s)).

---

#### 3.25.1.2.2 Search Space selection

##### 3.25.1.2.2.0-1 Search Space selection Overview (ID: 11168501)

**3.25.1.2.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11168509`)

Search Space selection For each RNTI, the 5G-L2-PS checks according to its value (SI-RNTI, P-RNTI, RA-RNTI, TC-RNTI, C-RNTI, CS-RNTI) or whether a specific procedure is ongoing (CBRA, CFRA, BFR, RRC reconfiguration) the availability of the expected search space in the slot according to the active PDCCH slot pattern and for the active BWP of the RNTI :

 Search space for System Information Radio Network Temporary Identifier (5G_UP_ALG_4047_replaced([11168597](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktxNsvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 Search space for Paging Radio Network Temporary Identifier (5G_UP_ALG_4047_replaced([11168597](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktxNsvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 Search space for the Random Access Radio Network Temporary Identifier (5G_UP_ALG_4049_replaced([11168607](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktxNtPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 Search space selection for the Temporary Cell Radio Network Temporary Identifier (5G_UP_ALG_4051_replaced([11168618](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktxNt_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 Search space selection for the Cell Radio Network Temporary Identifier (5G_UP_ALG_4053_replaced([11168627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktxNufvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 [CB008124-B] Search space selection for the Configured scheduling Radio Network Temporary Identifier (5G_UP_ALG_15277_replaced([11168657](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktxNwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). [End CB008124-B]

##### 3.25.1.2.2.0-3 Search Space selection Search Space, RNTI, BWP usage for the Contention Based Random Access procedure on gNB and UE side - TC-RNTI - CRI and RRC Setup in different transmission (ID: 11168527)

**3.25.1.2.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11168535`)

Search Space selection 11168535: Search Space selection CBRA: SA call setup with the contention resolution and RRC setup in different PDSCH transmissions

[image-0][image_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating a Random Access (RA) procedure and PDCCH/PNTI usage in a cellular network, likely 5G NR, differentiating between the gNB (base station) and UE (user equipment) perspectives. The diagram uses a sequence of messages and acknowledgments exchanged between the gNB and UE. Here's a breakdown of the diagram: **Left Side: gNB Perspective** * **RA procedure and PDCCH/PNTI usage (gNB)** : This section details the messages sent by the gNB. * **Random Access procedure (Initial BWP)** : This phase involves the initial steps of the RA procedure. * **Type1-PDCCH [RAITC-ANTI]** : The gNB sends a Type 1 Physical Downlink Control Channel (PDCCH) with a Random Access Radio Network Temporary Identifier (RA-RNTI). * **Nack/DTx** : The UE might send a Negative Acknowledgment (Nack) or Discontinuous Transmission (DTx). * **Ack** : The UE sends an Acknowledgment (Ack). * **Contention Resolution successfull** : This section describes the successful resolution of contention. * **Type1-PDCCH [C-ANTI]** : The gNB sends a Type 1 PDCCH with a Cell Radio Network Temporary Identifier (C-RNTI). * **Initial BWP** : Refers to the initial Bandwidth Part. * **Switch to UE Active BWP** : The UE switches to its active BWP. * **Active BWP** : This section covers the scenario when the UE is using its active BWP. * **Type1-PDCCH [C-ANTI]** : The gNB sends a Type 1 PDCCH with C-RNTI. * **Initial BWP** : Refers to the initial BWP. * **Active BWP: Dedicated BWP** : The UE is using a dedicated BWP. * **Type1-PDCCH [C-ANTI] or Type3-PDCCH UE-Specific [C-ANTI]** : The gNB can send either a Type 1 PDCCH or a Type 3 PDCCH, both with C-RNTI. **Middle Section: Message Exchange** This section shows the actual messages exchanged between the gNB and UE, indicated by arrows. * **PA Msg1 (CB-Preamble)** : The UE sends a preamble (Msg1) for the RA procedure. * **[DCI 1_0.RA-RNTI], RA-Msg2(macCE[RAPID], RAR*)** : The gNB responds with a Downlink Control Information (DCI) format 1_0 using RA-RNTI, containing RA-Msg2 with MAC Control Element (CE) and Random Access Response (RAR). * **RA-Msg3 (rrcSetupReq)** : The UE sends RA-Msg3, which includes an RRC Setup Request. * **DC 0_0 (TC-ANTI, NDI not toggled)** : The gNB sends a DCI format 0_0 with Temporary C-RNTI (TC-RNTI) and Non-Data Indicator (NDI) not toggled. * **reTx RA-Msg3 (rrcSetupReq)** : The UE retransmits RA-Msg3. * **[DCI 1_0.TC-RNTI], RA-Msg4(only macCE[CRI])** : The gNB sends DCI format 1_0 with TC-RNTI and RA-Msg4 containing only MAC CE. * **[DCI 1_0.TC-RNTI], RA-Msg4(only macCE[CRI])** : Another instance of RA-Msg4. * **[DCI 1_0.C-RNTI], PDSCH(SRB): rrcSetup)** : The gNB sends DCI format 1_0 with C-RNTI and a Physical Downlink Shared Channel (PDSCH) carrying an RRC Setup message for a Signaling Radio Bearer (SRB). * **[DCI 1_0.C-RNTI], PDSCH(SRB): rrcSetup)** : Another instance of PDSCH with RRC Setup. * **If BWPswitch triggered in the RRC setup:** This is a conditional note. * **No PubxCH, PDxCH transmissions before the DLslot of the last part RRC Msg sent (if segmented) and RRC time processing and BWP switch Delay (10+6 ms)** : Describes timing constraints. * **Slotn,endRrcMsg + (TRRCprocessingDelay + TBWPswitchDelayRRC) / nrSlotLength** : A formula for calculating a slot time. * **DCI 0_x*** (C-RNTI)** : The gNB sends DCI format 0_x with C-RNTI. * **PUSCH (rrcSetupComplete)** : The UE sends a Physical Uplink Shared Channel (PUSCH) containing the RRC Setup Complete message. **Right Side: UE Perspective** * **RA procedure and PDCCH/PNTI usage (UE)** : This section details the messages received by the UE. * **TC-RNTI Allocation** : The UE receives an allocation of TC-RNTI. * **Type1-PDCCH [RAITC-ANTI]** : The UE receives a Type 1 PDCCH with RA-RNTI. * **Random Access procedure (Initial BWP)** : The UE is in the initial RA procedure phase. * **TC-RNTI discard** : The UE discards the TC-RNTI. * **Contention Resolution successfull** : The UE experiences successful contention resolution. * **Type1-PDCCH [C-ANTI]** : The UE receives a Type 1 PDCCH with C-RNTI. * **Switch to Active BWP** : The UE switches to its active BWP. * **Type1-PDCCH [C-ANTI] or Type3-PDCCH UE-Specific [C-ANTI]** : The UE receives either a Type 1 or Type 3 PDCCH. * **RRC Setup without Type3 or UE-Specific** : Indicates RRC Setup without specific types. * **RRC Setup with Type3 or UE-Specific** : Indicates RRC Setup with specific types. **Bottom Section: Contention Based Random Access Procedure** * **Contention Based Random Access procedure:** * **SA call set up with contention resolution before the RRC setup** : Describes the context. * **RAR (7 Bytes):TA+ UL grant +TC-RNTI** : Details the content of the Random Access Response. * **"To be homogeneous with the RRC reconfiguration, it would be relevant to use the DCI Format x_0 until the RRC Setup Complete."** : A note on DCI format usage. * **"If the Type1 or Type3 is selected then DCI Format 0_0 must be used."** : Another note on DCI format usage.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_11848.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

##### 3.25.1.2.2.0-5 Search Space selection Search Space, RNTI, BWP usage for the Contention Based Random Access procedure on gNB and UE side - CRNTI - NSA (ID: 11168555)

**3.25.1.2.2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11168564`)

Search Space selection 11168564: Search Space selection CBRA: C-RNTI already configured in the UE on NSA cell

[image-0][image_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating the Random Access (RA) procedure and PDCCH/RNTI usage in a cellular network, differentiating between the gNB (base station) and the UE (user equipment). The diagram uses a sequence of messages and acknowledgments to depict the communication flow. On the left side, under the heading "Random Access procedure," the UE initiates the process. The diagram shows the UE sending "RA-Msg1 (CB-Preamble)" to the gNB. Following this, the gNB responds with "RA-Msg2 (macCE[RAPID], RAR)" and allocates a "TC-RNTI." The UE then receives a "Type1-PDCCH [RA/TC-RNTI]" which is part of the "Random Access procedure (Dedicated BWP)." The diagram then shows a potential retransmission scenario. The gNB sends "RA-Msg3 (macCE[C-RNTI]+...)" and the UE responds with "Nack/DTx" and "DCI 0_0 (TC-RNTI, NDI not toggled)." This leads to a retransmission of "RA-Msg3 (macCE[C-RNTI]+...)" by the gNB. The UE then sends "Ack" and "DCI 0_x (NDI toggled, C-RNTI)," followed by "PUSCH(C-RNTI)." A second, similar sequence is shown for "UE-Specific Type3-PDCCH (Dedicated BWP)." The gNB sends "DCI 0_x (NDI not toggled, C-RNTI)," and the UE responds with "Nack/DTx." The gNB then sends "PUSCH(C-RNTI)," and the UE acknowledges with "Ack." This part of the diagram also indicates "TC-RNTI discard" and "Type3-PDCCH or UE-Specific [C-RNTI]" on the gNB side, leading to "Contention Resolution successfull." At the bottom, there's a note explaining "Contention Based Random Access procedure: Cell NSA." It specifies that this occurs when "UE has already a C-RNTI configured but no CF-Preamble (HO, NSA call setup, BFRN)" and "TC-RNTI selected not equal to the UE C-RNTI." The text elements in the image are: **Left Side (UE Perspective):** * Random Access procedure * Contention Resolution successfull * Type1-PDCCH [TC-RNTI] (Dedicated BWP) * UE-Specific Type3-PDCCH (Dedicated BWP) **Right Side (gNB Perspective):** * RA procedure and PDCCH/RNTI usage (gNB) * RA procedure and PDCCH/RNTI usage (UE) * TC-RNTI Allocation * Type1-PDCCH [RA/TC-RNTI] * Random Access procedure (Dedicated BWP) * TC-RNTI discard * Type3-PDCCH or UE-Specific [C-RNTI] * Contention Resolution successfull **Messages and Flows:** * RA-Msg1 (CB-Preamble) * [DCI 1_0,RA-RNTI]=>RA-Msg2(macCE[RAPID], RAR) * RA-Msg3 (macCE[C-RNTI]+...) * Nack/DTx * DCI 0_0 (TC-RNTI, NDI not toggled) * reTx RA-Msg3 (macCE[C-RNTI]+...) * Ack * DCI 0_x (NDI toggled, C-RNTI) * PUSCH(C-RNTI) * DCI 0_x (NDI not toggled, C-RNTI) * PUSCH(C-RNTI) **Bottom Note:** * Contention Based Random Access procedure: Cell NSA * UE has already a C-RNTI configured but no CF-Preamble (HO, NSA call setup, BFRN) * TC-RNTI selected not equal to the UE C-RNTI[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_11852.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

##### 3.25.1.2.2.0-6 Search Space selection Search Space, RNTI, BWP usage for the Contention Free Random Access procedure on gNB and UE side (ID: 11168570)

**3.25.1.2.2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11168577`)

Search Space selection 11168577: Search Space selection CFRA: CF preamble and C-RNTI already configured in the UE

[image-0][image_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating a random access procedure and PDCCH/RNTI usage in a cellular network, likely 5G NR, involving a gNB (base station) and a UE (user equipment). The diagram uses blue text and arrows to depict the flow of information and control signals. Here's a breakdown of the text and the process: **Overall Context:** * **Title:** "RA procedure and PDCCH/RNTI usage (gNb)" and "RA procedure and PDCCH/RNTI usage (UE)" indicate the two main entities involved and the focus of the diagram. * **Left Side (gNB perspective):** "Random Access procedure" and "Type1-PDCCH [RA-RNTI] (active BWP)", "Type3-PDCCH or UE-Specific [C-RNTI]". * **Right Side (UE perspective):** "Random Access procedure (Dedicated BWP)", "Type1-PDCCH [RA-RNTI]", "Type3-PDCCH or UE-Specific [C-RNTI]". **Flow of Communication:** 1\. **gNB to UE (Initial Access):** * The gNB initiates with "RA Msg1 (CF-Preamble)". This is likely the Random Access Preamble sent on a Physical Random Access Channel (PRACH). * The UE responds with a message that includes "[DC1_0, RA-RNTI] => RA-Msg2 (macCE[RAPID], RAR)". This signifies the UE's response to the preamble, containing its identity (RA-RNTI) and a Random Access Response (RAR) message. 2\. **UE to gNB (Data Transmission):** * The UE transmits data on the "PUSCH (Data)". This is the Physical Uplink Shared Channel. 3\. **gNB to UE (Acknowledgement/Retransmission):** * The gNB sends back "Nack/DTx" followed by "[DC1_0 (C-RNTI, NDI not toggled)]". This indicates either a negative acknowledgement (NACK) or Discontinuous Transmission (DTX), meaning the data was not received correctly or the gNB is not ready to receive. The C-RNTI is a Cell Radio Network Temporary Identifier, used for UE-specific control. "NDI not toggled" suggests the New Data Indicator was not flipped, implying no new data was successfully processed. * If a retransmission is needed, the UE sends "reTx PUSCH(Data)". * Upon successful reception, the gNB sends an "Ack" (Acknowledgement). **Contention Free Random Access Procedure:** A separate section at the bottom describes a "Contention Free Random Access procedure". Key points are: * "UE has a CF preamble and a C-RNTI configured". This means the UE has been pre-assigned a specific preamble and a C-RNTI, avoiding the contention inherent in a normal random access procedure. * "(not applicable to BFR(CF) procedure)". This indicates a specific scenario where this procedure doesn't apply. * "PAR(TC-RNTI) not used by the UE (set to C-RNTI by gNB)". This clarifies that a Temporary C-RNTI (TC-RNTI) is not used by the UE in this context; instead, the gNB assigns the C-RNTI directly. **Diagram Elements:** * **Arrows:** Indicate the direction of data or control flow. Solid arrows represent transmissions, and dashed arrows represent acknowledgements or negative acknowledgements. * **Labels:** Describe the messages, channels, and identifiers involved. * **Brackets`[]`:** Enclose identifiers like RNTI (Radio Network Temporary Identifier), RAPID (Random Access Preamble ID), and BWP (Bandwidth Part). * **Parentheses`()`:** Enclose additional information or parameters.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_11854.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

##### 3.25.1.2.2.0-8 Search Space selection Search space selection for SI-RNTI or P-RNTI (ID: 11168597)

**3.25.1.2.2.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11168603`)

Search Space selection For SI-RNTI (SIB1 or SI-Msg) or a P-RNTI, the associated search space and PDCCH occasion are always available as the PDCCH slot pattern is built to handle the common channel transmissions when it is expected (as specified in 5G_UP_ALG_3970_replaced([11168960](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktzp_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The L2-PS triggers the AL selection (see requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4058_replaced([11170276](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt9a_vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_4060_replaced([11170287](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-CAfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

##### 3.25.1.2.2.0-9 Search Space selection Search space selection for RA-RNTI (ID: 11168607)

**3.25.1.2.2.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `11168612`)

Search Space selection The transmission of the RA-Msg2 uses always the type1-PDCCH of the UE active BWP. The 5G-L2-PS determines first which BWP is used before to check the availability of the search space as follow:

 If the received RA-Msg1 uses a Contention Free (CF) preamble, the RNTI context associated to this CF preamble is known and the 5G-L2-PS is able to determine the associated RNTI and its active BWP. If the received RA-Msg1 uses a Contention Based (CB) preamble with specific PRACH configuration (frequency domain or/and subset of CB preambles), the BWP identification is determined by the PRACH specific configuration itself.

There are up to three sets of CF preamble:

 The set for Beam Failure Recovery (not supported).

 The set for System Information on demand request (not supported).

 The Set for reconfiguration with synchronisation (Handover, NSA call setup…).

There are up to three sets of specific PRACH configurations on top of the default PRACH configuration:

 The PRACH configuration for Beam Failure Recovery (not supported).

 The PRACH configuration for System Information on demand request (not supported).

 The PRACH configuration for reconfiguration with synchronisation (not supported).

The gNB is configured with only one PRACH configuration and the same frequency and time domains are used whatever the BWP.

 If the received RA-Msg1 uses a Contention Based (CB) preamble without any PRACH specific configuration per BWP, the 5G-L2-PS is not able to identify which BWP is used, because the PRACH of the initial and dedicated BWP are configured at the same frequency and time domains. In that case the 5G-L2-PS considers that the RA-Msg1 is sent in the initial BWP if the Type1-PDCCH is configured in the initial BWP by the C-Plane. Otherwise, there is no Type1-PDCCH configured in the initial BWP and the 5G-L2-PS considers that the RA-Msg1 is sent in the dedicated BWP.

The 5G-L2-PS checks the availability of the Type1-PDCCH and a downlink PDCCH occasion in the expected BWP within the active PDCCH slot pattern used by both schedulers:

 If the search space and one or more PDCCH occasions are available, the 5G-L2-PS selects a PDCCH occasion allocated to the downlink and triggers the AL selection procedure (see requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4062_replaced([11170294](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-CA_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

 If the PDCCH resources are not available, the 5G-L2-PS triggers the dynamic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern procedure (5G_UP_ALG_3985_replaced([11169734](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt5JjvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the RNTI is not scheduled in this slot.

---

##### 3.25.1.2.2.0-10 Search Space selection Search space selection for TC-RNTI (ID: 11168618)

**3.25.1.2.2.0-10.0-1**  (ID: `11168621`)

Search Space selection The 5G-L2-PS considers that the RNTI is a TC-RNTI when the Random Access procedure is not successfully completed as detailed hereafter. In order to identify properly the contention phase, the TC-RNTI must be always a RNTI not configured in any UE (even for Handover, NSA call setup…in Contention Based Random Access). In Contention Free Random Access procedure, the RNTI used is a C-RNTI as it is known from the RA-Msg1 (the TC-RNTI sent in the RA-MsG2 is equal to the C-RNTI).

There are different procedures which could resolve the contention with the reception of Downlink and/or Uplink new transmission or retransmission. Nevertheless, to simplify the 5G-L2-PS, the Random Access procedure is successfully completed for the following cases:

 When the Downlink scheduler sends the RA-Msg2 after the RA-Msg1 using a CF preamble previously configured (after the RA-Msg2, the RNTI is a C-RNTI). In that case, due to the gNB implementation of the RA procedure, the gNB waits for an UL grant with a C-RNTI to complete the RA procedure (5G_UP_ALG_4053_replaced([11168627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktxNufvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 When the Downlink scheduler receives the acknowledgment of the transmission handling at least a UE Contention Resolution Identity MAC CE sent with the TC-RNTI.

 When the Uplink scheduler indicates that a new uplink transmission with C-RNTI, following the successful decoding of RA-Msg3 with the C-RNTI MAC Control Element (CE), was successfully received and decoded (5G_UP_ALG_4053_replaced([11168627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktxNufvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The 5G-L2-PS uses the same BWP as defined by the RA-Msg2 transmission.

The 5G-L2-PS checks the availability of the Type1-PDCCH and a PDCCH occasion in the expected BWP within the active PDCCH slot pattern used by both schedulers, when a TC-RNTI is used:

 If the search space and one or more PDCCH occasions are available for the expected direction (DL/UL), the 5G-L2-PS triggers the AL selection procedure (see requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4064_replaced([11170302](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-CBvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 If the PDCCH resources are not available, the 5G-L2-PS triggers the dynamic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern procedure (5G_UP_ALG_3985_replaced([11169734](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt5JjvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the RNTI is not scheduled in this slot.

---

##### 3.25.1.2.2.0-11 Search Space selection Search space selection for C-RNTI (ID: 11168627)

**3.25.1.2.2.0-11.0-7**  (ID: `12591679`)

Search Space selection For a C-RNTI, the UE active BWP is known (after RA-Msg1(CFRA) or after the contention resolution) and the 5G-L2-PS identifies the expected search space in the default SSSG or the active SSSG or the common slots between the SSSGs configured in the UE active BWP (se [11168730: Search Space Set Group management](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktx0yvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), according to the following cases:

 If the C-RNTI does not have any RRC configuration (Contention Resolution Identity MAC control element sent without RRC setup or the RRC setup does not activate a Type3-PDCCH or a UE-Specific search space), the Type1-PDCCH is used.

When the RRC setup is not acknowledged yet by the UE, the 5G-L2-PS uses the Type1-PDCCH of the initial BWP.

If the UE active BWP is the initial BWP after the RRC setup acknowledgement (initialActiveCellBwpId, received in the PsUser_UserSetupReq, is the initial BWP) and this BWP configured by the C-Plane through the PsCell_CellSetupReq does not have Type3 or UE-Specific Search Spaces, then the Type1-PDCCH of the initial BWP is used.

 If the RRC reconfiguration is ongoing and it will modify the DCI Formats x_1 sizes or UE is not configured with FR1 CA, the Type3-PDCCH is used if the RRC layer monitoring is activated. Otherwise, the UE-Specific search space is used.

 To close the contention resolution, with an uplink grant in the UE active BWP, after the reception of the RA-Msg3 including a C-RNTI MAC control element, the search space selection is done as follows:

 If the UE has a dedicated configuration activated with Type3 and UE-Specific search space, is not involved in the BFR procedure and NRCELL/actCbraContResDCI00 is set to false, the U-Plane uses the UE-Specific search space (DCI Format 0_1) in the UE active BWP, to close the contention.

 If the UE has a dedicated configuration activated with Type3 and UE-Specific search space, is not involved in the BFR procedure and **NRCELL/actCbraContResDCI00 is set to true, the U-Plane uses the type3 search space (DCI Format 0_0) in the UE active BWP, to close the contention.**

 When the UE dedicated configuration was never activated in the UE since the call setup (RRC setup (SA) or RRC reconfiguration (NSA)) or the UE in the initial BWP without dedicated configuration, the U-Plane uses only the Type1-PDCCH.

The 5G-L2-PS checks the BWP configuration search spaces by using the current active BWP in the UE context associated to the RNTI received in the CRNTI MAC CE and the BWP configuration (5G_UP_ALG_17926_replaced([11110850](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpH-SfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 If selected beam has changed after a Random Access procedure and the TCI State Indication MAC CE must be sent, the Type3-PDCCH is used.

 For all other cases, the UE-Specific search space is used.

The 5G-L2-PS checks the availability of the expected search space and PDCCH occasion in the expected BWP and Search Space Set Group within the active PDCCH slot pattern used by both schedulers:

 If the search space type with one or more PDCCH occasions is available for the expected direction, the 5G-L2-PS selects a PDCCH occasion and triggers the static AL selection procedure (see requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4066_replaced([11170311](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-CCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or the dynamic one (see requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4068_replaced([11170356](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-CEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), according to the AL selection mode activated for the active BWP

For non CA users, the PDCCH occasion selected could be updated if the selected one is not able to handle the expected Aggregation Level selected.

For CA UEs with distributed PUCCH allocation (5G_UP_ALG_2885_replaced([11123447](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), only the first Downlink PDCCH symbol (for example, symbol 0 for non-DSS, symbol 2 for DSS [CB007372-H] with NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false [End CB007372-H]) shall be used on FDD P(S)Cell, TDD P(S)Cell, FDD SCell and the first slot of TDD SCell.

When the first slot of TDD SCell is Uplink, the FDD PCell can use any Downlink PDCCH symbol.

For 5 MHz bandwidth, only the CORESET(0) starting in the first symbol is eligible for CA users.

When FDD PCell slot is LTE slot [CB007372-H] and NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false [End CB007372-H], the first slot of TDD Scell can use any Downlink PDCCH symbol.

 If the expected PDCCH resources are not available (see above), **the 5G-L2-PS triggers the dynamic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern procedure (5G_UP_ALG_3985_replaced([11169734](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt5JjvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the RNTI is not scheduled in this slot.**

---

##### 3.25.1.2.2.0-12 Search Space selection Search space selection for CS-RNTI (ID: 11168657)

**3.25.1.2.2.0-12.0-2**  (ID: `12709905`)

Search Space selection For a CS-RNTI, the UE active BWP is known (after RA-Msg1(CFRA) or after the contention resolution) and the 5G-L2-PS uses [CB012631-C] in the default Search Space Set Group (SSSG) or the active SSSG or the expected UE active SSSG but for the common slots between the SSSGs configured in the UE active BWP (see [11168730: Search Space Set Group management](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktx0yvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) [End CB012631-C]:

 Type3-PDCCH search space, when the DCI Format 0_0 must be sent to the UE only for CG deactivation order.

 UE-Specific search space, when the DCI Format 0_1 must be sent to the UE for CG activation or modification.

The 5G-L2-PS checks the availability of the expected search space and PDCCH occasion in the expected BWP within the active PDCCH slot pattern used by both schedulers:

 If the search space type with one or more PDCCH occasions is available for the expected direction, the 5G-L2-PS selects a PDCCH occasion and triggers the static AL selection procedure (see requirement 5G_UP_ALG_15279_replaced([11170341](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-CDPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or the dynamic one (see requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4068_replaced([11170356](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-CEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), according to the AL selection mode activated for the active BWP.

 If the expected PDCCH resources are not available (see above), **the 5G-L2-PS triggers the dynamic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern procedure (5G_UP_ALG_3985_replaced([11169734](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt5JjvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the RNTI is not scheduled in this slot.**

---

#### 3.25.1.2.3 Search Space List update for slot pattern

##### 3.25.1.2.3.0-1 Search Space List update for slot pattern Build list of search spaces (ID: 11168672)

**3.25.1.2.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11168699`)

Search Space List update for slot pattern 11168699: Search Space List update for slot pattern After the CORESET duration pattern selection, the 5G-L2-PS builds the list of available search spaces per bandwidth part with:  The search space identifier.  The position of the PDCCH occasion selected within the search space.  The distribution of the CCEs between the uplink and downlink by setting the list for each direction.  The list of preempted CCEs, due to an allocation of the common channel (SIB1, OSI or Paging) in the initial BWP. A search space, except for the search spaces of common channels (Type0-PDCCH and Type0A-PDCCH and Type2-PDCCH), is available in a slot when the following condition is met. [image-0][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is: $$(sfn \times 2^\mu \times 10 + rfSlot - slotOffset_{ts}) - periodicity_s \times \left\lfloor \frac{sfn \times 2^\mu \times 10 + rfSlot - slotOffset_{ts}}{periodicity_s} \right\rfloor < duration_s$$[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_11873.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] With, [image-1][image_desc]The image contains the text "sfn" in a stylized font. The background is white, and the text is framed by a black border on the right and bottom.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_11873.002.png[/image_path][/image-1]: System Frame Number. ##### 3.25.1.2.3.0-2 Search Space List update for slot pattern Update for common channels for DSS (ID: 11168705)

**3.25.1.2.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `12590737`)

Search Space List update for slot pattern For the CORESET associated to the common channels (SIB1, OSI and Paging), if the cell is a cell shared with LTE used for SA or SA+NSA mode (NRBTS/NRCELL/cellDepType is set as SA or both) [CB007372-A] and NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false [End CB007372-A],

then the CCEs are shared with a 1:1 split among downlink and uplink.

UL DCI link adaptation (5G_UP_ALG_5187_replaced([11172629](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuMrifvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be applied.

**Note1: at least 48PRBs are available for a CORESET for such a shared cell.**

**Note2: The CORESET associated to the common channels is also used in the slots reserved for msg2/msg4 (5G_UP_ALG_4716_replaced([11171969](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuJBIvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and CCE split shall be used in these slots as well.**

**Note3: downlink and uplink CCE areas are alternated**

else all CCEs are allocated to the downlink and the uplink CCE list for this search space is empty.

For the other direction(s), in the CORESET duration pattern, the CCEs are split or not according to search space capability and the number of uplink direction needed.

**Note: for DSS, this requirement applies to CORESET0**

##### 3.25.1.2.3.0-3 Search Space List update for slot pattern Update for CCE split (ID: 11168722)

**3.25.1.2.3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11168725`)

Search Space List update for slot pattern For the CORESET associated to the UE-Specific Search Spaces and when the CCE split is allowed, the 5G-L2-PS applies the split CCE pattern defined previously only if there are 2 directions allowed in the slot. Otherwise, the full CCE are allocated to the expected direction.

In the list, the 5G-L2-PS does not include the Common Search Space (Type1-PDCCH), if its CORESET identifier is not compatible or not the same as the one associated to UE-Specific Specific Search Space when the CCE are split between several directions (see [11168409](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_ect4ovvNEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

#### 3.25.1.2.4 Search Space Set Group management

##### 3.25.1.2.4.0-1 Search Space Set Group management Search Space Set Group(s) and Search Spaces excluded from any Search Space Set (ID: 12709882)

**3.25.1.2.4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `12709883`)

Search Space Set Group management The Common Search Spaces associated to the Type0/0A/1/2 are not included in any Search Space Set Group (SSSG).

The C-Plane configures the gNB-DU with the Type3 and UE-Specific search spaces defined in the BWP_PROFILE/PDCCH/PDCCH_CONFIG_DEDICATED in the default cell bandwidth part SSSG (ex: cellBwpSssg-0).

The gNB-DU uses the search spaces defined in the default cell bandwidth part SSSG or the Type1 as long as the UE is not yet identified or without any dedicated configuration or the UE does not support more than one SSSG.

When the C-Plane configure in a cell BWP several SSSGs associated to Type3 and UE-Specific search spaces, the gNB-DU gets from the C-Plane the mapping between the cell BWP SSSG identifier(s) (cellBwpSssgId) and the UE SSSG identifier(s) when the UE is configured with the default cell bandwidth part SSSG and at each time the UE configuration is updated with additional cell bandwidth part SSSG.

The default UE SSSG identifier is always 0 and if the C-Plane configures an additional one in the UE, by selecting a cell bandwidth part SSSG among the ones configured in the bandwidth part, the UE SSSG identifier is incremented by one.

When a UE is configured with more than one SSSG, it is expected by configuration to have some common slots (at least one slot) between all SSSGs configured for Uplink and Downlink grant capability.

In these slots, the search spaces in SSSGs must have common PDCCH occasion(s) with the same number of candidates for at least one Aggregation Level allowed in the cell BWP. If only a subset of AL has the same number of candidates, it will be used until the UE active SSSG is confirmed. These constraints simplifies the switching procedures between the configured SSSGs in the UE.

By configuration, the search space periodicities must fit within 2 consecutive radio frames starting from an even System Frame Number as long as the PDCCH slot pattern is not able to take into account the current even SFN to determine which search space is active within the 2 next radio frames according their configuration (periodicity, slot offset and duration). 

When the gNB-DU receives from the C-Plane the a BWP configuration handling several search spaces (Type3 and UE-Specific) with different cellBwpSssg identifier, the gNB-DU build the active SSSG slot pattern of each cell BWP SSSG over 20ms. It lists the slots where the at least one search space of this SSSG is active.

For each combination with the default SSSG and another SSSG, the gNB-DU builds the switching SSSG slot pattern over 20ms where the search space is active in both SSSGs and where coresetId, dci-Formats, monitoringSymbolsWithinSlot and searchSpaceType match.

The gNB-DU builds the AL SSSG switching list per search space type (Type3, UE-Specific) which includes only the AL for which the number of candidates is the same per PDCCH occasion in the common slots and for the search spaces with the expected type.

---

**3.25.1.2.4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12770206`)

Search Space Set Group management **[Before PR867429] ~~At the NIDD, the modification of the parameters related to the SSSG under NRBTS/BWP_PROFILE/PDCCH/PDCCH_CONFIG_DEDICATED/SEARCH_SPACE_GROUP must only be allowed if the NRCELL.actSssgSwitching is set to disabled, to guarantee that the U-Plane activates and confirms the switch to the SSSG-0 (default configuration) before to accept the cell modification for all UEs with more than one SSSG configured. The U-Plane must consider that the UE configuration of the additional SSSG is invalid.~~**

##### 3.25.1.2.4.0-3 Search Space Set Group management Search Space Set Group(s) and RIM mitigation (ID: 13313218)

**3.25.1.2.4.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13313219`)

Search Space Set Group management [PR863177-26R2] ; Before to activate the RIM mitigation impacting the k2 (NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM_PROFILE/actRimPdcchMuting is true) used by the Uplink scheduler to address a PUSCH transmission through a DCI 0_[0,1] or/and impacting the PDSCH transmission(s) of any additional SSSG configured in the cell, the U-Plane must first switch back to default SSSG (SSSG-0) successfully all UEs active on SSSG-1, before to activate the RIM mitigation.

As long as the RIM mitigation is active, the U-Plane must not trigger any SSSG switching to the SSSG-1.

When the RIM mitigation is deactivated, the U-Plane must restart the monitoring process for SSSG switching. [End PR863177-26R2]

##### 3.25.1.2.4.0-4 Search Space Set Group management Search Space Set Group(s) selection (ID: 12714956)

**3.25.1.2.4.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12714957`)

Search Space Set Group management [CB012631-D]

**[Before PR867429] ~~If the NRCELL.actSssgSwitching is set to disabled, the gNB-DU triggers the SSSG switch procedure to set back all UEs, with more than one SSSG configured, on the default SSSG and forbids any SSSG switch to the additional SSSG for all UEs with more than one SSSG configured.** By this way, it will allow the C-Plane to reconfigure SSSG or the gNB-DU to stop any new SSSG switch procedure to any other additional SSSG.**~~**

~~When the C-Plane requests to update the cell BWP SSSG configuration online, the gNB-DU accepts the new cell configuration when all UEs impacted by the modification have their confirmed active SSSG is set to the default one.~~

~~If the C-Plane removes the additional SSSG in the UE configuration whatever the UE active SSSG, then the gNB-DU uses the default SSSG as soon as the activation of the new configuration is activated when MAC layer monitoring is used. If the RRC layer monitoring is used, the C-Plane request to remove the additional SSG is accepted by the gNB-DU when the gNB-DU activated the default SSSG in order to be able to get the RRC reconfiguration complete from the UE using the default SSSG.~~**[End PR867429]**

[End CB012631-D]

During the call setup procedures (RRC setup, RRC reestablishment or RRC resume) or handover (RRC reconfiguration with sync), the default SSSG (see [12709882: Search Space Set Group(s) and Search Spaces excluded from any Search Space Set](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tQP00WS8EfCtwYrh0KQ_DA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) of the UE in its active BWP (according to the UE RRC configuration state) is the UE active SSSG.

After any BWP switch procedure (by DCI or by RRC or triggered by the UE itself), for a UE configured with only the default SSSG or with additional SSSG on top of the default one, the default SSSG of the UE active BWP is used as long as the gNB-DU does not trigger a new SSSG switch procedure.

As longs as the UE active SSSG is not confirmed, the gNB-DU uses only the common slots between all SSSG configured in the UE.

When a RA procedure is not completed (from the 3GPP point of view), the UE monitors the Type1 PDCCH when the RA-RNTI/TC-RNTI is used (see [11168607](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktxNtPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) & [11168618](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktxNt_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or the Type3/UE-Specific (according to the NRCELL.actCbraContResDCI00) when the C-RNTI is used and if the UE has already a dedicated configuration (see [11168627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktxNufvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

When Type3 or UE-Specific search space is used to close the contention resolution, the gNB-DU applies the following procedure:

· If the UE active SSSG is confirmed, the gNB-DU selects the Type3/UE-Specific search space defined in the UE active SSSG.

· If the UE active SSSG is not confirmed yet, the gNB-DU selects the Type3/UE-Specific search space defined in the UE active SSSG, but with the AL which must have the same number of candidates across the SSSG configured in the UE active BWP and for the active search space(s) in the slot used to send the grant.

---

##### 3.25.1.2.4.0-5 Search Space Set Group management SSSG Switching Definition (ID: 11168736)

**3.25.1.2.4.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11168740`)

Search Space Set Group management In order to save power and increase the battery duration on UE side, SSSG Switching functionality is introduced, which allows the gNB to switch the UE to different Search Space Set via DCI. The principle is to handle a virtual BWP in Time Domain for the search spaces Type3 and UE-Specific. 

It is applicable for all devices (i.e. RedCap, eMBB).

The gNB configures the UE at call setup (or during incoming Handover) with two different SSSG, depending on the UE capability:

· The default SSSG (SSSG-0) which contains the default Type3 and UE-Specific search spaces configured by the operator. 

· An additional SSSG (SSSG-1) which contains Type3 and UE-Specific search spaces with a different pattern compared to the default one.

Between the default SSSG and the additional one, there are common slots where the search spaces (Type3 and UE-Specific) are configured with the same number of candidates and common PDCCH occasions. The additional SSSG must have at least one slot with UL and DL grant capability per radio frame.

The criteria to select one for the SSSG configured in the UE are based on dedicated thresholds and parameters with the same algorithms as the ones used for the Power Saving BWP switching in Frequency Domain.

"DCI based SSSG Switching" is activated or deactivated when the higher layers configure or release searchSpaceGroupIdList-r17. The higher layers shall inform gNB-DU that the feature has been activated/deactivated. The gNB-DU shall not use the feature flag.

After the SSSG configuration and its activation, the DCI Format 0_1 and 1_1 sizes are modified and the U-Plane uses the "PDCCH monitoring adaptation indication" field in DCI Format x_1 (x=0, 1) to send the expected index of the active SSSG

---

##### 3.25.1.2.4.0-6 Search Space Set Group management SSSG Switching Procedure (ID: 11168744)

**3.25.1.2.4.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11168759`)

Search Space Set Group management 11168759: Search Space Set Group management **[Before PR867429] ~~[CB012631-D] ; The switching procedure can be triggered only if the SSSG configuration is valid (see[12770205: Search Space Set Group(s) reconfiguration procedure](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_LF7JwogMEfCrqOdGJPoCRA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). If the additional SSSG(>0) is set invalid, the U-Plane triggers a UE SSSG reconfiguration request towards the C-Plane) and will wait for the C-Plane SSSG reconfiguration and the new setting activation, before to restart the monitoring of the SSSG switching triggers.~~~~[End CB012631-D]~~ **[End PR867429]**_* The gNB-DU shall consider the expected SSSG configuration and the actual SSSG configuration. The expected SSSG configuration is set by triggering algorithm (see 5G_UP_ALG_31048_replaced([11168763](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktyb0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) based on DL/UL traffic rate and DL/UL buffer emptiness. The actual SSSG configuration is the configuration that UE has confirmed during synchronization (see 5G_UP_ALG_31049_replaced([11168840](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktzC4vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). After successful synchronization, the expected SSSG configuration and the actual SSSG configuration are equal. [image-0][image_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a process related to SSSG (likely a communication protocol or feature) states. The flowchart begins with a process box labeled "Triggering algorithm set the expected SSSG transmission state". An arrow points from this box to a rectangular box containing the text "There are two possible states: denseSSSG - SSSG#0 sparseSSSG - SSSG#1". An orange arrow points from the rectangular box to an oval shape labeled "The L2PS monitors toggling_expected SSSG configuration state". An arrow descends from the oval shape to a diamond shape with the text "sparse<->dense SSSG state toggled?". From the diamond shape, there are two possible paths: 1\. An arrow loops back up to the oval shape labeled "The L2PS monitors toggling_expected SSSG configuration state". 2\. An arrow points to an oval shape labeled "Synchronize configuration SSSG state between UE and gNB".[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_11884.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] The actual SSSG configuration can be in three states: denseSSSG, sparseSSSG, and ambiguous. The ambiguous state shall be set when a synchronization process fails due to, e.g., DTX detection. When the actual SSSG configuration is in the denseSSSG state, the gNB-DU shall use the search space set with group index 0, provided to UE in searchSpaceGroupIdList-r17. When the actual SSSG configuration is in the sparseSSSG state, gNB-DU shall use the search space set with group index 1, provided to UE in searchSpaceGroupIdList-r17. When the actual SSSG configuration is in an ambiguous state, gNB-DU shall use a recovery procedure (see 5G_UP_ALG_31051_replaced([11168868](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktzC6PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The initial state for the actual and expected configuration state is denseSSSS gNB-DU shall monitor the expected SSSG configuration state toggling. When expected SSSG has been toggled between sparseSSSG to denseSSSG or denseSSSG to sparseSSSG, the gNB-DU shall start a synchronization process. _*[CB012631-B-UPD001]** The synchronization process shall be executed in two steps:  configure the CS1 list for scheduling in slots defined by #SSSG1, internally synchronize DL/UL peers, and  send DCI with toggled value in the PDCCH monitoring adaptation indication field. **[End CB012631-B-UPD001]** When a synchronization process has been successfully completed, then the actual SSSG configuration state and the expected SSSG configuration state are equal. gNB-DU shall schedule according to the new actual SSSG configuration state.
