##### 3.25.1.2.4.0-7 Search Space Set Group management Triggering algorithm (ID: 11168763)

**3.25.1.2.4.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11168767`)

Search Space Set Group management **SSSG switching from sparseSSSG to denseSSSG**

---

**3.25.1.2.4.0-7.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11168772`)

Search Space Set Group management The gNB-DU shall evaluate the status of all UEs in the sparseSSSG state for every measurementDurationFromSparseSSSG ms.

The actual SSSG configuration state is in the sparseSSSG.

If the specific UE has high DL or UL throughput (5G_UP_ALG_31157_replaced([11168793](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktyb1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or 5G_UP_ALG_31159_replaced([11168813](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktyb2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or if a DL or UL full buffer status (5G_UP_ALG_31158_replaced([11168804](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktyb2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or 5G_UP_ALG_31160_replaced([11168822](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktyb3fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is triggered, then gNB-DU shall set the expected SSSG configuration state to denseSSSG.

**[CB012631-B-UPD001]**

[Before PR880751-26R2] If the specific UE has poor radio channel quality (5G_UP_ALG_31725_replaced([11168832](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktzC4PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) then gNB-DU shall set the expected SSSG configuration state to denseSSSG. [End PR880751-26R2]

If a UE's actual SSSG configuration state is equal to denseSSSG and a UE has poor radio channel quality, gNB-DU shall not evaluate DL/UL throughput and DL/UL emptiness.

Additionally, any pending RRC reconfiguration procedure (e.g DRX configuration procedure ) must be completed (RRC reconfiguration complete).

**[End CB012631-B-UPD001]**

Changing the expected SSSG configuration state to denseSSSG shall trigger a synchronization procedure (see 5G_UP_ALG_31049_replaced([11168840](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktzC4vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The SSSG switching uses the DCI format 0_1 or DCI format 1_1 with a 1-bit PDCCH monitoring adaptation indication field.

---

**3.25.1.2.4.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `11168776`)

Search Space Set Group management **SSSG switching from denseSSSG to sparseSSSG**

---

**3.25.1.2.4.0-7.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11168780`)

Search Space Set Group management The gNB-DU shall evaluate the status of all UEs not in the denseSSSG state for every measurementDurationToSparseSSSG _ms._

The actual SSSG configuration state is in the denseSSSG.

For specific UE, the gNB-DU shall set the expected SSSG configuration state if all conditions are filled :

 The UE has low DL and UL throughput (5G_UP_ALG_31157_replaced([11168793](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktyb1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_31159_replaced([11168813](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktyb2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 The UE has an empty DL and UL buffer status (5G_UP_ALG_31158_replaced([11168804](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktyb2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_31160_replaced([11168822](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktyb3fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

**[CB012631-B-UPD001]**

 The UE has good radio channel quality (5G_UP_ALG_31725_replaced([11168832](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktzC4PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) 

Additionally, any pending RRC reconfiguration procedure (e.g DRX configuration procedure ) must be completed (RRC reconfiguration complete).

**[End CB012631-B-UPD001]**

Changing the expected SSSG configuration state to sparseSSSG shall trigger a synchronization procedure (see 5G_UP_ALG_31049_replaced([11168840](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktzC4vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The SSSG switching uses the DCI format 0_1 or DCI format 1_1 with a 1-bit PDCCH monitoring adaptation indication field.

---

**3.25.1.2.4.0-7.0-3**  (ID: `11168784`)

Search Space Set Group management **The _measurementDurationSSSG **period definition_** **

---

**3.25.1.2.4.0-7.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11168788`)

Search Space Set Group management The measurementDurationSSSG can be either

 NRBTS/sssgSwitching/measurementDurationToSparseSSSG, for the non RedCap UE in the actual SSSG configuration state equal denseSSSG

 NRBTS/sssgSwitching/measurementDurationFromSparseSSSG for the non RedCap UE in the actual SSSG configuration state equal sparseSSSG.

 NRBTS/sssgSwitchingRedCap/measurementDurationToSparseSSSG, for the RedCap UE in the actual SSSG configuration state equal denseSSSG

 NRBTS/sssgSwitchingRedCap/measurementDurationFromSparseSSSG for the RedCap UE in the actual SSSG configuration state equal sparseSSSG.

If any parameters are changed, The gNB-DU shall apply the new parameters in the next measurement period.

---

**3.25.1.2.4.0-7.0-4**  (ID: `11168793`)

Search Space Set Group management **SSSG switching DL throughput criteria**

---

**3.25.1.2.4.0-7.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11168799`)

Search Space Set Group management If higher layers activate SSSG switching:

The gNB-DU shall estimate the average DL throughput of connected UEs at the end of every _measurementDurationSSSG ms periods.__[CB012631-B-UPD001] The_ measurementDurationSSSG is defiined in **5G_UP_ALG_31723_replaced([11168784](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktyb1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) **[End CB012631-B-UPD001]**_*_** *

**[Before CB012631-B-UPD001]**

The _measurementDurationSSSG can be either_

 NRBTS/sssgSwitching/measurementDurationToSparseSSSG, for the non RedCap UE in the actual SSSG configuration state equal denseSSSG

 NRBTS/sssgSwitching/measurementDurationFromSparseSSSG for the non RedCap UE in the actual SSSG configuration state equal sparseSSSG.

 NRBTS/sssgSwitchingRedCap/measurementDurationToSparseSSSG, for the RedCap UE in the actual SSSG configuration state equal denseSSSG

 NRBTS/sssgSwitchingRedCap/measurementDurationFromSparseSSSG for the RedCap UE in the actual SSSG configuration state equal sparseSSSG.

**[End CB012631-B-UPD001]**

To do so, the gNB-DU shall calculate _rrmAvgDlUeDataRate_BytesPerSlotForSSSGswitching based on rrmAvgDlUeDataRate_BytesPerSlotForBwpSwitch computed in[11111241](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpLop_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) but without the associated reinitialization conditions._

The _rrmAvgDlUeDataRate_BytesPerSlotForSSSGswitching must be evaluated for all UEs at the end of every measurement period of_ measurementDurationSSSG ms. The initialization condition of rmAvgDlUeDataRate_BytesPerSlotForSSSSGswitching shall be the same as the one for rmAvgDlUeDataRate_BytesPerSlotForBwpSwitch.**

 If the average DL throughput of a UE in the actual SSSG configuration state is equal to sparseSSSG and is higher than NRBTS/sssgSwitching/dlRateThresholdFromSparseSSSG for non RedCap UE **or** NRBTS/sssgSwitchingRedCap/dlRateThresholdFromSparseSSSG **for RedCap UE, then this UE shall be marked as having high DL throughput for the SSSG switching.** ****

 If the average DL throughput of a UE in the actual SSSG configuration state is equal to denseSSSG and is lower than NRBTS/sssgSwitching/dlRateThresholdToSparseSSSG for non RedCap UE or NRBTS/sssgSwitchingRedCap/dlRateThresholdToSparseSSSG for RedCap UE, then this UE shall be marked as having low DL throughput for the SSSG switching. 

_Note: A UE's DL throughput state is only valid for the next measurement period of_ measurementDurationSSSG ms.**

---

**3.25.1.2.4.0-7.0-5**  (ID: `11168804`)

Search Space Set Group management **SSSG switching DL buffer criteria**

---

**3.25.1.2.4.0-7.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11168809`)

Search Space Set Group management If higher layers activate SSSG switching:

The gNB-DU shall, for each UE, estimate if the sum of the current size of its non-VoNR buffer in 5G-L2-LO is null whenever the size of one of its associated buffers is updated. 5G-L2-PS shall use this measurement to compute the percentage of time when these buffers are empty over measurementDurationSSSG ms. [CB012631-B-UPD001] The measurementDurationSSSG is defiined in 5G_UP_ALG_31723_replaced([11168784](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktyb1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End CB012631-B-UPD001]

[Before CB012631-B-UPD001]

The measurementDurationSSSG can be either

 NRBTS/sssgSwitching/measurementDurationToSparseSSSG, for the non RedCap UE in the actual SSSG configuration state equal denseSSSG

 NRBTS/sssgSwitching/measurementDurationFromSparseSSSG for the non RedCap UE in the actual SSSG configuration state equal sparseSSSG.

 NRBTS/sssgSwitchingRedCap/measurementDurationToSparseSSSG, for the RedCap UE in the actual SSSG configuration state equal denseSSSG

 NRBTS/sssgSwitchingRedCap/measurementDurationFromSparseSSSG for the RedCap UE in the actual SSSG configuration state equal sparseSSSG.

[End CB012631-B-UPD001]

The ratio shall be considered invalid whenever a UE enters DRX mode and shall return to validity at the end of the measurement period following the one in which the UE returns to connected mode.

If a UE's actual SSSG configuration state is equal to sparseSSSG and these buffers are empty less than NRBTS/sssgSwitching/dlBufferEmptyRatioFromSparseSSSG for non RedCap UE or NRBTS/sssgSwitchingRedCap/dlBufferEmptyRatioFromSparseSSSG for RedCap UE percent of the time, then this UE shall be marked as having a full DL buffer state for SSSG switching.

If a UE's actual SSSG configuration state is equal to denseSSSG and these buffers are empty more than NRBTS/sssgSwitching/dlBufferEmptyRatioToSparseSSSG (for non RedCap UE) or NRBTS/sssgSwitchingRedCap/dlBufferEmptyRatioToSparseSSSG (for RedCap UE) percent of the time, then this UE shall be marked as having an empty DL buffer state for SSSG switching.

Note: A UE's DL buffer state is only valid for the next measurement period of measurementDurationSSSG ms.

---

**3.25.1.2.4.0-7.0-6**  (ID: `11168813`)

Search Space Set Group management **SSSG switching UL throughput criteria**

---

**3.25.1.2.4.0-7.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11168818`)

Search Space Set Group management If higher layers activate SSSG switching :

The gNB-DU shall estimate the average UL throughput of connected UEs at the end of every _measurementDurationSSSG ms periods.__[CB012631-B-UPD001] The_ measurementDurationSSSG is _defiined in_ _5G_UP_ALG_31723_replaced([11168784](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktyb1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) __[End CB012631-B-UPD001]_**_*_** *

**[Before CB012631-B-UPD001]**

The _measurementDurationSSSG can be either_

 NRBTS/sssgSwitching/measurementDurationToSparseSSSG, for the non RedCap UE in the actual SSSG configuration state equal denseSSSG

 NRBTS/sssgSwitching/measurementDurationFromSparseSSSG for the non RedCap UE in the actual SSSG configuration state equal sparseSSSG.

 NRBTS/sssgSwitchingRedCap/measurementDurationToSparseSSSG, for the RedCap UE in the actual SSSG configuration state equal denseSSSG

 NRBTS/sssgSwitchingRedCap/measurementDurationFromSparseSSSG for the RedCap UE in the actual SSSG configuration state equal sparseSSSG.

**[End CB012631-B-UPD001]**

To do so, the gNB-DU shall calculate _rrmAvgUlUeDataRate_BytesPerSlotForSSSGswitching based on rrmAvgUlUeDataRate_BytesPerSlotForBwpSwitch computed in[11111264](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpLorfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) but without the associated reinitialization conditions._

The _rrmAvgUlUeDataRate_BytesPerSlotForSSSGswitching must be evaluated for all UEs at the end of every measurement period of_ measurementDurationSSSG ms. The initialization condition of rmAvgUlUeDataRate_BytesPerSlotForSSSGswitching shall be the same as the one for rmAvgUlUeDataRate_BytesPerSlotForBwpSwitch.**

If the average UL throughput of a UE with no VoNR bearer in the actual SSSG configuration state is equal to sparseSSSG and is higher than NRBTS/sssgSwitching/ulRateThresholdNoVoNRFromSparseSSSG (for non RedCap UE) or NRBTS/sssgSwitchingRedCap/ulRateThresholdFromSparseSSSG (for RedCap UE), then this UE shall be marked as having high UL throughput for the SSSG switching. 

If the average UL throughput of a UE with no VoNR bearer in the actual SSSG configuration state is equal to denseSSSG and is lower than NRBTS/sssgSwitching/ulRateThresholdNoVoNRToSparseSSSG (for non RedCap UE) or NRBTS/sssgSwitchingRedCap/ulRateThresholdToSparseSSSG (for RedCap UE), then this UE shall be marked as having low UL throughput for the SSSG switching. 

If the average UL throughput of a UE with at least one VoNR bearer in the actual SSSG configuration state is equal to sparseSSSG and is higher than NRBTS/sssgSwitching/ulRateThresholdVoNRFromSparseSSSG (for non RedCap UE) or NRBTS/sssgSwitchingRedCap/ulRateThresholdFromSparseSSSG (for RedCap UE), then this UE shall be marked as having high UL throughput for the SSSG switching. 

If the average UL throughput of a UE with at least one VoNR bearer in the actual SSSG configuration state is equal to denseSSSG and is lower than NRBTS/sssgSwitching/ulRateThresholdVoNRToSparseSSSG (for non RedCap UE) or NRBTS/sssgSwitchingRedCap/ulRateThresholdToSparseSSSG (for RedCap UE), then this UE shall be marked as having low UL throughput for the SSSG switching.

_Note: A UE's UL throughput state is only valid for the next measurement period of_ measurementDurationSSSG ms.**

**3.25.1.2.4.0-7.0-7**  (ID: `11168822`)

Search Space Set Group management **SSSG switching UL Buffer criteria**

---

**3.25.1.2.4.0-7.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11168826`)

Search Space Set Group management If higher layers activate SSSG switching :

The gNB-DU, for each UE, at each utilization of the 5G UE's transmission buffer (see 5G_UP_ALG_5115_replaced([11203641](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwfxn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall measure whether the variable rrmBufferedDataUlLcg_bytes (see 5G_UP_ALG_5118_replaced([11203660](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwgYovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is equal to 0 for all LCGs that don't include VoNR bearer.

The gNB-DU shall use this measurement to compute the percentage of time where all concerned variable rrmBufferedDataUlLcg_bytes are equal to 0 over the measurementDurationSSSG ms period. [CB012631-B-UPD001] The measurementDurationSSSG is defiined in 5G_UP_ALG_31723_replaced([11168784](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktyb1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End CB012631-B-UPD001]

[Before CB012631-B-UPD001]

The measurementDurationSSSG can be either

 NRBTS/sssgSwitching/measurementDurationToSparseSSSG, for the non RedCap UE in the actual SSSG configuration state equal denseSSSG

 NRBTS/sssgSwitching/measurementDurationFromSparseSSSG for the non RedCap UE in the actual SSSG configuration state equal sparseSSSG.

 NRBTS/sssgSwitchingRedCap/measurementDurationToSparseSSSG, for the RedCap UE in the actual SSSG configuration state equal denseSSSG

 NRBTS/sssgSwitchingRedCap/measurementDurationFromSparseSSSG for the RedCap UE in the actual SSSG configuration state equal sparseSSSG.

[End CB012631-B-UPD001]

Then, this ratio shall be considered invalid whenever a UE enters DRX mode and shall return to being valid at the end of the measurement period following the one in which the UE returns to connected mode.

If a UE's actual SSSG configuration state is equal to sparseSSSG and all concerned variables rrmBufferedDataUlLcg_bytes are equal to 0 more than NRBTS/sssgSwitching/ulBufferEmptyRatioFromSparseSSSG (for non RedCap UE) or NRBTS/sssgSwitchingRedCap/ulBufferEmptyRatioFromSparseSSSG (for RedCap UE) percent of the time, then this UE shall be marked as having a full UL buffer state for SSSG switching.

If a UE's actual SSSG configuration state is equal to denseSSSG and all concerned variables rrmBufferedDataUlLcg_bytes are equal to 0 less than NRBTS/sssgSwitching/ulBufferEmptyRatioToSparseSSSG (for non RedCap UE) or NRBTS/sssgSwitchingRedCap/ulBufferEmptyRatioToSparseSSSG (for RedCap UE) percent of the time, then this UE shall be marked as having an empty UL buffer state for SSSG switching.

Note: A UE's UL buffer state is only valid for the next measurement period of measurementDurationSSSG ms.

**3.25.1.2.4.0-7.0-8**  (ID: `11168832`)

Search Space Set Group management **SSSG switching radio channel quality criteria**

---

**3.25.1.2.4.0-7.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11168834`)

Search Space Set Group management If higher layers activate SSSG switching:

The gNB-DU shall use the average CQI of connected UEs at the end of every _measurementDurationSSSG ms periods.__The_ measurementDurationSSSG is defiined in **5G_UP_ALG_31723_replaced([11168784](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktyb1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**. The average CQI is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_3005_replaced([11125595](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqvu4vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**_*_** *

If the average CQI is below the /NRBTS/sssgSwitching/SSSGCqiTreshold parameter for non-RadioCapUE or the /NRBTS/sssgSwitchingRedCap/SSSGCqiTreshold for RedCap UE, then his UE shall be marked as having a poor radio channel quality.

If the average CQI equals or exceeds the [PR835039] min(14, [End PR835039] /NRBTS/sssgSwitching/SSSGCqiTreshold parameter [PR835039] +rdSSSGCqiDelta R&D parameter) [End PR835039] for non-RadioCapUE or the [PR835039] min(14, [End PR835039] /NRBTS/sssgSwitchingRedCap/SSSGCqiTreshold [PR835039] +rdSSSGCqiDelta R&D parameter) [End PR835039] for RedCap UE, then his UE shall be marked as having a good radio channel quality.

[PR835039] Note: The rdSSSGCqiDelta R&D parameter shall be set 1 [End PR835039]

##### 3.25.1.2.4.0-8 Search Space Set Group management Synchronization between gNB and UE (ID: 11168840)

**3.25.1.2.4.0-8.0-2**  (ID: `12717016`)

Search Space Set Group management 12717016: Search Space Set Group management When the criteria to switch the UE SSSG from or to the default SSSG, the gNB-DU applies the following procedure until the UE active SSSG is confirmed (the first HARQ feedback acknowledged and a second one not Dtx or no HARQ feedback at the end of the confirmation timer) for any transmissions triggered by the DCI Format 0_1 or 1_1 :

· The gNB-DU uses the switching SSSG slot pattern to check if the UE can be added in the CS1 list.

· The gNB-DU uses the search spaces in the PDCCH common slot pattern corresponding to the UE active SSSG (see [12709882](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tQP00WS8EfCtwYrh0KQ_DA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

· The gNB-DU uses one AL within the AL SSSG switching list according to the UE radio conditions (see AL selection), if the dynamic AL is activated in the UE active BWP for DCI Format used for the SSSG switch.

If the dynamic AL is not allowed in the UE active BWP, the gNB-DU selects the highest level of AL in the common AL list that the UE can handle based on the current radio conditions.

· The gNB-DU uses DCI Format 0_1 and/or DCI Format 1_1 with the target UE SSSG identifier set in the DCI field "PDCCH monitoring adaptation indication".

Until the UE active SSSG is confirmed (See next requirement), if the gNB-DU has to use the DCI Format 0_0 and 1_0 for other purposes with a Type3, their feedbacks are no taken into account for the confirmation process. Nevertheless, theses transmissions must be done in the slots in the switching SSSG slot pattern. The AL used for these transmissions must be also allowed in the Type3 AL SSSG switching list.

During the synchronization process, as it is possible that the UE may discard the DCI if its buffers are empty and is configured to do it, the U-Plane must guarantee that a DL grant will be triggered during this phase. When the gNB has no data to send, the TCI update is triggered ([11168879: SSSG switching in case of absence of data for scheduling](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktzC6vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

[PR869406-26R2]

##### 3.25.1.2.4.0-9 Search Space Set Group management Confirmation of SSSG switching (ID: 11168850)

**3.25.1.2.4.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `12785592`)

Search Space Set Group management 12785592: Search Space Set Group management [Before CB012631-D] ;

Positively confirmation of switching SSSG is when:

o on DL transmission:

o If the gNB-DU receives ACK/NACK on PUCCH for DCI_1_1 containing the toggled value in the PDCCH monitoring adaptation indication field or

o If the gNB-DU receives ACK/NACK on PUSCH for DCI_1_1 containing the toggled value in the PDCCH monitoring adaptation indication field or

o on UL transmission:

o When UL transmission on PUSCH is detected, which was scheduled by UL Grant with DCI 0_1 containing the toggled PDCCH monitoring adaptation indication field,

then, the gNB-DU shall assume that UE has applied the new SSSG.

Note: If another UL transmission has been scheduled for the same slot when the acknowledgment is expected, ACK/NACK is bundled in the PUSCH transmission.

gNB-DU shall ignore the result of decoding PUSCH transmission, which UL Grant scheduled with DCI 0_1 containing the toggled PDCCH monitoring adaptation indication field.

When gNB-DU is not able to confirm switching SSSG, then gNB-DU shall:

o set the expected SSSG configuration state to ambiguous,

o start the DTX recovery procedure (see 5G_UP_ALG_31051_replaced([11168868](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktzC6PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[CB012631-D] ;

[Before PR869406-26R2] ; The SSSG switching procedure is completed when at least one positive HARQ acknowledgement is received for a DL or UL transmission triggered by a DCI Format 1_1 or 0_1 with the PDCCH monitoring adaptation indication field handling the target SSSG index and not using any MCS reserved (adaptive reTx) [End PR869406-26R2]

PR869406-26R2] ; After the reception of a first positive Acknowledgement of an HARQ process (UL or DL) triggered by a DCI Format 0_1 or 1_1 with the the PDCCH monitoring adaptation indication field handling the target SSSG index and not using any MCS reserved, during the synchronization procedure, the U-Plane starts a confirmation timer (20ms) and wait for a second non Dtx HARQ feedback:

· If there is no HARQ feedback (no DCI sent to the UE), at the end of the timer, the SSSG switching procedure is successfully confirmed.

· If the next HARQ feedback is received during the confirmation timer and it is not Dtx, the SSSG switching procedure is successfully confirmed.

· If the next HARQ feedback is Dtx during the confirmation timer, the confirmation timer is stopped and the SSSG switching procedure is failed and unconfirmed. Then, the SSSG recovery procedure is triggered. [End PR869406-26R2]

After the confirmation, the U-Plane will have the capability to use any valid slots defined in the active SSSG to schedule the UE with a DCI x_1 with the PDCCH monitoring adaptation indication field handling the active SSSG index.

Until the successful confirmation, the SSSG state is ambiguous and the U-Plane has to use only the common slots to schedule the UE when the UE-specific or Type3 search space is used. This behavior is allowed only because we have common slots between both SSSG configured in the UE with the common PDCCH occasions and candidates. [End CB012631-D]

[PR869406-26R2]

The overall structure suggests a decision-making or sequential process within the SSSG management system.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/img-02100959.png[/image_path][/image-0]

[image-1][image_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a process related to SSSG (Synchronous Secondary Synchronization Signal) pattern switching in a communication system. The flowchart is divided into two main vertical paths, starting from two separate entry points labeled "2" and "3". **Left Path (Starting from "2"):** * **Confirmation timer started:** This is the initial step. * **Wait for a second HARQ feedback triggered by DCI Format x_1 with tgtSssgld on switching SSSG pattern:** The system waits for a specific type of HARQ (Hybrid Automatic Repeat Request) feedback. * **HARQ feedback (filtering): for DCI 1_1 or reTx DCI 0_1 or non Dtx initial Tx DCI 0_1:** This is a decision point where the received HARQ feedback is filtered based on certain conditions related to DCI (Downlink Control Information) formats and transmission types. * If the condition is **No** , the flow returns to the "Wait for a second HARQ feedback..." step, indicating a loop. * If the condition is **Yes** , the flow proceeds to two parallel branches: * **Timer expiration without HARQ feedback:** This branch leads to "SSSG switching confirmed" and then to an "End" state. * **Timer running with HARQ feedback:** This branch leads to "Timer stopped", then to a decision point "HARQ feedback non Dtx?". * If "HARQ feedback non Dtx?" is **Yes** , it leads to "SSSG switching confirmed" and then to an "End" state. * If "HARQ feedback non Dtx?" is **No** , it leads to a process block "cellBwp[cellBwpld]-sssg[cellBwpSssgld]-confirmFailure + 1", then to "Set curUeSssgld = tgtUeSssld", followed by "SSSG recovery procedure", and finally to an "End" state. **Right Path (Starting from "3"):** * **cellBwp[cellBwpld]-sssg[cellBwpSssgld]-sucess + 1:** This is the initial step. * **Set curUeSssgld = tgtUeSssId:** The current UE SSSG ID is set. * **target SSSG slot pattern activation:** The target SSSG slot pattern is activated. * **SSSG HARQ feedback monitoring:** The system monitors SSSG HARQ feedback. * **End:** This path concludes with an "End" state. The flowchart uses standard flowchart symbols: * Rounded rectangles for start/end points. * Rectangles for process steps. * Diamonds for decision points. * Arrows to indicate the flow of control. * A parallelogram for input/output or data operations (though not explicitly used here, the rectangular boxes with double lines on the right could represent such operations).[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/img-02101000.png[/image_path][/image-1]

[End PR869406-26R2]

##### 3.25.1.2.4.0-10 Search Space Set Group management Unconfirmed SSSG Switching procedure (ID: 11168860)

**3.25.1.2.4.0-10.0-1**  (ID: `11168864`)

Search Space Set Group management [Before PR869406-26R2]**When the gNB-DU positively confirms switching SSSG and the subsequent transmission is not confirmed, and instead of confirmation DTX transmission is detected, gNB-DU shall consider false positive ACK/NACK and shall:**

o start the DTX recovery procedure (see 5G_UP_ALG_31051_replaced([11168868](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktzC6PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). [End PR869406-26R2]

[PR869406-26R2] ; When the SSSG switching procedure is not confirmed (the HARQ feedback following the the first positive acknowledgement is Dtx as specified in the previous requirement), the U-Plane starts the UE active SSSG recovery procedure. [End PR869406-26R2]

##### 3.25.1.2.4.0-11 Search Space Set Group management UE active SSSG Recovery procedure (ID: 11168868)

**3.25.1.2.4.0-11.0-1**  (ID: `11168874`)

Search Space Set Group management 11168874: Search Space Set Group management The recovery procedure shall start when:

· [Before PR869406-26R2] When the gNB-DU receives for the initial switching SSSG a DTX on DL or UL transmission ([11168850: Confirmation of SSSG switching](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktzC5PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). [End PR869406-26R2]

[PR869406-26R2] ; The SSG switching procedure is failed and unconfirmed ([11168850: Confirmation of SSSG switching](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktzC5PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). [End PR869406-26R2]

· [Before PR869406-26R2] ; When the gNB-DU positively confirms the initial switching SSSG and the subsequent transmission is not confirmed, and instead of confirmation, DTX transmission is detected ([11168860: Unconfirmed SSSG Switching procedure](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktzC5vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). [End PR869406-26R2]

[PR869406-26R2] ; The gNB-DU detects, after the SSSG switching confirmation, 20 consecutive Dtx HARQ feedbacks in response of DCI Format 0_1 or 1_1 sent in the non common slots or the common slot without a common AL between the UE configured SSSG patterns (SSSG-[0,1]). For each direction, the counter is initialized at each time a DCI Format 0_1 or 1_1 is sent on common slot with a common AL. [End PR869406-26R2]

[PR869406-26R2] ; When the recovery procedure is triggered, the gNB-DU applies the same constraint to send DCI Format 0_1 and 1_1 (SSSG switching slot pattern...) as in the synchronization procedure between gNB and UE (see [11168840](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktzC4vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

The recovery procedure is successful and completed when a HARQ feedback is not Dtx in response of a DCI Format 0_1 or 1_1.

From this main process, there are five branches, each representing a different condition or action. Branch 1: "Target SSSG-Id (tgtUeSssgld) not equal to the current SSSG-Id (curUeSssgld)" leads to a numbered step "1". Branch 2: "SSSG Switching confirmation" leads to a numbered step "2". Branch 3: "SSSG switching confirmed" leads to a numbered step "3". Branch 4: "SSSG recovery" leads to a numbered step "4". Branch 5: "SSSG HARQ feedback monitoring" leads to a numbered step "5". The flowchart is divided into two main columns, labeled "4" and "5", suggesting two parallel or sequential processes. **Column 4:** * **Start:** Begins with an input labeled "4". * **Identify cellBwpld associated to ueActiveBwp:** This step identifies a cell bandwidth identifier associated with the UE's active bandwidth part. * **Identify cellBwpSssgld associated to curUeSsgld:** This step identifies a cell bandwidth identifier associated with the UE's current SSSG identifier. * **cellBwp[cellBwpld]-sssg[cellBwpSssgld]-recovery + 1:** This appears to be a counter or state update related to cell bandwidth, SSSG, and recovery. * **Switching SSSG slot pattern activation:** This indicates the activation of a switching SSSG slot pattern. * **Wait for HARQ feedback triggered by DCI Format x_1 with curUeSssgld on switching SSSG pattern:** The process waits for HARQ feedback related to DCI Format x_1 and the current SSSG on a switching SSSG pattern. * **HARQ feedback non Dtx?:** A decision point asking if the HARQ feedback is not Discontinuous Transmission (Dtx). * **No:** If not non-Dtx, it loops back to "Wait for HARQ feedback triggered by DCI Format x_1 with curUeSssgld on switching SSSG pattern". * **Yes:** If it is non-Dtx, it proceeds to the next step. * **cellBwp[cellBwpld]-sssg[cellBwpSssgld]-recoverySuccessful + 1:** Another counter or state update, this time specifically for successful recovery. * **current SSSG slot pattern activation:** Activation of the current SSSG slot pattern. * **SSSG HARQ feedback monitoring:** The process enters a state of monitoring SSSG HARQ feedback. * **End:** The process concludes. **Column 5:** * **Start:** Begins with an input labeled "5". * **Wait for HARQ feedback triggered by DCI Format x_1 with curUeSssgld on current SSSG slot pattern:** The process waits for HARQ feedback related to DCI Format x_1 and the current SSSG on the current SSSG slot pattern. * **HARQ feedback for DCI Format x_1 on non common slots of all SSSG configured in the UE?:** A decision point asking if the HARQ feedback is for DCI Format x_1 on non-common slots of all configured SSSGs in the UE. * **No:** If not, it proceeds to "Reset nNonComSltDtx[DL,UL] according to the DL or UL". * **Yes:** If yes, it proceeds to the next step. * **HARQ feedback Dtx?:** A decision point asking if the HARQ feedback is Dtx. * **No:** If not Dtx, it proceeds to "HARQ feedback (filtering): for DCI 1_1 or reTx DCI 0_1 or non Dtx initial Tx DCI 0_1". * **Yes:** If it is Dtx, it proceeds to "Reset nNonComSltDtx[DL,UL] according to the DL or UL". * **Reset nNonComSltDtx[DL,UL] according to the DL or UL:** This step resets a counter or variable `nNonComSltDtx` for Downlink (DL) or Uplink (UL). * **HARQ feedback (filtering): for DCI 1_1 or reTx DCI 0_1 or non Dtx initial Tx DCI 0_1:** This step involves filtering HARQ feedback based on specific DCI formats and transmission types. * **Yes:** If the filtering condition is met, it proceeds to "nNonComSltDtx[DL, UL] + 1". * **No:** If the filtering condition is not met, it proceeds to "Reset nNonComSltDtx[DL,UL] according to the DL or UL". * **nNonComSltDtx[DL, UL] + 1:** Increments the `nNonComSltDtx` counter. * **nNonComSltDtx[DL,UL] >= Thershold?:** A decision point checking if the `nNonComSltDtx` counter has reached or exceeded a threshold. * **No:** If not, it loops back to "Wait for HARQ feedback triggered by DCI Format x_1 with curUeSssgld on current SSSG slot pattern". * **Yes:** If yes, it proceeds to "Reset nNonComSltDtx[DL,UL]". * **Reset nNonComSltDtx[DL,UL]:** Resets the `nNonComSltDtx` counter. * **SSSG recovery procedure:** The process enters the SSSG recovery procedure. * **End:** The process concludes. The flowchart uses standard flowchart symbols: rectangles for processes, diamonds for decisions, and rounded rectangles for start/end points. Arrows indicate the flow of control. The text is clear and legible.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/img-02101008.png[/image_path][/image-1]

[End PR869406-26R2]

**[Before CB012631-B-UPD001]**

TD scheduler (CS1 list) shall use the SSSG configuration defined in the space set with group index 1 (SSSG#1 sparseSSSG) for slot eligibility.

gNB-DU shall schedule only one HARQ process on the DL transmission or/and only one HARQ process on the UL transmission.

gNB-DU shall transmit data only in slots defined by the space set with group index 1 (SSSG#1 - sparseSSSG) until an acknowledgment is received on the HARQ process.

gNB-DU shall schedule DCI format 0_1 or 1_1 with the aggregation level boosted by one level.

gNB-DU shall set the PDCCH monitoring adaptation indication field to 1 (sparseSSSG)

When transmission is positively confirmed (see 5G_UP_ALG_31247_replaced([11168850](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktzC5PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and

 The expected SSSG configuration state is equal to the sparseSSSG recovery procedure completed.

 The expected SSSG configuration state is equal to denseSSSG, then gNB-DU shall start the synchronization process (see 5G_UP_ALG_31049_replaced([11168840](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktzC4vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

**[CB012631-B-UPD001]**

[Before PR869406-26R2] ; gNB-DU shall restart the synchronization procedure (5G_UP_ALG_31049_replaced([11168840](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktzC4vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). [End PR869406-26R2]

**[End CB012631-B-UPD001]**

##### 3.25.1.2.4.0-12 Search Space Set Group management SSSG switching in case of absence of data for scheduling (ID: 11168879)

**3.25.1.2.4.0-12.0-2**  (ID: `12805168`)

Search Space Set Group management If the expected SSSG configuration state is in sparseSSSG state and the actual SSSG configuration state is in denseSSSG state and after the next _measurementDurationSSSG period (5G_UP_ALG_31723_replaced([11168784](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktyb1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the expected SSSG configuration state has not been changed, and the gNB-DU has not scheduled any DCI with new SSSG configuration then:_

· [Before CB012631-D] ; gNB-DU shall set the UE to Low Priority Proactive UL Grant state as per 5G_UP_ALG_4833_replaced([11195231](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv6iyfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End CB012631-D].

##### 3.25.1.2.4.0-13 Search Space Set Group management SSSG Switching interaction with DC-GBR (ID: 11168888)

**3.25.1.2.4.0-13.0-2**  (ID: `12717200`)

Search Space Set Group management When DC-GBR (5QI:82-88) is setup, gNB-DU must abort any ongoing switching procedure from the default SSSG and must trigger the procedure to fallback to the default SSSG.

##### 3.25.1.2.4.0-14 Search Space Set Group management SSSG Switching interaction with limited bandwidth mode (ID: 13472356)

**3.25.1.2.4.0-14.0-1**  (ID: `13472357`)

Search Space Set Group management When limited bandwidth mode is activated or deactivated ( [12505866: Nominal and limited bandwidth modes](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_6-kc8RVSEfCV0v_Ffc8sJw)) L2 PS shall assume that UEs are switched to the SSSG#0 of the corresponding BWP. The new corresponding SSSG>0 configuration should be applied once the switching criterion are met.

The U-plane applies the new setting and initializes the UE active SSSG to the default SSSG (SSSG#0), for the UEs reconfigured with the new BWP characteristics of its active BWP (no BWP switch triggered), when the RRC Reconfiguration message (DL-DCCH) is delivered to the UE (see [11153286: DL-CCCH and DL-DCCH management](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kslh8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

##### 3.25.1.2.4.0-15 Search Space Set Group management Excluding UE from DL Pre-Scheduler Candidate Set according to the UE active SSSG and its  status (ID: 11168897)

**3.25.1.2.4.0-15.0-2**  (ID: `12717199`)

Search Space Set Group management When the gNB-DU adds a UE in the CS1 list for any direction, it will check even if the UE is configured with only the default SSSG, the availability of grant capability according to the UE active SSSG and its status:

· If the UE active SSSG is confirmed, the gNB-DU uses the associated UE active SSSG slot pattern to allow or not the UE in the CS1 list.

If the target slot corresponds to a slot with at least one active search space, the UE is allowed in the CS1 list. Otherwise it is delayed for another slot.

· If the UE active SSSG is not confirmed, the gNB-DU uses the UE switching SSSG slot pattern to allow or not the UE in the CS1 list.

If the target slot corresponds to a slot with at least one active search space, the UE is allowed in the CS1 list. Otherwise it is delayed for another slot.

---

### 3.25.1.3 PDCCH Slot Pattern

#### 3.25.1.3.0-1 PDCCH Slot Pattern Document Owner Marilyn Ma;  Sankha Bhattacharya (ID: 11168913)

#### 3.25.1.3.1 Initial Slot Pattern

##### 3.25.1.3.1.0-1 Initial Slot Pattern Slot pattern initialization (ID: 11168921)

**3.25.1.3.1.0-1.0-7**  (ID: `13387826`)

Initial Slot Pattern If distributed PUCCH allocation algorithm is not applicable according to 5G_UP_ALG_2885_replaced([11123447](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and if (_NRCELL.actAperCsi is disabled OR for FDD cell):_

To build the passive PDCCH slot pattern, the 5G-L2-PS initializes it, for each bandwidth part, with the smallest control resource set duration pattern allowing the allocation for each direction expected according to the values of the uplink and downlink slot offsets (K0 and K2) configured in the cell.

If NRCELL/actIncUlPdcchCapacity is TRUE, then singleK2PerULSlot is the default state at the initial slot pattern, for each dedicated BWP, the PDCCH slot pattern shall be initialized in the UL direction only in K2min valid slots.

 with CCE split:

When several control resource set duration patterns are available, the one allowing the CCE split for the UE-Specific search spaces, if there is, is selected first for the slots which handle more than one direction. Otherwise, there is only one direction expected and the smallest PDCCH occasion is selected.

 without CCE split:

If both directions are expected in a given slot, the control resource duration pattern selected must contain 2 PDCCH occasions in the front of the slot and starting from the symbol 0. Otherwise, the pattern selected must contain only one PDCCH occasion with the smallest coreset duration allowed in the first free symbol at the front of the slot.

Then, the default PDSCH start symbol is set to the first free OFDM symbol not booked by the control resource set duration pattern selected **and starting from the OFDM symbol 0.**

Note: If the cell is a cell shared with LTE and NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false first two symbols (0,1) are reserved by LTE thus PDCCH occasion will start from symbol 2.  
Note 2: For asymmetric DSS (NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true) PDCCH occasion(s) are available in first two symbols (0,1) but the CCE split is not allowed in first two symbols (0,1). CCE split is allowed in symbol #2 if any coreset overlaps the area shared with LTE ([12620260: Resource sharing in asymmetric DSS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_NsAEcDfZEfCYiuaHdt7wgQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) 

If (_NRCELL.actAperCsi is enabled and_ for TDD cell ) or If distributed PUCCH allocation algorithm is appliable according to 5G_UP_ALG_2885_replaced([11123447](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the 5G-L2-PS initializes the PDCCH slot pattern, the first PDCCH symbol only allowing CCE split or DL direction except for TDD BI slot without Downlink PDCCH grant.**

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is true and actBbPoolExtensionTddFr1 is true and actTddCsirsOpt is false (note: actTddCsirsOpt is not get from NIDD but from L3 indicator) and actTddCsirsAllocOptimization **is false, only up to 2 PDCCH symbols (symbol 0 and symbol 1) can be used for FR1-TDD BW 10MHz and 15MHz in the Cell Specific CSI-RS slots which are determined in 5G_UP_ALG_11874_replaced([11117149](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp9rwPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

**See 5G_UP_ALG_31995_replaced([11168951](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktzp-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the initialization in slots with 2 valid K2s in tdLte config0 frame structure (5G_UP_13579_replaced([11347038](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubJMyvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

[CB012733-A]

If NRCELL.actThreeSymbolPdcch = static and 3 symbols are configured in a K1 or a K2 valid slot see [12726683](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Yap2cXEnEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) for coreset duration pattern initialization. For a K1, K2 valid slot, above restrictions are valid for the first 2 symbols and for the direction of 3rd symbol refer [12726683](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Yap2cXEnEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

[End CB012733-A]

---

##### 3.25.1.3.1.0-2 Initial Slot Pattern Initialization in tdLte config0 frame structure in slots with 2 K2s (ID: 11168951)

**3.25.1.3.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `12658435`)

Initial Slot Pattern For tdLte config0 frame structure, the initialization in slots with 2 K2s for different BW sizes is as follows.

1\. If cell BW >=20 MHz and <=40MHz [CB009422-E] or if at least one BWP is configured with size BW >=20 MHz and <=40MHz with large BWP of size >40 MHz, then in all the BWPs [End CB009422-E],

  * in slots with 2 valid K2s and 1 valid K1, gNB DU shall allocate 3 PDCCH occasions in 3 symbols. 2 occasions are used for uplink direction corresponding to the 2 K2 values and 1 occasion is used for DL direction. The initialization in the first 2 symbols is same as in 5G_UP_ALG_3962_replaced([11168921](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktzp9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * In slots with 2 valid K2 values and no valid K1, gNB DU shall initialize 2 PDCCH occasions in 2 symbols where each occasion is used for uplink direction corresponding to each K2 value.
  * CCE split is not allowed in slots with 2 K2s



2\. If cell BW >40 MHz [CB009422-E] and no BWP is configured with size BW >=20 MHz and <=40MHz[End CB009422-E], then

  * in slots with 2 valid K2s and 1 valid K1, gNB DU shall allocate 2 PDCCH occasions in 2 symbols with CCE split enabled in both symbols. Refer 5G_UP_ALG_3955_replaced([11169860](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6Xp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for CCE allocation in the 2 symbols.
  * In case of 2 K2 values but no K1, there is no CCE split and the two PDCCH occasions shall be used by 2 UL schedulers.



3\. If BW <20 MHz, then gNB DU shall initialize 2 PDCCH occasions in following two cases:

  * in slots with 2 valid K2s and 1 valid K1. gNB DU shall initialize CCE split in the CORESET associated with the first PDCCH occasion and the CORESET associated with the 2nd PDCCH occasion shall be without CCE split.
  * In slots with 2 valid K2s and no valid K1, CCE split is not allowed.



Note: Refer 5G_UP_14028_replaced([11362289](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uc7VePvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_14029_replaced([11362317](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uc7VevvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the CORESET duration pattern examples in all BW types in slots with 2 K2s for tdLte config0 frame structure.

---

##### 3.25.1.3.1.0-3 Initial Slot Pattern Static booking of PDCCH resource for the common channels (ID: 11168960)

**3.25.1.3.1.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `12590740`)

Initial Slot Pattern In the passive PDCCH slot pattern (every odd radio frames), the 5G-L2-PS updates the slots which handle the common channels by selecting the Control Resource Set duration pattern including the position and duration of the CORESET associated to the expected search space (0, 0A or 2).

The slot selection for the common channels are computed and saved in the SI/Paging contexts during the SI/paging configuration.

In the passive PDCCH slot pattern, the static booking of PDCCH resources is applied at the slots with common channels if there is:

\- SI transmission

\- paging configuration planned according to the paging search spaces and the PCCH configuration received in the PsCell_SystemInfoConfigurationReq.

The CORESET duration pattern selected has only one direction (downlink) if there is no uplink grant capability in the slot (when several PDCCH occasions are available in the CORESET duration pattern selected, then all of them are allocated to the downlink scheduler). Otherwise the slot handles uplink grant capability, the pattern selected must have one or two more PDCCH occasions to address the other directions (uplink and supplementary uplink). If it is not possible to serve the uplink, then there will be no CCE allocation to the uplink. When there is only one PDCCH occasion, for the other directions, and if the CCE Split is not allowed, the 5G-L2-PS selects alternatively the other direction.

When NRCELL.actPagingSsbOptimization=twoBeamsPerSlot and 2 PDCCH occasions for paging are valid per slot within PO all CCE allocations within this coreset are assigned to DL direction.

For DSS [CB007372-A] with NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false [End CB007372-A], when 2 CORESETs are configured in the cell, the CORESET used by the common channels is activated alone in the slot only when there is a transmission scheduled within the 2 radio frames of the passive PDCCH slot pattern for the SI. For the paging, all candidates slots, even if there is no paging waiting for transmission, are booked in the PDCCH passive slot pattern.

For FR2, the slot pattern for common channels of PCell is applied to all cells in same cell group.

---

##### 3.25.1.3.1.0-4 Initial Slot Pattern Slot Pattern for DSS (ID: 11168978)

**3.25.1.3.1.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `12590743`)

Initial Slot Pattern The PDSCH start symbol is updated for all bandwidth parts overlapping the initial one, as they are not configured with a dedicated rate matching pattern.

It is set to the first free OFDM symbol not booked by the control resource set duration pattern selected and starting from the OFDM symbol 0.

Note: If the cell is a cell shared with LTE [CB007372-A] and NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false [End CB007372-A] first two symbols (0,1) are reserved by LTE thus PDCCH occasion will start from symbol 2.

---

#### 3.25.1.3.2 Periodic Evaluation

##### 3.25.1.3.2.1 Periodic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern

###### 3.25.1.3.2.1.0-1 Periodic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern Control Resource Set duration pattern selection for regular slots (ID: 11168996)

**3.25.1.3.2.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11169000`)

Periodic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern Overview

---

**3.25.1.3.2.1.0-1.0-1.0-5**  (ID: `12816267`)

Periodic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern Every periodic evaluations, in the initialized PDCCH slot pattern, after the selection of the control resource set duration pattern for the common channels (SIB1, SI-Msg(s) transmissions and Paging slots), the 5G-L2-PS evaluates, whether for the regular slots (without CCH), it is needed to change the control resource set duration pattern initialized previously. When the modification is needed, the 5G-L2-PS defines the new control resource set duration pattern for each BWP configured in the cell and handling UE-Specific search space(s) and defines for each PDCCH occasion the expected direction.

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is true and actBbPoolExtensionTddFr1 is true and actTddCsirsOpt is false **[CB015668-A] (note: actTddCsirsOpt is not get from NIDD but from L3 indicator)**[End CB015668-A]**_* and actTddCsirsAllocOptimization_ *is false, only up to 2 PDCCH symbols (symbol 0 and symbol 1) can be used for FR1-TDD BW 10MHz and 15MHz in the Cell Specific CSI-RS slots which are determined in 5G_UP_ALG_11874_replaced([11117149](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp9rwPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

To do this, the 5G-L2-PS applies the following steps when the CCE split is allowed in the PDCCH slot pattern:

 Hardware capabilities and cell configuration to maintain the CCE split, refer 5G_UP_ALG_8914_replaced([11169023](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt0RC_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 PDCCH capabilities and capacity to maintain the CCE split if not deactivated previously, refer 5G_UP_ALG_8917_replaced([11169038](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt04EPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 PDCCH distribution due to CCE split deactivation, refer 5G_UP_ALG_8929_replaced([11169066](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt04FvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**3.25.1.3.2.1.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11169023`)

Periodic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern Hardware capabilities and cell configuration to maintain CCE split

---

**3.25.1.3.2.1.0-1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11169033`)

Periodic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern Every periodic evaluations, the initialized CORESET duration pattern with CCE split is not modified if at least one of the following conditions is met:

 The cell is configured with only one SS/PBCH and without CSI-RS for beam management (NRCELL.nrBtsBeamRefinementP2 set to false).

The hardware configuration allows to handle more than one beam (SS/PBCH or CSI-RS(BM)) per OFDM symbol whatever the number of BWP configured in the cell.

The hardware configuration allowing this capability requires eCPRI and digital beamforming or CRPI and 2 subcells with digital beamforming and with DL MU-MIMO deactivated. the beamforming type is defined in the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_1886_replaced([11111439](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the CPRI or eCPRI configuration.

For the configuration with CPRI and only one subcell, the number of connected UEs in the cell is lower or equal to 4 and they have the same active beam index.

 The hardware configuration does not allow to handle several beams (SS/PBCH or CSI-RS(BM)) per OFDM symbol and only one UE context exists in the cell and and the CORESETs configured in the cell have a duration of 1 symbol and are activated on the same symbols in the Type1, 3 and UE-Specific search spaces.

The hardware configuration which forbids several beams in one OFDM symbol is the analog beamforming. The beamforming type is defined in the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_1886_replaced([11111439](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

  * [CB009422-A-UPD001]The frame configuration is tdLte config0, cell BW is <20 MHz or >40 MHz, slot index is 2, 3, 12 or 13 and 2 K2s and 1 K1 are configured in the slot,
  * then for >40 MHz, the CORESETs associated with the two PDCCH occasions are always having CCE split. [End CB009422-A-UPD001]
  * [CB009422-D ]For <20 MHz, the CORESET associated with first PDCCH occasion is always having CCE split.[End CB009422-D ]



Otherwise, the split CCE is forbidden.

---

**3.25.1.3.2.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11169038`)

Periodic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern PDCCH capabilities and capacity to still maintain CCE split

---

**3.25.1.3.2.1.0-1.0-3.0-6**  (ID: `12646731`)

Periodic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern After this first set of checks, if the CCE split is still eligible, the 5G-L2-PS checks if CCE split is allowed in the cell (actCceSplit) and when FDM is activated, the number of connected UEs to determine if the CCE split is still allowed:

[CB007372-B]  
 For NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true and if any coreset overlaps the area shared with LTE ([12620260: Resource sharing in asymmetric DSS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_NsAEcDfZEfCYiuaHdt7wgQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) the CCE split is allowed and activated in symbol#2 regardless of value of NRCELL.actCceSplit.  
[End CB007372-B]

 If the CCE split is not allowed in the cell (PsCell_CellSetupReq.pdcchConfig.actCceSplit is set to false), the 5G-L2-PS deactivates the CCE split. The associated NIDD parameter is NRCELL.actCceSplit.

 For FR1-TDD 10MHz or 15MHz cell

  * if only one CORESET is configured in a slot and it is associated to the UE-Specific search space then the CCE split is allowed.



 When the FDM feature is activated in the PsCell_CellSetupReq (actFdmScheduling is set to true), the 5G-L2-PS checks according to the number of UE contexts in the whether the CCE split must be deactivated or not (see hereafter).

If PDCCH load is not activated to define the time domain allocation of the PDCCH resource (actDynPdcchTdMode set to disabled) under NRCELL, to maintain the CCE split, the number of existing UE context in the cell must be not be larger than the maximum value between the parameter ueCtxForCceSplitDeactivation and the number of grants allowed by the smallest part of the CCE split for the CORESET associated to the UE-Specific search space. Otherwise, the number of existing UE context is larger than the threshold and the CCE split is deactivated. The CORESET used in this check is the smallest one in the list of CORESETref,Bwp used to defined the CCE split CORESET duration pattern in the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_3949_replaced([11168409](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktv_kvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The AL used is defined by the dciDedicatedAggregationLevel. the number of CCE used to check the number of grants, corresponds to the CCE index defined in the 5G_UP_ALG_3955_replaced([11169860](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6Xp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with the CORESET selected for the CCE split and the regular slots.

If nUeCtx <= max (rounddown (_CCEsplitindex /_ ALref ), _ueCtxForCceSplitDeactivation ), then CCE split is allowed;_ **

[CB007372-B]  
else if NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true and if any coreset overlaps the area shared with LTE ([12620260: Resource sharing in asymmetric DSS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_NsAEcDfZEfCYiuaHdt7wgQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), then CCE split is allowed in symbol#2;  
[End CB007372-B]

Otherwise, CCE split is not allowed;

With,

nUeCtx:

Number of existing UE context in the cell.

_ALref :_

Aggregation Level (dciDedicatedAggregationLevel) used to identify whether the CORESET associated to a UE-Specific search space is able to be split in two directions. For 15MHz FR1-TDD and if the CORESET is associated to more than one BWP then the largest dciDedicatedAggregationLevel of all BWPs that use the CORESET for UE-Specific search spaces shall be used (dciDedicatedAggregationLevel of each BWP shall be <= 4 to allow CCE split of CORESET#0 with 8CCEs available).

_CCEsplitindex :_

Index of the CCE where the split is done as defined in the 5G_UP_ALG_3955_replaced([11169860](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6Xp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The CORESET used for the CCE split is associated to UE-Specific Search Space and the CORESET is activated at least in the symbol 0 through the "monitoringSymblosWithinSlot". if several CORESETs are compatible with this constraint, the 5G-L2-PS selects the CORESET according to the following conditions:

 All candidate CORESETs have the same duration, in that case, the one with the largest number of CCEs is selected.

 All candidate CORESETs have not the same duration, in that case, the one with the smallest duration is selected.

_ueCtxForCceSplitDeactivation :_

Parameter defining the number of UE contexts expected to deactivate the CCE split received during the cell setup procedure. The associated NIDD parameter is NRCELL.nUeCtxForCceSplitDeactivation.

Whatever the AL selection configured in BWPs within the cell, the 5G-L2-PS monitors the PDCCH blocking rate for the slots which handled the cce split in the previous monitoring window with the counters (nSlotStarvation[D,U]l and nSlotCceSplitStarvation[D,U]l) defined in the requirment 5G_UP_ALG_19443_replaced([11169338](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt2tR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). When there is at least one slot with CCE split, and the ratio between the slots with CCE split for which a PDCCH starvation was detected and the total number of CCE split slots is above the PDCCH blocking threshold (if actDynPdcchTd is set to largestBwp, then NRBTS/NRCELL/cellBwpList/pdcchBlockingThresholdUl = NRBTS/NRCELL/cellBwpList/pdcchBlockingThresholdDl **see 5G_UP_ALG_4007_replaced([11169421](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt3UWPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) defined, the 5G-L2-PS deactivates the CCE split for the next PDCCH slot pattern. **The CORESET used in this check is the smallest one in the list of CORESETref,Bwp used to defined the CCE split CORESET duration pattern in the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_3949_replaced([11168409](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktv_kvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). **If actDynPdcchTd is set to perBwp, then the ratio between the slots with CCE split for which a PDCCH starvation was detected and the total number of CCE split slots is above the PDCCH blocking threshold is checked for each BWP and each direction separately.** ****

 If the FDM feature is not activated, the number of connected UEs does not change the CCE split decision made after the first set of checks above and the actCceSplit state.

---

**3.25.1.3.2.1.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `11169066`)

Periodic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern PDCCH distribution due to CCE split deactivation

---

**3.25.1.3.2.1.0-1.0-4.0-6**  (ID: `12551663`)

Periodic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern When the split CCE is forbidden, the 5G-L2-PS, for each slots without common channels, changes the CORESET duration pattern in order to have at least 2 PDCCH occasions for each impacted slot with the direction allocation detailed hereafter.

For the following slots without enough downlink symbols, the 5G-L2-PS allocates the PDCCH occasions to the Uplink schedulers:

If NIDD parameter actEnhancedPDSCHSchSplSlot is FALSE

 The slots with less than 6 OFDM symbols allocated to the downlink when the dmrsTypeAPosition attribute is set to “pos2”.

 The slots with less than 7 OFDM symbols allocated to the downlink when the dmrsTypeAPosition attribute is set to “pos3”.

If NIDD parameter actEnhancedPDSCHSchSplSlot is TRUE**, BI4,4 slot (as specified in 5G_UP_ALG_2375_replaced([11115218](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpr-_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is not eligible for PDSCH scheduling.**

For the slot without any uplink and supplementary uplink grant capabilities, the PDCCH occasion(s) are allocated to the downlink scheduler.

For the slots which require more than one direction, the 5G-L2-PS allocates the directions as follows:

 If distributed PUCCH allocation algorithm is not appliable according to 5G_UP_ALG_2885_replaced([11123447](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and if (_actAperCsiCell is disabled in the cell setup message[Before CB014093-C-UPD001][CB014093-C]NRCELL.actAperCsi = false [End CB014093-C][End CB014093-C-UPD001]or_ cellTechnology in the cell setup message is not TDD) or for analog beamforming with several CORESETs configured in the cell but not activated on the same symbols for the Type1, Type3 or UE-Specific search spaces, or for analog beamforming with several CORESET duration:**

If NRBTS/NRCELL/actPdcchSharingWithPdsch is set to False;

 For the even slots, the first PDCCH occasion is dedicated to the downlink, and the second one dedicated to the uplink scheduler.

For the odd slots, the first PDCCH occasion is dedicated to the uplink, and the second one dedicated to the downlink scheduler.

If NRBTS/NRCELL/actPdcchSharingWithPdsch is set to True**;**

For all slots, the first pdcch occasion is dedicated to the uplink, and the second one dedicated to the downlink scheduler. **In tdLte config0 frame structure, slots with 2 valid K2s configured are not eligible for PDSCH sharing with PDCCH.**

 The first pdcch occasion is allocated to the downlink, the second one is allocated to the uplink scheduler, if at least one of the following conditions is met:

 The parameter "actAperCsiCell" is enabled in the cell setup message[Before CB014093-C-UPD001][CB014093-C] NRCELL.actAperCsi = true [End CB014093-C][End CB014093-C-UPD001] and "cellTechnology" in the cell setup message is TDD.

 The distributed PUCCH allocation algorithm is appliable according to 5G_UP_ALG_2885_replaced([11123447](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and the control resource set duration pattern for the slot has the following characteristics:

 For any even slots, handling a control resource set duration pattern with **2** PDCCH occasions and whatever the duration of each PDCCH occasion and not updated by a dynamic evaluation (5G_UP_ALG_3984_replaced([11169730](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt5JjfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or updated by a dynamic evaluation with** _*2_ *PDCCH occasions handling the same list of search spaces (Type1 or/and Type3 or/and UE-Specific).****_*_** *

 For any odd slots, handling a control resource set duration pattern with 2 **PDCCH occasions, without any search spaces for the common channels (Type0,Type0A, Type2) and not updated by a dynamic evaluation (5G_UP_ALG_3984_replaced([11169730](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt5JjfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or updated by a dynamic evaluation with 2 **PDCCH occasions handling the same list of search spaces (Type1 or/and Type3 or/and UE-Specific).****

 For analog beamforming with several CORESETs configured in the cell with a CORESET duration on 1 symbol, the Type1, Type3 and UE-Specific search spaces activate the same symbols in the monitoringSymbolWithinSlot.

When the PDCCH load is activated to define the time domain allocation of the PDCCH resources **(actDynPdcchTdMode set to largestBWP under NRCELL)** and before to broadcast the passive PDCCH slot pattern, the 5G-L2-PS will take into account the PDCCH resource usage to increase, if needed, the configured PDCCH resources (as describe in the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4000_replaced([11169133](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt1fJ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).****

Note1: In tdLte config0 frame structure, in BWs <= 40MHz or in the cell when at least one BWP is >= 20 MHz and <= 40MHz and in slots with 3 PDCCH occasions, the number of UEs scheduled in 1st UL slot can be lower than the 2nd UL slot in UE specific search spaces due to the existence of CORESET0.

Note2: UL scheduler 1 _refers to the UL slot with lowest K2 and UL scheduler 2_ refers to the UL slot with highest K2.

Note2: In tdLte config0 frame structure, in slots 2/3/12/13 PDCCH slot pattern can be predefined based on the restrictions in [11168951](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktzp-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) and bypass periodic evaluation for each PDCCH slot pattern period.

---

**3.25.1.3.2.1.0-1.0-5.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12746131`)

Periodic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern * If NRCELL.NRRIM_PROFILE.rimDlMutingMaxRange is configured, then if the muted slots support a valid K2 and PDCCH is not muted, three UL PDCCH symbols can be allocated given that the search space configuration is permitting. * If NRCELL.actEnhancedPDSCHSchSplSlot is online deactivated, then up to three UL PDCCH symbols can be allocated in the special slot with a valid K2 given that the search space configuration is permitting. This is applicable to frame structures other than tdLteConfig0.

Periodic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern States and transition of states up to 3 PDCCH symbols

**3.25.1.3.2.1.0-1.0-5.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12726797`)

Periodic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern 12726797: Periodic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern [Before CB012733-A-UPD001] If NRCELL.actThreeSymbolPdcch is Dynamic, 3 symbols are configured in a K1, K2 or K1, K2 valid slot in the UE specific search space, and actDynPdcchTdMode is Disabled, based on the number of UE contexts in the cell, switching between three states shall occur: 1\. Low load: 1\. In K1 valid slots 1 PDCCH symbol 2\. In K1, K2 valid slots, if NRCELL.actCceSplit is enabled, and when CCE split is activated, there shall be 1 PDCCH symbol in a slot or when CCE split is deactivated, there shall be 2 PDCCH symbols in a slot. * If NRCELL.actCceSplit is disabled, there shall be 2 PDCCH symbols in K1,K2 valid slots with one symbol for DL and one for UL in this state. 3\. in K2 valid slots 1 UL PDCCH symbol 2\. Medium load: 1\. in K1 valid slots 2 PDCCH symbols and 2\. in K1, K2 valid slots 3 PDCCH symbols 3\. in K2 valid slots 2 UL PDCCH symbols 3\. High load: 1\. in K1 slots 3 PDCCH symbols and 2\. in K1, K2 valid slots 3 PDCCH symbols 3\. in K2 valid slots 3 UL PDCCH symbols * State transition between each state is triggered when the number of **3.25.1.3.2.1.0-1.0-5.0-4**  (ID: `12729594`)

Periodic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern Extension to 3 PDCCH symbols when multiple BWPs are configured

---

**3.25.1.3.2.1.0-1.0-5.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12729595`)

Periodic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern [Before CB012733-A-UPD001]Handling multiple BWPs when NRCELL.actThreeSymbolPdcch is dynamic and actDynPdcchTdMode is disabled is based on the number of UEs in a BWP, the state transition and the thresholds defined in [12729940](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_LulH8nKREfCRE7eh4Ndkrw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) are applicable per BWP.

  * When both BWPs are 20-40 MHz, if smaller BWP coreset overlaps >= 50% with larger BWP CORESET (nested BWP [11169245](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt2GQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), consider the aggregation of UEs in both BWPs in determining the state of PDCCH load for the larger BWP. 
  * Both BWPs get the same number of PDCCH symbols based on the state of the larger BWP.
  * If one BWP is >40 MHz and the other is 20-40 MHz, then only the smaller BWP state is determined by the number of UEs in the smaller BWP and the corresponding threshold of the smaller BWP
  * If smaller BWP coreset overlaps < 50% with larger coreset, consider the number of UEs in each BWP separately in determining the state of PDCCH load 
  * Each BWP with size 20-40 MHz gets PDCCH symbols independently based on their states



CB012733-A-UPD001] This requirement is removed.[End CB012733-A-UPD001]

---

###### 3.25.1.3.2.1.0-2 Periodic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern Control Resource Set duration pattern selection SS/PBCH slots (ID: 11169095)

**3.25.1.3.2.1.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `12679203`)

Periodic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern If PRACH multiplexing is enabled (NRBTS/NRCELL/actPrachMultiplexing = true), to increase PDCCH capacity for scheduling PUSCH, the PDCCH occasions in SS/PBCH slots can be used for scheduling PUSCH as well. The algorithm for allocating PDCCH occasions is defined in this requirement.

For the SS/PBCH slots, the number of PDCCH occasions allowed in front of the slot could be reduced according to the position of the SS/PBCH activated, the combination of the SCSSS/PBCH and the SCSCommon for FR2 configurations.

For each SS/PBCH slot (identifiied with the formulas available in 5G_UP_ALG_2515_replaced([11117229](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp-S0vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the gNB-DU determines first the number of OFDM symbols starting from first one in the slot until one of the following conditions:

 The position of the DM-RS type A.

 The first symbol allocated to the SS/PBCH (identifiied with the formulas available in 5G_UP_ALG_2515_replaced([11117229](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp-S0vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 The last symbol before the first SS/PBCH symbol for FR2 configuration with different SCSSS/PBCH and the SCSCommon (identifiied with the formulas available in 5G_UP_ALG_2515_replaced([11117229](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp-S0vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 Symbols shared with LTE in the case of FDD carrier shared with LTE.

In FDD carrier shared with LTE [CB007372-B] and NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false [End CB007372-B], if there is no PDCCH occasion available, the gNB-DU extends the symbol selection (not shared with LTE) to the first PDCCH occasion available even if the PDCCH occasion selected overlaps SS/PCCH symbol(s).   
[CB007372-B] In FDD carrier shared with LTE and if NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true and any coreset overlaps the LTE shared area ([2620260: Resource sharing in asymmetric DSS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_NsAEcDfZEfCYiuaHdt7wgQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) then PDCCH occasion selected may overlap the SS/PBCH symbol(s). [End CB007372-B]

If PDCCH occasion cannot be allocated, no PDCCH can be scheduled in current slot. Otherwise, the gNB-DU identifies the expected number of PDCCH occasions allowed for the dedicated traffic (UE-Specific search space(s)) and the number of directions expected according to the k2 configuration. The expected number of PDCCH occasions are two, if DL/UL DCIs need to be scheduled in current slot. The expected number is one, if only DL or UL DCIs need to be scheduled.

If the number of allocated PDCCH occasions is equal or higher than expected number, the gNB-DU applies the same principle to distribute them as for the regular slot without common channels.

If the number of allocated PDCCH occasions is less than expected number, the gNB-DU applies the CCE split as defined in the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_3951_replaced([11169826](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6XoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

In FDD carrier shared with LTE, if the overlapping is detected, the gNB-DU removes any CCEs overlapping the SS/PBCH resource elements for both CCE bitmaps (DL and UL) by taking into account the list of REG overlapped by the SS/PBCH resource elements and additional REG to not cross the power budget of the OFDM symbol defined by the parameter NRBTS.NRCELL.actPdschAtSsbSlots **received at the cell setup and cell reconfiguration.**

The gNB-DU removes the additional REGs in order to maximize AL capability in each part and proportionally to size of the CCE areas.

Each set of CCEs must be alternatively allocated between DL/UL schedulers at each occurrence of the SS/PBCH slot in order to have a fair allocation for both directions over the whole radio frames. However, DL scheduler has higher priority than UL. If there is no DL CCE but there is UL CCE after the alternative allocation, the alternative allocation of the CCE shall not be performed.  
[CB007372-B] In FDD carrier shared with LTE and NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true and if any coreset overlaps the LTE shared area ([2620260: Resource sharing in asymmetric DSS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_NsAEcDfZEfCYiuaHdt7wgQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) then CCE alternation is done according to the [12658544: CCE split for asymmetric DSS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_vqrj8UqyEfC0Ye3M8ARUWQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). [End CB007372-B]

---

###### 3.25.1.3.2.1.0-3 Periodic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern Control Resources Set duration pattern selection for the slots handling the RA procedure with Dynamic Spectrum Sharing (ID: 11169108)

**3.25.1.3.2.1.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `12590746`)

Periodic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern When the DSS [CB007372-A] with NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false [End CB007372-A] is activated within SA or SA+NSA cell and two Control Resource Sets are configured in dedicated BWP(s), the 5G-L2-PS, for the slots reserved to handle the RA procedure (5G_UP_ALG_4716_replaced([11171969](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuJBIvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), activates only the CORESET associated to the Type1-PDCCH and allows the CCE split.

When only one CORESET is configured in the dedicated BWP(s), the CORSET is activated and split as any other regular slots.

###### 3.25.1.3.2.1.0-4 Periodic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern Control Resources Set duration pattern selection for the sufframes 5 and 9 with Dynamic Spectrum Sharing (ID: 11168714)

**3.25.1.3.2.1.0-4.0-3**  (ID: `12590738`)

Periodic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern When the DL PRB sharing in subframe 5 and 9 is enabled (rrmLteDLPrbSharing=TRUE 5G_UP_ALG_4722_replaced([11172097](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuJoPfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the LTE PDSCH allocation area is defined according to the Control Format Indicator (CFI) and may overlap the NR PDCCH occasion.

Therefore In the PDDCH slot pattern built every 20ms, when the NR allocation is allowed in these slots, the CCEs of the PDCCH occasion allowed in these slots and which overlap the LTE PDSCH area, are preempted (unavailable for PDCCH allocation) according to the latest EN DSS DL CELL RESOURCE AREA ALLOCATION REQUEST ( 5G_UP_ALG_4744_replaced([11172253](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuK2VPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and whatever the CCE distribution between DL and UL schedulers.

The NR DSS cell resources allocation pattern corresponds to 4 consecutive PDCCH slot patterns.

[CB007372-M] ; When NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true, several PDDCH occasions can be activated in these slots and the CCE preemption specified above is applied only for the PDCCH occasion overlapping the LTE PDSCH shared area ([12620260: Resource sharing in asymmetric DSS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_NsAEcDfZEfCYiuaHdt7wgQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). [End CB007372-M]
