##### 3.25.1.3.2.2 PDCCH Symbol Usage Control (Periodic pattern modification according to the PDCCH load)

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.1 Overview

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.1.0-1 Overview (ID: 11169142)

**3.25.1.3.2.2.1.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `11169174`)

Overview 11169174: Overview When NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is set to largestBWP (PDCCH load usage control is applied to the largest dedicated BWP) or NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is set to perBWP (PDCCH load usage control is applied per each dedicated BWP) [CB013305-C, CB013305-D] or (NRCELL/actIncUlPdcchCapacity is set to TRUE [Before CB013305-C-UPD001, CB013305-D-UPD001] and rdFixedMultipleK2ForIncUlPdcchCapacity is 0 [End CB013305-C-UPD001, CB013305-D-UPD001]) [End CB013305-C, CB013305-D], to define the time domain allocation of the PDCCH resources and before to broadcast the passive PDCCH slot pattern, the gNB-DU takes into account the PDCCH resource usage to increase, if needed, the configured PDCCH resources (as described hereafter).

The dedicated BWPs taken into account are the ones which are configured in the UE after the first DRB setup. Therefore, if the UE call setup procedure is using the initial BWP as a dedicated BWP (with DCI Format [0,1]_1 and dedicated PUCCH), and at the end the UE is switched to a dedicated BWP with an BWP ID greater than 0, then the initial BWP, configured as a temporary dedicated BWP in the UE, must not be the reference of the largest dedicated BWP. For the U-Plane, a BWP tagged as "initial" must not be used as the largest BWP if there is another BWP which is largest one too.

The gNB-DU builds the PDCCH slot pattern for the 2 next radio frames during the last 5ms of each odd radio frames and based to the PDCCH usage montoring over the last 20ms overlapping the first 15ms of the current active slot pattern and the last 5ms of the end of the previous pattern (see the figure hereafter).

[image-0][image_desc]The image depicts a timeline illustrating the concept of PDCCH (Physical Downlink Control Channel) slot patterns across different System Frame Numbers (SFNs). The timeline is divided into sections representing SFN$_{n-1}$, SFN$_n$, SFN$_{n+1}$, and SFN$_{n+2}$. Each SFN is further subdivided into subframes, labeled with numbers from 0 to n, and indicated with ellipses (...) to represent intermediate subframes. Some subframes are highlighted with a hatched pattern, signifying a specific PDCCH slot pattern. Below the subframe timeline, a "Monitoring" bar spans across the SFNs, indicating periods where monitoring is active. The diagram also highlights "Next PDCCH slot pattern under construction" for the SFN$_{n-1}$ and SFN$_{n+1}$ periods, suggesting that the patterns for these future SFNs are being prepared or defined. The text elements in the image are: \- "Previous PDCCH slot pattern" \- "SFN$_{n-1}$" \- "Current PDCCH slot pattern" \- "SFN$_n$" \- "SFN$_{n+1}$" \- "Next PDCCH slot pattern" \- "SFN$_{n+2}$" \- "subframe" \- Numbers within the subframe boxes: 0, 1, n-5, n-4, and n. \- "Monitoring" (repeated) \- "Next PDCCH slot pattern under construction" (repeated)[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_11971.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

For Algorithm of periodic pattern modification according to the PDCCH load [CB013305-C, CB013305-D] when NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is set to largestBWP [End CB013305-C, CB013305-D], see 5G_UP_ALG_17373_replaced([11169178](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt1fPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For Algorithm of periodic pattern modification according to the PDCCH load for multipe dedicated BWPs in TDD FR1 [CB013305-C, CB013305-D] when NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is set to perBWP [End CB013305-C, CB013305-D], see 5G_UP_ALG_16720_replaced([11169210](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt2GNvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For Algorithm of periodic pattern modification according to the PDCCH load [CB013305-C, CB013305-D] when NRCELL/actIncUlPdcchCapacity is set to TRUE and NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is set to Disabled , see 5G_UP_ALG_30681_replaced([11169231](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt2GP_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).[End CB013305-C, CB013305-D]

---

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.1.0-2 Overview Algorithm of periodic pattern modification according to the PDCCH load (ID: 11169178)

**3.25.1.3.2.2.1.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11169204`)

Overview 11169204: Overview To determined the PDCCH slot pattern for the next 20ms, the gNB-DU applies the following steps **if** NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is set to largestBWP:****

 Initialize the PDCCH slot pattern with the smallest PDCCH size allowed for the next 20ms, including the common channels, (5G_UP_ALG_3961_replaced([11168917](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktzp8_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with the control resource set duration pattern (5G_UP_ALG_3975_replaced([11168992](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt0RBPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 Compute the initial PDCCH slot pattern characteristics (5G_UP_ALG_4002_replaced([11169280](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt2GRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 Compute the expected resources for the next 20ms (5G_UP_ALG_4006_replaced([11169416](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt3UV_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) according to the resource usage in the last 20ms (5G_UP_ALG_4002_replaced([11169280](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt2GRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

  * **[CB013305-C, CB013305-D] If NRCELL/actIncUlPdcchCapacity is set to TRUE, then after calculating the expected resources in UL, the required number of PDCCH symbols in UL (nSymbolsReqUL = nCceReqUL/coresetSize) is compared against a predefined threshold. If the UL PDCCH resources required in the next 20 ms period exceed the threshold, then from each relevant slot, one symbol becomes eligible for UL PDCCH (refer 5G_UP_ALG_30709_replaced([11169569](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt4icvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for detailed algorithm). **[End CB013305-C, CB013305-D]****



 Modification of the PDCCH slot pattern with the expected resources (5G_UP_ALG_4014_replaced([11169598](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt4iefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Select the CORESET duration pattern according to the number of symbols and PDCCH occasions expected (5G_UP_ALG_4020_replaced([11169720](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt5Ji_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and update the search space list (5G_UP_ALG_4022_replaced([11168667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktx0wfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), PDCCH start symbol before to broadcast the pattern to both schedulers.

[image-0][image_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a process for adjusting PDCCH slot pattern capacity. The flowchart begins with adjusting PDCCH slot pattern capacity and determining initial pattern characteristics. It then retrieves the last 20ms PDCCH resource usage. The process branches based on resource availability for downlink and uplink. For downlink, it checks if resources are to be released or increased, leading to computations for releasing, adding, or keeping DL resources. Similarly, for uplink, it checks for resource release or increase, leading to computations for releasing, adding, or keeping UL resources. Following these computations, an algorithm for increased UL load (5G_UP_ALG_30709) is applied. Resources are then adjusted for both directions based on the largest PDCCH capacity. This is followed by uplink and downlink resource mapping. The process then moves to selecting a CORESET duration pattern for each slot and updating the search space list for the CORESET duration pattern. Finally, it selects the initial BWP CORESET duration pattern based on the presence and direction of CORESET(0) in dedicated BWP, broadcasts the passive PDCCH slot pattern to both schedulers, and ends.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_11975.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

**Note: Figures are for illustration. The sequence of 'Resource to increase' and 'Resource to release' refers to 5G_UP_ALG_4007_replaced([11169421](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt3UWPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

**[CB013305-C-UPD005, , CB013305-D-UPD005] change in figure**[EndCB013305-C-UPD005, , CB013305-D-UPD005]****

---

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.1.0-3 Overview Algorithm of periodic pattern modification according to the PDCCH load for multipe dedicated BWPs in TDD FR1 (ID: 11169210)

**3.25.1.3.2.2.1.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11169227`)

Overview 11169227: Overview If **NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is set to perBWP** in a TDD FR1 cell with n > 1 dedicated BWPs configured, before broadcasting the passive PDCCH slot pattern, the gNB-DU takes the PDCCH resource usage of a dedicated BWP into account if needed to increase or decrease allocated PDCCH resources of each BWP (as described hereafter).****

To determine the PDCCH slot pattern for the next 20ms, the gNB-DU applies the 5 steps in same order as in 5G_UP_ALG_17373_replaced([11169178](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt1fPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with following differences.

  * **_*Step 3 which is "Compute the expected resources for the next 20ms (5G_UP_ALG_16772_replaced([11169394](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt3UU_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) according to the resource usage in the last 20ms" is computed per dedicated BWP,_***
  * **[CB013305-C, CB013305-D] If NRCELL/actIncUlPdcchCapacity is set to TRUE, then after calculating the expected resources in UL, the required number of PDCCH symbols in UL (nSymbolsReqUL = nCceReqUL/coresetSize) is compared against a predefined threshold [Before PR832886-25R3] in large BWP or small BWP(s) [PR832886-25R3] for each dedicated BWP(s) [End PR832886-25R3]. If the UL PDCCH resources required in the next 20 ms period exceed the threshold in at least one [PR832886-25R3] dedicated [End PR832886-25R3] BWP, then in each relevant slot, the same symbol becomes eligible for UL PDCCH (refer 5G_UP_ALG_30709_replaced([11169569](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt4icvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for detailed algorithm) in all the dedicated BWPs [PR832886-25R3] and powerSaving BWP [End PR832886-25R3]. **[End CB013305-C, CB013305-D]****
  * **Step 4 "Modification of the PDCCH slot pattern with the expected resources" (5G_UP_ALG_4014_replaced([11169598](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt4iefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is done separately per nested BWP (5G_UP_ALG_16892_replaced([11169245](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt2GQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with highest priority given to the largest dedicated BWP and lowest priority given to the smallest dedicated BWP and**
  * **_*Step 5 "Select the CORESET duration pattern according to the number of symbols and PDCCH occasions expected and update the search space list (5G_UP_ALG_4020_replaced([11169720](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt5Ji_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) PDCCH start symbol before to broadcast the pattern to both schedulers" are done separately per each dedicated BWP. See figure below for complete flow of the algorithm._***



[image-0][image_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a process related to PDCCH slot pattern capacity adjustment in a 5G network. The flowchart begins with "Adjust PDCCH slot pattern capacity" and "Determine the initial pattern characteristics." The main part of the flowchart, enclosed in a dashed rectangle, details resource management based on PDCCH resource usage. It starts with "Get the last 20ms PDCCH resource usage." From there, it branches into decisions regarding downlink and uplink resource release and increase. For downlink, if resources are to be released, "Compute DL resources to release." If not, it checks if resources are to increase. If yes, "Compute DL resources to add." If no, "Compute DL resources to keep." Similarly, for uplink, if resources are to be released, "Compute UL resources to release." If not, it checks if resources are to increase. If yes, "Compute UL resources to add." If no, "Compute UL resources to keep." Following these resource computations, there's a step labeled "Algorithm for increased UL load (5G_UP_ALG_30709)." After the dashed rectangle, the flowchart continues with: \- "Adjust resources for both direction according to the largest PDCCH capacity." \- "Uplink and Downlink resources mapping." \- "Select CORESET duration pattern for each slot." \- "For CORESET duration pattern: Update the search Space list." \- "Select the initial BWP CORESET duration pattern according to the presence and direction of the CORESET(0) in dedicated BWP." \- "Broadcast the passive PDCCH slot pattern to both schedulers." The flowchart concludes with an "End" node. Additionally, there are numbered annotations pointing to specific sections: \- "3. PDCCH resource usage monitoring and compute the expected resources (repeated per dedicated BWP)" points to the section starting with "Get the last 20ms PDCCH resource usage." \- "4. Modification of the initialized PDCCH slot pattern (repeated per nested BWP)" points to the "Adjust resources for both direction according to the largest PDCCH capacity" step. \- "5. CORESET duration pattern selection and update the search space list (repeated per dedicated BWP)" points to the "Select CORESET duration pattern for each slot" step.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_11978.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

**Note: Figures are for illustration. The sequence of 'Resource to increase' and 'Resource to release' refers to 5G_UP_ALG_4007_replaced([11169421](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt3UWPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

**[CB013305-C-UPD005, CB013305-D-UPD005] change in figure**[End CB013305-C-UPD005, CB013305-D-UPD005]****

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.1.0-4 Overview Algorithm of periodic pattern modification according to the PDCCH load for increased UL capacity (ID: 11169231)

**3.25.1.3.2.2.1.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `12727907`)

Overview Algorithm of periodic pattern modification according to the PDCCH load for increased UL capacity

---

**3.25.1.3.2.2.1.0-4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12727908`)

Overview 12727908: Overview **[CB013305-C, CB013305-D]**

When NRCELL/actIncUlPdcchCapacity is set to TRUE and NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is set to disabled, gNB shall determine the PDCCH slot pattern for the next 20ms in the following steps. Compared to 5G_UP_ALG_17373_replaced([11169178](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt1fPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the main differences (highlighted in red in the figure below) are

  * PDCCH resource usage in the previous PDCCH slot pattern is only monitored in UL [Before PR834382-25R3] in in largest BWP [PR834382-25R3] in the dedicated BWP(s) [End PR834382-25R3].
  * Expected resources for the next 20 ms are computed only for UL [Before PR834382-25R3] in largest BWP [PR834382-25R3] in the dedicated BWP(s) [End PR834382-25R3].
  * If the UL PDCCH resources required in the next 20 ms period exceed a predifined threshold in [Before PR834382-25R3] largest BWP [PR834382-25R3] the dedicated BWP(s) [End PR834382-25R3], then the relevant slots become eligible for UL PDCCH in all the dedicated BWPs (refer 5G_UP_ALG_30709_replaced([11169569](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt4icvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for detailed algorithm). **[Before CB013305-C-UPD005, CB013305-D-UPD005]Then CCE split is disabled in the initial slot pattern (5G_UP_ALG_8917_replaced([11169038](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt04EPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**[End CB013305-C-UPD005, CB013305-D-UPD005]****



[image-0][image_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a process related to PDCCH slot patterns in a 5G network. The flowchart uses rectangular boxes for process steps and a diamond shape for a decision point. Arrows indicate the flow of the process. Here's a breakdown of the steps: 1\. **Adjust PDCCH slot pattern capacity** : This is the starting point, indicating an initial adjustment of the PDCCH slot pattern capacity. 2\. **Determine the initial pattern characteristics** : The next step involves determining the characteristics of this initial pattern. 3\. **Get the last 20 ms UL PDCCH resource usage** : This step focuses on obtaining information about the usage of UL PDCCH resources over the last 20 milliseconds. 4\. **Compute the expected UL resources** : Following the resource usage, the expected UL resources are computed. 5\. **Algorithm for increased UL load (5G_UP_ALG_30709)** : This section, enclosed in a red border, deals with an algorithm for increased UL load. * **Check nSymbolsReqUI >= threshold**: A decision point is reached, checking if the required number of symbols (nSymbolsReqUI) is greater than or equal to a threshold. * **Yes** : If the condition is met, the process moves to "Make symbols in the relevant DL slots eligible for UL PDCCH". * **No** : If the condition is not met, the process proceeds directly to the next main step. 6\. **Make symbols in the relevant DL slots eligible for UL PDCCH** : This step, executed when the threshold condition is met, makes symbols in relevant DL slots eligible for UL PDCCH. 7\. **Modification of the initialized slot pattern** : After the decision point (or the eligibility step), the initialized slot pattern is modified. 8\. **Select CORESET duration pattern for each slot and update the search space list** : The next step involves selecting a CORESET duration pattern for each slot and updating the search space list. 9\. **Select the initial BWP CORESET duration pattern according to the presence and direction of the CORESETO in dedicated BWP** : This step focuses on selecting the initial BWP CORESET duration pattern based on the presence and direction of CORESETO in a dedicated BWP. 10\. **Broadcast the passive PDCCH slot pattern to the schedulers** : Finally, the passive PDCCH slot pattern is broadcast to the schedulers. 11\. **End** : The flowchart concludes with an "End" state.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_11980.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

Overview Algorithm of periodic pattern modification according to the PDCCH load for increased UL capacity

---

**3.25.1.3.2.2.1.0-4.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12727154`)

Overview 12727154: Overview **[CB013305-C, CB013305-D]**

When NRCELL/actIncUlPdcchCapacity is set to TRUE and NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is set to disabled, gNB shall determine the PDCCH slot pattern for the next 20ms in the following steps. Compared to 5G_UP_ALG_17373_replaced([11169178](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt1fPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the main differences (highlighted in red in the figure below) are

  * Expected resources for the next 20 ms are computed only for UL [Before PR834382-25R3] in largest BWP [PR834382-25R3] in the dedicated BWP(s) [End PR834382-25R3].
  * If the UL PDCCH resources required in the next 20 ms period exceed a predifined threshold in [Before PR834382-25R3] largest BWP [PR834382-25R3] the dedicated BWP(s) [End PR834382-25R3], then the relevant slots become eligible for UL PDCCH in all the dedicated BWPs (refer 5G_UP_ALG_30709_replaced([11169569](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt4icvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for detailed algorithm). **[Before CB013305-C-UPD005, CB013305-D-UPD005]Then CCE split is disabled in the initial slot pattern (5G_UP_ALG_8917_replaced([11169038](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt04EPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**[End CB013305-C-UPD005, CB013305-D-UPD005]****

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.1.0-5 Overview Definition of a nested BWP (ID: 11169245)

**3.25.1.3.2.2.1.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `11169270`)

Overview 11169270: Overview Let there be dedicated BWPs B1, B2 and B3 where larger BWPs are represented by lower numbered indices.

  * Each of these BWPs have an associated set of UEs U1, U2 and U3 that belong to the respective BWPs (this is a volatile property when power saving BWP is enabled as UEs can switch between BWPs).
  * Each of these BWPs have an associated set of PRBs/RBGs where the UEs can be allocated resources denoted as R1, R2 and R3. These sets of PRBs typically have the relationship R3 R2 R1.
  * Each of these BWPs have an associated set of CCEs where these UEs can be allocated PDCCH resources denoted as C1, C2 and C3. Note that these sets of CCEs can be fully overlapping, partially overlapping or non-overlapping.



A nested BWP can be denoted βi such that the lower-numbered indices represent larger nested BWPs. A nested BWP can be defined as follows:

[image-0][image_desc]The image contains a pseudocode snippet. The pseudocode describes a process involving nested loops and conditional statements. Here is the extracted text: For i = 1 to 3 βᵢ = {Bᵢ} For j = i + 1 to 3 If |Cⱼ ∩ Cᵢ| / |Cᵢ| > 0.5, then βᵢ = βᵢ ∪ Bⱼ End for j End for i[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_11983.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

Each nested BWP is associated with a set of UEs, RBGs/PRBs and CCEs as follows:

[image-1][image_desc]The image contains three bullet points with mathematical equations. * $U_{\beta_i} = U_{B_j \in \beta_i} U_j$ * $R_{\beta_i} = R_{B_j \in \beta_i} R_j$ * $C_{\beta_i} = C_i$[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_11983.002.png[/image_path][/image-1]

[CB008954-H] The algorithm above is also valid for 4 BWPs [End CB008954-H]

---

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.2 Initial PDCCH slot pattern characteristics

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.2.0-1 Initial PDCCH slot pattern characteristics (ID: 11169280)

**3.25.1.3.2.2.2.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `12730659`)

Initial PDCCH slot pattern characteristics When NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is set to largestBWP (PDCCH load usage control is activated) or NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is set to perBWP (PDCCH load usage control if n > 1 dedicated BWPs are configured in a TDD FR1 cell) **or NRCELL/actIncUlPdcchCapacity is set to TRUE** to define the time domain allocation of the PDCCH resources, then before broadcasting the passive PDCCH slot pattern, the gNB-DU takes into account the PDCCH resource usage to increase, if needed, the configured PDCCH resources (as described hereafter).****

For that purpose, the gNB-DU computes the following data which is common to all BWPs configured in the cell:

 The number of slots with a coreset shared between DL and UL schedulers in the passive pattern (nSlotCceSplit). If NRCELL/actDynPdcchTd is set to largestBWP only one shared CORESET and if NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is set to perBWP only one shared CORESET per BWP **is allowed per slot linked to a UE-Specific search space, but it could be on 1 or 2 OFDM symbols.**

 The number of symbols configured for the downlink and uplink (nSymbInitDl ; nSymbInitUl)

 The number of CCEs configured in each direction (nCceInitDl ; nCceInitUl), including the CCE of the CORESET shared between both directions. For this CORESET, half of the CCEs are counted per direction (even if it is not true all the time).

 The number of slots with DL and UL grant capabilities (CCE allocated to a given direction greater than 0) and the number of slots with at least one direction (DL or/and UL) (nSlotGrantInitDl ; nSlotGrantInitUl, nSlotGrantInit).

**If NRCELL/actIncUlPdcchCapacity is set to TRUE and NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is set to LargestBWP or disabled, then above calculations are done similar to NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is set to largestBWP case where the calculations are relevant to only largest BWP. If NRCELL/actIncUlPdcchCapacity is set to TRUE and NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is set to perBWP, then above calculations are done similar NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is set to perBWP case where the calculations are relevant to all BWPs.**

---

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.3 Resource usage monitoring

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.3.0-1 Resource usage monitoring (ID: 11169308)

**3.25.1.3.2.2.3.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11169324`)

Resource usage monitoring When NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is set to largestBWP (PDCCH load usage control is activated) to define the time domain allocation of the PDCCH resources, the gNB-DU checks the PDCCH resource usage in the last 20ms and determines the expected resources for each direction for the 2 next radio frames.

[CB013305-C] When NRCELL/actIncUlPdcchCapacity is set to TRUE and NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is Disabled, then PDCCH resource usage monitoring is only in the UL direction. [End CB013305-C]

The gNB-DU monitors the unexpected lack of PDCCH resources which forbid to fulfil the PDSCH and the PUSCH, as well as the number of unused CCEs.

For each slots starting from the last subframe 5 of the previous PDCCH slot pattern to the current subframe 5 of the odd radio frame triggering the process to build the next PDCCH slot pattern, the CORESET(s) monitored are the ones associated to the UE-Specific search spaces with DCI Format x_1, and with the largest number of RBs.

The monitoring process saves for each direction:

 The number symbols configured (nSymbDl ; nSymbUl) and the number of CCE configured (nCceDl ; nCceUl) as detailed in the 5G_UP_ALG_19442_replaced([11169329](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt2tRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 The number of slots where a lack of PDCCH resource are detected, leading unused resources in the shared channels PDSCH for the downlink (nSlotStarvationDl) and PUSCH for the uplink (nSlotStarvationUl) as detailed in the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_19443_replaced([11169338](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt2tR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 The number of free CCEs (not used, not pre-empted) after the scheduling in each slot and associated to the largest frequency domain CORESET linked to the UE-Specific search spaces as detailed in the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_19444_replaced([11169364](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt2tTPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.3.0-2 Resource usage monitoring Number of symbols and CCEs configured (ID: 11169329)

**3.25.1.3.2.2.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `12731029`)

Resource usage monitoring The monitoring process saves for each direction:

 The number symbols configured (nSymbDl ; nSymbUl).

If the largest CORESET is on 1 OFDM symbol and CCEs are share between UL and DL, half of the CCEs is counted per direction and half of the PDCCH symbol is counted per direction.

If the largest CORESET is on 2 OFDM symbols and CCEs are share between UL and DL, half of the CCEs is counted per direction and the number of PDCCH symbol is spread in both directions (1+1)

Without CCE split, the CORESET is fully allocated to a direction and its duration is the number of symbol allocated to the direction.

The configurations with a CORESET on 2 symbols used for the dedicated traffic, if present, could be 5, 10, 20 MHz in 15 kHz, 20 MHz in 30kHz, 50 MHz or 100MHz in 120kHz. For other configurations, the CORESET on 2 symbols, if present, is mainly for specific allocation.

[CB012733-B] If NRCELL.actThreeSymbolPdcch is Dynamic and actDynPdcchTdMode is not disabled, the 3rd symbol shall be only fully DL or fully UL regardless of CCE split is activated in the slot or not thus the symbol and CCEs should be counted accordingly to the direction. [End CB012733-B]

 The number of CCE configured (nCceDl ; nCceUl)

The number of configured CCE is the concatenation of the latest 5 subframes from the previous PDCCH slot pattern and the 15 first subframes of the current active PDCCH slot pattern.

When the CORESET is shared between both directions, the same principle as for the symbols is applied (see above). Only the CCEs associated to the largest CORESET in frequency domain are counted, when several CORESETs are overlapping. Otherwise, the CCEs are defined by the CORESET size and duration.

---

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.3.0-3 Resource usage monitoring Number of slots with lack of PDCCH resources (ID: 11169338)

**3.25.1.3.2.2.3.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `11169359`)

Resource usage monitoring [Before 04980679-25R3] ; The monitoring process saves for each direction **[CB013305-C] (If NRCELL/actIncUlPdcchCapacity is set to TRUE and NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is Disabled, then monitoring process saves the following parameters only in the UL direction.)**[End CB013305-C]:****

 The number of slots where a lack of PDCCH resource are detected, leading unused resources in the shared channels PDSCH for the downlink (nSlotStarvationDl) and PUSCH for the uplink (nSlotStarvationUl).

At each time, the schedulers are not able to fulfil the shared channels (PDSCH for the DL, and PUSCH for the UL), due lack of PDCCH resources (UE rejected) with the following conditions, then the nSlotStarvation[D,U]l is pegged:

 No more enough consecutive CCEs (according to the list of AL allowed) are available to allocated this type of Aggregation Level.

 At least one UE, not scheduled by a Low Priority UL proactive grant (5G_UP_ALG_4833_replaced([11195231](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv6iyfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or a TCP Boost proactive grant (5G_UP_ALG_16872_replaced([11195403](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv7w8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), is waiting for PDCCH resources and maximum number of scheduled UEs per slot in the considered direction has not been reached.

 At least, the shared channels (PDSCH, PUSCH) handle at least one initial transmission.

 The PDCCH is reduced (CCE split activated) in the slot, there is no more free CCEs and the shared channel (PDSCH or PUSCH) handles only retransmission(s) leading to not fulfil it.

 No resource allocation for shared channels in the slot are skipped due to the overload reason.

 The following starvations (nSlotCceSplitStarvation[D,U]l) are not reported in the regular starvation counters (reported to PM counters), but are taken into account to measure the PDCCH blocking threshold on CCE split slots and to increase/decrease the PDCCH resources decision:

 The PDCCH is reduced (CCE split activated) in the slot, there is no more free PDCCH candidates for a rejected UE, even if there are enough free consecutive CCEs available for the expected AL in the expected direction. The lack of free PDCCH candidates could be due to the previous UE(s) PDCCH allocation or the missing search space (Search Space not allowed in the slot due to the presence of the CCE split for the UE-Specific search space(s)) or the CCE distribution incompatible with the expected AL.

 No resource allocation for shared channels in the slot are skipped due to the overload reason.[End 04980679-25R3]

[04980679-25R3] ; The monitoring process applies the following rules for each direction **[CB013305-C] (If NRCELL/actIncUlPdcchCapacity is set to TRUE and NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is Disabled, then monitoring process apply the following rukes only in the UL direction).**[End CB013305-C]:****

The potential sources of the PDCCH blocking are the followings:

· The expected search space is not allowed or not available in the PDCCH occasion:

\- When the combination of COERSETs is incompatible with the CCEs resource sharing between UL and DL for at least the UE-Specific search space(s).

\- When the PDCCH occasion used by DL or UL scheduler is not configured with the expected search space(s) (Type1 & Type3 configured in only one symbol among several). 

· The initial CCE sharing distribution between UL and DL schedulers (before any PDCCH allocation) is not compatible with the requested Aggregation Level for the UE (ex: CCE sharing with 4 CCEs for each direction in the same PDCCH occasion and the requested AL for the RNTI is AL8).

· No candidate configured for the expected AL in the PDCCH occasion allocated and another PDCCH occasion is able to handle this AL.

· Not enough PDCCH candidates configured in the search space to guarantee at least one opportunity to grant the UE in a PDCCH occasion where the CCEs are shared between UL and DL schedulers (ex: one candidate A8 configured in the search space associated to a CORESET with 16 CCEs).

When this case is detected, the scheduler did not check yet whether for this RNTI in the target slot will have a configured PDCCH candidate for the expected direction or not. Therefore, the UE may or may not be scheduled, nevertheless, the U-Plane checks and updates the PDCCH, if needed, to guarantee the availability the expected resources by deactivating the CCE split in a slot with at least one slot delay.

· During the PDCCH allocation for a RNTI in the target slot, there are enough consecutive CCEs free starting at a CCE index compatible to the initial expected AL and the scheduler is not able to find a free PDCCH candidate in the PDCCH occasion allocated for the initial expected AL and for the reselected AL (next more robust AL if allowed without power mitigation) and for the previous AL (less robust) with power mitigation.

· During the PDCCH allocation for a RNTI in the target slot, there are no more enough consecutive CCEs free starting at a CCE index compatible to the initial expected AL and the reselected AL(s) (more robust without power mitigation or less robust with power mitigation).

To count the number of slots with not enough PDCCH resources and to determine whether the PDCCH starvation counter, the U-Plane checks the shared channel for each BWP where a RNTI is blocked due to the lack of PDCCH (list of cases above). The number of RBs available in a BWP depends on the DCI Format used (1_0, 0_0 or x_1), the size of the COERSET(0), the size of the initial Uplink BWP and the BWP size itself.

The total number of RBs allowed for the PDSCH can be lower than the size of the BWP according to the cell configuration (blanked RBs, power available for PDSCH in SS/PBCH and/or CSI-RS for tracking slots) or according internal constraints (pooling...)

For each BWP it is possible to compute 4 sets of shared resources according to the DCI Format:

· Downlink shared Resource Blocks for DCI Format 1_0 in a common search space.

The number of RB is determined by the CORESET(0) size, and the start RB is defined by the first CRB of the COERSET used in the common search space. If the BWP is configured with a Random Access Channel (RACH), the CORESET linked to the Type1 and the CORESET linked to the Type3 define the Downlink shared resource blocks for DCI Format 1_0. If both PDCCH does not have the same CORESET, then there are 2 set of RBs for DCI Format 1_0. The set of RBs for DCI 1_0 can be computed at the cell setup. 

· Downlink shared Resource Blocks for DCI Format 1_1 in an UE-Specific search space.

When the Resource Allocation Type 0 is used, the BWP is segmented in Resource Block Group (RBG) where the sizes of RBG depends on the size and location of BWP. If for RBGs, at least one RB is not available due to any constraint, the whole RBG is not available for PDSCH allocation.

· Uplink shared Resource Blocks for DCI Format 0_0 in a common search space.

The number of RB is determined by the smallest size between the uplink initial BWP and the uplink BWP considered.  
The start RB is defined by the first CRB of the considered BWP.

· Uplink shared Resource Blocks for DCI Format 0_1 in an UE-Specific search space.

The minimum RB allocation for a RNTI depends on the type of data to send, the MCS (radio condition for the RNTI), the number of PDSCH symbols and the number of RBs. If the data can be segmented, the smallest size is 1 byte, otherwise the data can not be segmented (ex RLC Status) and the minimum number of RBs expected can be more than 1 RB. On top, the U-Plane will add the MAC and RLC headers. At each time a RNTI is blocked due to the PDCCH, the U-Plane determines the minimum number of RB expected for the RNTI according to the internal constraint, its current radio condition (MCS) and the number of PDSCH symbols in the current slot.

Then, at the end of the slot, if there is not enough free resources for the smallest expected RB allocation according to the DCI Format, the U-Plane considers the shared channel fully used. 

To check the PDCCH usage at the end of the slot, the U-Plane for each BWP and DCI Format types identifies the available consecutive CCEs aligned to the location of the whole PDCCH candidates for the AL allowed (per search space type (Type1,Type3 and UE-Specific) according their CORESET Id). Then, at the end of the slot, according to the RNTI AL expected and blocked, the U-Plane checks whether there is a valid PDCCH candidate which is started at a CCE index compatible with AL and with enough consecutive CCEs in the expected CORESET.

When the RNTI will be not scheduled for the 4 first cases linked to the PDCCH configuration and the current PDCCH slot pattern, it is expected to not peg the starvation counters, because, the objective is to check and if needed to update in few slots the PDCCH to guarantee the availability of the expected resources to schedule the RNTI. Nevertheless, the PDCCH slot pattern needs to take into account the number of slots with not enough PDCCH resource whatever the root cause to build the PDCCH slot pattern for the next 20ms.

When the RNTI using DCI Format x_1 will be not scheduled due to a PDCCH blocking during the PDCCH allocation process (2 last cases in the PDCCH blocking reasons), the U-Plane takes into account the lack of PDCCH to estimate the number of CCEs needed in the next 20ms and check whether the starvation counter(s) must be pegged or not as specified hereafter.

If the shared resources are not fully used (see above) and the number of expected UE to be scheduled is not reached, the starvation counter(s) (nSlotStarvation[D,U]l) can be pegged if: 

· At least one RNTI is blocked with DCI Format x_1 for an initial transmission and it has not the request class set to Low Priority UL proactive grant ([11195231](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv6iyfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) or a TCP Boost proactive grant ([11195403](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv7w8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

· No RNTI are skipped due to overload reason or no RNTI is blocked for any other reason which is not linked to the PDCCH (ex: lack of PUCCH Format [1,3]).

· ~~The PDCCH occasion does not share the PDCCH resources between UL and DL (CCE split). This case needs to be correlate with the number of slots used (when the slot usage is low (lot of slots are unused), the PDCCH starvation is not an issue. If the usage ratio is high the pegging counter is welcome)~~.

[End 04980679-25R3]

---

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.3.0-4 Resource usage monitoring Number of free CCEs (ID: 11169364)

**3.25.1.3.2.2.3.0-4.0-4**  (ID: `11169384`)

Resource usage monitoring The monitoring process saves for each direction [CB013305-C] (If NRCELL/actIncUlPdcchCapacity is set to TRUE and NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is Disabled, then monitoring process saves the following parameters only in the UL direction.) [End CB013305-C]:

 The number of free CCEs (not used, not pre-empted) after the scheduling in each slot and associated to the largest frequency domain CORESET linked to the UE-Specific search spaces.

If the number of free CCEs for a given direction is larger than the number of CCE configured in the same direction, the number of free CCE is set to the number of CCE configured.

If actPdcchCceFragmentControl is set to true, for the slots with lack of PDCCH resources (5G_UP_ALG_19443_replaced([11169338](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt2tR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the number of free CCEs shall be set to zero.

Note: pdcchCceFragmentControl is defined from NRCELL/cellBwpList/actPdcchCceFragmentControl

---

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.4 Resource usage monitoring for multiple dedicated BWPs in TDD FR1

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.4.0-1 Resource usage monitoring for multiple dedicated BWPs in TDD FR1 (ID: 11169394)

**3.25.1.3.2.2.4.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11169411`)

Resource usage monitoring for multiple dedicated BWPs in TDD FR1 When NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is set to perBWP (PDCCH load usage control is activated per dedicated BWP), following metrics are monitored during step3 of the dynamic PDCCH algorithm for multiple BWPs in 5G_UP_ALG_16720_replaced([11169210](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt2GNvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

1\. The number of symbols allocated to dedicated BWP i for each direction (nSymbDl[i]; nSymbUl[i]).

If two dedicated BWPs B1, B2 satisfy the definition of a nested BWP in 5G_UP_ALG_16892_replaced([11169245](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt2GQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), then if BWP B1 gets a PDCCH symbol, both nSymbDl[1] and nSymbDl[2] are incremented for DL or nSymbUl[1] and nSymbUl[2] are incremented for UL. If only B2 gets a PDCCH symbol, nSymbX[2] is incremented for the respective direction.

Otherwise, if BWP B1 gets a PDCCH symbol, nSymbX[1] is incremented for the respective direction, and if B2 gets a PDCCH symbol, nSymbX[2] is incremented for the respective direction.

2\. The number of CCEs allocated to dedicated BWP i for each direction (nCceDl[i], nCceUl[i]).

The number of CCEs allocated to UEs of dedicated BWP i in each direction (nCceDl[i], nCceUl[i]) are counted. CCEs allocated to the UEs of dedicated BWP i shall increment nCceDl[i] for DL and nCceUl[i] for UL.

3\. The number of free CCEs (not used and not pre-empted) after the scheduling in each slot and associated to each dedicated BWP (nFreeCceDl[i] and nFreeCceUl[i]).

The number of free CCEs (not used and not pre-empted) after the scheduling in each slot and associated to dedicated BWP i for each direction (nFreeCceDl[i] and nFreeCceUl[i]) are counted. CCEs allocated to UEs of dedicated BWP j ≠ i in the CORESET of dedicated BWP i shall be preempted from the count for BWP i.

4\. Τhe slots wherein a lack of PDCCH resources leading to unused resources in the shared channels are detected for dedicated BWP i for each direction (nSlotStarvationDl[i], nSlotStarvationUl[i]).

For dedicated BWP i, the slots wherein a lack of PDCCH resources is detected (e.g. lack of CCEs in a CORESET for a UE) leading to unused resources (e.g. PRBs/RBGs) in the shared channels shall increment nSlotStarvationX[i]. If PDSCH resources are unused in DL, nSlotStarvationDl[i] is incremented, and if PUSCH resources are unused in UL, nSlotStarvationUl[i] is incremented.

For dedicated BWP i, [CB008927-I] if the NIDD parameter NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = false, [End CB008927-I] an RBG cannot be used/unused for the PDSCH for a UE of BWP i because another UE from dedicated BWP j ≠ i is using at least a portion of that RBG. Then, the RBG shall not be considered free for BWP, i. The RBG size considered here shall be the RBG size of BWP i. 

[CB008927-I] else

a PRB from PDSCH area (n) cannot be used/unused for a UE of BWP i for PDSCH or PUSCH, because another UE from dedicated BWP j≠i is using the PRB from PDSCH area (n), and thus the PRB should not be considered free within PDSCH area (n) in BWP i [End CB008927-I].

For dedicated BWP i, if a PRB cannot be used/unused for a UE of BWP i for PUSCH because another UE from dedicated BWP j ≠ i is using that PRB, then the PRB shall not be considered free for BWP i.

For dedicated BWP i, nSlotStarvationX[i] is incremented by 1 when at least 1 UE from dedicated BWP is i rejected in a slot. A dedicated BWP is not able to fulfill the shared channels due to a lack of PDCCH resources and thus a UE is rejected (see 5G_UP_ALG_19443_replaced([11169338](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt2tR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

5\. Τhe number of slots with DL/UL grant capabilities of dedicated BWP i for each direction (nSlotGrantDl[i], nSlotGrantUl[i]).

A slot with valid K1/K2 shall increment the metrics for grant capabilities (nSlotGrantX[i]) for all dedicated BWPs ( i = {1, 2, 3, 4 }) and for all directions (X = {UL, DL}). Other slots with valid K1 shall only increment nSlotGrantDL[i] for all dedicated BWPs ( i = {1, 2, 3, 4}) and slots with valid K2 shall increment nSlotGrantUL[i] for all dedicated BWPs.

[CB009510-A-UPD001]Note1: When NRBTS.NRCELL.pucchModeSelect is set to longPucch and actFdmScheduling is True, the K1 value shall be computed for SSB and TRS slots regardless of the values of NRBTS.NRCELL.actPdschAtSsbSlots and NRBTS.NRCELL.actPdschRmCsirsForTracking. However, the usage of K1 depends on the values of NRBTS.NRCELL.actPdschAtSsbSlots and NRBTS.NRCELL.actPdschRmCsirsForTracking.[End CB009510-A-UPD001]

[PR797110-25R1]Note2: If NRBTS.NRCELL.cellTechnology is equal to TDD, K1 value shall be computed for SSB slots and TRS slots, regardless of NRBTS.NRCELL.actPdschAtSsbSlots and NRBTS.NRCELL.actPdschRmCsirsForTracking, when NRBTS.NRCELL.pucchModeSelect = longPucch and actFdmScheduling = True and NRBTS.NRCELL.numOfSubSectors = 0 and NRBTS.NRCELL.actSuperCell = False. However, the usage of K1 depends on the values of NRBTS.NRCELL.actPdschAtSsbSlots and NRBTS.NRCELL.actPdschRmCsirsForTracking.[End PR797110-25R1]

---

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.5 Resource expected to build the passive PDCCH slot pattern

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.5.0-1 Resource expected to build the passive PDCCH slot pattern Compute the expected resources (ID: 11169421)

**3.25.1.3.2.2.5.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `11169443`)

Resource expected to build the passive PDCCH slot pattern If NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is not 'disabled', for each direction and for each BWP, the gNB-DU computes the expected PDCCH resources (CCEs) to add on top of the initialized PDCCH slot pattern by taking into account the data of the monitoring PDCCH usage window (last 20ms) and the thresholds defined at the NIDD allowing to control the PDCCH pattern modification:

 pdcchBlockingThreshold: percentage of the slots with grant capability for a given direction leading to request additional PDCCH resources.

If NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is set to perBWP, then NRBTS/NRCELL/cellBwpList/pdcchBlockingThresholdUl and NRBTS/NRCELL/cellBwpList/pdcchBlockingThresholdDl are used for uplink and dowlink respectively and per given dedicated BWP profile (large BWP, small BWP, PS BWP).

If NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is set to largestBWP, then same value is used for uplink and downlink NRBTS/NRCELL/cellBwpList/pdcchBlockingThresholdUl = NRBTS/NRCELL/cellBwpList/pdcchBlockingThresholdDl, and all BWP profiles use the value selected from the largest BWP.

[CB013305-C] If NRCELL/actIncUlPdcchCapacity is set to TRUE and NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is Disabled then only NRBTS/NRCELL/cellBwpList/pdcchBlockingThresholdUl shall be configured and used per given dedicated BWP profile (large BWP, small BWP). [End CB013305-C]

 pdcchFreeThreshold: percentage of the free CCEs for a given direction leading to request less PDCCH resources.

If NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is set to perBWP, then NRBTS/NRCELL/cellBwpList/pdcchFreeThresholdUl and NRBTS/NRCELL/cellBwpList/pdcchFreeThresholdDl are used for uplink and dowlink respectively and per given dedicated BWP profile (large BWP, small BWP, PS BWP).

If NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is set to largestBWP, then same value is used for uplink and downlink RBTS/NRCELL/cellBwpList/pdcchFreeThresholdUl = NRBTS/NRCELL/cellBwpList/pdcchFreeThresholdDl , and all BWP profiles use the value selected from the largest BWP.

[CB013305-C] If NRCELL/actIncUlPdcchCapacity is set to TRUE and NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is Disabled, then only NRBTS/NRCELL/cellBwpList/pdcchFreeThresholdUl shall be configured and used per given dedicated BWP profile (large BWP, small BWP). [End CB013305-C]

If pdcchResourcePreference is not configured or set to 'peakRate', then first if it is possible to reduce the PDCCH resources before checking if it is needed to increase them.

Else if pdcchResourcePreference is 'capacity', then first if it is possible to increase the PDCCH resources before checking if it is needed to reduce them.

Note: pdcchResourcePreference is defined from NRCELL/cellBwpList/pdcchResourcePreference.

---

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.5.0-2 Resource expected to build the passive PDCCH slot pattern Resources to release (ID: 11169449)

**3.25.1.3.2.2.5.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11169456`)

Resource expected to build the passive PDCCH slot pattern If NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is set to largestBWP, gNB-DU shall do the below functionality with nCceDl, nCceUl, nFreeCceDl and nFreeCceUl computed as 5G_UP_ALG_11235_replaced([11169304](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt2tQPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For each direction the gNB-DU computes the ratio between the number of free CCEs at the end of the monitoring window and the number of CCEs configured the same period. If the ratio is lower than the “pdcchFreeThreshold” and the number of Common Channels (SI/Paging) during the monitoring window is lower or equal to the number of Common Channels (CCH) for the next PDCCH slot pattern, then the gNB-DU initializes the number of expected CCEs (nCceReq[D,U]l) for the direction with number of CCEs configured during the monitoring window.

Otherwise, the number of expected CCEs is computed from the number of CCEs configured during the monitoring window by removing the number of free CCEs for the same period. When the number of expected CCE is decreased, the corresponding metric about the grant starvation is set to 0 (it is not possible at the same time to request more resources and not use them).

If the number of expected CCEs is equal or lower than the number of CCEs initialized for the next PDCCH slot pattern, the number of expected CCEs (nCceReq[D,U]l) is set to 0.

Otherwise, the number of CCE intialized (nCceInit[D,U]l) for the next PDCCH slot pattern is subtracted from the expected CCEs (nCceReq[D,U]l).

[CB013305-C] If NRCELL/actIncUlPdcchCapacity is set to TRUE and NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is Disabled, then above calculation is only applicable to UL and nCceReq[D] = 0.[End CB013305-C]

---

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.5.0-3 Resource expected to build the passive PDCCH slot pattern Resources to release for multiple dedicated BWPs in TDD FR1 (ID: 11169462)

**3.25.1.3.2.2.5.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11169468`)

Resource expected to build the passive PDCCH slot pattern If NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is set to perBWP, gNB-DU shall repeat the below functionality for each dedicated BWP i. nCceDl[i], nCceUl[i], nFreeCceDl[i] and nFreeCceUl[i] shall be computed per each dedicate BWP as in 5G_UP_ALG_16772_replaced([11169394](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt3UU_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For each direction the gNB-DU computes the percentage (FreeCcePercentageX[i]) between the number of free CCEs (nFreeCceX[i]) at the end of the monitoring window and the number of CCEs allocated (nCceX[i]) at the same period: FreeCceRatioX[i] = nFreeCceX[i] ÷ nCceX[i] × 100%.

If FreeCceRatioX [i] < pdcchFreeThresholdX[i] and the number of Common Channels (SI/Paging) during the monitoring window (k) is lower or equal to the number of Common Channels (CCH) for the PDCCH slot pattern in the next window (k+1), then the gNB-DU initializes the number of expected CCEs (nCceReqX[i]) for the direction with number of CCEs allocated during the monitoring window k: nCceReqX[i] = nCceX[i].

Otherwise, the number of expected CCEs is computed from the number of CCEs allocated during the monitoring window by removing the number of free CCEs for the same period: nCceReqX[i] = nCceX[i] - nFreeCceX[i]. When the number of required CCEs is decreased, the corresponding metric about the grant starvation for the dedicated BWP is set to 0 and the step for Resources to increase (5G_UP_ALG_17041_replaced([11169491](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt37Z_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is not triggered (it is not possible at the same time to request more resources and not use them).

If nCceReqX[i] ≤ nCceInitX then, nCceReqX[i] = 0.

If nCceReqX[i] > nCceInitX then, the number of CCE intialized (nCceInitX) for the next PDCCH slot pattern is subtracted from the required CCEs: nCceReqX[i] = nCceReqX[i] - nCceInitX

---

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.5.0-4 Resource expected to build the passive PDCCH slot pattern Resources to increase (ID: 11169474)

**3.25.1.3.2.2.5.0-4.0-3**  (ID: `11169486`)

Resource expected to build the passive PDCCH slot pattern If NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is set to largestBWP, gNB-DU shall do the below functionality with nCceDl, nCceUl, nFreeCceDl and nFreeCceUl computed as 5G_UP_ALG_11235_replaced([11169304](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt2tQPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

According to the cell technology and the frame structure, the gNB-DU computes (already known when the PDCCH slot pattern is initialized) the number of slots with downlink grant capability and the number of slot with uplink grant capability (nSlotGrantDl and nSlotGrantUl) for the 2 consecutive radio frames. The grant capability for a given direction is defined when the number of CCEs allocated to this direction is greater than 0.

For each direction the gNB-DU computes the ratio between the number of slots with lack of PDCCH resources (nSlotStarvation[D,U]l) at the end of the monitoring window and the number of slots with the grant capability for the same direction.

If the ratio is lower than the “pdcchBlockingThreshold”, then the gNB-DU initializes the number of expected CCEs for the direction with number of CCEs configured during the monitoring window.

Otherwise the number of expected CCEs is computed from the number of CCEs configured during the monitoring window by adding the number times the lack of PDCCH was detected (nSlotStarvation[D,U]l) multiplied by the number of CCEs for one symbol (nCceCoreset), minus the number of free CCEs for the same period and the same direction.

If the number of expected CCEs is equal or lower than the number of CCEs initialized for the next PDCCH slot pattern, the number of expected CCEs is set to 0.

Otherwise, the number of CCE intialized (nCceInit[D,U]l) for the next PDCCH slot pattern is subtracted from the expected CCEs (nCceReq[D,U]l).

[CB013305-C] If NRCELL/actIncUlPdcchCapacity is set to TRUE and NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is Disabled, above calculation is only applicable to UL and nCceReq[D] = 0.[End CB013305-C]

---

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.5.0-5 Resource expected to build the passive PDCCH slot pattern Resources to increase for multiple dedicated BWPs in TDD FR1 (ID: 11169491)

**3.25.1.3.2.2.5.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11169495`)

Resource expected to build the passive PDCCH slot pattern If NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is set to perBWP, gNB-DU shall repeat the below functionality for each dedicated BWP. nSlotGrantDl[i], nSlotGrantUl[i], nSlotStarvationDl[i] and nSlotStarvationUl[i] shall be computed per each dedicated BWP i as in 5G_UP_ALG_16772_replaced([11169394](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt3UU_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

According to the frame structure, the gNB-DU computes the number of slots with downlink grant capability and the number of slots with uplink grant capability ( both already known when the PDCCH slot pattern is initialized) for a dedicated BWP (nSlotGrantX[i]) for 2 consecutive radio frames. The grant capability for a given direction is defined when the number of CCEs allocated to this direction is greater than 0.

For each direction and each dedicated BWP, the gNB-DU computes the percentage (starvSlotPercentageX[i]) between the number of slots with lack of PDCCH resources when PDSCH/PUSCH resources are available (nSlotStarvationX[i]l) at the end of the monitoring window and the number of slots with the grant capability for the same direction (nSlotGrantX[i]) such that starvSlotPercentageX[i] = nSlotStarvationX[i] ÷ nSlotGrantX[i] × 100.

If starvSlotPercentageX[i] < pdcchBlockingThresholdX[i], then the gNB-DU initializes the number of expected CCEs for the direction with number of CCEs allocated during the monitoring window: nCceReqX[i] = nCceX[i].

Otherwise the number of expected CCEs is computed from the number of CCEs configured during the monitoring window by adding the number times a lack of PDCCH was detected (starvSlotPercentageX[i]) multiplied by number of CCEs allocated to the largest CORESET in one PDCCH symbol of the dedicated BWP (nMaxCce[i]), minus the number of free CCEs for the same period and the same direction: nCceReqX[i] = nCceX[i] + nSlotStarvationX[i] × nMaxCce[i] - nFreeCceX[i].

If nCceReqX[i] ≤ nCceInitX, then nCceReqX[i] = 0.

If nCceReqX[i] > nCceInitX then, the number of CCEs intialized (nCceInitX) for the next PDCCH slot pattern is subtracted from the required CCEs: nCceReqX[i] = nCceReqX[i] - nCceInitX.

---

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.5.0-6 Resource expected to build the passive PDCCH slot pattern Expected resources adjustment for both directions (ID: 11169499)

**3.25.1.3.2.2.5.0-6.0-5**  (ID: `12816270`)

Resource expected to build the passive PDCCH slot pattern 12816270: Resource expected to build the passive PDCCH slot pattern The gNB-DU checks that the expected number of CCEs for both directions does not exceed the largest PDCCH capacity defined according to the configuration of the UE-Specific search spaces and the “dmrsTypeAPosition” received in the PsCell_CellSetupReq message. To compute the PDCCH capacity, the gNB-DU checks the UE-Specific search spaces configured, in the cell, to get the maximum symbol used, not higher than the “dmrsTypeAPosition”. This will define the maximum number of PDCCH symbols (nPdcchSymbmax) allowed per slot. If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is true and actBbPoolExtensionTddFr1 is true and actTddCsirsOpt is false and actTddCsirsAllocOptimization **is false and FR1-TDD BW 10MHz or 15MHz, nPdcchSymbmax shall be <= 2 in the Cell Specific CSI-RS slots which are determined in 5G_UP_ALG_11874_replaced([11117149](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp9rwPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).** The CORESET selected to define the number of CCEs per symbol (nCcecoreset) is the one defined for a UE-Specific search space on one OFDM symbol repeated more than once in the front of the slot and with the largest number of RBs. The PDCCH capacity is the sum of number of CCEs per symbol multiplied by maximum number of PDCCH symbols over the downlink slots of 2 consecutive radio frames. If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is true and actBbPoolExtensionTddFr1 is true and actTddCsirsOpt is false and actTddCsirsAllocOptimization **is false and FR1-TDD BW 10MHz or 15MHz, nPdcchSymbmax may be different in Cell Specific CSI-RS slots (which are determined in 5G_UP_ALG_11874_replaced([11117149](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp9rwPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and other slots, and this shall be considered for the PDCCH capacity.** [image-0][image_desc]nCcePdchmax = nPdchSymbmax × nCcecoverage × 2 × nDlSlotPerRadioFrame[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12032.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] If the sum of expected CCEs for both directions on top of the initial CCE distribution (nCceDl, nCceUl) does not exceed the maximal PDCCH capacity, the gNB-DU adds the expected CCEs as define in the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4014_replaced([11169598](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt4iefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Otherwise, the gNB-DU reduces the requested CCEs by taking into account the number of available slots for each direction in order to fit the maximum PDCCH capacity. For a cell in FDD, when the requestd CCEs is larger than the PDCCH capacity, the expected resources are proportionnaly spread in each direction with the formulas hereafter. Then, the gNB-DU adds the resources as detailed in the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4014_replaced([11169598](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt4iefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [image-1][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation with two parts, enclosed in a large curly brace. The equation defines two variables, `nCceReqDl` and `nCceReqUl`. The first part of the equation is: `nCceReqDl = [nCceReqDl / (nCceReqDl + nCceReqUl)] * (nCcePdcchmax - nCceDl - nCceUl)` The second part of the equation is: `nCceReqUl = [nCceReqUl / (nCceReqDl + nCceReqUl)] * (nCcePdcchmax - nCceDl - nCceUl)`[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12032.002.png[/image_path][/image-1] For TDD cells, when one direction has less candidate slots than the other direction (nSlotGrantInitDl, nSlotGrantInitUl) or less than the number of slot with PDCCH (nSlotGrantInit), the adjustement is not needed, as at least the allocations will be restricted during the modification pattern as described in the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4014_replaced([11169598](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt4iefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Otherwise, all available slots handle the grant capabilities for both directions and the same principle as the FDD cell is applied (see above). **[CB015668-A]** Note: in this artifact, actTddCsirsOpt is not get from NIDD but from L3 indicator. **[End CB015668-A]** ****

---

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.5.0-7 Resource expected to build the passive PDCCH slot pattern Expected resources adjustment in both directions for multiple dedicated BWPs in TDD FR1 (ID: 11169549)

**3.25.1.3.2.2.5.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11169559`)

Resource expected to build the passive PDCCH slot pattern 11169559: Resource expected to build the passive PDCCH slot pattern If NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is set to perBWP, the gNB-DU checks that the expected number of CCEs for both directions of a dedicated BWP does not exceed the largest PDCCH capacity defined according to the configuration of the UE-Specific search spaces of a cell and the “dmrsTypeAPosition” received in the PsCell_CellSetupReq message.

To compute the PDCCH capacity of a dedicated BWP, the gNB-DU checks the UE-Specific search spaces configured in the cell to get the maximum symbols used, not higher than the “dmrsTypeAPosition”. This will define the maximum number of PDCCH symbols (nPdcchSymbmax) allowed per slot for the dedicated BWP.

The number of CCEs per symbol (nCcecoreset [i]) of the dedicated BWP i includes the region of the respective CORESET of the BWP where UE-Specific search spaces on one OFDM symbol are repeated more than once at the front of the slot.

The PDCCH capacity (nCcePdcchmax [i]) of nested BWP i is the sum of the number of CCEs per symbol multiplied by the maximum number of PDCCH symbols (nPdcchSymbmax) over the downlink slots of 2 consecutive radio frames.

[image-0][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in blue text. The formula is: nCcePdcchMax[i] = nPdcchSymbmax × nCceCORESET[i] × 2 × nDlSlotPerRadioFrame[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12034.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

If the sum of expected CCEs for both directions on top of the initial CCE distribution (nCceD[i]l, nCceUl[i]) do not exceed the maximal PDCCH capacity, the gNB-DU adds the expected CCEs as defined in the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4014_replaced([11169598](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt4iefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Otherwise, the gNB-DU reduces the requested CCEs by taking into account the number of available slots for each direction in order to fit the maximum PDCCH capacity.

For TDD cells, when one direction has less candidate slots than the other direction in BWP i (nSlotGrantInitDl[i], nSlotGrantInitUl[i]) or less than the number of slots with PDCCH (nSlotGrantInit), the adjustment is not needed, as at least the allocations will be restricted during the modification pattern as described in the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4014_replaced([11169598](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt4iefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Otherwiise, all available slots handle the grant capabilities for both directions in a nested BWP when the requested CCEs is larger than the PDCCH capacity, the expected resources are proportionally spread in each direction with the formulas hereafter.

[image-1][image_desc]The image contains two mathematical equations written in blue text. The first equation is: $nCceReqDl[i] = \left[ \frac{nCceReqDl[i]}{nCceReqBwpDl+nCceReqBwpUl} \times (nCcePdcchMax[i] - nCceDl[i] - nCceUl[i]) \right]$ The second equation is: $nCceReqUl[i] = \left[ \frac{nCceReqUl[i]}{nCceReqDl[i]+nCceReqUl[i]} \times (nCcePdcchMax[i] - nCceDl[i] - nCceUl[i]) \right]$[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12034.002.png[/image_path][/image-1]

---

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.6 Algorithm for dynamic switching between a single K2 state and a multi K2 state

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.6.0-1 Algorithm for dynamic switching between a single K2 state and a multi K2 state Single K2 state (singleK2PerULSlot) and multi K2 state (multipleK2PerULSlot) (ID: 11169569)

**3.25.1.3.2.2.6.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11169576`)

Algorithm for dynamic switching between a single K2 state and a multi K2 state 11169576: Algorithm for dynamic switching between a single K2 state and a multi K2 state [CB013305-C, CB013305-D]

The algorithm for dynamic switching between a single K2 state (singleK2PerULSlot) and multi K2 state (multipleK2PerULSlot) provides increased flexibility to UL PDCCH. Following figure is an example for multipleK2PerULSlot state.

[image-0][image_desc]The image displays a timeline or sequence of events, likely related to wireless communication scheduling. The timeline is represented by a series of colored blocks, each labeled with a letter. The blocks are arranged horizontally and are colored in shades of blue, gray, and light blue. From left to right, the labels are: \- D (repeated multiple times in dark blue) \- S (in gray) \- U (in light blue, repeated twice) Above the timeline, there are annotations indicating scheduling events: \- "UL scheduler run 1" is indicated by a green arrow pointing to a dark blue "D" block. \- "UL scheduler run 2" is indicated by a red arrow pointing to a dark blue "D" block. Below the timeline, there are further annotations related to "UL PDCCH" (Uplink Physical Downlink Control Channel) with associated "K2" values, indicated by dotted arrows: \- "UL PDCCH with K2 = 4" is indicated by a green dotted arrow originating from a dark blue "D" block and pointing to a later dark blue "D" block. \- "UL PDCCH with K2 = 3" is indicated by a green dotted arrow originating from a dark blue "D" block and pointing to the gray "S" block. \- "UL PDCCH with K2 = 3" is indicated by a red dotted arrow originating from a dark blue "D" block and pointing to the gray "S" block. \- "UL PDCCH with K2 = 2" is indicated by a red dotted arrow originating from a dark blue "D" block and pointing to the first light blue "U" block. The overall visual suggests a process where different scheduling runs and control channel assignments occur at different points in time, influencing the state or transmission type (represented by D, S, U) of the timeline blocks.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12037.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

[Before CB013305-C-UPD001, CB013305-D-UPD001] If rdFixedMultipleK2ForIncUlPdcchCapacity is set to 1, multipleK2PerULSlot state is always maintained.[End CB013305-C-UPD001, CB013305-D-UPD001]

If NRCELL/actIncUlPdcchCapacity is TRUE [Before CB013305-C-UPD001, CB013305-D-UPD001] and rdFixedMultipleK2ForIncUlPdcchCapacity is set to 0 [End CB013305-C-UPD001, CB013305-D-UPD001], two states are maintained for dynamic switching of UL PDCCH resources.

Definition of the two states:

  * State 0: singleK2PerULSlot where UEs in a given UL slot can be scheduled with only single k2 value as 5G_UP_ALG_2484_replaced([11116264](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp2XB_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

  * Default state at the initial slot pattern [Before CB013305-C-UPD001, CB013305-D-UPD001] when rdFixedMultipleK2ForIncUlPdcchCapacity is set to 0 [End CB013305-C-UPD001, CB013305-D-UPD001]

  * Low UL load state single K2 for lower latency and higher PDCCH or PDSCH capacity in DL slots.

  * One UL scheduler run allocates PDCCH resources in at most 1 DL slot for 1 UL slot.

  * State 1: multipleK2PerULSlot (5G_UP_13617_replaced([11348263](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubTk3vvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) where UEs in same UL slot can be scheduled with multiple different k2 values




[Before CB013305-C-UPD001, CB013305-D-UPD001] - Default state at the initial slot pattern when rdFixedMultipleK2ForIncUlPdcchCapacity is set to 1 [End CB013305-C-UPD001, CB013305-D-UPD001]

[Before CB013305-C-UPD005, CB013305-D-UPD005]- CCE split is deactivated in the PDCCH slot pattern [End CB013305-C-UPD005, CB013305-D-UPD005]

  * High UL load state where one UL scheduler run allocates PDCCH resources in at most 2 DL slots for 1 UL slot. 

  * Slots 0, 1, 10 and 11 in tdLte 0 ms (14, 15 and 4, 5 in tdLte 3 ms) can be converted from 'DL slots without any uplink grant capability (5G_UP_ALG_4018_replaced([11169689](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt5JhPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))' to 'DL slots handling uplink grant capability (5G_UP_ALG_4016_replaced([11169667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt4if_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))'.

  * Compared to the singleK2PerULSlot state, eligible PDCCH symbols for UL direction are incremented by a maximum of 8 symbols and eligible PDCCH symbols for DL direction are decremented by a maximum of 8 in the PDCCH slot pattern.

  * multipleK2PerULSlot state is only applicable to the PDCCH slot pattern (n) where nSymbolsReqUL exceeds the threshold. Once the PDCCH slot pattern is constructed and resources allocated, the state is reset to singleK2PerULSlot state for the PDCCH slot pattern n+1.




Refer 5G_UP_ALG_30809_replaced([11169581](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt4idfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the state transition and functions in each state.

[End CB013305-C, CB013305-D]

---

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.6.0-2 Algorithm for dynamic switching between a single K2 state and a multi K2 state Single K2 state (singleK2PerULSlot) and multi K2 state (multipleK2PerULSlot) (ID: 13386490)

**3.25.1.3.2.2.6.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13386491`)

Algorithm for dynamic switching between a single K2 state and a multi K2 state 13386491: Algorithm for dynamic switching between a single K2 state and a multi K2 state [CB013305-C, CB013305-D]

The algorithm for dynamic switching between a single K2 state (singleK2PerULSlot) and multi K2 state (multipleK2PerULSlot) provides increased flexibility to UL PDCCH. Following figure is an example for multipleK2PerULSlot state.

[image-0][image_desc]The image displays a timeline or sequence of events, likely related to wireless communication scheduling. The timeline is represented by a series of colored blocks, each labeled with a letter. The blocks are arranged horizontally and are colored in shades of blue, gray, and light blue. From left to right, the labels are: \- D (repeated multiple times in dark blue) \- S (in gray) \- U (in light blue, repeated twice) Above the timeline, there are annotations indicating scheduling events: \- "UL scheduler run 1" is indicated by a green arrow pointing to a dark blue "D" block. \- "UL scheduler run 2" is indicated by a red arrow pointing to a dark blue "D" block. [Before CB013305-C-UPD001, CB013305-D-UPD001] If rdFixedMultipleK2ForIncUlPdcchCapacity is set to 1, multipleK2PerULSlot state is always maintained.[End CB013305-C-UPD001, CB013305-D-UPD001]

If NRCELL/actIncUlPdcchCapacity is TRUE [Before CB013305-C-UPD001, CB013305-D-UPD001] and rdFixedMultipleK2ForIncUlPdcchCapacity is set to 0 [End CB013305-C-UPD001, CB013305-D-UPD001], two states are maintained for dynamic switching of UL PDCCH resources.

Definition of the two states:

  * State 0: singleK2PerULSlot where UEs in a given UL slot can be scheduled with only single k2 value as 5G_UP_ALG_2484_replaced([11116264](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp2XB_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

  * Default state at the initial slot pattern [Before CB013305-C-UPD001, CB013305-D-UPD001] when rdFixedMultipleK2ForIncUlPdcchCapacity is set to 0 [End CB013305-C-UPD001, CB013305-D-UPD001]

  * Low UL load state single K2 for lower latency and higher PDCCH or PDSCH capacity in DL slots.

  * One UL scheduler run allocates PDCCH resources in at most 1 DL slot for 1 UL slot.

  * State 1: multipleK2PerULSlot (5G_UP_13617_replaced([11348263](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubTk3vvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) where UEs in same UL slot can be scheduled with multiple different k2 values




[Before CB013305-C-UPD001, CB013305-D-UPD001] - Default state at the initial slot pattern when rdFixedMultipleK2ForIncUlPdcchCapacity is set to 1 [End CB013305-C-UPD001, CB013305-D-UPD001]

[Before CB013305-C-UPD005, CB013305-D-UPD005]- CCE split is deactivated in the PDCCH slot pattern [End CB013305-C-UPD005, CB013305-D-UPD005]

  * High UL load state where one UL scheduler run allocates PDCCH resources in at most 2 DL slots for 1 UL slot. 

  * Slots 0, 1, 10 and 11 in tdLte 0 ms (14, 15 and 4, 5 in tdLte 3 ms) can be converted from 'DL slots without any uplink grant capability (5G_UP_ALG_4018_replaced([11169689](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt5JhPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))' to 'DL slots handling uplink grant capability (5G_UP_ALG_4016_replaced([11169667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt4if_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))'.

  * Compared to the singleK2PerULSlot state, eligible PDCCH symbols for UL direction are incremented by a maximum of 8 symbols and eligible PDCCH symbols for DL direction are decremented by a maximum of 8 in the PDCCH slot pattern.

  * multipleK2PerULSlot state is only applicable to the PDCCH slot pattern (n) where nSymbolsReqUL exceeds the threshold. Once the PDCCH slot pattern is constructed and resources allocated, the state is reset to singleK2PerULSlot state for the PDCCH slot pattern n+1.




Refer 5G_UP_ALG_30809_replaced([11169581](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt4idfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the state transition and functions in each state.

[End CB013305-C, CB013305-D]
