###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.6.0-3 Algorithm for dynamic switching between a single K2 state and a multi K2 state State transition and the functions in singleK2PerULSlot and multipleK2PerULSlot states (ID: 11169581)

**3.25.1.3.2.2.6.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `12874892`)

Algorithm for dynamic switching between a single K2 state and a multi K2 state The transition from one state to another is triggered by comparing nSymbolsReqUL with a threshold consisting of the following 2 parameters:

  * nPdcchSymbolMax,UL,singleK2PerULSlot: maximum number of UL PDCCH symbols available in the singleK2PerULSlot state. This is equal to the number of PUSCH slot in a PDCCH slot pattern period.
  * rdhystULPDCCHSymbol: an R&D parameter (5G_UP_ALG_31132_replaced([11171859](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuHzB_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) acting as hysteresis to prevent frequent switching between the two states.

  * nSymbolsReqUL shall be calculated as follows:

  * nSymbolsReqUL = nCceReqUL/nCceCORESET (refer 5G_UP_ALG_4016_replaced([11169667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt4if_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) where 
    * nCceReqUl = nCceUl + nSlotUlStarvation*nCceCORESET – nFreeCceUl (refer nCceReqUl calculation before subtracting nCceInitUl in 5G_UP_ALG_4010_replaced([11169474](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt37Y_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))



State transition and the functions:

> If the state is singleK2PerULSlot in current PDCCH slot pattern period
>
>> If nSymbolsReqUL >= nPdcchSymbolMax,UL,singleK2PerULSlot + rdhystULPDCCHSymbol
>>
>>> gNB-DU shall change the state to multipleK2PerULSlot.
>> 
>> Else
>>
>>> gNB-DU shall keep in singleK2PerULSlot state.
>> 
>> EndIf
> 
> Else (the state is multipleK2PerULSlot in current PDCCH slot pattern period)
>
>> If nAvgSymbolsReqUL < nPdcchSymbolMax,UL,singleK2PerULSlot + rdEpsilonOffsetUlPdcchSymbol
>>
>>> gNB-DU shall change the state to singleK2PerULSlot.
>> 
>> Else
>>
>>> gNB-DU shall keep in multipleK2PerULSlot state.
>> 
>> EndIf
> 
> Endif

nAvgSymbolsReqUL: [12422164: Metric of IIR filtered average of nSymbolsReqUL: nAvgSymbolsReqUL](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_p2edoQV6EfCD_KNtuTnR7g?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

rdEpsilonOffsetUlPdcchSymbol: [12421343: rdEpsilon Offset UlPdcchSymbol](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_8HJDggV4EfCD_KNtuTnR7g?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

If above decision makes the state change in next PDCCH slot pattern period:

  * gNB-DU shall switch to new timing pattern as mentioned in 5G_UP_13619_replaced([11388869](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufMmV_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) in the entire PDCCH slot pattern.



If above decision decides to use multipleK2PerULSlot state in next PDCCH slot pattern period, gNB-DU shall do following for next PDCCH slot pattern:

  * If nSymbolsReqUL <= # of available UL PDCCH occasions in the PDCCH slot pattern with '1 additional UL PDCCH slot having 1 UL PDCCH occasion per half frame' compared to nPdcchSymbolMax,UL,singleK2PerULSlot in initial slot pattern (refer 5G_UP_ALG_3962_replaced([11168921](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktzp9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for slot pattern initialization) [PR857385-26R2] and ((NRBTS/NRCELL.actIncreaseMaxULScheduleUE is false) or (NRBTS/NRCELL.actIncreaseMaxULScheduleUE is true and (none of the UL slots in the current 20ms monitoring cycle had more than 16 UEs scheduled))) [End PR857385-26R2]
  * gNB-DU shall convert (refer 5G_UP_ALG_31072_replaced([11169588](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt4id_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for conversion) the slot corresponding to maximum K2 value in each half frame from 'DL slot without any uplink grant capability' to 'DL slot¨ handling uplink grant capability' by changing the CORESET duration pattern in order to have at least 2 PDCCH occasions (for UL and DL).
  * Update the initial PDCCH slot pattern characteristics computed in 5G_UP_ALG_4002_replaced([11169280](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt2GRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): nSymbInitDl, nSymbInitUl, nCceInitDl, nCceInitUl, nSlotGrantInitDl, nSlotGrantInitUl and nSlotGrantInit
  * [Before PR857385-26R2] If nSymbolsReqUL > # of available UL PDCCH occasions in the PDCCH slot pattern with '1 additional UL PDCCH slot having 1 UL PDCCH occasion per half frame' compared to nPdcchSymbolMax,UL,singleK2PerULSlot in initial slot pattern (refer 5G_UP_ALG_3962_replaced([11168921](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktzp9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for slot pattern initialization) [PR857385-26R2] Else [End PR857385-26R2]
  * gNB-DU shall convert (refer 5G_UP_ALG_31072_replaced([11169588](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt4id_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for conversion) each slot with valid K2 in the multipleK2PerULSlot state from 'DL slots without any uplink grant capability' to 'DL slots handling uplink grant capability' by changing the CORESET duration pattern in order to have at least 2 PDCCH occasions (for UL and DL).
  * Update the initial PDCCH slot pattern characteristics computed in 5G_UP_ALG_4002_replaced([11169280](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt2GRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): nSymbInitDl, nSymbInitUl, nCceInitDl, nCceInitUl, nSlotGrantInitDl, nSlotGrantInitUl and nSlotGrantInit

---

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.6.0-4 Algorithm for dynamic switching between a single K2 state and a multi K2 state Metric of IIR filtered average of nSymbolsReqUL: nAvgSymbolsReqUL (ID: 12422164)

**3.25.1.3.2.2.6.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12422165`)

Algorithm for dynamic switching between a single K2 state and a multi K2 state Metric of IIR filtered average of nSymbolsReqUL: nAvgSymbolsReqUL

· nAvgSymbolsReqUL[t] = (1-a) * nAvgSymbolsReqUL[t-1] + a * nSymbolsReqUL[t]

with:

· t: index of PDCCH slot pattern period.

· nSymbolsReqUL: see 5G_UP_ALG_30809_replaced([11169581](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt4idfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

· a = 1/rdAvgSymbolsReqUlFilterConst, [12421329: rdAvg SymbolsReqUl FilterConst](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_akGKoQV4EfCD_KNtuTnR7g?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

nAvgSymbolsReqUL is only maintained in multipleK2PerULSlot state.

When the state is changed from singleK2PerULSlot to multipleK2PerULSlot, nAvgSymbolsReqUL = nSymbolsReqUL calculated in the PDCCH slot pattern period with singleK2PerULSlot. Refer 5G_UP_ALG_30809_replaced([11169581](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt4idfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.6.0-5 Algorithm for dynamic switching between a single K2 state and a multi K2 state Converting a slot from 'DL slots without any uplink grant capability' to 'DL slots handling uplink grant capability' (ID: 11169588)

**3.25.1.3.2.2.6.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11169593`)

Algorithm for dynamic switching between a single K2 state and a multi K2 state [CB013305-C, CB013305-D]

  * Converting a slot without common channels shall be similar to PDCCH distribution after deactivating CCE split (5G_UP_ALG_8929_replaced([11169066](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt04FvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * If the slot includes common channels, then 5G_UP_ALG_3970_replaced([11168960](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktzp_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be followed for converting a slot, if (NRCELL.actAperCsi is enabled and for TDD cell ) or if distributed PUCCH allocation algorithm is applicable according to 5G_UP_ALG_2885_replaced([11123447](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), then 5G_UP_ALG_3962_replaced([11168921](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktzp9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be followed.



[End CB013305-C, CB013305-D]

---

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.6.0-6 Algorithm for dynamic switching between a single K2 state and a multi K2 state Extension to 3 PDCCH symbols in singleK2PerULSlot  or multipleK2PerULSlot states (ID: 13379464)

**3.25.1.3.2.2.6.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `13379465`)

Algorithm for dynamic switching between a single K2 state and a multi K2 state Behavior of PS BWP:

If NRCELL/actIncUlPdcchCapacity is TRUE and NRCELL/actThreeSymbolPdcch is not disabled

When gNB switches to singleK2PerULSlot state, gNB-DU shall activate three PDCCH symbols in PS BWP only in K1, K2 slots relevant in singleK2PerUlSlot state.  
When gNB switches to multipleK2PerULSlot state, gNB-DU shall activate three PDCCH symbols in PS BWP in K1, K2 slots relevant in multipleK2PerUlSlot state.

If NRCELL/actThreeSymbolPdcch is static:

After activation of the third symbol, CORESET duration pattern in PS BWP in valid K1, K2 slots is as per [12728772](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_JQkEEnHmEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

If NRCELL/actThreeSymbolPdcch is dynamic and NRCELL.actDynPdcchTdMode is perBWP:

After activation of the third symbol, CCE distribution in PS BWP in valid K1, K2 slots is as per [11169667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt4if_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

Behavior of large or small BWP between 20-40 MHz:

If NRCELL/actIncUlPdcchCapacity is TRUE and NRCELL/actThreeSymbolPdcch is not disabled, for large or small BWP between 20-40MHz[CB012733-C-UDP001],

in singleK2perUlSlot state, gNB-DU shall not use:

  * the 3rd PDCCH symbol in K1, K2 slots
  * the 3rd PDCCH symbol in K1 slots relevant in multipleK2perUlSlot modes
  * the 2nd symbol in actThreeSymbolPdcch static mode for non-common channel search spaces in K1 slots relevant in multipleK2perUlSlot modes.



[End CB012733-C-UDP001]

in multipleK2perUlSlot state, gNB-DU shall activate the third PDCCH symbol in K1, K2 slots as follows:

  * In K2 = 4,3;3 sub-mode ([11348263](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubTk3vvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), all K1, K2 slots relevant to 4,3;3 sub-mode
  * In K2 = 4,3;3,2 sub-mode ([11348263](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubTk3vvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), all K1, K2 slots relevant to 4,3;3,2 sub-mode
  * In K2=4;3,2 sub-mode third PDCCH symbol is not activated



After activation of the third symbol in multipleK2perUlSlot state, CCE distribution in the UL direction in K1, K2 slots is as per [11169667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt4if_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) based on nSymbolsReqUL.

---

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.7 Modification of the initialized PDCCH slot pattern

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.7.0-1 Modification of the initialized PDCCH slot pattern Modification of the initialized slot pattern for multiple dedicated BWPs in TDD FR1 (ID: 11169603)

**3.25.1.3.2.2.7.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `12730847`)

Modification of the initialized PDCCH slot pattern Modification of the slot pattern for multiple BWPs in 20-40MHz in TDD FR1

---

**3.25.1.3.2.2.7.0-1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12730841`)

Modification of the initialized PDCCH slot pattern If NRCELL.actThreeSymbolPdcch is set to Dynamic with NRCELL.actDynPdcchTdMode set to largestBwp, then

  * If large BWP (<=40 MHz), then the # PDCCH symbols in a slot can reach up to 3 symbols in the large BWP. Small BWP gets the same number of PDCCH symbols as the large BWP.
  * If large BWP >40 MHz but small BWP is 20-40 MHz
  * Large BWP gets a maximum of 2 PDCCH symbols
  * If nCceReqUl or nCceReqDl is >0 even after distributing all the CCEs to the larger BWP (>40 MHz), a third symbol can be assigned to the smaller BWP. In such case, each additional symbol provides # of CCEs of size of the CORESET that is the largest CORESET in a BWP between 20-40 MHz. This concerns both "number of slot modifications" and "nCceReq" remaining after each modification as per [11169667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt4if_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_kt4if_vsee-aqvopbp1qhq?oslc_config.context=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2fgc%2fconfiguration%2f9") and [11169689](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt5JhPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_kt5jhpvsee-aqvopbp1qhq?oslc_config.context=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2fgc%2fconfiguration%2f9").



If NRCELL.actThreeSymbolPdcch is set to Dynamic with NRCELL.actDynPdcchTdMode set to perBwp, then

  * Dedicated BWPs with size >40 MHz get a maximum of 2 PDCCH symbols.
  * Dedicated BWPs with size 20-40MHz or PS BWP get a maximum of 3 PDCCH symbols in a slot.
  * If the smaller BWP CORESET (20-40 MHz) overlaps >= 50% with the larger BWP CORESET
  * When the larger BWP gets 1 PDCCH symbol, then smaller BWP can get 1, 2 or 3 PDCCH symbols.
  * When the larger BWP gets 2 PDCCH symbols, then smaller BWP can get either 2 or 3 PDCCH symbols.
  * When the larger BWP (20-40 MHz) gets 3 PDCCH symbols , then smaller BWP also gets 3 PDCCH symbols.
  * If the smaller BWP CORESET overlaps < 50% with the larger BWP CORESET
  * When the larger BWP gets 1 PDCCH symbol, then smaller BWP can get 1, 2 or 3 PDCCH symbols.
  * When the larger BWP gets 2 PDCCH symbols, then smaller BWP can get 1, 2 or 3 PDCCH symbols.
  * When the larger BWP (20-40 MHz) gets 3 PDCCH symbols, then smaller BWP can get 1, 2 or 3 PDCCH symbols.

---

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.7.0-2 Modification of the initialized PDCCH slot pattern Direction Selection (ID: 11169658)

**3.25.1.3.2.2.7.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11169662`)

Modification of the initialized PDCCH slot pattern The gNB-DU selects the first direction to add the expected CCEs according to the smallest number of slots with a given grant capability for the next PDCCH slot pattern. If both directions have the same set of slots, the direction requesting the smallest number of expected CCEs is managed first.

---

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.7.0-3 Modification of the initialized PDCCH slot pattern Uplink resources management (ID: 11169667)

**3.25.1.3.2.2.7.0-3.0-6**  (ID: `13386486`)

Modification of the initialized PDCCH slot pattern If the uplink direction is selected, the gNB-DU selects randomly a starting slots among the possible slots in the PDCCH slot pattern. The gNB-DU scans the slot with uplink grant capability in the following order to increase by one the number of symbols within the slot:

  * The DL slots handling uplink grant capability with a CORESET shared between both directions.

  * The Bidirectional (BI) slots without any DL grant capability.

  * The BI slots with uplink and downlink grant capabilities.

  * The DL slots handling uplink grant capability without common channel(s) configured in the same slot.

  * The DL slots handling uplink grant capability.




In order to spread the resource increase among the PDCCH slot pattern, the gNB-DU estimates the number of slots modification by dividing the number of CCEs requested (nCceReqUl) by the number of CCE per symbol used as reference (nCcecoreset).

For the two BI slot types above, the gNB-DU switches between both sets of slots when all slots with a given type are modified once. The gNB-DU adds only one symbol at a time and changes the slot to apply the next modification.

When the two BI slots types have no more free symbols for PDCCH, the gNB-DU selects the type of slots in the order above and fulfills the selected type before to select the next one. [CB012733-C]If NRCELL.actThreeSymbolPdcch is set to dynamic, then the Bidirectional (BI) slots without any DL grant capability can have up to three UL PDCCH symbols in 20-40 MHz BWs. [End CB012733-C]

At each time the number of slot modifications for a given type of slot is lower than the number of slots with this type, the gNB-DU spreads homogeneously the modifications over the set of given slot type defined above.

At each time the gNB-DU adds an uplink symbol on a given slot, if the nPdcchSymbmax is not already reached, it checks the type of the resources previously initialized:

  * If the slot contains a PDCCH occasion with a CCE split, then this capability is not more allowed:

  * if the PDCCH occasion uses 2 symbols, one symbol is tagged as DL and the other one is dedicated for the UL. As one uplink symbol is added (see above), the nCcecoreset is removed from the nCceReqUl.

  * if the PDCCH occasion uses 1 symbol, the symbol is tagged as DL. As one symbol is added (see above), half of the nCcecoreset is removed from the nCceReqUl. After the CCE split is deactivated, the other direction automatically gets back half of the nCcecoreset which is removed from the nCceReqDl.

  * If the slot does not contain a PDCCH occasion with a CCE split, the gNB-DU set one more symbol for the uplink and removed nCcecoreset from the nCceReqUl.




When there is no more symbols candidates or when at least the number of CCE requested are allocated, the gNB-DU proceeds with the next direction, if needed.

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is true and actBbPoolExtensionTddFr1 is true and actTddCsirsOpt (note: actTddCsirsOpt is not get from NIDD but from L3 indicator) is false, only up to 2 PDCCH symbols (symbol 0 and symbol 1) can be used for FR1-TDD BW 10MHz and 15MHz in the Cell Specific CSI-RS slots which are determined in 5G_UP_ALG_11874_replaced([11117149](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp9rwPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If the frame structure is tdLte Config0, then gNB-DU shall not modify the initialized slot pattern in slot indices 2, 3, 12 and 13 in the UL direction if 2 K2 values are configured.

---

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.7.0-4 Modification of the initialized PDCCH slot pattern Downlink resources management (ID: 11169689)

**3.25.1.3.2.2.7.0-4.0-7**  (ID: `13387629`)

Modification of the initialized PDCCH slot pattern If the downlink direction is selected, the gNB-DU selects randomly a starting slot among the possible slots in the PDCCH slot pattern. The gNB-DU scans the slot with downlink grant capability in the following order to increase by one the number of symbols within the slot:

 The DL slots, with 14 symbols and handling downlink grant capability with a CORESET shared between both directions.

 The DL slots without any uplink grant capability and with common channel(s) configured in the same slot.

 The DL slots without any uplink grant capability.

 The DL slots, with less than 14 symbols and handling downlink grant capability with a CORESET shared between both directions.

 The DL slots with uplink and downlink grant capabilities.

In order to spread the resource increase among the PDCCH slot pattern, the gNB-DU could estimate the number of slots modification by dividing the number of CCEs requested (nCceReqDl) by the number of CCE per symbol used as reference (nCcecoreset).

If the number of slot modifications is lower than the number of slots for given characteristic defined above, the gNB-DU spreads homogeneously the modifications over the set of given slot characteristic.

The gNB-DU selects the slots with next characteristics (see above) when the previous slots selected have no more free symbol for the PDCCH.

For a given set of slots, the gNB-DU adds only one symbol at a time and changes the slot to apply the next modification.

At each time the gNB-DU adds a downlink symbol on a given slot, if the nPdcchSymbmax is not already reached, it checks the type of the resources previously initialized:

 If the slot contains a PDCCH occasion with a CCE split, then this capability is not more allowed:

 if the PDCCH occasion uses 2 symbols, one symbol is tagged as DL and the other one is dedicated for the UL. As one downlink symbol is added (see above), the nCcecoreset is removed from the nCceReqDl.

 if the PDCCH occasion uses 1 symbol, the symbol is tagged as UL. As one symbol is added (see above), half of the nCcecoreset is removed from the nCceReqDl. After the CCE split is deactivated, the other direction automatically gets back half of the nCcecoreset which is removed from the nCceReqUl.

 If the slot does not contain a PDCCH occasion with a CCE split, the gNB-DU set one more symbol for the downlink and removed nCcecoreset from the nCceReqDl.

When there is no more symbols candidates or when at least the number of CCE requested are allocated, the gNB-DU proceeds with the next direction, if needed.

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is true and actBbPoolExtensionTddFr1 is true and actTddCsirsOpt is false **(note: actTddCsirsOpt is not get from NIDD but from L3 indicator) and actTddCsirsAllocOptimization** is false, only up to 2 PDCCH symbols (symbol 0 and symbol 1) can be used for FR1-TDD BW 10MHz and 15MHz in the Cell Specific CSI-RS slots which are determined in 5G_UP_ALG_11874_replaced([11117149](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp9rwPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).****

If the frame structure is tdLte Config0, then gNB-DU shall not modify the initialized slot pattern in slot indices 2, 3, 12 and 13 in the DL direction if 2 K2 values are configured.

[CB012733-C-UPD001]If actThreeSymbolPdcch is static, then the K1, K2 slots that are activated only in the multipleK2PerULSlot state shall use the same number of DL PDCCH symbols as configured in the K1 valid slots in the singleK2PerULSlot state. e.g. DLULUL or ULDLUL used in multiple K2 state by K2=4 slot, but only one DL symbol in the singleK2PerULSlot state and no UL PDCCH symbols allocated. Note: This example assumes only 1 PDCCH symbol is configured in K1 valid slots.[End CB012733-C-UPD001]

---

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.8 CORESET duration pattern selection

###### 3.25.1.3.2.2.8.0-1 CORESET duration pattern selection (ID: 11169720)

**3.25.1.3.2.2.8.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `12730820`)

CORESET duration pattern selection When the processing is completed for both directions, the gNB-DU must determine the coreset duration pattern expected according to the number of symbols of each slot and coreset duration pattern of the common channels already booked for the next PDCCH slot pattern.

The CORESET duration pattern selection processing applies the same principle as the one used to build the initial PDCCH slot pattern extended by the number of symbols expected.

For the slots modified in the initial PDCCH slot pattern, the gNB-DU selects, from the list of CORESET duration pattern identified at the Cell setup procedure (5G_UP_ALG_3949_replaced([11168409](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktv_kvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the CORESET duration pattern which handles the same number of symbols and the same number of PDCCH occasion(s) determined by the number of direction expected. When 2 symbols are required for a given direction and a CORESET on 2 symbols is configured in cell, the gNB-DU sets both in front of the slot in order to select the CORESET duration pattern with this CORESET on 2 symbols. Otherwise, if CCE split is removed, the same principle as in the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_8929_replaced([11169066](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt04FvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), is applied to define which direction is allocated first. 

Note: 5G_UP_ALG_8929_replaced([11169066](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt04FvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) has been updated for CA to ensure the the first pdcch occasion is dedicated to the downlink

If the slot has common channels configured, the downlink direction must be kept as defined in the initialized slot pattern as the number of PDCCH occasions for them. When one PDCCH occasion is added (whatever the direction), it is done after the booked resources.

For each slot with a CORESET duration pattern updated, the compatible pattern within the initial BWP is selected based of the presence of the CORESET(0) in the dedicated BWP.

The gNB-DU builds the search space lists for each slot as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_4022_replaced([11168667](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktx0wfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and updates the PDSCH start symbol.

[CB012733-B-UPD001] If NRCELL.actThreeSymbolPdcch is dynamic and actDynPdcchTdMode is not disabled, then   
CORESET duration patterns ULULDL shall be replaced by ULDLUL and DLDLUL shall be replaced by DLULDL . [End CB012733-B-UPD001]

---

#### 3.25.1.3.3 Dynamic Evaluation

##### 3.25.1.3.3.0-1 Dynamic Evaluation Lack of PDCCH resource (ID: 11169734)

**3.25.1.3.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `12785795`)

Dynamic Evaluation Priority of dynamic CORESET duration pattern evaluation and modification

---

**3.25.1.3.3.0-1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `12785796`)

Dynamic Evaluation With the introduction of the Search Space Set Group (SSSG) management, the UEs with or without SSSG RRC configuration share the same default PDCCH configuration (default SSSG config). when the UEs are configured with more than one SSSG configuration, the U-Plane may activate the UE on the additional SSSG (SSSG[>0]) or the default one (SSSG[0]).

The default and additional SSSG handles only the Type3 and UE-Specific search spaces. Therefore when the UE is involved in the RA procedure, the Type1 is used until the RA completion state (CFRA: transmission of the RA-Msg2, CBRA: DL or UL contention resolution according to the content of the RA-Msg3 and DCI format use for the contention resolution)

Whatever the active SSSG (default or additional), until the completion of the RA procedure, a lack of PDCCH triggered for the Type1 usage has the highest priority and the default procedures ([11169738: Dynamic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern for FDD configuration](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt5wkPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) & [11169758: Dynamic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern for TDD configuration](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt5wk_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) are applied.

When the lack of PDCCH is triggered for a Type3 or a UE-Specific search space, the priority depends on the active SSSG of the UE which trigger the lack of PDCCH.

If the trigger of the lack of PDCCH (Type3/UE-Specific) is for a UE scheduled with the additional SSSG index (confirmed or not), the dynamic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern in a target slot has the priority compared to a procedure triggered by a UE on the default SSSG even if it is not the first lack of PDCCH detected in the slot.

When a slot was already updated by a previous dynamic PDCCH update, Any new attempt to modify the PDDCH in this slot can be acknowledged only according the priority:

· Lack of PDCCH for Type1 when the previous update was triggered by Type3 or UE Specific search space whatever SSSG used

· Lack of PDCCH for Type3/UE-Specific for an additional SSSG when the previous update was not triggered for a Type1 or for a type3/UE-specific search space for the same additional SSSG.

· Lack of PDCCH for Type3/UE-Specific for a default SSSG when the previous update was not triggered for a Type1 or for a type3/UE-specific search space for the same additional SSSG or for Type3/UE-Specific for a default SSSG.

---

**3.25.1.3.3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11169738`)

Dynamic Evaluation Dynamic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern for FDD configuration

---

**3.25.1.3.3.0-1.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `13435683`)

Dynamic Evaluation 13435683: Dynamic Evaluation The lack of PDCCH, the schedulers are able to detect, in a slot of the active PDCCH slot pattern, are :  The expected search space is not allowed in the PDCCH occasion, because the associated CORESET is not not available for the expected direction in the PDCCH occasion. In that case, the UE is rejected in the current slot as it cannot be scheduled. The lack of PDCCH is a corrective defense procedure according to the context:  The lack of PDCCH is about Type 3 or UE-Specific.  The lack of PDCCH is about the Type 1 search space. For the lack of PDCCH Type 1, the presence of the CSI-RS or/and CSI-IM in the slots for which the procedure will check the availability of Type 1 must be taken into account when the RNTI triggering the lack of PDCCH is not able to apply a rate matching around CSI-RS and/or CSI-IM (RA-RNTI, TC-RNTI and C-RNTI without dedicated configuration). If the TDRA avoiding the overlap with the CSI-RS or/and CSI-IM are configured, then the regular procedure is applied. If no valid TDRA is configured, then for the pending RA-RNTI, the PDCCH update must not be in a slot with CSI-RS or/and CSI-IM (see hereafter the procedure).  The search space is allowed in the PDCCH occasion, but the CCE distribution in the associated CORESET (CCE allocated for the direction) is not compliant with the AL expected due to the CCE split. In that case, the UE is rejected in the current slot as it cannot be scheduled. The lack of PDCCH is a corrective defense procedure. When the lack of PDCCH Type 1 is detected the same principle as the previous case is applied when CSI-RS/IM will collide with the PDCCH update in a target slot.  The number of PDCCH candidate configured for the expected AL is not enough large to guarantee at least one DL & UL grant capability with a CCE split in the slot. In that case, the UE is maintained in the slot, because it may be scheduled anyway. The lack of PDCCH is a preventive defense procedure (see [11170311: Aggregation level for the C-RNTI](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-CCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) & [11170396: Dynamic AL selection procedure](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-pF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). If distributed PUCCH allocation algorithm is appliable according to 5G_UP_ALG_2885_replaced([11123447](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the L2PS add one PDCCH occasion and will select the first one for the direction which triggered the procedure. Now, it must check that it is possible to allocate the first PDCCH occasion for the DL and the second one for the UL. In case of dynamic re-evaluation for DL retransmission by DL scheduler, the PDCCH occasion for the other direction shall be skipped if it overlaps with the PDSCH symbols of the initial transmission in order to avoid lack of PDSCH. When the dynamic evaluation output, for a regular slot (without any common channel), handles 2 directions and contains 2 PDCCH occasions with the same list of search spaces (Type1 or/and Type3 or/and UE-Specific), the 5G-L2-PS allocates the first PDCCH occasion to the downlink scheduler and the second one to the uplink scheduler. If the dynamic evaluation output has only one direction the 5G-L2-PS must not change the new CORESET duration pattern allocation. Then, the scheduler checks in the active/passive PDCCH slot pattern whether this CORESET duration pattern is available from the current slot to a specific slot offset defined according to the source of scheduler and the current slot. If the expected CORESET duration pattern is not available, each scheduler changes the CORESET duration pattern in the slot offset(s) defined hereafter if the target slot does not handle the common channels:  For the downlink scheduler:  If the current slot is an even one and the current slot with the slot offset is not muted by PRB pooling feature or is not a slot with only CSI-IM and without the compatible TDRA when rate matching is not possible or is not a SS/PBCH slot handling the CSI-IM too, the slot offset applied is set to 2.  If the current slot is an even one and the current slot with the slot offset set to 2 is muted by PRB pooling feature or if the target slot is a slot handling the SS/PBCH (no check about the number of PDSCH RBs allowed for PDSCH), then the slotOffset is extended to 4.  If the current slot is an even one and the current slot with the slot offset set to 2 is handling a CSI-IM in symbol 4 and a RA-Msg2 is pending, then the slot offset is equal to 3 (it may have an interaction with the UL scheduler, but it is assumed that it would be rare enough collision between DCI Format 0_0 (TC-RNTI/C-RNTI) requested in the same target slot as the RA-Msg2 ).  If the current slot is an even one and the current slot with the slot offset set to 2 is handling a SS/PBCH slot (no check about the number of PDSCH RBS allowed for PDSCH) and a RA-Msg2 is pending, then the slot offset is equal to 4 to avoid the SS/PBCH slot (where the RA6msg2 may be rejected due to lack of PDSCH resources).  If the current slot is an odd one and the current slot with the slot offset is not muted by PRB pooling feature or is not a slot with only CSI-IM and without the compatible TDRA when rate matching is not possible or is not a SS/PBCH slot handling the CSI-IM too, the slot offset applied is set to 3.  If the current slot is an odd one and the current slot with the slot offset set to 3 is muted by PRB pooling feature or if the target slot is a slot handling the SS/PBCH (no check about the number of PDSCH RBs allowed for PDSCH), then the slotOffset is extended to 5.  If the current slot is an odd one and the current slot with the slot offset set to 3 is handling a CSI-IM in symbol 4 and a RA-Msg2 is pending, then the slot offset is equal to 2 (it may have an interaction with the UL scheduler, but it is assumed that it would be rare enough collision between DCI Format 0_0 (TC-RNTI/C-RNTI) requested in the same target slot as the RA-Msg2 ).  If the current slot is an odd one and the current slot with the slot offset set to 3 is handling a SS/PBCH slot (no check about the number of PDSCH RBS allowed for PDSCH) and a RA-Msg2 is pending, then the slot offset is equal to 5 to avoid the SS/PBCH slot (where the RA-Msg2 may be rejected due to lack of PDSCH resources).  For the uplink scheduler:  If the current slot is an even one and the current slot with the slot offset is not muted by PRB pooling feature, the slot offset applied is set to 3.  If the current slot is an even one and the current slot with the slot offset set to 3 is muted by PRB pooling feature, then the slotOffset is extended to 5.  If the current slot is an odd one and the current slot with the slot offset is not muted by PRB pooling feature, the slot offset applied is set to 2.  If the current slot is an odd one and the current slot with the slot offset set to 2 is muted by PRB pooling feature, then the slotOffset is extended to 4. [image-0][image_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating dynamic PDCCH slot updates in a communication system, likely a cellular network. It depicts four rows, each representing a different type of update over time. The horizontal axis represents time, marked with "even" and "odd" slots. The vertical axis is divided into four sections, labeled: 1\. **UL Dynamic PDCCH slot update** : This row shows a series of "UL" (Uplink) slots in light blue. There are several dashed arrows and solid blue arrows indicating dynamic updates or transmissions within these UL slots. Some UL slots are highlighted with a light grey diagonal pattern, suggesting a specific type of transmission or status. 2\. **DL Dynamic PDCCH slot update** : This row displays a series of "DL" (Downlink) slots in orange. Similar to the UL row, there are dashed and solid blue arrows indicating dynamic updates. A section of DL slots is highlighted with a darker orange hatched pattern, labeled as "Muted slot" in the legend at the bottom. 3\. **UL Dynamic PDCCH slot update** : This row is identical in appearance to the first row, showing "UL" slots in light blue with various arrows and grey highlighted slots. 4\. **DL Dynamic PDCCH slot update** : This row is identical in appearance to the second row, showing "DL" slots in orange, with arrows and a section of "Muted slot" highlighted with the hatched pattern. The legend at the bottom clarifies that the orange hatched slots represent "Muted slot". The diagram visually represents the scheduling and dynamic allocation of PDCCH (Physical Downlink Control Channel) slots for both uplink and downlink communications, with specific periods marked as muted.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12066.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] File: dynamicPdcchOneSlotUpdate.vsdx Folder: When the CORESET duration pattern modification is triggered for the initial BWP, the CORESET duration pattern must be determined for the BWPs overlapping the initial BWP in order to activate at least the same CORESET as for the initial BWP, the additional direction if needed and additional search spaces compatible with the allowed CORESET duration pattern for these BWPs. When the CORESET duration pattern modification is triggered for the dedicated BWP which overlaps the initial one, the CORESET duration pattern must be determined for the initial BWP by activating only the CORESET defined in the initial BWP which are also activated in the dedicated BWP with the same allocation (Direction/split CCE) within the dedicated BWP. If from the current slot to the slot offset, the CORESET duration pattern is not the one expected, the scheduler updates the PDCCH slot pattern (active or passive) with the new CORESET duration pattern and sends an intra scheduler message to the other scheduler in order to request an update, on its side, of its PDCCH slot pattern (active or passive) for the slot offset. Otherwise, the scheduler discards the new pattern built. If the modification of the CORESET duration pattern is for a slot in the passive PDCCH slot pattern and it is not yet built, the request is taken into account in the periodic PDCCH slot pattern evaluation if the target slot is not handling a common channel. After a dynamic CORESET duration pattern update, the scheduler which sent the message, waits for at least 2 slots before to request a new modification of the pattern. Note: Procedure described above doesn't apply if the cell is a cell shared with LTE and NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false. [Before PR877389] Note 2: In cells with NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true, Carrier Aggregation enabled and Coreset0 on two symbols the first PDCCH occasion is allocated to DL and lack of PDCCH for UL Grant using the first PDCCH occasion will not change the UL/DL PDCCH allocation. UL Grant in the first PDCCH occasion is needed for example for Type1 SS when msg3 re-transmission is needed. Coreset0 on two symbols may be used only by one PDCCH occasion. Such limitation may be common for or cells with CA and Coreset0 on two symbols. [PR877389] Note 2: After the lack of PDCCH procedure only two PDCCH occasions may be available in the slot even if three PDCCH occasions were available before starting the procedure. [End PR877389]

---

**3.25.1.3.3.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11169758`)

Dynamic Evaluation Dynamic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern for TDD configuration

---

**3.25.1.3.3.0-1.0-3.0-9**  (ID: `12816280`)

Dynamic Evaluation 12816280: Dynamic Evaluation The lack of PDCCH, the schedulers are able to detect, in a slot of the active PDCCH slot pattern, are :  The expected search space is not allowed in the PDCCH occasion, because the associated CORESET is not not available for the expected direction in the PDCCH occasion. In that case, the UE is rejected in the current slot as it cannot be scheduled. The lack of PDCCH is a corrective defense procedure.  The search space is allowed in the PDCCH occasion, but the CCE distribution in the associated CORESET (CCE allocated for the direction) is not compliant with the AL expected due to the CCE split. In that case, the UE is rejected in the current slot as it cannot be scheduled. The lack of PDCCH is a corrective defense procedure according the context: \- The lack of PDCCH is about Type 3 or UE-Specific search space. \- The lack of PDCCH is about Type 1 search space.  The search space is allowed in the PDCCH occasion, but the CCE distribution in the associated CORESET (CCE allocated for the direction) is not compliant with the AL expected due to the CCE split. In that case, the UE is rejected in the current slot as it cannot be scheduled. The lack of PDCCH is a corrective defense procedure.  The number of PDCCH candidate configured for the expected AL is not enough large to guarantee at least one DL & UL grant capability with a CCE split in the slot. In that case, the UE is maintained in the slot, because it may be scheduled anyway. The lack of PDCCH is a preventive defense procedure (see [11170311: Aggregation level for the C-RNTI](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-CCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) & [11170396: Dynamic AL selection procedure](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-pF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). For tdLte config0, as both schedulers will update the same target slot, it is not possible to have a configuration which may have an additional constraint on 1 PDCCH occasion among the ones available in the configuration (all search spaces must be configured in 2 PDCCH occasions and with the same set of AL allowed per search space type). By this way the slot updated will have always the capability to schedule the UE whatever the PDCCH occasion allocated in the schedulers. When the downlink scheduler detects a lack of PDCCH resource due to the DCI BWP switch constraint (no guarantee to have at least one PDCCH candidate in the set of CCEs allocated to the downlink (see 5G_UP_ALG_4066_replaced([11170311](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-CCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_4071_replaced([11170399](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-pGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))), it computes the new expected pattern by selecting the CORESET duration pattern with the expected CORESET and adding one more PDCCH occasion for the other direction if needed in order to remove a potential CCE split in a specific target slot (detailed hereafter). If distributed PUCCH allocation algorithm is appliable according to 5G_UP_ALG_2885_replaced([11123447](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqjhoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the L2PS add one PDCCH occasion and will select the first one for the direction which triggered the procedure. Now, it must check that it is possible to allocate the first PDCCH occasion for the DL and the second one for the UL. When the dynamic evaluation output, for a regular slot (without any common channel), handles 2 directions and contains 2 PDCCH occasions with the same list of search spaces (Type1 or/and Type3 or/and UE-Specific), the 5G-L2-PS allocates the first PDCCH occasion to the downlink scheduler and the second one to the uplink scheduler. If the dynamic evaluation output has only one direction the 5G-L2-PS must not change the new CORESET duration pattern allocation. Then, the scheduler checks in the active/passive PDCCH slot pattern whether this CORESET duration pattern is available from the current slot on a slot window defined hereafter according to the source of scheduler and the frame structure. If the expected CORESET duration pattern is not available, each scheduler changes the CORESET duration pattern in the first slot within the monitored window which does not handle the common channels and the following constraints: · For the downlink scheduler and cell configuration handling some slots with only DL grant capability: \- For the lack of specific search space or CCE, the scheduler selects the first slot without uplink grant capability within a window of 11 slots starting from the current slot to apply the CORESET duration pattern modification. When the modification trigger is about a common search space (searchSpaceType set to "type1", "type3" or "common" in the PsCell_CellSetupReq), the BI slots are not eligible. As the modification is applied to downlink slot only, the scheduler does not need to update the other direction \- For the lack of guarantee about the presence of at least one PDCCH candidate and for a DCI BWP switch in tdLte frame structure, the scheduler selects the next slot with a gap of 10 slots to apply the CORESET duration pattern modification which leads to deactivate the CCE split. As the modification is applied to a slot with downlink and uplink grant capability, the scheduler must update the PDCCH slot pattern of the uplink scheduler · For the downlink scheduler and cell configuration handling only slots with UL & DL grant capability: \- For the configuration with a fame structure 4 slots DL and 4 slots UL, If the current slot is an even one and the current slot with the slot offset is not muted by PRB pooling feature, the slot offset applied is set to 2 slots with DL and UL grant capability. If the current slot is an odd one and the current slot with the slot offset is not muted by PRB pooling feature, the slot offset applied is set to 3. \- In tdLte config0 frame structure, for the lack of CCEs in first 2 bi-directional slots with starting in index N, slot N+10 is selected to deactivate the CCE split and for the next two bidirectional slots, slot N+11 is selected to deactivate the CCE split. · For the uplink scheduler and cell configuration handling some slots with only DL grant capability: \- The scheduler selects the first slot **compatible with the restricted candidate slots for a UE whose scheduling was impacted in case RIM mitigation extension was triggered (seen in 5G_UP_ALG_27198_replaced([11195190](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv6iwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **among the one with only uplink grant capability or the one with uplink and downlink grant capabilities and with at least 1 additional slot gap from the current slot within a window of 11 slots starting from the current slot to apply the CORESET duration pattern modification. As the slot selected may handle downlink grant capability, the scheduler must update the PDCCH slot pattern of the downlink scheduler. In case of UE scheduled in Sparse SSSG the window of 21 slots starting from the current slot can be used.**_* · For the uplink scheduler and cell configuration handling only slots with UL & DL grant capability: \- For the configuration with a fame structure 4 slots DL and 4 slots UL, If the current slot is an even one and the current slot with the slot offset is not muted by PRB pooling feature, the slot offset applied is set to 3 slots with DL and UL grant capability. If the current slot is an odd one and the current slot with the slot offset is not muted by PRB pooling feature, the slot offset applied is set to 2. \- In tdLte config0 frame structure, for the lack of CCEs in first 2 bi-directional slots with starting in index N, slot N+10 is selected to deactivate the CCE split and for the next two bidirectional slots, slot N+11 is selected to deactivate the CCE split. [image-0][image_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating different frame structures and their corresponding UL (Uplink) and DL (Downlink) Dynamic PDCCH (Physical Downlink Control Channel) slot updates over time. The diagram is organized into several rows, each representing a specific frame structure with a defined number of UL and DL slots. Within each row, there are two sub-rows: one for UL Dynamic PDCCH slot updates and another for DL Dynamic PDCCH slot updates. The time axis is shown at the bottom, marked with "even" and "odd" intervals, indicating the progression of time. Different colored blocks represent different types of slots, and arrows indicate the timing and dependencies of the PDCCH slot updates. A legend at the bottom explains the meaning of each color: * _*Green:** Slots with DL and UL grant capabilities with reduced DL symbols. * **Light Green:** Slots with DL and UL grant capabilities. * **Purple:** Slots with DL grant capability and reduced DL symbols. * **Blue:** Slots without UL grant capability. * **Yellow:** Slots without DL grant capability. * **Orange:** Slots with DL and UL(2 x k₂) grant capabilities. * **Hatched areas:** Indicate a combination of DL and UL grant capabilities. The diagram shows how the UL and DL Dynamic PDCCH slots are scheduled and updated across various frame structures, including: * **Frame structure 3 UL; 7 DL slots:** Depicts UL and DL PDCCH slot updates. * **Frame structure 1 UL; 4 DL slots:** Shows UL and DL PDCCH slot updates. * **Frame structure 2 UL; 8 DL slots:** Illustrates UL and DL PDCCH slot updates, including a "DCI BWP switch (workaround for lack of candidates slots)" indicated by a blue arrow. * **Frame structure 4 UL; 4 DL slots:** Presents UL and DL PDCCH slot updates. * **Frame structure tdLte config0 6 UL; 4 DL slots:** Shows UL and DL PDCCH slot updates. The arrows connecting different slots represent the timing of control information transmission and reception. Dotted arrows typically indicate a potential or indirect relationship, while solid arrows show direct dependencies or transmissions. The "D" and "U" labels within the slots denote Downlink and Uplink transmissions, respectively, and "D/U" indicates a slot that can be used for either Downlink or Uplink.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/img-09281159.png[/image_path][/image-0] File: dynamicPdcchOneSlotUpdate.vsdx Folder: If a slot is selected, the CORESET duration pattern is modified and the scheduler updates the PDCCH slot pattern (active or passive) with the new CORESET duration pattern and sends, if needed, an intra scheduler message to the other scheduler in order to request an update, on its side, of its PDCCH slot pattern (active or passive) for the slot offset. Otherwise, the scheduler discards the new pattern built. If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is true and actBbPoolExtensionTddFr1 is true and actTddCsirsOpt is false **[CB015668-A] (note: actTddCsirsOpt is not get from NIDD but from L3 indicator)**[End CB015668-A]**_* and actTddCsirsAllocOptimization_ *is false**, only up to 2 PDCCH symbols (symbol 0 and symbol 1) can be used for FR1-TDD BW 10MHz and 15MHz in the Cell Specific CSI-RS slots which are determined in 5G_UP_ALG_11874_replaced([11117149](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp9rwPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). When the CORESET duration pattern modification is triggered for the initial BWP, the CORESET duration pattern must be determined for the BWPs overlapping the initial BWP in order to activate at least the same CORESET as for the initial BWP, the additional direction if needed and additional search spaces compatible with the allowed CORESET duration pattern for these BWPs. When the CORESET duration pattern modification is triggered for the dedicated BWP which overlaps the initial one, the CORESET duration pattern must be determined for the initial BWP by activating only the CORESET defined in the initial BWP which are also activated in the dedicated BWP with the same allocation (Direction/split CCE) within the dedicated BWP. If the modification of the CORESET duration pattern is for a slot in the passive PDCCH slot pattern and it is not yet built, the request is taken into account in the periodic PDCCH slot pattern evaluation if the target slot is not handling a common channel. If the modification of the CORESET duration pattern triggered by USS PDCCH shortage during the period PDCCH slot pattern calculation interval, targets a slot in the passive PDCCH slot pattern and it is being built, the modification request is ignored to avoid CCE resources mismatch between DL and UL schedulers due to overlapped writing. After a dynamic CORESET duration pattern update, the scheduler which sent the message, waits for at least 2 slots before to request a new modification of the pattern.

---

**3.25.1.3.3.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `12785802`)

Dynamic Evaluation **Dynamic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern for UE configured with more than one SSSG**

---

**3.25.1.3.3.0-1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12785803`)

Dynamic Evaluation When the UE is configured with more than one SSSG and when the active SSSG is the additional one or until the active SSSG confirmation procedure, it is needed to avoid UL and DL lack of PDCCH for the same target slot.

When two types of slots (with and without k2) are configured within the additional SSSG, the dynamic PDCCH updates triggered by DL use only the slots without k2 and dynamic PDCCH updates triggered by UL the slots with k2.

When all slots within the additional SSSG are k2 slots, the dynamic PDCCH updates triggered by DL use the even occurrences of the SSSG slots (SSSG slots are indexes from 0 in the PDCCH slot pattern). The dynamic PDCCH updates triggered by UL use the odd occurrences of the SSSG slots.

When the dynamic PDCCH updates are triggered during the reevaluation of the PDCCH slot pattern and modify the next 20ms PDCCH slot pattern (5 last ms in odd SFN), the U-Plane must save the expected updates and apply them when the next PDCCH slot pattern is activated.

---

##### 3.25.1.3.3.0-2 Dynamic Evaluation TDD perBWP - Lack of PDSCH resources (ID: 11169802)

**3.25.1.3.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11169813`)

Dynamic Evaluation [CNI-115833]

For TDD NRCELL.actDynPdcchTdMode is set to 'perBWP': [End CNI-115833]

When the downlink schedulers detects the lack of PDSCH resources to handle a retransmission (due to number of PDSCH symbols is not enough) in a slot in the active PDCCH slot pattern, it computes the new expected pattern by selecting the CORESET duration pattern with the expected CORESET and keep the PDCCH occasion same as initial transmission, in order to get the expected PDSCH time domain allocation for the retransmission.

When the dynamic evaluation output, for a regular slot (without any common channel), handles 2 directions and contains 2 PDCCH occasions with the same list of search spaces (Type1 or/and Type3 or/and UE-Specific), the 5G-L2-PS allocates the first PDCCH occasion to the downlink schduler and the second one to the uplink scheduler. If the dynamic evaluation output has only one direction the 5G-L2-PS must not change the new CORESET duration pattern allocation.

Then, the scheduler checks in the active/passive PDCCH slot pattern whether this CORESET duration pattern is available according to a specific slot offset defined hereafter and the current slot:

[Before CNI-115833]

For FDD:

· If the current slot is an even one, the slot offset applied is set to 2.

· If the current slot is an odd one, the slot offset applied is set to 3.

If from the current slot to the slot offset, the CORESET duration pattern is not the one expected, the scheduler updates the PDCCH slot pattern (active or passive) with the new CORESET duration pattern and sends an intra scheduler message to the other scheduler in order to request an update, on its side, of its PDCCH slot pattern (active or passive) for the slot offset. Otherwise, the scheduler discards the new pattern built.

After a dynamic CORESET duration pattern update, the scheduler which sent the message, waits for at least 2 slots before to request a new modification of the pattern.

[CNI-115833]

the slot offset shall refer to the 'For the downlink scheduler' part in 5G_UP_ALG_3986_replaced([11169738](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt5wkPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CNI-115833]

Note: Procedure described above doesn't apply if the cell is a cell shared with LTE.

[End Before CNI-115833]

For TDD:

[End Before CNI-115833]

The scheduler selects the first slot without uplink grant capability within a window of 20 slots starting from the current slot to apply the CORESET duration pattern modification. As the modification is applied to downlink slot only, the scheduler does not need to update the other direction.

[CNI-115833] Note: CNI-115833's update in SFS part is just to keep aligned with software implementation. [End CNI-115833]

### 3.25.1.4 CCE Candidates

#### 3.25.1.4.0-1 CCE Candidates Document Owner Oleksandr Andryeyev (ID: 11169821)

#### 3.25.1.4.1 Search Spaces and Control Channel Element distribution

##### 3.25.1.4.1.0-1 Search Spaces and Control Channel Element distribution Overview (ID: 11169830)

**3.25.1.4.1.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13117224`)

Search Spaces and Control Channel Element distribution For each UE-Specific Search Space and the Common Search Space for the RA procedure (Type1-PDCCH), the 5G-L2-PS checks the capability to support the CCE split allocation between the downlink and uplink direction according to the value of the BWP_PROFILE.PDCCH.dciDedicatedAggregationLevel and during the cell setup [CB014330-F-UPD001] or reconfiguration [End CB014330-F-UPD001] procedure. The AL selection mode, i.e., BWP_PROFILE.PDCCH.alSelection (static or dynamic) could be activated/deactivated online and this capability is not compatible with the adaptive PDCCH algorithm.

---

##### 3.25.1.4.1.0-2 Search Spaces and Control Channel Element distribution CCE split condition (ID: 11169840)

**3.25.1.4.1.0-2.0-5**  (ID: `13343056`)

Search Spaces and Control Channel Element distribution **Whatever the PDCCH configuration, the 5G-L2-PS considers first the CORESET(s) associated to the UE-Specific search spaces starting to the lowest symbol in the front of the slot. For these ones, the following formula is used to define whether the CORESET could split or not with the BWP_PROFILE.PDCCH.dciDedicatedAggregationLevel. If several CORESETs with several duration allows the CCE split, then the 5G-LS-PS selects the CORESET according to the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_3949_replaced([11168409](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktv_kvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) defining the combination of the CORESET allowed for the CCE split.**

If there is a CORESET not used in any UE-Specific search space, activated through a search space and with its last duration symbol not after the CORESET used for the CCE split of the UE-Specific search space, the 5G-L2-PS checks first if the CORESET may handle the CCE split according to its frequency domain position and the interaction with the UE-Specific search space (see 5G_UP_ALG_3949_replaced([11168409](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktv_kvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). If its frequency domain and CCE mapping are compatible with the CCE split, the 5G-L2-PS checks if the CCE split is allowed for this CORESET [Before CB014330-G] with the largest AL configured between the BWP_PROFILE.PDCCH.dciRaCompletionAggregationLevel and BWP_PROFILE.PDCCH.dciDedicatedAggregationLevel [CB014330-G] based on the following formula [End CB014330-G]. 

If _N_ CCE _> = 2x _CCE _AL_ and number of candidates belongs to n2 to n8, then***** *

CCE split is allowed;

else if DSS with NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true and if any dedicated coreset>0 overlaps the LTE shared area (see [12620260: Resource sharing in asymmetric DSS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_NsAEcDfZEfCYiuaHdt7wgQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))   
the CCE split is allowed in symbol#2  
Note: the CCE split is allowed in symbol#2 regardless of the supported aggregation levels. For asymmetric DSS, CCEs are available in symbols #0 and #1 with no CCE split and the symbol#2 doesn't need to have CCEs for maximum aggregation level for both UL and DL. 

Otherwise, CCE split is not allowed;

With,

_CCE_ AL _:_ **

Number of CCEs according to [Before CB014330-G] the Aggregation Level (dciDedicatedAggregationLevel) for the dedicated traffic (UE-Specific search space) or the largest AL between the dciRaCompletionAggregationLevel and dciDedicatedAggregationLevel for the CORESET not used in the UE-Specific search space [CB014330-G] 

  * Aggregation level dciDedicatedAggregationLevel in case of CORESET used in UE-Specific search space
  * Aggregation level dciRaCompletionAggregationLevel in case of CORESET used in Type1 search space but not used in UE-Specific search space



where dciDedicatedAggregationLevel and dciRaCompletionAggregationLevel are [End CB014330-G] received during cell setup or cell reconfiguration:

 1 CCE for AL1,

 2 CCEs for AL2,

 4 CCEs for AL4,

 8 CCEs for AL8,

 16 CCEs for AL16.

_N_ CCE _:_ **

The 5G-L2-PS compute the number of CCE within a given PDCCH occasion of a search space with the following formula.

_N_ CCE _= rounddown (_ coresetSize * _coresetDuration / 6 );_ ****

With,

_coresetSize :_

CORESET size (RB) computed by the 5G-L2-PS from the coresetFreqDomain attribute (each bit represents 6 RBs) received at the PsCell_CellSetupReq message and associated to the search space.

_coresetDuration :_

The coresetDuration attribute is received in the PsCell_CellSetupReq message for the coreset associated to the search space.

When NRCELL.actPagingSsbOptimization=twoBeamsPerSlot and 2 PDCCH occasions for paging are valid per slot within PO CCE Split is allowed only in the last duration symbol.

When NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true the CCE Split is not allowed if none of coresets overlaps the LTE shared area. If any coreset overlaps the LTE shared area the CCE split is allowed in symbol #2.  
Note: for DSS with NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true the common channels (Paging, SIB1, OSI) are not using CCEs in symbol #2, and only symbol#2 may have a CCE split for asymmetric DSS. 

Parameter full name:

 dciRaCompletionAggregationLevel: NRBTS.BWP_PROFILE.PDCCH.dciRaCompletionAggregationLevel

 dciDedicatedAggregationLevel: NRBTS.BWP_PROFILE.PDCCH.dciDedicatedAggregationLevel

---

##### 3.25.1.4.1.0-3 Search Spaces and Control Channel Element distribution CCE Split starting index (ID: 11169860)

**3.25.1.4.1.0-3.0-5**  (ID: `12590748`)

Search Spaces and Control Channel Element distribution If the cell is a cell shared with LTE [CB007372-A] and NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false [End CB007372-A]

Then 

  * For a CORESET size between AL * dssMaxNumberOfDlDcis and AL * (dssMaxNumberOfDlDcis + 1 ) – 1 the split is starting at CCE index AL.
  * For a CORESET size larger than or equal to AL * (dssMaxNumberOfDlDcis + 1 ) the split is starting at CCE index AL * dssMaxNumberOfDlDcis.



where AL is defined by 

max(dciDedicatedAggregationLevel, dciRaMsg2AggregationLevel, [CB014330-SR-F-UPD001] dciRaCompletionAggregationLevel) (Note: dciRaCompletionAggregationLevel added to keep alignment with implementation, this mismatch found during CB014330-F) [End CB014330-SR-F-UPD001]

of the dedicated BWP.

When the split is allowed, the CCEs starting from lowest available index are allocated to DL and the CCEs in the second area are allocated to UL. There is no alternation among DL and UL.

**When the DL PRB sharing in subframe 0/5/9 is enabled (rrmLteDLPrbSharing=TRUE 5G_UP_ALG_4722_replaced([11172097](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuJoPfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) CCE split mode (5G_UP_ALG_12060_replaced([11169840](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6Xo_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in subframe 0,5 and 9 shall be calculated based on available number of CCEs - Ncce'.**

Ncce' considers only CCE assigned to NR in these subframes according to according to values received in EN DSS DL CELL RESOURCE AREA ALLOCATION REQUEST 5G_UP_ALG_4744_replaced([11172253](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuK2VPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

else if the CCE split is allowed in slots with Paging [CB007372-B] and the cell is not shared with LTE [End CB007372-B], in these slots:

The split is starting at the CCE index = (CCEs for dciPagingAggregationLevel) + (((CCEs in the CORESET) - (CCEs for dciPagingAggregationLevel)) /2 )

CCEs starting from lowest available index are allocated to DL and the CCEs in the second area are allocated to UL.

When NRCELL.actPagingSsbOptimization=twoBeamsPerSlot and 2 PDCCH occasions for paging are valid per slot within PO, **CCEs allocated to DL and UL are determined in 5G_UP_ALG_29416_replaced([11169895](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6-sPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

There is no alternation among DL and UL **in slots with Paging.**

else if the CCE split is allowed in slots with SIB1 or OSI (Type0-PDCCH, Type0A-PDCCH) [CB007372-B] and the cell is not shared with LTE [End CB007372-B], in these slots:

The split is starting at the CCE index = (CCEs for dciSiAggregationLevel) + (((CCEs in the CORESET) - (CCEs for dciSiAggregationLevel)) /2 )

CCEs starting from lowest available index are allocated to DL and the CCEs in the second area are allocated to UL.

There is no alternation among DL and UL **in slots with SIB1 or OSI.**

else

For the CORESET associated to the UE-Specific Search Spaces and the Common Search Space (Type1-PDCCH), when the CCE split is allowed, the 5G-L2-PS applies the split starting from the following CCE according to the size of the CORESET:

 For a CORESET size between 4 and 7 CCEs, the split is starting at CCE index 2 (it requires to not cross AL2 for the RA procedure and the dedicated traffic)

 For a CORESET size between 8 and 11 CCEs, the split is starting at the CCE index 4.

 For a CORESET size between 12 and 23 CCEs, the split is starting at the CCE index 8.

 For a CORESET size between 24 and 47 CCEs, the split is starting at the CCE index 16.

 For a CORESET size above 47 CCEs, the split is starting at the CCE index 32.

[CB007372-B] For DSS with NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true the two areas defined by the CCE split are allocated to each direction according to [12658544: CCE split for asymmetric DSS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_vqrj8UqyEfC0Ye3M8ARUWQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). Otherwise [End CB007372-B] The two areas defined by the CCE split are allocated alternately to each direction according to the slot number handling the search space.

For the even slots and when the CCE split is allowed, then the CCEs starting from CCE 0 are allocated to the downlink and the CCEs of the second area are allocated to the uplink.

For the odd slots, both areas are swapped.

Refer 5G_UP_ALG_32469_replaced([11169885](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6XrPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for CCE split start index computation in 5G FR1 TDD frame compatible with tdLte configuration0 in slots with 2 K2 and 1 K1 values.

Note: for DSS [CB007372-A] with NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false [End CB007372-A], this requirement applies to CORESET0 and CORESET1 depending on USS configuration  
[CB007372-A]  
Note2: For NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true with all coresets not overlapping the LTE shared area this requirement is not applicable.  
[End CB007372-A]  
[CB007372-B] For DSS with NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true and if any dedicated coreset>0 overlaps the LTE shared area (see [12620260: Resource sharing in asymmetric DSS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_NsAEcDfZEfCYiuaHdt7wgQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) this requirement applies to coreset>0 overlapping the LTE shared area. [End CB007372-B] 

Parameter full name:

dssMaxNumberOfDlDcis: NRBTS.NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.dssMaxNumberOfDlDcis

dciDedicatedAggregationLevel: NRBTS.BWP_PROFILE.PDCCH.dciDedicatedAggregationLevel

dciRaMsg2AggregationLevel: NRBTS.BWP_PROFILE.PDCCH.dciRaMsg2AggregationLevel

dciRaCompletionAggregationLevel: NRBTS.BWP_PROFILE.PDCCH.dciRaCompletionAggregationLevel

dciPagingAggregationLevel: NRBTS.BWP_PROFILE.PDCCH.dciPagingAggregationLevel

dciSiAggregationLevel: NRBTS.BWP_PROFILE.PDCCH.dciSiAggregationLevel

---

##### 3.25.1.4.1.0-4 Search Spaces and Control Channel Element distribution CCE Split starting index for tdLte config0 frame structure (ID: 11169885)

**3.25.1.4.1.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `12658466`)

Search Spaces and Control Channel Element distribution In case of 5G FR1 TDD frame compatible with tdLte configuration0 in cell BWs >40MHz [CB009422-E]and when at least one BWP with 20-40MHz is not configured in the cell[End CB009422-E] in slots with 2 K2 and 1 K1 values, if slot indices are 2 and 12 below CCE split shall be followed in symbols 0 and 1:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |   
---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---  
Coreset sizes for split index | CCE # in 1 symbol | CCE # in 2 symbols | CCE split index in symbol0 | CCE split index in symbol1 | CCE # for DL in slot 2/12 | CCE # for UL scheduler1 | CCE # for UL scheduler2  
**192-270** | 32-45 | 64-90 | 16 | 24 | 24-37 | 16 - 29 | 24  
**144-186** | 24-31 | 48-62 | 8 | 16 | 16-23 | 16 - 23 | 16  
**96-138** | 16-23 | 32-46 | 8 | 8 | 16-23 | 8 - 15 | 8  
  
and in slots 3 and 13, following CCE split shall be followed in symbols 0 and 1:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |   
---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---  
Coreset sizes for split index | CCE # in 1 symbol | CCE # in 2 symbols | CCE split index in symbol0 | CCE split index in symbol1 | CCE # for DL in slot 3/13 | CCE # for UL scheduler 1 | CCE # for UL scheduler 2  
**240-270** | 40-45 | 80-90 | 32 | 16 | 24-29 | 32 | 24-29  
**192-234** | 32-39 | 64-78 | 24 | 8 | 24-31 | 24 | 16-23  
**144-186** | 24-31 | 48-62 | 16 | 8 | 16-23 | 16 | 16-23  
**96-138** | 16-23 | 32-46 | 8 | 8 | 16-23 | 8 | 8-15  
  
When multiple BWPs are configured and the size of the smallest BWP is >40 MHz, then the CCE split index in all the BWPs are determined by the smallest dedicated CORESET referring above tables. 

Note1: Only 1 symbol Coreset is supported for above BWs in 5G FR1 TDD frame compatible with tdLte configuration0.

Note2: in case of 2 K2 values but no K1, there is no CCE split as there is 2 symbol PDCCH and it shall be used for 2 UL schedulers. UL scheduler 1 refers to the UL slot with lowest K2 and UL scheduler 2 refers to the UL slot with highest K2.

In tdLte configuration0 and BWs <20 MHz, in slots with with 2 K2s and 1 K1, **in the CORESET of 1st PDCCH occasion the CCEs starting from CCE 0 are allocated to DL** for even and odd slots and CCEs of the second area are allocated to UL. UL scheduler 1 uses the second area of the CORESET of 1st PDCCH occasion and UL scheduler 2 uses the CORESET of the 2nd PDCCH occasion. **Refer 5G_UP_14028_replaced([11362289](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uc7VePvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for examples.******

Note: As the CCE split result in above tables are only applicable to tdLte config0 frame structure in BWs >40MHz and in slots with 2 K2 and 1 K1 values, the CCE split indices need to be hardcoded and injected to periodical (2 SFN) PDCCH slot pattern result.

##### 3.25.1.4.1.0-5 Search Spaces and Control Channel Element distribution CCE list with multiple  PDCCH occasions for paging per slot within PO (ID: 11169895)

**3.25.1.4.1.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11169902`)

Search Spaces and Control Channel Element distribution 11169902: Search Spaces and Control Channel Element distribution When NRCELL.actPagingSsbOptimization=twoBeamsPerSlot and 2 PDCCH occasions for paging are valid per slot within PO, for every bandwidth parts overlaping the initial one 5G-L2-PS shall prepare list with CCEs available for paging in every configured symbol (0,1) and shall determine PDCCH direction assignment as below:

All CCEs in symbol 0 shall be assigned do DL direction and pree-empted according to 5G_UP_ALG_4032_replaced([11169907](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6-svvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

All CCEs in symbol 1 which are using at least one position of a Resource Element Group (REG) needed for the Paging transmissions shall be marked as not-available for UL direction.

Irrespectivaly of NIDD parameter NRBTS/BWP_PROFILE/PDCCH/dciPagingAggregationLevel value the whole area covered by Coreset#0 shall be considered here as reserved for paging within this symbol.

CCEs marked as not-available for UL direction shall be then assigned do DL direction and pree-empted according to 5G_UP_ALG_4032_replaced([11169907](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6-svvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

##### 3.25.1.4.1.0-6 Search Spaces and Control Channel Element distribution CCE split for asymmetric DSS (ID: 12658544)

**3.25.1.4.1.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `13398550`)

Search Spaces and Control Channel Element distribution 13398550: Search Spaces and Control Channel Element distribution If the cell is a cell shared with LTE and NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true and if any dedicated coreset>0 overlaps the LTE shared area (see [12620260: Resource sharing in asymmetric DSS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_NsAEcDfZEfCYiuaHdt7wgQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) then CCE split is allowed on the symbol #2. The dedicated coreset used in symbol #2 has always coresetDuration=1 and shall be non-interleaved. If the dedicated coreset overlapping the shared area is interleaved then Cell Setup shall be failed. PDCCH without CCE split is also available on symbols #0 and 1.

The two areas defined by the CCE split are allocated to each direction according to direction of the first PDCCH occasion.  
The first area size in CCEs, starting from CCE0, is equal to CCE split index.  
The second area size in CCEs, starting from CCE split index, is equal to coreset size divided by 6 - CCE split index.

If the first PDCCH occasion is allocated to DL and LTE shared area is bottom aligned or   
If the first PDCCH occasion is allocated to UL and LTE shared area is top aligned  
then  
\- the CCEs starting from CCE 0 are allocated to the downlink and the CCEs of the second area are allocated to the uplink. nCCE_DL equals to the first area size. nCCE_UL equals to the second area size

otherwise  
\- the CCEs starting from CCE 0 are allocated to the uplink and the CCEs of the second area are allocated to the downlink. nCCE_UL equals to the first area size. nCCE_DL equals to the second area size

Reasoning: If the first PDCCH occasion is allocated to one direction then, in symbol with CCE split, in NR dedicated area we want to have CCEs allocated to another direction. 

Note 1: If the CCE split is disabled in the first PDCCH occasion then the first PDCCH occasion is allocated to DL in even slots and to UL in odd slots. In slots with any search spaces for the common channels (Type0,Type0A, Type2) the first PDCCH occasion is allocated to DL. The allocation of the first PDCCH occasion may be modified by dynamic evaluation ([11169730](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt5JjfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [Before PR877389]. See [11169066](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt04FvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) for more details. [PR877389] or periodic evaluation ([11168988](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt0RA_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).  
If the allocation of the first PDCCH occasion is modified by the dynamic evaluation:  
\- if coreset0 has 24 PRBs, two symbols then symbols 0&1 are enforced in the desired direction and symbol 2 is enforced in the opposite direction (no more splitted).  
\- if coreset0 has 48 PRBs, one symbol then symbol 0 is enforced in the desired direction, symbol 1 is enforced in the opposite direction and symbol 2 is not used.  
[End PR877389] 

Note 2: CCE split in symbol#2 is present if both UL and DL Grants are needed in given slot. Otherwise, there is no PDCCH on symbol#2 and only symbols 0&1 are used for PDCCH. For example, such situation may happen in SSB slots when numPdschPrbInSsbSlots=0 or in TRS slots when numPdschPrbInTrsSlots=0. 

[CB007372-E]  
Note 3: When more than one dedicated BWP is configured and the dedicated CORESET of the largest BWP overlaps the shared area then the CCE split index is selected for the dedicated CORESET of the largest BWP. Dedicated CORESET(s) from smaller BWP(s) may have the CCE split or not, depending on the CRB split index of the dedicated CORESET of the largest BWP. See [11168434: Control Resource Set Duration Pattern in Case of Multiple Dedicated BWPs](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktv_lfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).  
[End CB007372-E] 

Examples for LTE shared area at bottom of the NR carrier:
