#### 3.25.1.4.2 CCE pre-emption List update

##### 3.25.1.4.2.0-1 CCE pre-emption List update CCE Pre-emption List Update (ID: 11169911)

**3.25.1.4.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11169915`)

CCE pre-emption List update As for the common channels, the Control Channel Elements used are identified before the search space list update process. Then, the 5G-L2-PS computes the list of preempted CCEs for each UE-Specific Search Space in the list, which are using at least one position of a Resource Element Group (REG) already booked for the SIB1, OSI or Paging transmissions.

This pre-emption is done for all bandwidth parts overlapping the initial one.

To build this list, the 5G-L2-PS builds at the PsCell_CellSetupReq the following information in order to identify the CCE pre-empted in all PDCCH occasions by any allocation in a specific PDCCH occasion:

 For the channel bandwidth, the 5G-L2-PS builds for each CRB and ODFM symbol handling PDCCH occasion, the data identifying the search space and CORESET identifiers, the PDCCH occasion, CCE, REG and bundle indexes.

 For each CORESET, the 5G-L2-PS builds the list of CCEs characteristics (bundle, list of REG within the bundle, CRB and symbol indexes).

The 5G-L2-PS idenfies the position within the channel bandwidth of each REG of each CORESET configured in the cell.

A Resource Element Group equals one Resource Block during one OFDM symbol. REG within a given CORESET are numbered in increasing order in a time first manner, starting with 0 for the first OFDM symbol of the CORESET and the lowest numbered Common Resource Block in the control resource set.

The REG bundle index of a REG within a CORESET is computed as follows.

bundleIdxREG,CORESET = rounddown ( regIdxCORESET / regBundleSizeCORESET )

With,

regIdxCORESET: REG index within the CORESET selected.

regBundleSizeCORESET: Number of REG within a bundle dedined in the CORESET structure received in the PsCell_CellSetup message.

The REG to CCE mapping could be interleaved or not according to the parameter set by the operator for each CORESET.

The interleaving, when activated, is done at the bundle level according to the interleaver row attribute received in the PsCell_CellSetupReq. The relation between the bundle and CCE indexes are detailed hereafter.

cceIdx = rounddown (cceBundleIdx x regBundleSize / 6 )

With,

regBundleSize: Number of REG per bundle received in the PsCell_CellSetupReq.

cceBundleIdx: Absolute bundle index between 0 and the maximum index computed as follow

maxCceBundleIdx = NRB x coresetDuration / regBundleSize - 1

With,

coresetDuration: Number of symbols within the CORESET and received in the PsCell_CellSetupReq.

NRB: Number of RB within the CORESET derived from the coresetFreqDomain attribute received in the PsCell_CellSetupReq.

Then, the 5G-L2-PS compute the CORESET bundle associated to each CCE bundle index as follows.

coresetBundlecceBundleIdx = [ (cceBundleIdx mod interleaverRows ) x ( NRB x coresetDuration / (regBundleSize x interleaverRows))+ rounddown (cceBundleIdx / interleaverRows ) + nShift ] mod ( NRB x coresetDuration / regBundleSize )

Each CCE contains 1, 2 or 3 consecutives CCE bundle index according to the size of the bundle to reach 6 REG per CCE.

When the non interleaving is activated, the bundle sze is equal to 6 REGs and each CCE contains only one bundle. The index of the bundle is equal to the index of the CCE.

---

##### 3.25.1.4.2.0-2 CCE pre-emption List update CCE Pre-emption List Update with Several Dedicated Bandwidth Parts per Cell (ID: 11169919)

**3.25.1.4.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11169924`)

CCE pre-emption List update 5G-L2-PS shall update CCE pre-emption list as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_4033_replaced([11169911](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6-s_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) also if two dedicated bandwidth parts per cell are configured with one common dedicated PDCCH configuration.

#### 3.25.1.4.3 PDCCH Capacity Re-Evaluation with PRB Pooling

##### 3.25.1.4.3.0-1 PDCCH Capacity Re-Evaluation with PRB Pooling Resources Elements Group (REG) monitoring and Number of Usable CCEs (ID: 11169932)

**3.25.1.4.3.0-1.0-10**  (ID: `12678906`)

PDCCH Capacity Re-Evaluation with PRB Pooling 12678906: PDCCH Capacity Re-Evaluation with PRB Pooling When PRB pooling is enabled (slowPrbPoolingAllowed is set to 'true') or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is True (5G_CP_ARC_ALG_4283_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed is set to 'true' , all CCEs may not be available for use and the number of CCEs that can be used is limited by the total amount of usable PRB in DL. The total usable PRB limit in DL as per amount of DL PRBs (numAllocCellPrb(DL)) granted by the Based Band Resource Manager (BBRM) _and this may change every bbPoolEvalPeriod (refer 5G_UP_ALG_6781_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) as per 5G_UP_ALG_6500_replaced([11212285](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The minimum number of RBs DL available in any slot is never lower than the limit computed by the C-Plane according to the state of the DSS mode, the DL largest dedicated BWP in the cell (5G_CP_ARC_ALG_4269_replaced([11277368](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpMt7fvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))._ When only one PDCCH occasion is used in a slot with Dl and UL grant capabilities, the CCEs within this PDCCH occasion is split in two areas and each of them is allocated to a given direction. The number of available CCEs in each area is impacted by the number of RBs available. Only the number of available CCEs could be modified and the CCE split index (5G_UP_ALG_3955_replaced([11169860](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6Xp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) must not be modified. In any case, the number of RBs available always respects the split condition defined in 5G_UP_ALG_12060_replaced([11169840](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6Xo_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G_UP_ALG_3955_replaced([11169860](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6Xp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Each scheduler applies the following computations from the PDCCH slot pattern and their direction. For each slot and according to the active PDCCH slot pattern, when the number of RB granted by the BBRM is least lower than the largest number of RBs handling a CORESET (frequency domain) among the PDCCH occasions per symbol and configured in the cell, the U-Plane will apply the following algorithm to compute the PDCCH capacity in the slot according to the number of PDCCH occasions allocated to each direction and whether the PDCCH occasion is shared between both direction:  One or several PDCCH occasions are allocated per direction without any overlapping between PDCCH occasions with different CORESET duration. Each PDCCH occasion handles only one direction. The Whole PDCCH must not overlaps the DM-RS Type A position (as long as the PDSCH mapping type B is not supported). The PDCCH configuration must be aligned with the overlapping constraints above. The U-Plane translates the number of RB per symbol allowed by BBRM for each slot in number of REG available per symbol (n) and per direction. The number of REG per symbol is initialized with the number of RB allocated by the BBRM (numAllocCellPrb or rrmMaxNumUsablePrb(DL) (refer 5G_UP_ALG_26582_replaced([11214591](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in case eCPRI 7.2e layer PRB based pooling is enabled (slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed = TRUE)) and the number of symbols is defined according to the different symbols used by the CORESET(s) of the PDCCH occasion(s) allocated to each direction. nRegAvailableSymbol[DL,UL](n) = max(numAllocCellPrb(DL),rrmMaxNumUsablePrb(DL)) If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed is set to true, then numAllocCellPrb(DL is expected to be equal to 0. Otherwise, slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed is set to false and rrmMaxNumUsablePrb(DL) is equal to 0.  When NRCELL.actPagingSsbOptimization=twoBeamsPerSlot and 2 PDCCH occasions for paging are valid per slot within PO and the PDCCH occasion used by the Paging overlaps a PDCCH occasion allocated to the Uplink scheduler, the U-Plane translates the number of RB per symbol allowed by BBRM for each slot in number of REG available per symbol (n) and per direction. The number of REG per symbol is initialized with the number of RB allocated by the BBRM (numAllocCellPrb or rrmMaxNumUsablePrb(DL) (refer 5G_UP_ALG_26582_replaced([11214591](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in case eCPRI 7.2e layer PRB based pooling is enabled (slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed = TRUE)) and the number of symbols is defined according to the different symbols used by the CORESET(s) of the PDCCH occasion(s) allocated to each direction as detailed hereafter. The Whole PDCCH must not overlaps the DM-RS Type A position (as long as the PDSCH mapping type B is not supported). For the symbol (n) handling only one direction, the number of available REGs is initialized with the following formula: nRegAvailableSymbol[DL,UL](n) = max(numAllocCellPrb(DL),rrmMaxNumUsablePrb(DL)) For the symbol(s) (n) handling two directions, the number of available REGs is initialized with the following formula according to the direction:  For the downlink: nRegAvailableSymbolDL(n) = min(coresetZeroSize,max(numAllocCellPrb(DL),rrmMaxNumUsablePrb(DL))) / coresetZeroDuration.  For the uplink: nRegAvailableSymbolUL(n) = max(numAllocCellPrb(DL),rrmMaxNumUsablePrb(DL)) - nRegAvailableSymbolDL(n)  One PDCCH occasion is shared between both directions (CCE split) and all CORESET used have the same location and duration. In this case there is only one Control Resource Set duration pattern (1 symbol, 2 symbols or 3 symbols) for all CORESETs available.  For FDD not shared with LTE **or the cell is FR1 TDD, the U-Plane translates the number of RB per slot allowed by BBRM in number of REG available per symbol (n) and per direction.** If the first area is allocated to the downlink: nRegAvailableSymbol[DL](n) = 6 x cceSplitIndex / coresetDuration nRegAvailableSymbol[UL](n) = max(numAllocCellPrb(DL),rrmMaxNumUsablePrb(DL)) - (6 x cceSplitIndex / coresetDuration) If the first area is allocated to the uplink: nRegAvailableSymbol[UL](n) = 6 x cceSplitIndex / coresetDuration nRegAvailableSymbol[DL](n) = max(numAllocCellPrb(DL),rrmMaxNumUsablePrb(DL)) - (6 x cceSplitIndex / coresetDuration) Where numAllocCellPrb(DL) is the number of RB granted by the BBRM, the cceSplitIndex is determined from the number of CCEs of the largest CORESET configuration available in the slot and coresetDuration is the symbols of this CORESET (see 5G_UP_ALG_3955_replaced([11169860](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6Xp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). It is never below 4 due to the C-Plane cell configuration (see above).  For FDD shared with LTE [CB007372-B] and NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false [End CB007372-B]**, the U-Plane translates the number of RB per slot allowed by BBRM in number of REG available per symbol (n) and per direction.** [Before CB007372-B] If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed = TRUE, N_CCE(usable) is determined as per 5G_UP_ALG_26598_replaced([11214630](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOxY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [CB007372-B] If slowPrbPoolingAllowed is set to 'true', and if numAllocCellPrb(DL) < RB size (number of PRBs) of the largest splitted CORESET or the CORESET selected in the slot. N_CCE(usable) = floor(numAllocCellPrb(DL) * coresetDuration / 6) Else N_CCE(usable) = floor(coresetSize * coresetDuration / 6 ) End If Note: slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed can't be true for DSS, CB007372-B cleans up the legacy requirement. No code change is expected for N_CCE(usable) calculation in CB007372-B. This note shall be removed in the next release version. [End CB007372-B] If the first area is allocated to the downlink: nRegAvailableSymbol[DL](n) = 6 x max(AL;Ceiling(N_CCE(usable)_DL_area_size/CORESET_CCE_size/AL_min)_ AL_min) / coresetDuration nRegAvailableSymbol[UL](n) = (6 x max(AL;Ceiling(N_CCE(usable)_DL_area_size/CORESET_CCE_size/AL_min)_ AL_min) / coresetDuration) - numAllocCellPrb(DL) If the first area is allocated to the uplink: nRegAvailableSymbol[UL](n) = 6 x max(AL;Ceiling(N_CCE(usable)_DL_area_size/CORESET_CCE_size/AL_min)_ AL_min) / coresetDuration nRegAvailableSymbol[DL](n) = (6 x max(AL;Ceiling(N_CCE(usable)_DL_area_size/CORESET_CCE_size/AL_min)_ AL_min) / coresetDuration) - numAllocCellPrb(DL) Where, AL is defined by max(BWP_PROFILE/PDCCH.dciDedicatedAggregationLevel, BWP_PROFILE/PDCCH.dciRaMsg2AggregationLevel). AL_min is defined as smallest AL with non-zero PDCCH candidates in all searchspaces provided in PDCCH configuration at cell setup. DL_area_size is the size of the DL area according 5G_UP_ALG_3955_replaced([11169860](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6Xp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or 5G_UP_ALG_4024_replaced([11168705](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktx0xPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). CORESET_CCE_size is the number of CCEs of the CORESET use in this slot. There is one CORESET per slot and RB size of that shall be used for the computation.  [CB007372-B] For FDD shared with LTE and NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true **, the U-Plane translates the number of RB per slot allowed by BBRM in number of REG available per symbol (n) and per direction.** For the symbol (n) handling only one direction, the number of available REGs is initialized with the following formula: nRegAvailableSymbol[DL,UL](n) = numAllocCellPrb(DL) For the symbol #2 handling two directions, the number of available REGs is initialized with the following formula according to the direction: If the first PDCCH occasion is allocated to the uplink: nRegAvailableSymbol[DL](2) = min(numAllocCellPrb(DL), 6 x nCCE_DL) nRegAvailableSymbol[UL](2) = max(0, numAllocCellPrb(DL) - nRegAvailableSymbol[DL](2) ) If the first PDCCH occasion is allocated to the downlink : nRegAvailableSymbol[UL](2) = min(numAllocCellPrb(DL), 6 x nCCE_UL) nRegAvailableSymbol[DL](2) = max(0, numAllocCellPrb(DL) - nRegAvailableSymbol[UL](2) ) Note: the dedicated coreset used in symbol #2 has always coresetDuration=1 nCCE_DL, nCCE_UL: the number of CCEs for DL and UL of largest BWP are defined in [12658544: CCE split for asymmetric DSS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_vqrj8UqyEfC0Ye3M8ARUWQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_vqrj8uqyefc0ye3m8aruwq?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9") Reasoning: Direction allocated to CCEs in NR dedicated area should have a higher priority in symbol with CCE split (see[12658544: CCE split for asymmetric DSS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_vqrj8UqyEfC0Ye3M8ARUWQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). The other direction gets remaining resources, if there are still any available. coresetDuration is equal 1 for the coreset in symbol #2 which may have the CCE split for asymmetric DSS. Note: The nRegAvailableSymbol[DL,UL](2) doesn't take into account the number of resources allocated in the LTE shared area ([11172253: Handling of DL CELL RESOURCE AREA ALLOCATION REQUEST](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuK2VPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) and it contains the maximum allowed number of available PRBs. [End CB007372-B]  One or several PDCCH occasions are shared between both directions (CCE split) and all CORESETs used have the same location and different durations. This type of configuration is not supported.  One or several PDCCH occasions are shared between both directions (CCE split) and all CORESETs used have different locations and potentially different durations. This type of configuration is not supported. To control the capability to handle the expected AL required by the UE, the U-Plane maintains the number of REGs per symbols nRegAvailableSymbol[UL,DL](n) after each sucessfull PDCCH allocation according to the search space selected for the UE and the CORESET duration associated to the search space. When the PDCCH allocation is checked, the U-Plane verifies whether the number of REGs available is compatible with the AL selected according to the CORESET duartion used in the search space selected. If the following check is not successful, the UE is discarded. [image-0][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical inequality with a piecewise function. The inequality is: $$ \frac{6 \times AL[1,2,4,8,16]}{coresetDuration} \le \begin{cases} nRegAvailableSymbol[DL, UL](n), & \text{CORESET duration} = 1 \ \min(nRegAvailableSymbol[DL, UL](n), nRegAvailableSymbol[DL, UL](n+1)), & \text{CORESET duration} = 2 \ \min(nRegAvailableSymbol[DL, UL](n), nRegAvailableSymbol[DL, UL](n+1), nRegAvailableSymbol[DL, UL](n+2)), & \text{CORESET duration} = 3 \end{cases} $$[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12110.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] Where, AL[1,2,4,8,16] is the AL selected for the grant coresetDuration is the duration of the CORESET starting at symbol (n) associated to the search space selected. For each symbol used by the PDCCH allocation defined by the start symbol of the CORESET and its duration, the U-Plane removes the number of REG per symbol when the PDCCH allocation is successful. nRegAvailableSymbol[DL,UL](n)(t) = nRegAvailableSymbol[DL,UL](n)(t-1) - (6 x AL / coresetDuration) This requirement cannot handle the CCE split requirement in 5G_UP_ALG_32469_replaced([11169885](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6XrPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Since there is no L1 PRB limitation in tdLte config0 frame structure and PRB pooling is enabled only due to CSI-RS slot offset, this requirement shall not be followed in all slots with PDCCH.

##### 3.25.1.4.3.0-2 PDCCH Capacity Re-Evaluation with PRB Pooling Computation of the number of usable CCEs with dynamic PDCCH for multiple dedicated BWPs in TDD FR1 (ID: 11169994)

**3.25.1.4.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `12731814`)

PDCCH Capacity Re-Evaluation with PRB Pooling When PRB pooling is enabled (slowPrbPoolingAllowed is set to 'true') or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is True (5G_CP_ARC_ALG_4283_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), all CCEs may not be available for use and the number of CCEs that can be used is limited by the total amount of usable PRB in DL. When NRCELL/actDynPdcchTdMode is set to perBWP in a TDD FR1 cell with multiple dedicated BWPs where PRB pooling is limiting the usable PRBs in DL (numAllocCellPrb(DL)), following procedure shall be used to determine the number of usable CCEs (N_CCE (usable)).

The CORESET region (which can consist of multiple CORESETs from different BWPs) is available at the beginning of each slot when NRCELL/actDynPdcchMultBwp is enabled, but the CCE allocation in the CORESET region shall obey the available PRBs (numAllocCellPrb (DL)) limit from the BBRM in each symbol.

If a particular slot is allocated only one PDCCH symbol or gets two PDCCH symbols with equal size for the CORESET region, then N_CCE (usable) shall be determined based on 5G_UP_ALG_6933_replaced([11169932](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6-uPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). If a particular slot gets two PDCCH symbols with different sizes for the CORESET region in the two symbols, then 

  * For symbol 0, N_CCE (usable) shall be determined based on 5G_UP_ALG_6933_replaced([11169932](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6-uPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * For symbol 1,



if numAllocCellPrb (DL) ≥ number of PRBs in the CORESET region in symbol 1, then

N_CCE (usable) = floor((number of PRBs in the CORESET region in symbol 1)/6)

If CCE split is enabled in symbol 1, same algorithm as 5G_UP_ALG_6933_replaced([11169932](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6-uPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be used to split the CCEs in the two areas

otherwise, N_CCE (usable) = floor(numAllocPrb (DL)/6)

If CCE split is enabled in symbol 1, same algorithm as 5G_UP_ALG_6933_replaced([11169932](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6-uPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be used to split the CCEs in the two areas

[CB012733-C] When PRB pooling is enabled (slowPrbPoolingAllowed is set to 'true') or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is True with NRCELL.actThreeSymbolPdcch not Disabled and multiple BWPs are enabled, N_CCE (usable) in each PDCCH symbol is calculated as the calculation for symbol 1 above. [End CB012733-C]

#### 3.25.1.4.4 CCE evaluation for dummy PDCCH

##### 3.25.1.4.4.0-1 CCE evaluation for dummy PDCCH CCE capacity for dummy PDCCH (ID: 11170009)

**3.25.1.4.4.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `11170026`)

CCE evaluation for dummy PDCCH The number of CCEs for dummy PDCCH grant (see 5G_UP_ALG_15296_replaced([11171785](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuHL-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is determined by the size of dummy CORESET (see 5G_UP_ALG_15299_replaced([11168360](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktvYk_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

_N_CCE_ dummy = rounddown (_Size_ dummy _/ 6 );_ ****

Where _Size_ dummy _is the size of dummy CORESET from 5G_UP_ALG_15299_replaced([11168360](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktvYk_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))._**

When NRCELL.actConfDlInterferenceGen is set to "2" or "3",

 according to the value of NRCELL.targetTotalLoadSectorBeam, dummy PDCCH shall be granted. (See 5G_UP_ALG_17661_replaced([11183983](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvOmS_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

 **[CB013305-C-UPD008, CB013305-D-UPD008] When multiple K2 is being used (5G_UP_13617_replaced([11348263](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubTk3vvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), UL PDCCH candidates are from multiple slots (5G_UP_ALG_11159_replaced([11170811](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuAeQ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU shall grant UL dummy PDCCH in all these slots. N_CCEdummy is calculated per slot. **[End CB013305-C-UPD008, CB013305-D-UPD008]****

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is set to 'true' (5G_CP_ARC_ALG_4283_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed is set to 'true', all CCEs may not be available for use and the number of CCEs that can be used is limited by the total amount of usable PRBs in DL. The available number of CCEs is provided by _N_CCE_ usable defined in 5G_UP_ALG_6933_replaced([11169932](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6-uPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

_N_CCE_ dummy = min (_N_CCE_ dummy _,__N_CCE_ usable );**_*_** *

According to 5G_UP_ALG_29306_replaced([11171200](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuCTevvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), if PDCCH power boosting is applied (5G_UP_ALG_29346_replaced([11171327](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuC6lPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G_UP_ALG_29348_replaced([11171360](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuDhmPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

) in the slot, dummy PDCCH shall be limited with the remaining PDCCH power resource. _N_CCE_ power defined in 5G_UP_ALG_29358_replaced([11170031](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt7ly_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

_N_CCE_ dummy = min (_N_CCE_ dummy _,__N_CCE_ power )**_*_** *

##### 3.25.1.4.4.0-2 CCE evaluation for dummy PDCCH CCE capacity from PDCCH power for dummy PDCCH (ID: 11170031)

**3.25.1.4.4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11170036`)

CCE evaluation for dummy PDCCH N_CCEpower = rounddown (N / 6)

Where:

· N = min(rrmPdcchPowerResource[i, DL])

· rrmPdcchPowerResource: PDCCH power resource defined in 5G_UP_ALG_29308_replaced([11171220](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuCTf_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

### 3.25.1.5 Configuration Error Handling

#### 3.25.1.5.0-1 Configuration Error Handling Document Owner Marilyn Ma (ID: 11170045)

#### 3.25.1.5.1 PUSCH allocation with a Type[1,3] PDCCH not allowed

##### 3.25.1.5.1.0-1 PUSCH allocation with a Type[1,3] PDCCH not allowed PUSCH resource check for DCI format 0_0 (ID: 11170053)

**3.25.1.5.1.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `12658980`)

PUSCH allocation with a Type[1,3] PDCCH not allowed 12658980: PUSCH allocation with a Type[1,3] PDCCH not allowed [Before PR855649-26R2] ; When the gNB uses a Type3 PDCCH (DCI Format 0_0) for a PUSCH allocation, the Frequency Domain Resource Assignment is restricted by the size of the initial BWP, even if the UE is activated on a different dedicated BWP. With the constraint and when the long PUCCH is activated (NRCELL/pucchModeSelect set to longPucch), the PUSCH allocation must be done outside the PUCCH region (static and dynamic) defined by the C-Plane. There is no check and no defense mechanism during the PUSCH allocation when the configuration is not aligned with the capability of the FDRA. The gNB shall apply the following check for all cell BWP configured with RB(s) for the long PUCCH by the C-Plane. To compute the long PUCCH RBs in the BWP to check, the gNB computes the difference between the BWP PUSCH start CRB configured when the long PUCCH is activated and the the CRB start of the uplink BWP. The first condition, associated with "Ok", states that `nRBinitBwp - nRbLgPucchbwp - nRbMinPuschAlloc` must be greater than or equal to 0. The second condition, associated with "Nok", states that `nRBinitBwp - nRbLgPucchbwp - nRbMinPuschAlloc` must be less than 0. [End PR855649-26R2] [PR855649-26R2] ; When the gNB uses a Type[1,3] PDCCH (DCI Format 0_0 scrambled with a C-RNTI) for a PUSCH allocation, the Frequency Domain Resource Assignment is restricted by the size of the initial BWP, even if the UE is activated on a different dedicated BWP and the first RB of the UE active BWP is the reference RB. For a TC-RNTI (reTx RA-Msg3) reference RB is the first RB of the initial BWP even if the UE is active in another BWP. With the constraint and when the long PUCCH is activated (NRCELL/pucchModeSelect set to longPucch), the PUSCH allocation must be done outside the PUCCH region(s) (static and dynamic) defined by the C-Plane. There is no check and no defense mechanism during the PUSCH allocation when the configuration is not aligned with the capability of the FDRA of DCI Format 0_0. When the NRCELL/actEnhRrcReconfUlPrbRandom, NRCELL.actRrcReconfProcessingDelay parameters are set to true and NRCELL/actCbraContResDCI00 is set to false, and NRCELL/cellTechnology is set to FDD and NRCELL/lteNrDssMode is not set to none, the following check is applied only to the initial BWP configured in NRCELL.cellBwpList. At least it will validate the PUSCH allocation by the Type1 and Type3 if the search space is configured in the BWP. For all other cases, the following check is applied to each BWP configured in the NRCELL.cellBwpList where the Type3 is configured and the initial BWP (for at least the Type1). If the check is passed in at least one PUSCH area among the configured one(s) by the C-Plane in each verified BWP, it guarantees that the smallest number of PUSCH RBs is available for the DCI Format 0_0. Otherwise, the cell setup procedure is rejected as specified in the requirement [11170099: Diagnostic Information report](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt8M1PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). The formula is as follows: `checkPuschAllocRntiDci0_0 = {` `Ok, nRBinitBwp - nRbReserved_bwp - nRbMinPusch ≥ 0 and nPuschRBbwp ≥ nRbMinPusch` `Nok, nRBinitBwp - nRbReserved_bwp - nRbMinPusch < 0 or nPuschRBbwp < nRbMinPusch` `}`[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/img-10201339.png[/image_path][/image-6] With nRBinitBwp : Number of Resource Blocks (RB) allocated for the Cell BWP defined as the initial BWP. nRbReservedbwp : Number of Resource Blocks (RB) used for other purposes for a given PUSCH area and defined for each BWP as follows: nRbReservedbwp = longPucchStartPusch[Prb,Prb2] nPuschRBbwp: Number of Resource Blocks (RB) allowed for PUSCH allocation in the PUSCH area per BWP: nPuschRBbwp= longPucchNumPusch[Prb,Prb2] nRbMinPusch : Minimal number of consecutive Resource Blocks (RB) for a PUSCH transmission in the BWP defined by minSupportedNumPrbsUl (specified in: [5G L2 Entity : 11183158](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_3vmcsPvOEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End PR855649-26R2]

##### 3.25.1.5.1.0-2 PUSCH allocation with a Type[1,3] PDCCH not allowed Diagnostic Information report (ID: 11170099)

**3.25.1.5.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11170102`)

PUSCH allocation with a Type[1,3] PDCCH not allowed By default all diagnosticInformation[0-13] fields are initialized to 0x00000000 and when the check is failed, then the gNB reports a negative acknowledgement with the following information:

 The status is set to “NOK” (EStatus5G_NotOk).

 The cause is set to 0x00000002 (ECause5G_InvalidParameter).

 The “diagnosticInformation“ array is fulfilled with data used for the check as follow:

 The “diagnosticInformation[0]” element is filled with the value 0x00000001.

 The “diagnosticInformation[1]” element is set with the cell BWP identifier for which the check is failed.

 The “diagnosticInformation[2]” element is set to the value of the "location" of the cell BWP.

 The “diagnosticInformation[3]” element is set to the value of longPucchStartPuschPrb of the cell BWP.

 The “diagnosticInformation[4]” element is set to the computed size of the PUCCH for the cell BWP.

 The “diagnosticInformation[5]” element is set to initial uplink BWP size.

 The “diagnosticInformation[6]” element is set to minimal number of consecutive RB used for the check (nRbMinPuschAlloc).

 The “diagnosticInformation[7-13]” elements are set to 0x00000000.

---

##### 3.25.1.5.1.0-3 PUSCH allocation with a Type[1,3] PDCCH not allowed Fault report (ID: 11170107)

**3.25.1.5.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11170113`)

PUSCH allocation with a Type[1,3] PDCCH not allowed The gNB will raise a BTS Fault to the fault service with the following fields:

 The Fault Identifier (faultId): EFaultId_GnbCpRtCellUpdateFailedAl.

 The fault state (faultState): EFaultState_Start.

 The fault severity (faultSeverity): EFaultSeverity_OutOfOrder.

 The object type (objectType): EObjectType_Cell.

 The object identifier (objectId): Internal cell instance

 The fault information (extraFaultInfo[14]), array of 14 elements of 4 bytes:

 The extraFaultInfo[0] corresponding to the "diagnosticInformation[0] "defines the additional cause: 0x00000001.

This cause indicates “Initial uplink Bandwidth Part not enough large to handle PUSCH transmission with DCI Format 0_0 in the UE active BWP"

 The extraFaultInfo[1-13] elements are set to the “diagnosticInformation[1-13]”elements reported by the gNB.

---

##### 3.25.1.5.1.0-4 PUSCH allocation with a Type[1,3] PDCCH not allowed The Additional Text Information (ID: 11170118)

**3.25.1.5.1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11170123`)

PUSCH allocation with a Type[1,3] PDCCH not allowed The additional text sent in the alarm by the gNB is detailed hereafter, when faultId is set to EFaultId_GnbCpRtCellUpdateFailedAl with the extraFaultInfo[0] set to 0x00000001.

Cause: Initial uplink Bandwidth Part not enough large to handle PUSCH transmission with DCI Format 0_0 in the UE active BWP

Cell BWP identifier: 

Cell BWP CRB start : 

Cell BWP PUSCH CRB start: 

Cell BWP PUCCH size: 

Initial uplink BWP size: 

Minimal PUSCH allocation size:

#### 3.25.1.5.2 Missing UE-Specifc search space(s) in BWP

##### 3.25.1.5.2.0-1 Missing UE-Specifc search space(s) in BWP Lack of UE-Specific search space in BWP (ID: 11170130)

**3.25.1.5.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11170134`)

Missing UE-Specifc search space(s) in BWP The gNB shall check that each BWP not defined as "initial" are configured without at least one UE-Specific search space.

If a dedicated BWP (including power saving) is not configured with at least one UE-Specific search space, the gNB reports a cell configuration failure with the cause "invalid parameter" and additional information for the operator.

---

##### 3.25.1.5.2.0-2 Missing UE-Specifc search space(s) in BWP Diagnostic Information (ID: 11170138)

**3.25.1.5.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11170142`)

Missing UE-Specifc search space(s) in BWP By default all diagnosticInformation[0-13] fields are initialized to 0x00000000 and when the check is failed, then the gNB reports a negative acknowledgement in the PSCell_CellSetupResp message with the following information:

 The status is set to “NOK” (EStatus5G_NotOk).

 The cause is set to 0x00000002 (ECause5G_InvalidParameter).

 The “diagnosticInformation“ array is fulfilled with data used for the check as follow:

 The “diagnosticInformation[0]” element is filled with the value 0x00000005.

 The “diagnosticInformation[1]” element is set with the cell BWP identifier for which the check is failed.

 The “diagnosticInformation[2]” element is set to the value of the cell BWP type.

 The “diagnosticInformation[3-13]” elements are set to 0x00000000.

---

##### 3.25.1.5.2.0-3 Missing UE-Specifc search space(s) in BWP Fault report (ID: 11170147)

**3.25.1.5.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11170151`)

Missing UE-Specifc search space(s) in BWP The gNB will raise a BTS Fault to the fault service with the following fields:

 The Fault Identifier (faultId): EFaultId_GnbCpRtCellUpdateFailedAl.

 The fault state (faultState): EFaultState_Start.

 The fault severity (faultSeverity): EFaultSeverity_OutOfOrder.

 The object type (objectType): EObjectType_Cell.

 The object identifier (objectId): Internal cell instance

 The fault information (extraFaultInfo[14]), array of 14 elements of 4 bytes:

 The extraFaultInfo[0] corresponding to the "diagnosticInformation[0] "defines the additional cause: 0x00000005.

This cause indicates “Incorrect PDCCH Configuration, missing UE-Specific search space(s) in dedicated or power saving Bandwidth Part (gNB modifications may require a reset for recovery)"

 The extraFaultInfo[1-13] elements are set to the “diagnosticInformation[1-13]”elements reported by the gNB.

---

**3.25.1.5.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11170159`)

Cause: Incorrect PDCCH Configuration, missing UE-Specific search space(s) in dedicated or power saving Bandwidth Part (gNB modifications may require a reset for recovery)

Cell BWP identifier:

##### 3.25.1.5.3 Minimum RB Reserved For Non SI/Paging Validation

###### 3.25.1.5.3.0-1 Minimum RB Reserved For Non SI/Paging Validation Minimum RB Reserved for Non Si/Paging check (ID: 11170168)

**3.25.1.5.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11170172`)

Minimum RB Reserved For Non SI/Paging Validation [PR681860]

L2-PS shall validate configured minimum RBs reserved for Msg2/Msg4/SRB1(for transient phase UEs) (NRCELL.minRbReservedForNonSiPaging) in Cell Setup Request message does not exceed 70 percent of Coreset(0) RBs.

minRbReservedForNonSiPaging <= Ceil(70 percent of Coreset(0) RBs)).

Coreset(0) RB : Number of Resource Block available for the CORESET(0) bandwidth (24, 48 or 96) according to the value of the type0CoresetConfigurationIndex parameter, SCS and operating band.

If it exceeds the size, L2-PS shall feedback NOK with cause as "MinRBReservedForNonSiPaginExceededTheLimit"

[End PR681860]

#### 3.25.1.5.4 dciDedicatedAggregationLevel not allowed

##### 3.25.1.5.4.0-1 dciDedicatedAggregationLevel not allowed dciDedicatedAggregationLevel check against CORESET size and the number of PDCCH occasions in slots that may have K2 (ID: 13359336)

**3.25.1.5.4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13359339`)

dciDedicatedAggregationLevel not allowed If there is only one PDCCH occasion with UE-Specific SS in [Before CB014330-H-UPD001] slots with K2 [CB014330-H-UPD001] in a slot that may have K2 (considering potential dynamic K2 set change) [End CB014330-H-UPD001] and the corresponding CORESET size for that occasion is smaller than 2*dciDedicatedAggregationLevel received in cell setup or cell re-configuration request message, L2-PS shall not use this dciDedicatedAggregationLevel value and status NotOk due to invalid parameter (ECause5G_InvalidParameter) shall be reported in cell setup or cell re-configuration response message, respectively, together with additional information for the operator defined in [13359340: Diagnostic Information report](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_7tLkp_H3EfC0Z6kKit-MzQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

[CB014330-H-UPD001] 

  * In TDD case, for [CB014330-H-UPD002] channel bandwiths equal or higher than 20 MHz and [End CB014330-H-UPD002] frame structures for which PDCCH muting due to RIM mitigation is supported (i.e. for which k2rim is specified in [13242857: Determine RIM mitigated PDCCH symbols](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2uvgIMKhEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)), it shall be assumed that all DL and special slots that are <=k2rimMax slots ahead of the next UL slot may have K2 (where k2rimMax is the maximum value that k2rim may take according to [13242857: Determine RIM mitigated PDCCH symbols](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2uvgIMKhEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) for a given frame structure assuming that NRCELL/actNrRim is not equal to 0 and NRCELL/NRRIM_RPOFILE/actRimPdcchMuting is greater than 1 i.e. assuming that PDCCH muting on DL slots due to RIM is activated) regardless of the current actNrRim and actRimPdcchMuting configuration. [CB014330-H-UPD002] An exception to this is the case when NRCELL.actInfTddFrameMuting is equal to TRUE and at least one of the following conditions is fulfilled:
  * NRCELL.infTddFrameStructure.infUlDlDataSlotRatio is not equal to '4/6'
  * NRCELL.tddFrameStructure.frameStructureType is not equal to 'tdLte'
  * NRCELL.tddFrameStructure.lteToNrFrameShift is not equal to '0ms' [End CB014330-H-UPD002]
  * In [Before CB014330-H-UPD002] TDD case, for frame structures for which PDCCH muting due to RIM mitigation is not supported, hence k2rim = 'none' [CB014330-H-UPD002] all other TDD cases [End CB014330-H-UPD002], is shall be assumed that downlink and special slots that are rrmK2min slots ahead of UL slots may have K2, where rrmK2min is defined in [11116264: K2 value shall be computed for each slot in the pattern configured with PUSCH in the respective slot used for scheduling.](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp2XB_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)
  * In FDD case, it shall be assumed that all DL slots may have K2, even in a DSS cell.



[End CB014330-H-UPD001]

Typical scenario is attempt to configure dciDedicatedAggregationLevel = AL8 on BWP , as in case of FR1-TDD 10 MHz, FR1-TDD 15 MHz, or FDD 5 MHz cell that would cause lack of bi-directional scheduling capability in slots with K2 that have only one PDCCH occasion with CORESET smaller than 2*AL8 = AL16.

In case dciDedicatedAggregationLevel is received in cell setup request, gNB shall raise BTS Faults with severity level OutOfOrder and the cell is disabled/failed.

In case dciDedicatedAggregationLevel is received in cell re-configuration request, gNB shall raise BTS Faults with severity level Degraded and the cell remains online degraded. L2-PS continues to use previously configured dciDedicatedAggregationLevel. The fault (Degraded) is cancelled by CPlane when cell re-configuration request with allowed dciDedicatedAggregationLevel (i.e. value passes the check above) is received with status Ok.

NOTE: This check shall be done regardless of alSelection configuration (static or dynamic). With the current implementation of CCE splitting and CCE direction assignment, there might be no UL scheduling capability in K2 slots with single PDCCH occasion smaller than 2*dciDedicatedAggregationLevel even if alSelection = dynamic and L2-PS selects an AL smaller than dciDedicatedAggregationLevel.

---

##### 3.25.1.5.4.0-2 dciDedicatedAggregationLevel not allowed Diagnostic Information report (ID: 13359340)

**3.25.1.5.4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13359341`)

dciDedicatedAggregationLevel not allowed By default all diagnosticInformation[0-13] fields are initialized to 0x00000000 and when the check is failed, then the gNB reports a negative acknowledgement with the following information:

  * The status is set to “NOK” (EStatus5G_NotOk).
  * The cause is set to 0x00000002 (ECause5G_InvalidParameter).
  * The “diagnosticInformation“ array is fulfilled with data used for the check as follow:
  * The “diagnosticInformation[0]” element is filled with the value 0x0000000B.
  * The “diagnosticInformation[1]” element is set with the cell BWP identifier for which the check is failed.
  * The “diagnosticInformation[2]” element is set to the cell BWP type.
  * The “diagnosticInformation[3]” element is set to the BWP size.
  * The “diagnosticInformation[4]” element is set to CORESET identifier.
  * The “diagnosticInformation[5]” element is set to CORESET size in frequency [PRBs].
  * The “diagnosticInformation[6]” element is set to CORESET duration.
  * The “diagnosticInformation[7-13]” elements are set to 0x00000000.

---

## 3.25.2 PDCCH Selection Management

### 3.25.2.0-1 PDCCH Selection Management Document Owner Oleksandr Andryeyev; Marilyn Ma; Sankha Bhattacharya (ID: 11170179)

### 3.25.2.1 PDCCH Tokens

#### 3.25.2.1.0-2 PDCCH Tokens PDCCH token definition and restriction (ID: 11170193)

**3.25.2.1.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `12639212`)

PDCCH Tokens 12639212: PDCCH Tokens one PDCCH token corresponds to a set of common resources for DL/UL scheduling. They are used to split the total available common resources according to the needs of each scheduling entity and the L1 capabilities. Allocation of PDCCH tokens from each slot in the slot pattern to scheduling entities is performed in 5G_UP_ALG_2470_replaced([11116084](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp0h3PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). In TDD, PDCCH common resources shall be split in time domain such that each PDCCH token corresponds to the resources available on a given PDCCH symbol. On an FDD carrier shared with LTE [CB007372-A] when NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false [End CB007372-A], PDCCH common resources shall be split in time and in frequency domain such that 2 PDCCH tokens are available on a given PDCCH symbol. **[Before CNI-151163-A**]**_* The parameter NRBTS/NRCELL/actCaWimaxInterferenceAvoidance=true allows to remove grant capability (PDCCH tokens) in the Bidirectional slot (BI or Special slot (Sp)) which is colliding with the Transmit/receive Transition Gap (TTG) and the Uplink Wimax subframe. In the slot format DL14 just before the BI slot, UL and DL grant capability are allowed. Nevertheelss, the DL grant capability in this slot is restricted to the C-RNTI requesting for a DCI Format 1_1 for a BWP switch (see 5G_UP_ALG_26213_replaced([11174934](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kue_bvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and a regular k1 value compatible the BWP switch constraint is associated to this slot. These UEs will not request PDSCH in the same slot and therefore no PDSCH tranmission will collide to the TTG of Wimax. After the BI slot, 2 uplink slots are available and the UL PDCCH tokens for these 2 slots should be allowed in the 2 DL14 slots before the BI slot and k2 values will computed accordignly. [image-0][image_desc]The image displays a timeline diagram illustrating WiMAX (Worldwide Interoperability for Microwave Access) frame structure. The diagram is divided into two main sections: a top section representing the overall frame duration and a bottom section showing the slot allocation within the frame. The top section shows a total duration of 3291.42 microseconds, which is further divided into two parts: a 105.7 microsecond segment and a 1542.90 microsecond segment. The first segment is labeled "WiMAX DL" (Downlink) and includes a "TTG" (Transmit/Receive Transition Gap) indicated by a dotted pattern. The second, longer segment is labeled "WiMAX UL" (Uplink). Below the main frame, a timeline is depicted with numbered slots from 0 to 13. The first part of the timeline, corresponding to the "WiMAX DL" section, is divided into 14 "DL" (Downlink) slots, numbered 0 through 13. Two "PDCCH" (Physical Downlink Control Channel) blocks are shown preceding these DL slots, indicating control information transmission. The second part of the timeline, corresponding to the "WiMAX UL" section, is more complex. It begins with "DL" slots numbered 0 through 3, followed by "GP" (Guard Period) slots numbered 4 through 9, and finally "UL" (Uplink) slots numbered 10 through 13. This section is further described as a "Bidirectional (BI4,4) slot" and a "Special (SP4,4) slot". A legend at the bottom indicates that the dotted pattern signifies "DL/UL grant capability not allowed". The overall structure suggests a time-division duplex (TDD) system where the frame is split into downlink and uplink periods, with specific slots allocated for control channels, data, guard periods, and special bidirectional use.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12152.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] File: tdlteWimax.vsd Folder: _*[End CNI-151163-A**]****

---

#### 3.25.2.1.0-3 PDCCH Tokens PDCCH token distribution between UL and DL schdeuler (ID: 11170216)

**3.25.2.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11170221`)

PDCCH Tokens If the UL scheduler has a PDCCH token allocated from a DL or a special slot with configured PDSCH, then it shall be using common or UE dedicated search space configured in the PDCCH slot pattern (see 5G_UP_ALG_3958_replaced([11168909](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktzp8fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

If the UL scheduler has a PDCCH token allocated from a DL or a special slot without configured PDSCH, then it shall be using common or UE dedicated search space configured in the PDCCH slot pattern (see 5G_UP_ALG_3958_replaced([11168909](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktzp8fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

See 5G_UP_ALG_2372_replaced([11115213](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpr--vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) to determine whenever a slot is configured with PDSCH (slot with k1 value).

See 5G_UP_ALG_2484_replaced([11116264](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp2XB_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) to determine whether a PDCCH token is for UL scheduler (slot with k2 values).

---

#### 3.25.2.1.0-4 PDCCH Tokens Token configuration based upon frame structure and slot configuration for TDD (ID: 11170225)

**3.25.2.1.0-4.0-3**  (ID: `12631862`)

PDCCH Tokens In case of semiStatic or tdLte frameStructure:

 For FR1 TDD the PDCCH token allocation shall consider the resultant slot pattern format as per 5G_UP_ALG_2313_replaced([11114697](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpnGefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 DLx slots where x=0 shall be configured with 0 PDCCH tokens. (x=0 represents a fully muted downlink slot).

 DLx slots where x>0 shall be configured with 2*rrmMaxNumUesFdmDl PDCCH tokens (definition of rrmMaxNumUesFdmDl in 5G_UP_ALG_4478_replaced([11178989](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2y2vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Allowing DL slots to grant uplink traffic minimizes uplink scheduling latency and supports frame structure patterns with multiple consecutive uplink slots (such as those of 5GC001116). When Long PUCCH is configured this allows the relation k2 < k1min to be achieved.

 BIx,y slots (ie special slots) where x = 0 shall have 0 PDCCH tokens configured. (This case covers a special slot in the configured frame slot pattern where the downlink symbols are muted in the resultant frame slot pattern).

 BIx,y slots (ie special slots) with SSB are configured with rrmMaxNumUesFdmDl PDCCH tokens.

[Before CB014093-E]

 If NIDD parameter actEnhancedPDSCHSchSplSlot is FALSE:

 BIx,y slots (ie special slots) without SSB and greater than or equal to 10 DL symbols (BIx,y where x>=10) **are configured with 2** rrmMaxNumUesFdmDl PDCCH tokens.***

 BIx,y slot (ie special slots) without SSB and less than 10 DL symbols (BIx,y where x<10) are configured with _rrmMaxNumUesFdmDl PDCCH tokens._

 If NIDD parameter actEnhancedPDSCHSchSplSlot is TRUE: 

 BIx,y slots (ie special slots) without SSB and greater than or equal to 5 DL symbols (BIx,y where x >= **5 ) are configured with 2*rrmMaxNumUesFdmDl PDCCH tokens**

 BIx,y slot (ie special slots) without SSB and less than 5 DL symbols (BIx,y where x < **5**) are configured with _rrmMaxNumUesFdmDl PDCCH tokens._ ****

[CB014093-E]

 BIx,y slots (ie special slots) without SSB and greater than or equal to 5 DL symbols (BIx,y where x >= 5 ) shall be configured with

  * 2*rrmMaxNumUesFdmDl PDCCH tokens [CB008453-E] in case of FR1 TDD or FR2 TDD 4-4 frame structure. [End CB008453-E]
  * [CB008453-E] rrmMaxNumUesFdmDl PDCCH tokens in case of FR2 TDD 4-1 frame structure. [End CB008453-E]



 BIx,y slot (ie special slots) without SSB and less than 5 DL symbols (BIx,y where x < 5 ) are configured with rrmMaxNumUesFdmDl PDCCH tokens. 

[End CB014093-E]

 ULy slots shal have 0 PDCCH tokens configured.

  * BIx,y slots (ie special slots) without SSB and greater than or equal to 5 DL symbols (BIx,y where x >= 5 ) are configured with 2*rrmMaxNumUesFdmDl PDCCH tokens.
  * BIx,y slot (ie special slots) without SSB and less than 5 DL symbols (BIx,y where x < 5 ) are configured with rrmMaxNumUesFdmDl PDCCH tokens.



For DL MU-MIMO (TDD, FR1), the PDCCH token configuration shall use the same configurations which are defined by **5GC000679 feature.**

---

#### 3.25.2.1.0-5 PDCCH Tokens Token configuration based upon frame structure and slot configuration for FDD (ID: 11170237)

**3.25.2.1.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11170242`)

PDCCH Tokens On FDD carrier, the DL and UL scheduler must operate in parallel and simultaneously in every slot, due to the duplex mode.

When the gNB computes for the slots a k1 and a k2, then PDCCH tokens are configured (rrmMaxNumUesFdmDl + rrmMaxNumUesFdmUl). The DL/UL PDCCH resource distribution (PDCCH occasion(s) and CCEs) are defined in the PDCCH slot pattern every 20ms (5G_UP_ALG_3958_replaced([11168909](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktzp8fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

### 3.25.2.2 Aggregation Level Management

#### 3.25.2.2.0-1 Aggregation Level Management Document Owner Marilyn Ma;  Sankha Bhattacharya (ID: 11170249)

#### 3.25.2.2.1 Selection of Static and Dynamic Aggregation Level

##### 3.25.2.2.1.0-1 Selection of Static and Dynamic Aggregation Level (ID: 11170257)

**3.25.2.2.1.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11170268`)

Selection of Static and Dynamic Aggregation Level For the transmissions associated to SI-RNTI, P-RNTI, RA-RNTI or TC-RNTI, only the static AL is used as specified hereafter and according to the active BWP selected and its configuration defined by the operator (5G_UP_ALG_4057_replaced([11170273](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt9a_fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

For UE, the static AL is used until the Random Access successful completion and then after this step, the static (5G_UP_ALG_4066_replaced([11170311](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-CCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or dynamic (5G_UP_ALG_4068_replaced([11170356](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-CEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) AL is applied according to NRBTS/BWP_PROFILE/PDCCH/alSelection of the UE active BWP.

When NRBTS/NRCELL-actDlPaWarmUp is set to 'true', for dummy PDCCH grant with a dedicated C-RNTI, gNB-DU shall select various aggregation level(s) to attempt filling all un-used CCEs.

[CB008509-B] When NRCELL.actConfDlInterferenceGen is set to "2" or "3", for generating dummy PDCCH:

  * According to the value of the total load which is specified by NRCELL.targetTotalLoadSectorBeam,

  * With a dedicated C-RNTI,

  * gNB-DU shall select various aggregation level(s) (from highest to lowest, [PR709500] refer to 5G_UP_ALG_110_replaced([11095231](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kmkZgPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End PR709500]) in order to fill all requested CCEs.[End CB008509-B]

---

#### 3.25.2.2.2 Static aggregation level management

##### 3.25.2.2.2.0-1 Static aggregation level management Aggregation level for the SI-RNTI (ID: 11170276)

**3.25.2.2.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11170282`)

Static aggregation level management The gNB-DU selects the aggregation level for a SI-RNTI defined by NRBTS/BWP_PROFILE/PDCCH/dciSiAggregationLevel for the initial BWP.

After the AL selection, the PDCCH candidate used within the PDCCH occasion of the search space selected is detailed in the following requirements according to the type of System Information:

 For the SIB1 management, see requirement 5G_UP_ALG_3730_replaced([11165095](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kte53vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 For the SI-Msg transmission, see requirement 5G_UP_ALG_3811_replaced([11166382](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktlAcfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

##### 3.25.2.2.2.0-2 Static aggregation level management Aggregation level for the P-RNTI (ID: 11170287)

**3.25.2.2.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11170290`)

Static aggregation level management The gNB-DU selects the aggregation level for a P-RNTI defined by NRBTS/BWP_PROFILE/PDCCH/dciPagingAggregationLevel for the initial BWP.

After the AL selection, the PDCCH candidate used within the PDCCH occasion of the search space selected is detailed in paging section (see requirement 5G_UP_ALG_3903_replaced([11167436](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktp4-_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

##### 3.25.2.2.2.0-3 Static aggregation level management Aggregation level for the RA-RNTI (ID: 11170294)

**3.25.2.2.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11170298`)

Static aggregation level management The gNB-DU selects the aggregation level for a RA-RNTI defined by NRBTS/BWP_PROFILE/PDCCH/dciRaMsg2AggregationLevel of the selected BWP for the transmission as defined in the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4049_replaced([11168607](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktxNtPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For the selected search space and PDCCH occasion, the gNB-DU checks whether the number of the initial CCEs distribution for the downlink is compatible with the AL expected:

 If the CCE distribution is compatible, the gNB-DU will apply the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4433_replaced([11170857](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuAeTvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

 If the CCE distribution is not compatible, the gNB-DU triggers the dynamic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern procedure (5G_UP_ALG_3985_replaced([11169734](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt5JjvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the RNTI is not scheduled in this slot.

---

##### 3.25.2.2.2.0-4 Static aggregation level management Aggregation level for the TC-RNTI (ID: 11170302)

**3.25.2.2.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11170306`)

Static aggregation level management The gNB-DU selects the aggregation level for a TC-RNTI defined by NRBTS/BWP_PROFILE/PDCCH/dciRaCompletionAggregationLevel of the selected BWP for the transmission as defined in the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4049_replaced([11168607](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktxNtPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For the selected search space and PDCCH occasion, the gNB-DU checks whether the number of the initial CCEs distribution for the downlink is compatible with the AL expected:

 If the CCE distribution is compatible, the gNB-DU will apply the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4433_replaced([11170857](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuAeTvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

 If the CCE distribution is not compatible, the gNB-DU triggers the dynamic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern procedure (5G_UP_ALG_3985_replaced([11169734](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt5JjvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the RNTI is not scheduled in this slot.

---

##### 3.25.2.2.2.0-5 Static aggregation level management Aggregation level for the C-RNTI (ID: 11170311)

**3.25.2.2.2.0-5.0-5**  (ID: `12592034`)

Static aggregation level management 12592034: Static aggregation level management When the parameter NRBTS/BWP_PROFILE/PDCCH/alSelection of the UE active BWP is set to static, the gNB-DU selects the aggregation level for a C-RNTI defined :  by NRBTS/BWP_PROFILE/PDCCH/dciRaCompletionAggregationLevel until the RA completion procedure is successful.  by NRBTS/BWP_PROFILE/PDCCH/dciDedicatedAggregationLevel, after the successful RA completion and for basic reliability UE.  by NRBTS/BWP_PROFILE/PDCCH/dciDedicatedAggregationLevelHR , after the successful RA completion and for high reliability UE. All NIDD parameters above are the ones defined for the selected BWP for a transmission as defined in the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4049_replaced([11168607](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktxNtPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_17926_replaced([11110850](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpH-SfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Until the successful RA completion procedure (see the condition to have it in the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4051_replaced([11168618](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktxNt_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or until the UE is RRC configured (RRC setup acknowledged (SA)), the gNB-DU uses the parameter dciRaCompletionAggregationLevel and checks the PDCCH resources configured:  If the CCE distribution is compatible (number of CCEs allocated to the scheduler at least equal to the AL selected) but the coreset is shared between both directions and the number of candidates of the selected AL configured guarantees at least one grant in each direction (as detailed hereafter), the gNB-DU will apply the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4433_replaced([11170857](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuAeTvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with the AL selected. Otherwise, the CCE distribution is compatible, but the number of candidates configured in the selected search space (Type3 or UE-Specific search space) does not guarantee at least one grant in each direction, the gNB-DU triggers the dynamic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern procedure (5G_UP_ALG_3985_replaced([11169734](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt5JjvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the UE remains in the CS list if it is not a DCI for a BWP switch. To be sure that there is at least one PDCCH candidate in each direction for the AL selected, the following minimal number of candidates configured for the AL selected (ALs) in the search space selected must be met. Otherwise, there is no guarantee that the UE has a PDCCH candidate in the expected direction (it will depends on the slot and C-RNTI value). [image-0][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula defining `nCandidate_min`. The formula is a piecewise function with three cases: Case 1: `n1,` if `(⌈nCCE / ALs⌉ × ALs) < (2 × ALs)` Case 2: `n2,` if `((⌈nCCE / ALs⌉ × ALs) mod 16 = 0 and nCCE > (2 × ALs)) or (⌈nCCE / ALs⌉ × ALs = (2 × ALs) or ⌈nCCE / ALs⌉ × ALs = (4 × ALs) or ⌈nCCE / ALs⌉ × ALs = (8 × ALs)) and nCCE < 46` Case 3: `n3,` otherwise[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12178.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] with, nCandidatemin: minimal number of candidate for ALs in the search space to guarantee the presence of at least one PDCCH candidate in each direction in case of CCE split. nCCE: number of CCE in the CORESET associated to the selected search space. ALs: selected AL for the C-RNTI with the static or dynamic AL selection according to the NIDD configuration.  If the CCE distribution is not compatible, the gNB-DU triggers the dynamic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern procedure (5G_UP_ALG_3985_replaced([11169734](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt5JjvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the RNTI is not scheduled in this slot. After the successful RA completion procedure (see the condition to have it in the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4051_replaced([11168618](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktxNt_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), for a UE RRC configured (RRC setup acknowledged), the aggregation level is one one of the following cases:  The gNB-DU uses the parameter dciDedicatedAggregationLevel for basic reliability UE.  The gNB-DU uses the parameter the dciDedicatedAggregationLevelHR for high reliability **UE .**  The gNB applies for the uplink, on DSS cell [CB007372-AA] with NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false [End CB007372-AA], the UL DCI Link Adaptation (5G_UP_ALG_5187_replaced([11172629](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuMrifvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Then, the gNB checks the PDCCH resources configured:  If the CCE distribution is not compatible, the gNB-DU triggers the dynamic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern procedure (5G_UP_ALG_3985_replaced([11169734](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt5JjvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the RNTI is not scheduled in this slot.  For any DCI Format (x_0 and x_1), if the CCE distribution is compatible (number of CCE allocated to the scheduler at least equal to the AL selected) but the coreset is shared between both directions and the number of candidates of the selected AL configured guarantees at least one grant in each direction (as detailed hereafter), the gNB-DU will apply the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4433_replaced([11170857](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuAeTvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with the AL selected. Otherwise, If the CCE distribution is compatible, but the number of candidates configured in the selected search space (Type3 or UE-Specific search space) does not guarantee at least one grant in each direction, the gNB-DU triggers the dynamic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern procedure (5G_UP_ALG_3985_replaced([11169734](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt5JjvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the UE remains in the CS list if it is not a DCI for a BWP switch. To be sure that there is at least one PDCCH candidate in each direction for the AL selected, the following minimal number of candidates configured for the AL selected (ALs) in the search space selected must be met (this check is not applicable to slots 2, 3, 12, 13 in tdLte config0 frame structure). Otherwise, there is no guarantee that the UE has a PDCCH candidate in the expected direction (it will depend on the slot and C-RNTI value). [image-1][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula defining `nCandidate_min`. The formula is a piecewise function with three cases: Case 1: `n1,` if `(⌈nCCE / ALs⌉ × ALs) < (2 × ALs)` Case 2: `n2,` if `((⌈nCCE / ALs⌉ × ALs) mod 16 = 0 and nCCE > (2 × ALs)) or (⌈nCCE / ALs⌉ × ALs = (2 × ALs) or ⌈nCCE / ALs⌉ × ALs = (4 × ALs) or ⌈nCCE / ALs⌉ × ALs = (8 × ALs)) and nCCE < 46` Case 3: `n3,` otherwise[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12178.001.png[/image_path][/image-1] with, nCandidatemin: minimal number of candidate for ALs in the search space to guarantee the presence of at least one PDCCH candidate in each direction in case of CCE split. nCCE: number of CCE in the CORESET associated to the selected search space. ALs: selected AL for the C-RNTI with the static or dynamic AL selection according to the NIDD configuration.
