##### 3.25.2.2.2.0-6 Static aggregation level management Aggregation level for the CS-RNTI (ID: 11170341)

**3.25.2.2.2.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `11170351`)

Static aggregation level management When the parameter NRBTS/BWP_PROFILE/PDCCH/alSelection of the UE active BWP (defined in the UE context) is set to static, the gNB-DU selects the aggregation level for a CS-RNTI defined by:

 NRBTS/BWP_PROFILE/PDCCH/dciRaCompletionAggregationLevel whenever DCI 0_0 is requested.

 NRBTS/BWP_PROFILE/PDCCH/dciDedicatedAggregationLevel whenever DCI 0_1 is requested [CB008246-J] for basic reliability UE [End CB008246-J].

 [CB008246-J] NRBTS/BWP_PROFILE/PDCCH/dciDedicatedAggregationLevelHR whenever DCI 0_1 is requested for high reliability UE [End CB008246-J].

And then, it checks the PDCCH resources configured:

 If the CCE distribution is compatible, the gNB-DU will apply the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4433_replaced([11170857](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuAeTvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with the AL selected.

 If the CCE distribution is not compatible, the gNB-DU triggers the dynamic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern procedure (5G_UP_ALG_3985_replaced([11169734](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt5JjvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the RNTI is not scheduled in this slot.

---

#### 3.25.2.2.3 Dynamic aggregation level

##### 3.25.2.2.3.1 Overview

###### 3.25.2.2.3.1.0-1 Overview (ID: 11170363)

**3.25.2.2.3.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11170378`)

Overview When the AL selection of the UE active BWP (BWP_PROFILE.PDCCH.alSelection) is set to dynamic, at any time, the gNB-DU applies the dynamic algorithm for the grant with a C-RNTI **or a CS-RNTI** and when the following conditions are met:****

 The RA procedure is successfully completed:

 When the Downlink scheduler sends the RA-Msg2 when the RA-Msg1 uses a CF preamble previously configured.

 When the Downlink scheduler receives the acknowledgment of the transmission handling at least a UE Contention Resolution Identity MAC CE sent with the TC-RNTI.

 When the Uplink scheduler indicates that a new uplink transmission with C-RNTI, following the successful decoding of RA-Msg3 with the C-RNTI MAC Control Element (CE), is sucessfully received and decoded.

 At least one valid CQI is received for the C-RNTI after the completion of the RA procedure.

When the above conditions are not met, the aggregation level defined by BWP_PROFILE.PDCCH.dciRaCompletionAggregationLevel for the C-RNTI or CS-RNTI in the UE active BWP is used (see requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4070_replaced([11170396](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-pF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Otherwise, the dynamic AL selection procedure is triggered (see requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4070_replaced([11170396](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-pF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

In case that the DCI is addressed to CS-RNTI, same procedure applies as CS-RNTI is only used for DCI CRC scrambling. In the following section, whenever the procedure is called for CS-RNTI, it’s executed for C-RNTI and the result is applied to CS-RNTI.

To allow the dynamic AL, the gNB-DU shall:

· Maintain **[Before CB008246-B]an**[CB008246-B]parallel**[End CB008246-B] Outer Loop Control loops and the CQI for the PDCCH**[CB008246-B] for Basic Reliability and High Reliability separately (see requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4072_replaced([11170490](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-pHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**_*_** *

· Support PDCCH LA mode (BR or HR OLC) per UE **[End CB008246-B]**[CB008246-H] and support switching between PDCCH HR and BR OLC mode (see requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4072_replaced([11170490](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-pHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **[End CB008246-H]** ****

· **[CB008246-B] Aggregation Level selection according PDCCH LA mode (BR or HR), 5G_UP_ALG_4071_replaced([11170399](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-pGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). **[End CB008246-B]****

---

###### 3.25.2.2.3.1.0-2 Overview Basic reliability PDCCH and High reliability PDCCH (ID: 11170383)

**3.25.2.2.3.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11170390`)

Overview 11170390: Overview Below procedure shall be supported for dynamic AL selection for PDCCH LA:

  * Dyanmic AL selectoin procedure, refer to 5G_UP_ALG_4070_replaced([11170396](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-pF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

  * cqiCorrectionDown, refer to 5G_UP_ALG_4073_replaced([11170495](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt_QIPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

  * CQI offset Computation, refer to 5G_UP_ALG_4074_replaced([11170531](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt_QJ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

  * DCI size offset compution, refer to 5G_UP_ALG_4074_replaced([11170531](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt_QJ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

  * Downlink and uplink feedbacks filtering, refer to 5G_UP_ALG_4079_replaced([11170587](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt_QLfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

  * CQI PDCCH management, refer to 5G_UP_ALG_4082_replaced([11170623](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt_3MPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))




Following flowchart depcts the behavior of the procedure

[image-0][image_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a process titled "Dynamic AL trigger". The flowchart begins with a decision point: "CQI is received properly". If the answer is "NO", the process moves to "CQI erasure process". If the answer is "YES", the process continues to "Preparing the list of valid AL". From "Preparing the list of valid AL", the flow proceeds to "Computing CQI for AL", then to "Expected AL Selection". Following "Expected AL Selection", there is another decision point: "Enough resources to apply AL?". If the answer is "NO", the process goes to "Postpone AL application". If the answer is "YES", the process moves to "Applying selected AL". There is also an arrow from "CQI erasure process" pointing to "Preparing the list of valid AL", and an arrow from "Postpone AL application" pointing to "Applying selected AL".[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12189.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

---

##### 3.25.2.2.3.2 Dynamic AL selection procedure

###### 3.25.2.2.3.2.0-1 Dynamic AL selection procedure (ID: 11170399)

**3.25.2.2.3.2.0-1.0-7**  (ID: `12714847`)

Dynamic AL selection procedure 12714847: Dynamic AL selection procedure Before the first valid CQI received after the RA procedure completion, the aggregation level defined by BWP_PROFILE.PDCCH.dciRaCompletionAggregationLevel, for the RNTI (C-RNTI or CS-RNTI) in its active BWP, is used and the associated DL or UL feedbacks will be filtered in order to not trigger the Outer Loop Control (OLC). The gNB-DU checks the PDCCH resources from the PDCCH slot pattern for the expected slot: · If the CCE distribution is compatible, the gNB-DU will apply the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4433_replaced([11170857](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuAeTvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with the AL selected, · If the CCE distribution is not compatible, the gNB-DU triggers the dynamic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern procedure (5G_UP_ALG_3985_replaced([11169734](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt5JjvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the RNTI is not scheduled in this slot. After the first valid CQI received following the RA procedure completion and without any ongoing RA procedure, the gNB-DU computes CQI for AL selection (cqiAlSelection) as detailed hereafter. [image-0][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a sans-serif font. The formula is: cqiAlSelection(t,k) = cqiPdcch(t, k) + cqiPdcchOffset(t, k) + dciSizeOffset + mcsTableOffset - pdcchOffsetHR[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12196.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] With, _k:_ basic reliability or high reliability PDCCH LA, refer to 5G_UP_6298_replaced([11362772](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uc-YxvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). _cqiPdcch(t) :_ This is the CQI computed for the PDCCH based on the unfiltered CQI received periodically and a CQI erasure processing for the missing CQI (see requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4082_replaced([11170623](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt_3MPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). _cqiPdcchOffset(t) :_ This is the CQI compensation offset computed with the valid previous DL and UL feedbacks from last OLC activation (RA procedure completion and a valid CQI received from the C-RNTI) (see the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4074_replaced([11170531](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt_QJ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). _dciSizeOffset:_ This is the offset linked to the size of the DCI selected for the C-RNTI in the slot (see requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4077_replaced([11170560](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt_QKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). _mcsTableOffset:_ This is the offset linked to the MCS table configured for the C-RNTI in the slot (see requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4077_replaced([11170560](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt_QKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The mcsTableOffset is determined by parameter mcs-Table is received in the PsUser_UserSetupReq message(cellConfiguration.pdschConfig.mcs-Table) or in the PsUser_UserModifyReq(cellConfiguration.pdschConfig.mcs-Table) after their activation (see 5G_UP_ALG_17940_replaced([11153286](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kslh8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):  When the mcs-Table index is 0 (64QAM) **or 2(LowSE MCS), the mcsTableOffset is set to 0.**  When the mcs-Table index is 1 (256QAM), the mcsTableOffset is equal to rdMcsTableOffset256Qam (5G_L2_1452_replaced([11185317](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27xZwfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).  [CB008949-A] When the mcs-Table index is 3 (1024QAM), the mcsTableOffset is equal to rdMcsTableOffset1024Qam ([12815562: rdMcsTableOffset1024Qam](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_An8LQKZFEfCrANRYxAlR5A)). [End CB008949-A].  [PR859107] During the transient phase that is corresponding to the period between receiving RRC Reconfiguration and RRC Reconfiguration Complete, if mcs-table (as in 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2246_replaced(11282471)) in RRC Reconfiguration is different than that stored then the mcsTableOffset is determined by parameter mcs-Table used for the PDSCH scheduling during the transient phase. [End PR859107]. _pdcchOffsetHR:_ _Configurable by operator, parameter NRBTS/BWP_PROFILE/PDCCH_ /_pdcchCqiOffsetHR for high reliability data scheduling. 0 for basic reliability data scheduling._ ** Then, cqiAlSelection is compared with the CQI thresholds cqiDciCssAl[1, 2, 4, 8, 16] for basic reliability and cqiDciCssAlHR[1,2,4,8,16]>0 for high reliability received in the PsCell_CellSetupReq or the PsCell_CellReconfigurationReq messages, starting from the highest threshold value to the lowest one. The selected AL x is the first one for which: · [image-1][image_desc]The image contains the following text: cqi.AIS selection >= cqi.DctCssAI[x][/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12196.002.png[/image_path][/image-1] for basic reliability and [image-2][image_desc]The image contains the text "cqiAISelection ≥ cqiDctCssAIHR [x]". The text is slightly blurry.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12196.003.png[/image_path][/image-2] for high reliability, · And it belongs to the set of valid ALs for the selected search space [CB012631-C] of the expected SSSG (see [11168496: Search Space selection](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktwmofvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) or the list of valid ALs during the SSSG switching period if the UE active SSSG confirmation if not done already (see[11168730: Search Space Set Group management](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktx0yvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). [End CB012631-C] For each UE-Specific and Type3 search space defined under a cell BWP with aggregationLevelSelection = ‘dynamic’, L2-PS builds the corresponding set of valid ALs for the dynamic AL Selection. This action is performed at cell setup (PsCell_CellSetuReq) and by a cell reconfiguration (PsCell_CellReconfigurationReq) which affects the configuration of the dynamic AL Selection. For a given search space, the set of valid ALs is given by the common elements of the sets below:  The set of dynamic ALs configured by the parameter aggregationLevelList for basic reliability and aggregationLevelListHR for high reliability [Before CB014330-F] received in the PsCell_CellSetuReq [End CB014330-F];  For basic reliability, the set of ALs for which the corresponding CQI threshold cqiDciCssAl[x] > 0, where cqiDciCssAl[1,2,4,8,16] are configured by PsCell_CellSetupReq/PsCell_CellReconfigurationReq; For high reliability, the set of ALs for which corresponding CQI threshold cqiDciCssAlHR[x] > 0, where cqiDciCssAlHR comes from NRBTS/BWP_PROFILE/PDCCH/dynamicAggregationLevelHRSet/cqiDciCssAlXHR.  The set of ALs allowed for the selected search space (IE numOfPdcchCandidatesInALx != n0). If there are other search spaces with the same type defined in the BWP, the gNB-DU appends to the previous list, all more robust additional valid ALs available in these search spaces.  gNB shall record the intended AL if it is not configured. The intended AL is the first AL satisfied with cqiAlSelection >= cqiDciCssAl[x] or cqiDciCssAlHR[x] as above (cqiDciCssAl[x]>0, cqiDciCssAlHR[x]>0). “Not configured” means the intended AL NOT allowed for the selected search space (IE numOfPdcchCandidatesInALx == n0). The search space selection is defined in the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4053_replaced([11168627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktxNufvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) If none of the valid ALs is such that cqiAlSelection is greater or equal to cqiDciCssAl[x] for basic reliability and cqiDciCssAlHR[x] for high reliability, the valid AL associated to the lowest threshold is selected. If the set of valid ALs is empty dciRaCompletionAggregationLevel is used. After the selection of the expected AL, the gNB-DU checks the PDCCH resources from the PDCCH slot pattern for the expected slot: · If the CCE distribution is not compatible or if the the AL selected is not allowed for the search space selected, the gNB-DU triggers the dynamic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern procedure (5G_UP_ALG_3985_replaced([11169734](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt5JjvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the RNTI is not scheduled in this slot. · For any DCI Format (x_0 and x_1), if the CCE distribution is compatible (number of CCE allocated to the scheduler at least equal to the AL selected) but the coreset is shared between both directions and the number of candidates of the selected AL configured guarantees at least one grant in each direction (as detailed hereafter), the gNB-DU will apply the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4433_replaced([11170857](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuAeTvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with the AL selected. The gNB-DU sets the associated feedback as valid for the outer loop control too. Otherwise, the CCE distribution is compatible, but the number of candidates configured in the selected search space (Type3 or UE-Specific search space) does not guarantee at least one grant in each direction, the gNB-DU triggers the dynamic evaluation of the CORESET duration pattern procedure (5G_UP_ALG_3985_replaced([11169734](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt5JjvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the UE remains in the CS1 list for the current slot, if it is not a DCI for a BWP switch. To be sure that there is at least one PDCCH candidate in each direction for the AL selected, the following minimal number of candidates configured for the AL selected (ALs) in the search space selected must be met (this check is not applicable to slots with 2 K2s and 1 K1 in tdLte config0 frame structure (4:6) in cells >40 MHz when multiple BWPs are not configured. Nevertheless, this restriction is maybe not valid as it will just deactivate the CCE split in a later slots!!!). Otherwise, there is no guarantee that the UE has a PDCCH candidate in the expected direction (it will depends on the slot and C-RNTI value). [image-3][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula presented as a piecewise function. The function is defined as `nCandidate_min` and has three cases labeled n1, n2, and n3. Case n1: `[nCCE / AL_y] * AL_x < (2 * AL_x)` Case n2: `((( [nCCE / AL_y] * AL_x ) mod 16 = 0 and nCCE > (2 * AL_x)) or ([nCCE / AL_y] * AL_x = (2 * AL_x)) or ([nCCE / AL_y] * AL_x = (4 * AL_x)) or ([nCCE / AL_y] * AL_x = (8 * AL_x))) and nCCE < 46` Case n3: `otherwise` The formula uses mathematical notation including floor division `[]`, multiplication `*`, modulo `mod`, greater than `>`, less than `<`, and equality `=`. The variables used are `nCandidate_min`, `nCCE`, `AL_x`, and `AL_y`.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12196.004.png[/image_path][/image-3] with, nCandidatemin: minimal number of candidate for ALs in the search space to guarantee the presence of at least one PDCCH candidate in each direction in case of CCE split. nCCE: number of CCE in the CORESET associated to the selected search space. ALs: selected AL for the C-RNTI with the static or dynamic AL selection mechanism.

##### 3.25.2.2.3.3 PDCCH Outer Loop Control and CQI management

###### 3.25.2.2.3.3.0-1 PDCCH Outer Loop Control and CQI management cqiCorrectionDown (ID: 11170495)

**3.25.2.2.3.3.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `11170527`)

PDCCH Outer Loop Control and CQI management 11170527: PDCCH Outer Loop Control and CQI management The gNB-DU maintains a CQI offset compensation for each UE connected in the cell, based on an Outer Loop Control (OLC) using the status of the HARQ feedback from any downlink transmissions using a DCI and the feedback of the PUSCH decoding attempt, when the uplink transmission was also triggered by a DCI.

The downlink and uplink transmission feedbacks, received from the L1 and before any potential gNB-DU modification, are taken into account only after the RA successful procedure completion (see requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4069_replaced([11170363](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-pEfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). When the Uplink scheduler detects a C-RNTI MAC CE or Contention Free preamble identifying a unique C-RNTI, the associated CQI compensation offset is set to 0.

When the dynamic AL is activated in a BWP, the gNB-DU computes the cqiCorrectionDown as follows.

[image-0][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in English. The equation is: `cqiCorrectionDown[k] = cqiCorrectionUp[k] * (1 - targetBler) / targetBler` The equation defines `cqiCorrectionDown[k]` in terms of `cqiCorrectionUp[k]` and `targetBler`. The term `targetBler` is likely a variable representing a target Block Error Rate. The equation suggests a correction factor is applied to `cqiCorrectionUp[k]` based on the ratio of `(1 - targetBler)` to `targetBler`.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12202.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

With,

k: basic reliability or high reliability PDCCH LA, refer to 5G_UP_6298_replaced([11362772](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uc-YxvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

cqiCorrectionUp:

Parameter defined by the operator and transmitted in the pdcchConfig structure within the PsCell_CellSetupReq or in the pdcchReconfiguration structure within the PsCell_CellReconfigurationReq. It corresponds to the added correction when the DL/UL transmission feedbacks are not received with the Dtx status. For high reliability, this parameters defined by corresponding NRBTS/BWP_PROFILE/PDCCH/dynamicAggregationLevelHRSet/cqiCorrectionUpHR.

targetBler:

For basic reliability: Expected BLER set to hardcoded 0.01 for the PDCCH (1%) [Before CNI-122436-C] NRCELL.tmpParam1 [CNI-122436-C] NRCELL.pdcchBlerTarget [End CNI-122436-C] (default value 1% will be used in case the parameter not configured).

For high reliability: Expected BLER set to hardcoded 0.001 for the PDCCH (0.1%) [Before CNI-122436-C] NRCELL.tmpParam2 [CNI-122436-C] NRCELL.pdcchBlerTargetHR [End CNI-122436-C] (default value 0.1% will be used in case the parameter not configured).

 If the downlink or uplink HARQ feedback status is not Dtx, the formula, hereafter, is applied.

[CB008246-B]For basic reliability, [End CB008246-B]The gNB-DU identifies the first valid parameter cqiDciCssAl[1,2,4,8,16] received in the PsCell_CellSetupReq or PsCell_CellReconfigurationReq for which the value is greater than zero and lower than the cqiDciCss computed above. Selected factor to mitigate the real DCI size of the DCI to transmit according to the valid computed CQI for the PDCCH and current value of the cqiPdcchOffset and for a DCI with the size associated to the common CSS (see requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4074_replaced([11170531](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt_QJ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

###### 3.25.2.2.3.3.0-4 PDCCH Outer Loop Control and CQI management Downlink and Uplink feedbacks filtering (ID: 11170587)

**3.25.2.2.3.3.0-4.0-4**  (ID: `12821551`)

PDCCH Outer Loop Control and CQI management 12821551: PDCCH Outer Loop Control and CQI management The gNB-DU manages 2 types of feedback filtering:

 The anticipated feedback filtering defined when the AL is selected as hereafter:

 If the DCI, scrambled with a C-RNTI is sent with a AL normalized to a DCI size of a common search space and more robust than the target AL for cqiAlSelection (see hereafter), the expected feedback will be filtered if the status is not Dtx (as it is expected when a more robust AL is used, the UE will receive it).

The target AL is selected by comparing cqiAlSelection to the set of thresholds (cqiDciCssAl[1,2,4,8,16]>0 for basic reliability and cqiDciCssAlHR[1,2,4,8,16]>0 for high reliability) without considering the additional AL limitations applied by the dynamic AL selection in the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4071_replaced([11170399](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-pGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 If UE is configured for skippable grants (5G_UP_ALG_4839_replaced([11195286](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv7J1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), any PUSCH DTX indication shall be managed per 5G_UP_ALG_16415_replaced([11195380](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv7w7PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 If NRCELL.actULSchedInactiveBwp = TRUE, uplink HARQ feedback status during the inactive BWP scanning procedure (5G_UP_ALG_16104_replaced([11111313](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpMPyvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be excluded from the PDCCH CQI compensation offset computation.

[CB013244-B]

 If NRCELL.actDLSchedInactiveBwp = TRUE, downlink HARQ feedback status during the inactive downlink BWP scanning procedure ([12682751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_7Vn41VGcEfCeeMlEb49MrQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) shall be excluded from the PDCCH CQI compensation offset computation.

[End CB013244-B]

 The subsequent feedback filtering triggered for the following reasons:

 When the OLC triggers a cqiCorrectionDown, due to one downlink transmission feedback (DL HARQ DTX), the downlink scheduler applies a filtering of the next potential feedbacks (DL HARQ DTX) if the associated grants were sent before the cqiCorrectionDown as well as all additional HARQ feedbacks multiplexed within the same Uplink Control Information (UCI) tagged as Dtx.

 When the OLC triggers a cqiCorrectionDown, due to uplink transmission feedback and a given HARQ process, the uplink scheduler applies a filter on the next UL HARQ DTX feedbacks if the associated grants were sent before the cqiCorrectionDown.

This indicates a filtered Dtx for a given serving cell. * **Correction Indicators:** 'correctionDown' and 'correctionUp' are positioned above the timeline, suggesting adjustments or corrections being applied. A legend at the bottom explains the abbreviations: * **Dtx:** Dtx count for a given serving cell. * **Dtx:** Dtx filtered for a given serving cell. * **Ack/Nack:** Any valid feedback (not Dtx) are used for OLC. * **DCIUL(x):** DCI 0_x for HARQ(x). The overall diagram illustrates how different types of uplink control information and feedback are managed over time in a wireless communication system.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12212.002.png[/image_path][/image-1]

 When the parameter actUpperThrAckNackFiltering (NRBTS/NRCELL/cellBwpList) is set to true, and when the DL or UL feedback statu for basic reliability **is not Dtx, the non Dtx feedback is filtered if the computed cqiAlSelection (5G_UP_ALG_4071_replaced([11170399](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-pGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for that PDCCH grant is equal or greater than the upper threshold of AL[x] and computed hereafter.**

The upper threshold of AL[x] is the first cqiDciCssAl[x-n] > 0 and included in the parameter aggregationLevelList or 15 if (x-n) is equal or lower than 0, with n, an integer value starting from 1 to x (step 1).

When the parameter actUpperThrAckNackFiltering (NRBTS/NRCELL/cellBwpList) is set to false, and when the DL or UL feedback status for basic reliability **is not Dtx, the non Dtx feedback is filtered if the computed cqiAlSelection (5G_UP_ALG_4071_replaced([11170399](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-pGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for that PDCCH grant is equal or greater than the highest threshold (cqiDciCssAl[x]) for AL configured to be used in the BWP (cqiDciCssAl[1,2,4,8,16] above 0 **and included in the parameter aggregationLevelList).****

 When the DL or UL feedback status for high reliability is not Dtx and the computed cqiAlSelection (5G_UP_ALG_4071_replaced([11170399](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-pGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for that PDCCH grant is equal or greater than the highest threshold (cqiDciCssAlHR[x] ) for AL configured to be used in the BWP (cqiDciCssAlHR[1,2,4,8,16] above 0 **and included in the _aggregationLevelListHR ), the non Dtx feedback is filtered_**

When the parameter actUpperThrAckNackHrFiltering (NRBTS/NRCELL/cellBwpList) is set to true, and when the DL or UL feedback status for high reliability **is not Dtx, the non Dtx feedback is filtered if the computed cqiAlSelection (5G_UP_ALG_4071_replaced([11170399](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-pGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for that PDCCH grant is equal or greater than the upper threshold of AL[x] and computed hereafter.**

The upper threshold of AL[x] is the first cqiDciCssAlHR[x-n] > 0 and included in the parameter aggregationLevelListHR or 15 if (x-n) is equal or lower than 0, with n, an integer value starting from 1 to x (step 1).

When the parameter actUpperThrAckNackHrFiltering (NRBTS/NRCELL/cellBwpList) is set to false, and when the DL or UL feedback status for high reliability **is not Dtx, the non Dtx feedback is filtered if the computed cqiAlSelection (5G_UP_ALG_4071_replaced([11170399](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-pGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for that PDCCH grant is equal or greater than the highest threshold (cqiDciCssAlHR[x]) for AL configured to be used in the BWP (cqiDciCssAlHR[1,2,4,8,16] above 0 **and included in the parameter aggregationLevelListHR).****

 When the DL feedback status or UL feedback statusfor basic reliability not corresponding to CS-RNTI **is Dtx and the computed cqiAlSelection (5G_UP_ALG_4071_replaced([11170399](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-pGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for that PDCCH grant is equal or lower than the lowest threshold (cqiDciCssAl[x]) for AL configured to be used in the BWP (cqiDciCssAl[1,2,4,8,16] above 0 and included in the _aggregationLevelList), the Dtx feedback is filtered._**

 When the DL feedback status or UL feedback status for high reliability **not corresponding to CS-RNTI** is Dtx and the computed cqiAlSelection (5G_UP_ALG_4071_replaced([11170399](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-pGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for that PDCCH grant is equal or lower than the lowest threshold (cqiDciCssAlHR[x]) for AL configured to be used in the BWP (cqiDciCssAlHR[1,2,4,8,16] above 0 and included in the _aggregationLevelListHR ), the Dtx feedback is filtered._ ****

###### 3.25.2.2.3.3.0-5 PDCCH Outer Loop Control and CQI management CQI PDCCH management (ID: 11170623)

**3.25.2.2.3.3.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `12659460`)

PDCCH Outer Loop Control and CQI management 12659460: PDCCH Outer Loop Control and CQI management The gNB-DU uses for each UE, the associated unfiltered CQI value reported periodically by the L1.

When at the expected period configured in the UE, no valid CQI is detected (see hereafter) and after NRBTS/BWP_PROFILE/PDCCH/pCqiErasureActTimer for basic reliability and NRBTS/BWP_PROFILE/PDCCH/dynamicAggregationLevelHRSet/pCqiErasureActTimerHR for high reliability has expired, the gNB-DU applies the CQI erasure process to degrade the CQI used for the PDCCH until the lowest allowed value for the PDCCH CQI set to 1.

A CQI is not valid, when at least one of the following condition is met:

 The L1 indicates that no CQI was received (dtx IE set in UlData_PucchReceiveRespPs/UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs).

 The CQI received is equal to 0 (invalid value).

 The CQI is received on the PUCCH [Before CNI-137616-C], the rdEnableCsiPlausibilityCheck is set to true [End CNI-137616-C] and PUCCH SINR is lower than the rdPucchLowSinrThreshold (this check will replace the one in 5G_UP_ALG_4620_replaced([11187546](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvcBofvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the scope of cqiPdcch calculation).

The pCqiErasureActTimer is started when a pCQI is missed after a valid one has been received. If a valid CQI is received before the timer has expired, the timer is stopped. 

The timer(pCqiErasureActTimer) duration is received in PsCell_CellSetup/PsCell_CellReconfigurationReq (pCqiErasureActTimer IE). If 0 is configured, there is no CQI erasure allowed.

For high reliability LA the same handling is applied as for basic reliability LA but the high reliability specific timer (pCqiErasureActTimerHR) is used. 

[image-0][image_desc]The image is a line graph illustrating the concept of CQI (Channel Quality Indicator) over time. The y-axis is labeled "CQI" and the x-axis is labeled "Time". The graph shows several horizontal lines representing different CQI values at different points in time. Some lines are solid, indicating a reported CQI, while one line is dashed, suggesting a missing or estimated CQI. There are markers on the x-axis labeled "CQI period" and "Missing CQI". The "Missing CQI" section is further highlighted with "x" marks, indicating instances where CQI data is not available. Arrows point from the "Missing CQI" section to segments of the graph, with labels "pCqiErasureTimer" and "deltaCqi". These labels suggest that when CQI is missing, a timer ("pCqiErasureTimer") is initiated, and the CQI value might be adjusted by a "deltaCqi" amount. The graph shows a step-down in the CQI value after these events. The overall trend depicted is that CQI values are reported periodically, but there can be periods of missing CQI, which trigger specific mechanisms to handle the situation, potentially involving timers and adjustments to the CQI value.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12215.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

This timer is mainlly to avoid to reduce the PDCCH CQI used if the CQI reports are configured with a short periodicity. In that case, it is relevant to not degrade the CQI until the end of the timer (several CQI report period).

[image-1][image_desc]The image contains the mathematical expression "cqiPdcc[t,k] =". The text is in a sans-serif font and appears to be in a dark color against a light background. The expression is written in a single line.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12215.002.png[/image_path][/image-1] [image-2][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula presented as a piecewise function. The formula defines a variable, likely `cqiPdcch(t, k)`, based on two conditions. The first condition, "when valid CQI received," states that `cqiPdcch(t, k)` is calculated as: `(1 - rdPdcchCqiAvg) * cqiPdcch(t-1, k) + rdPdcchCqiAvg * CQI(t)` The second condition, "when missing CQI and erasure activated," states that `cqiPdcch(t, k)` is calculated as: `cqiPdcch(t-1, k) - deltaCqi[k]` The text is presented in a clear, mathematical notation.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12215.003.png[/image_path][/image-2]

With,

k:

basic reliability or high reliability PDCCH LA, refer to 5G_UP_6298_replaced([11362772](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uc-YxvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

This is the PDCCH CQI used to select the AL according to the UE radio conditions. The value is evaluated every CQI report period (t) configured in the UE.

Initialization for cqiPdcch(0, basic reliability) = cqiDciCssAl[x] , cqiPdcch(0, high reliability)=cqiDciCssAl[x]HR when valid CQI received, where AL[x] is aggregation level defined by dciRaCompletionAggregationLevel. 

_rdPdcchCqiAvg:_

This is R&D parameter with default value set to 0.5, step 0.1, range 0.1 to 1.

_CQI(t):_

Periodic CQI reported by the L1 (CQI_L1(t)) every periods (t) with Rank compensation.

 CQI(t) = CQI_L1(t) for Rank equals to 1.

 CQI(t) = min (15.0, CQI_L1(t) + rdPdcchRI12Comp) for Rank equals to 2.

 CQI(t) = min (15.0, CQI_L1(t) + rdPdcchRI13Comp) for Rank equals to 3.

 CQI(t) = min (15.0, CQI_L1(t) + rdPdcchRI14Comp) for Rank equals to 4.

The rdPdcchRI12Comp is R&D parameter with default value is 3.0, step 0.1, range 0 to 30.

The rdPdcchRI13Comp is R&D parameter with default value is 5.0, step 0.1, range 0 to 30.

The rdPdcchRI14Comp is R&D parameter with default value is 6.0, step 0.1, range 0 to 30. 

_deltaCqi:_

For basic reliability, Offset computed according to the CQI report period configured in the UE (ueCqiPeriod) through the Psuser_UserSetupReq and the pCqiErasureReduction received in the PsCell_CellSetup or in the PsCell_CellReconfigurationReq. The delta CQI is computed as follows.

[image-3][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is: $\text{deltaCqi} = \frac{\text{ueCqiPeriod}}{1000} \times \text{pCqiErasureReduction}$[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12215.004.png[/image_path][/image-3]

For high reliability, pCqiErasureReductionHR from correspondng NRBTS/BWP_PROFILE/PDCCH/dynamicAggregationLevelHRSet/pCqiErasureReductionHR shall be used to calculate the deltaCqi.

[image-4][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is: $\text{deltaCqi} = \frac{\text{ueCqiPeriod}}{1000} \times \text{pCqiErasureReductionHR}$[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12215.005.png[/image_path][/image-4]

The "ueCqiPeriod" is computed as follow according to the periodicity parameter received in the perCsiReportConfig structure of the PsUser_UserSetupReq indicating the number of slots and SCScommon received in PsCell_CellGroupSetupReq.

[image-5][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is written in a light blue color on a white background. The equation reads: `ueCqiPeriod = periodicity / 2μ`[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12215.006.png[/image_path][/image-5]

|   
---|---  
Numerology | _SCS_ common (kHz)**  
0 | 15  
1 | 30  
2 | 60  
3 | 120

###### 3.25.2.2.3.3.0-6 PDCCH Outer Loop Control and CQI management CQI PDCCH offset range validation after PDCCH CQI computation (ID: 12652652)

**3.25.2.2.3.3.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `12652653`)

PDCCH Outer Loop Control and CQI management [PR828787-25R3] ; When the PDCCH CQI is computed upon reception of a valid CQI or due to the CQI erasure process (see [11170623: CQI PDCCH management](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt_3MPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), the U-Plane checks the sum of the new PDCCH CQI and the current PDCCH CQI offset is in the valid range [0-15]. If the sum is outside the range, then the PDCCH CQI offset is truncated in order to have a sum equal to the closest boundary (0 or 15). [End PR828787-25R3]

cqiDciCssAl[x]HR - reference thresholds to use AL[x=1,2,4,8,16] for HR, refer to 5G_UP_ALG_4071_replaced([11170399](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-pGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), NIDD parameter BWP_PROFILE.PDCCH.dynamicAggregationLevelHRSet.cqiDciCssAl[x]HR

[PR724453]

cqiDciCssAl[x]HR - the minimum value of those greater than 0 CQI thresholds cqiDciCssAL[1,2,4,8,16]HR (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_4071_replaced([11170399](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-pGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and corresponding AL is included in BWP_PROFILE.PDCCH.aggregationLevelListHR

[End PR724453]

[CB008246-H-UPD001]

Valid sample collection is done as below:

\- At calculation of the cqiAlSelection in PDCCH resource availability check in DL FDM scheduler 5G_UP_ALG_4297_replaced([11177362](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuu3A_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), this value is taken as sample N times, where N is the distance in slots between this calculation and the calculation of the previous sample (or the beginning of the period, if this is the first sample calculated in the period);

\- At CQI reception, cqiAlSelection used in this percentage formula will be updated and the value is taken as sample one time and the previous calculated sample is taken as sample (N-1) times where N is the distance in slots between this calculation and the calculation of the previous sample (or the beginning of the period, if this is the first sample calculated in the period);

\- Before the evaluation of this period, a fresh cqiAlSelection is calculated and taken as sample N times, where N is the distance in slots between this calculation and the calculation of the previous sample (or the beginning of the period, if this is the first sample calculated in the period).

Samples in transient phase shall be excluded.

[End CB008246-H-UPD001]

If this percentage is greater than or equal to pdcchHRBlerOutagePercentage (NIDD NRBTS.NRPDCCHHRLA.pdcchHRBlerOutagePercentage),

Then:

  * L2PS shall switch the DL PDCCH from HR OLC to BR OLC

  * L2PS shall also switch the PDSCH data scheduling to BR Link Adaptation

  * L2PS shall restart the timer with period dlHRBlerRecoverPeriod for DL PDCCH to monitor the recovery conditions (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_17138_replaced([11170742](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt_3QPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))




Otherwise, L2PS shall restart the timer with period pdcchHRBlerOutagePeriod for the UE.

 switch fallback triggered by PDSCH LA, refer to 5G_UP_ALG_16320_replaced([11129978](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kq-YYvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

Then:

  * L2PS shall switch the DL PDCCH OLC mode from HR to BR OLC

  * L2PS shall restart the timer with period dlHRBlerRecoverPeriod for DL PDCCH waiting for recovery (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_17138_replaced([11170742](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt_3QPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

cqiDciCssAl[x]HR - reference thresholds to use AL[x=1,2,4,8,16] for HR, refer to 5G_UP_ALG_4071_replaced([11170399](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-pGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), NIDD parameter BWP_PROFILE.PDCCH.dynamicAggregationLevelHRSet.cqiDciCssAl[x]HR

[PR724453]

cqiDciCssAl[x]HR - the minimum value of those greater than 0 CQI thresholds cqiDciCssAL[1,2,4,8,16]HR (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_4071_replaced([11170399](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-pGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and corresponding AL is included in BWP_PROFILE.PDCCH.aggregationLevelListHR

[End PR724453]

[CB008246-H-UPD001]

Valid sample collection is done as below:

\- At calculation of the cqiAlSelection in PDCCH resource availability check in UL FDM scheduler 5G_UP_ALG_11920_replaced([11196444](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwCeo_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), this value is taken as sample N times, where N is the distance in slots between this calculation and the calculation of the previous sample (or the beginning of the period, if this is the first sample calculated in the period);

\- At CQI reception, cqiAlSelection used in this percentage formula will be updated and the value is taken as sample one time and the previous calculated sample is taken as sample (N-1) times where N is the distance in slots between this calculation and the calculation of the previous sample (or the beginning of the period, if this is the first sample calculated in the period);

\- Before the evaluation of this period, a fresh cqiAlSelection is calculated and taken as sample N times, where N is the distance in slots between this calculation and the calculation of the previous sample (or the beginning of the period, if this is the first sample calculated in the period).

Samples in transient phase shall be excluded.

[End CB008246-H-UPD001]

If this percentage is greater than or equal to pdcchHRBlerOutagePercentage (NIDD NRBTS.NRPDCCHHRLA.pdcchHRBlerOutagePercentage),

Then:

  * L2PS shall switch the UL grant PDCCH from HR OLC to BR OLC

  * L2PS shall also switch the PUSCH data scheduling to BR Link Adaptation

  * L2PS shall restart the timer with period ulHRBlerRecoverPeriod for UL grant PDCCH to monitor the recovery conditions (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_17263_replaced([11170766](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt_3QvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).




Otherwise, L2PS shall restart the timer with period pdcchHRBlerOutagePeriod for the UE.

 switch fallback triggered by PUSCH LA, refer to 5G_UP_ALG_16426_replaced([11138318](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kreHrfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

Then:

  * L2PS shall switch the UL grant PDCCH OLC mode from HR to BR OLC

  * L2PS shall restart the timer with period ulHRBlerRecoverPeriod for UL grant PDCCH waiting for recovery (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_17263_replaced([11170766](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt_3QvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

###### 3.25.2.2.3.4.0-6 Switch between High Reliability and Basic Reliability PDCCH Outer Loop Control Skip condition for switching from basic reliability Link adaptation to high reliability Link adaptation (ID: 11170789)

**3.25.2.2.3.4.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11170794`)

Switch between High Reliability and Basic Reliability PDCCH Outer Loop Control In below condition, L2PS shalll not start timer with period mentioined in 5G_UP_ALG_17138_replaced([11170742](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt_3QPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the UE to switch from basic reliability Link adaptation to high reliability Link adaptation:

1\. UE is configured with configured grant and mcs-table in configuredGrantConfig is set to 'qam256'

  1. [CB008246-K]At least one 5QI-1 DRB is configured[End CB008246-K]



Rational: As agreed, the service shall be aligned to conifgure same reliablity in DL and UL. If UE is configured with CG and 'qam256' is used, basic reliablity LA shall be applied in UL, so basic reliabity LA shall also be applied in DL.

In below condition, L2PS shalll not start timer with period mentioined in 5G_UP_ALG_17263_replaced([11170766](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt_3QvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the UE to switch from basic reliability Link adaptation to high reliability Link adaptation:

1\. UE is configured with configured grant and mcs-table in configuredGrantConfig is set to 'qam256'

2\. UL of UE works with DFT-s-OFDM mode

  1. [CB008246-K]At least one 5QI-1 DRB is configured[End CB008246-K]

### 3.25.2.3 Selection of start CCE index

#### 3.25.2.3.0-2 Selection of start CCE index Overview (ID: 11170811)

**3.25.2.3.0-2.0-5**  (ID: `13387854`)

Selection of start CCE index gNB-DU shall select a free PDCCH candidate from the list of PDCCH candidates to send the DCI grant. The start CCE index of the PDCCH candidate is selected as following:

[CB012733-A]When NRCELL.actThreeSymbolPdcch is not disabled, CA UEs are not allocated PDCCH candidates in the third symbol when the third symbol is DL only according to [12728772](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_JQkEEnHmEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) in K1, K2 valid slots. [End CB012733-A]

**In case multiple K2 are available for the to be scheduled UL slot (5G_UP_ALG_2484_replaced([11116264](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp2XB_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_30394_replaced([11116305](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp2-FPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_13167_replaced([11372025](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ud6M8PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then the list of PDCCH candidates shall include UL PDCCH from multiple slots and follow the priority specified in 5G_UP_ALG_30880_replaced([11199230](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwMPkPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**When NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true only one K2 value is available.****

In case that the DCI is addressed to CS-RNTI, same procedure applies as CS-RNTI is only used for DCI CRC scrambling. In the following section, whenever the procedure is called for CS-RNTI, it’s executed for C-RNTI and the result is applied to CS-RNTI.

When there is only one UE can be scheduled per slot for FR2, the fixed start CCE index is used (refer 5G_UP_ALG_11164_replaced([11170835](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuAeSfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

When FDM is disabled (NRBTS.actFdmScheduling is false) for FR1, the start CCE index is determined statically by uniformly distributing the available PDCCH candidates over the CORESET.

  * For non-DSS, the full bandwidth will be available for PDCCH candidates with one slot for uplink and one slot for downlink.

  * For DSS with NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false, the full bandwidth for PDCCH candidates will be CCE split for uplink and downlink. Refer to 5G_UP_ALG_4430_replaced([11170844](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuAeS_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_4432_replaced([11170853](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuAeTfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).




When FDM is enabled (NRBTS.actFdmScheduling is true) for FR1,the start CCE index is selected from the list of available PDCCH candidates which is calculated dynamically for each RNTI.

  * The list of PDCCH candidates includes the PDCCH candidates can be used is derived per each RNTI, refer 5G_UP_ALG_11024_replaced([11170873](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuBFUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

  * One free PDCCH candidate is selected from the list of PDCCH candidates, refer 5G_UP_ALG_11025_replaced([11171067](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuBFXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

  * If multiple dedicated BWPs are configured, the start CCE selection shall consider multiple BWP with common or different dedicated PDCCH configuration, refer to 5G_UP_ALG_4434_replaced([11171104](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuBsYvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

  * If PRB pooling is enabled, the PDCCH capacity may be further restricted by the number of usable PRB limit available in DL, refer to 5G_UP_ALG_11026_replaced([11171146](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuBsZ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).




For MU-MIMO (FR1, TDD) conduct test mode, the fixed CCE start index is used (5G_UP_ALG_11156_replaced([11171188](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuCTd_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Note: Fir FR1 TDD and FR1 FDD it is recommended to configure parameter actfdmscheduling with value 1.

---

#### 3.25.2.3.1 Static selection of start CCE index

##### 3.25.2.3.1.0-1 Static selection of start CCE index Start CCE index for TDD (ID: 11170835)

**3.25.2.3.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11170841`)

Static selection of start CCE index For TDD, the start CCE shall take the value 0 if single UE can be scheduled in one slot.

Note: Not valid for TDD FR1 from 20A onward, replaced by 5G_UP_ALG_4433_replaced([11170857](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuAeTvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

##### 3.25.2.3.1.0-2 Static selection of start CCE index Start CCE for FDD FR1 carrier shared with LTE (DSS) (ID: 11170844)

**3.25.2.3.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11170853`)

Static selection of start CCE index Start CCE and CCE split for FDD FR1 carrier shared with LTE (DSS)

---

**3.25.2.3.1.0-2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `12618834`)

Static selection of start CCE index For FDD on FR1 carrier shared with LTE (DSS) [CB007372-A] with the same carrier bandwidth (NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false) [End CB007372-A], this requirement defines the PDCCH scheduling algorithm for supporting simultaneous transmission of DL and UL DCI on a single CORESET extending over symbol.

The algorithm can only work under below assumptions:

1\. The same CCE aggregation level (L) is used in all Common and UE-dedicated Search Spaces

2\. The number of candidates **at aggregation level** shall follow below equations:****

 M = floor(Ncce/L)

 where Ncce is the number CCEs in PDCCH CORESET. See 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2162_replaced([11308743](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TrE9NPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If above assumptions can be met, the startCCE will be any value in the set of **{0, 1 * L, …, (M - 1) * L}.**

For example, if the aggregation level is 4 (L = 4), the set of start CCE indices for different bandwidths are defined in the below table. The scheduler shall select start CCE index from related set based on bandwidth configuration.

|  |   
---|---|---  
Num of CCEs in the CORESET | Num of candidates | Start CCE Index Set  
17 | 4 | {0, 4, 8, 12}  
13 | 3 | {0, 4, 8}  
8 | 2 | {0, 4}  
  
Note: this avoids computation of the complex formula for the startCCE given in 38.213 10.1.

Hint for implementation: the implementation of 5G_UP_ALG_4433_replaced([11170857](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuAeTvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) can be re-used.

---

#### 3.25.2.3.2 Dynamic selection of start CCE index

##### 3.25.2.3.2.1 Control Channel Element management

##### 3.25.2.3.2.1-1 Control Channel Element management

###### 3.25.2.3.2.1-1.0-9 Control Channel Element management For UL PDCCH, if PDCCH candidates are from multiple slots (5G_UP_ALG_11159_replaced( 11170811 )), gNB-DU shall try to find available PDCCH with slot priority defined in 5G_UP_ALG_30880_replaced( 11199230 ). For each RNTI candidate for a grant in the slot, the gNB-DU selects a free PDCCH candidate among the set of PDCCH candidates available in the selected search space for the grant and according to the previous grant allocations already done in the slot (gNB-DU shall remember which candidates and their CCEs are used). When several PDCCH occasions are available in the slot allocated for the same direction, the gNB-DU checks in each of them if there is a free PDCCH candidate for the RNTI selected. [Before CB012732-A] For all RNTI (except the SI-RNTI), if more than one free candidate is available, the gNB-DU selects randomly one of them to reduce PDCCH interference between neighbouring cells by a cell specifically derived seed. [CB012732-A] If (NRCELL.actPdcchLeastBlockingAlg is True and rdActLeastBlocking is True) For all C-RNTIs in UE specific SS not configured with CORESET0, if more than one free candidate is available, the gNB-DU selects one of them using UE sorting and least blocking algorithm ( 13354860: UE sorting and PDCCH least blocking algorithm ). For all other RNTIs (except the SI-RNTI) and C-RNTIs in type3 SS or when CORESET0 is configured in UE specific search space, if more than one free candidate is available, the gNB-DU selects randomly one of them to reduce PDCCH interference between neighbouring cells by a cell specifically derived seed. Else For all RNTI (except the SI-RNTI), if more than one free candidate is available, the gNB-DU selects randomly one of them to reduce PDCCH interference between neighbouring cells by a cell specifically derived seed. [End CB012732-A] When the SI-RNTI is allocated, among the available PDCCH candidates, the SI-RNTI (SIB1 and SI-Msg) uses alternatively each possible PDCCH candidates as defined in the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_3736_replaced( 11165142 ). The gNB-DU books the resources according to the Aggregation Level (AL) used and computes, for all search spaces allowed in the slot (5G_UP_ALG_3958_replaced( 11168909 ) and followings), the list of CCEs pre-empted by the allocation in the Type0-PDCCH (5G_UP_ALG_4032_replaced( 11169907 )), when the gNB-DU builds the PDCCH slot pattern (5G_UP_ALG_3958_replaced( 11168909 )). When the P-RNTI is allocated, among the available PDCCH candidates, the grant is using the PDCCH candidates defined in the requirements 5G_UP_ALG_3903_replaced( 11167436 ) and followings. For each RNTI (P-RNTI, RA-RNTI, TC-RNTI or C-RNTI) is allocated, the gNB-DU books the resources according to AL used and computes, for all search spaces allowed in the slot (5G_UP_ALG_3958_replaced( 11168909 ) and followings), the list of CCEs pre-empted by the allocation in the corresponding search space type respectively (5G_UP_ALG_4032_replaced( 11169907 )). With dynamic AL activated for the BWP and if no free PDCCH candidate is found (impossible for SI-RNTI and P-RNTI) with the expected Aggregation Level and for a grant in the Type3 or UE-Specific search space:       [CB012732-A] If (NRCELL.actPdcchLeastBlockingAlg is false or when rdActLeastBlocking is false) [End CB012732-A] then [CB012732-A] for UEs where PDCCH candidates are searched randomly [End CB012732-A]  gNB-DU attempts to find a free PDCCH candidate, only with the next and more robust Aggregation Level allowed (number of candidate for the target AL not equal to 0 in the selected search space and the cqiDciCssAl[x] of the target AL is not equal to 0.0). It is not expected to bypass the next AL and to try to find a PDCCH candidates with more CCEs than 2 times the CCEs for the initial expected AL. If there is one free PDCCH candidate with the reselected AL (max 2 times the initial AL), then gNB-DU selects it and applies the regular allocation procedure with the new AL selected. [CB012732-A] If (NRCELL.actPdcchLeastBlockingAlg is true and rdActLeastBlocking is true) then for UEs whose PDCCH candidates are searched using least blocking algorithm, the next robust aggregation is not used to find a free candidate. [End CB012732-A].  If downgradeALProactive is set to true, the gNB-DU attempts to find a free PDCCH candidate for uplink proactive scheduling or TCP boost proactive scheduling (TCP boost PUG), only with the lower and less robust Aggregation Level allowed (number of candidate for the target AL not equal to 0 in the selected search space and the cqiDciCssAl[x] of the target AL is not equal to 0.0). If there is one free PDCCH candidate with the reselected AL (max 0.5 times the initial AL), then gNB-DU selects it and applies the regular allocation procedure with the new AL selected.  Otherwise, there is no free PDCCH candidate with this new Aggregation Level. If PDCCH allocation is requested from 5G_UP_ALG_23036_replaced( 11177323 ) for "For the step after MU mode" or the UE skips PDCCH power boosting (not put into waiting list as 5G_UP_ALG_29306_replaced( 11171200 )).  then, the RNTI is not scheduled,  else, the final scheduling decision is decided as 5G_UP_ALG_29348_replaced( 11171360 ). For FDD 10/15/20MHz carrier shared with LTE, when the C-RNTI using DCI Format 1_1 is allocated, and NRBTS.NRCELL.actPdschAtSsbSlots got from PsCell_CellSetupReq and PsCell_CellReconfigurationReq is larger than 0, gNB-DU  shall determine the start CCE index in SSB slot, and calculate the startCce from the available PDCCH CCEs ( 11169095 ). Note: For FDD cell shared with LTE and NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true the CCE split is allowed on the symbol #2 if any dedicated coreset&gt;0 overlaps the LTE shared area (see 12620260: Resource sharing in asymmetric DSS ) . Note: downgradeALProactive is defined from BWP_PROFILE/PDCCH/downgradeALProactive.**** (ID: 13354609)

##### 3.25.2.3.2.1-2 Control Channel Element management

###### 3.25.2.3.2.1-2.0-1 Control Channel Element management gNB-DU shall select the start CCE Index as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_11024_replaced( 11170873 ) and 5G_UP_ALG_11025_replaced( 11171067 ) if two or more dedicated bandwidth parts per cell are configured with common or different dedicated PDCCH configurations. (ID: 11171110)

##### 3.25.2.3.2.1-4 Control Channel Element management

###### 3.25.2.3.2.1-4.0-1 Control Channel Element management When actLongPucchResourceOpt = TRUE in a FDD cell, and index 13 is chosen (see 11187231 ) the set of initial cyclic shift is made by (0, 3, 6, 9). When actLongPucchResourceOpt = TRUE in a FDD cell, and index 12 is chosen (see 11187231 ) the set of initial cyclic shift is made by (0, 3, 6, 9). When actLongPucchResourceOpt = TRUE in a FDD cell, and index 11 is chosen (see 11187231 ) the set of initial cyclic shift is made by (0, 6). C-Plane provides Delta PRI to U-plane (see in 11309603 ) Then U-Plane (PDCCH) has to select n_CCE in order to force the usage of a specific Cyclic Shift (CS) in the UE. U-Plane shall chose n_CCE such that the final CS value chosen by UE is either 0 or 6 in even PCI cells,  3 or 9 in odd PCI cells (by index 12). Please, consider that in order to have the same CS values for common and dedicated PUCCH (thus decreasing potential interference), common PUCCH has to use even CS (value 0 and 6) in cells with even PCI, and odd CS (values 3 and 9) in cells with odd PCI. Always in FDD cell when actLongPucchResourceOpt = TRUE, if  NRCELL.reqMinNumPuschPrb =0 then the Delta PRI provided by C-Plane is only  0 or 1, and U-Plane shall chose n_CCE such that the final CS value chosen by UE is either 0 (in even PCI cells) or 1 (in odd PCI cells). (ID: 12714177)

##### 3.25.2.3.2.1-5 Control Channel Element management

###### 3.25.2.3.2.1-5.0-1 Control Channel Element management Overview (ID: 11171148)

**3.25.2.3.2.1-5.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11171153`)

Control Channel Element management CCE allocation is limited in 2 different ways based on the type of pooling that is enabled.

-When stream PRB based pooling is enabled i.e. slowPrbPoolingAllowed set to 'true' or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is True, the limitations are mentioned in 5G_UP_ALG_26603_replaced([11171157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuBsavvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

-When layer PRB based pooling is enabled i.e. slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed = TRUE, the limitations are mentioned in 5G_UP_ALG_26604_replaced([11171172](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuBsbvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

###### 3.25.2.3.2.1-5.0-2 Control Channel Element management Limitation by stream PRB pooling (ID: 11171157)

**3.25.2.3.2.1-5.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11171169`)

Control Channel Element management If slowPrbPoolingAllowed set to 'true' or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is True (5G_CP_ARC_ALG_4283_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), while selecting a free PDCCH candidate, gNB-DU shall ensure that PDCCH capacity may be further restricted by the number of usable PRB limit available in DL. The usable DL PRB limit is determined by the PRB pooling algorithm in 5G_UP_ALG_6500_replaced([11212285](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and may change every [Before CB009215-D]bbPoolingPeriod (NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod)[CB009215-D]bbPoolEvalPeriod (refer 5G_UP_ALG_6781_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))[End CB009215-D]). As a result, not all CCEs in the search space may be available for use due to the PRB limit in DL.

-If PDCCH split is not performed in the slot, a free PDCCH candidate ( for DL or UL) is available only if the number of PRB consumed by all CCEs of PDCCH candidate allocated so far and the number of PRB of the CCEs to be used for PDCCH candidate in the slot does not exceed the total PRB limit in DL, otherwise no free PDCCH candidate is available.

  * If PDCCH split is performed in the slot, amount of usable CCEs is computed based on the usable DL PRB in 5G_UP_ALG_6933_replaced([11169932](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6-uPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). 

  * for DL DCIs to be checked only by the DL scheduler, PDCCH candidate is available only if the amount of CCEs used so far and CCEs to be used does not exceed the total number of usable CCEs available for DL in the slot (5G_UP_ALG_6933_replaced([11169932](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6-uPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

  * for UL DCIs to be checked only by the UL scheduler, PDCCH candidate is available only if the amount of CCEs used so far and CCEs to be used does not exceed the total number of usable CCEs available for UL in the slot (5G_UP_ALG_6933_replaced([11169932](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6-uPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))




Note: Rationale for the PDCCH limitation with the PRB pooling is that: not all PRBs of the configured CORESET size(RB) may be available for use due to the limited number of usable PRB in the cell, numAllocCellPrb, and the usable number of RBs determines the usable umber of CCEs that can be used.

---

###### 3.25.2.3.2.1-5.0-3 Control Channel Element management Limitation by layer PRB pooling (ID: 11171172)

**3.25.2.3.2.1-5.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11171177`)

Control Channel Element management If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed = TRUE, while selecting a free PDCCH candidate, gNB-DU shall ensure that PDCCH capacity may be further restricted by the number of usable layer PRB limit available in DL (rrmMaxNumLayerPrbPerSlot) mentioned in 5G_UP_ALG_26582_replaced([11214591](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). As a result, not all CCEs in the search space may be available for use due to the PRB limit in DL. The max available number of CCEs per slot is described in 5G_UP_ALG_26598_replaced([11214630](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOxY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

-If PDCCH split is not performed in the slot, a free PDCCH candidate ( for DL or UL) is available only if the number of layer PRB consumed by all CCEs of PDCCH candidate allocated so far and the number of layer PRB of the CCEs to be used for PDCCH candidate in the slot does not exceed the total layer PRB limit (rrmMaxNumLayerPrbPerSlot in DL; refer 5G_UP_ALG_26582_replaced([11214591](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), otherwise no free PDCCH candidate is available. Layer PRBs used by each of the PDCCH candidates is calculated as rrmNumLayerPrbUsedPerAllocation described in 5G_UP_ALG_26582_replaced([11214591](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

  * If PDCCH split is performed in the slot, amount of usable CCEs is computed based on the usable DL PRB in 5G_UP_ALG_6933_replaced([11169932](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6-uPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). 

  * for DL DCIs to be checked only by the DL scheduler, PDCCH candidate is available only if the amount of CCEs used so far and CCEs to be used does not exceed the total number of usable CCEs available for DL in the slot (5G_UP_ALG_6933_replaced([11169932](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6-uPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

  * for UL DCIs to be checked only by the UL scheduler, PDCCH candidate is available only if the amount of CCEs used so far and CCEs to be used does not exceed the total number of usable CCEs available for UL in the slot (5G_UP_ALG_6933_replaced([11169932](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6-uPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))




Note 1: Rationale for the PDCCH limitation with layer PRB pooling is that: not all PRBs of the configured CORESET size(RB) may be available for use due to the limited number of usable layer PRB in the cell, and the usable number of RBs determines the usable umber of CCEs that can be used.

Note 2: gNB-DU shall assume that a minimum amount of layer PRBs and eventually cell PRBs (since gNB-DU allocates PDCCH resources in terms of Cell PRBs) are always reserved in DL and it will usually be the size (in PRB) of CORESET0.

---

##### 3.25.2.3.2.1-6 Control Channel Element management

###### 3.25.2.3.2.1-6.0-1 Control Channel Element management gNB-DU shall select the start CCE Index for downgraded AL with power boost as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_11025_replaced( 11171067 ) with additional conditions:  the allocation must use the requested AL from 5G_UP_ALG_29348_replaced( 11171360 ).  the PDCCH candidate must be allocated on the PDCCH symbol applicable for PDCCH power boosting as 5G_UP_ALG_29362_replaced( 11171368 ). (ID: 11171183)

##### 3.25.2.3.2.1-7 Control Channel Element management

###### 3.25.2.3.2.1-7.0-2 Control Channel Element management If DL MU-MIMO (FR1, TDD, conduct mode only) is activated, the scheduler shall always use start CCE index 0 to scheduler users because DL channels of co-scheduled users are isolated with each other under RF conduct mode. Up to 8 co-scheduled UEs shall be supported by PDCCH scheduling. The UE specific PDCCH CORESET is defined in 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_2162_replaced( 11308743 ). ~~To co-schedule 8 UEs under conduct mode, the aggregation level shall be set to 2~~. [CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A] (ID: 13459797)

###### 3.25.2.3.2.1.0-2 Control Channel Element management List of PDCCH candidates (ID: 11170873)

**3.25.2.3.2.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11170884`)

Control Channel Element management For different RNTIs, the PDCCH candidates are computed as follows:

###### 3.25.2.3.2.1.0-3 Control Channel Element management PDCCH candidates for Common Search Spaces (ID: 11170890)

**3.25.2.3.2.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11170939`)

Control Channel Element management 11170939: Control Channel Element management For the DCI transmitted in a common search space, the CCE start position depends on :

 CORESET identifier associated to the common search space(s).

 The CORESET size expressed in number of CCEs.

 The number of PDCCH candidates configured per Aggregation Level (AL)

The gNB-DU computes the CCE start indexes allowed according to the common search space type, the associated CORESET, the number of PDCCH candidates defined in the common search space, using the following formula.

[image-0][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is: $cceStart_m = CCE_{AL} \times \left\lfloor \frac{m_s \times N_{CCE,p}}{CCE_{AL} \times M_{p,s,max}^{(AL)}} \right\rfloor \mod \left\lfloor \frac{N_{CCE,p}}{CCE_{AL}} \right\rfloor$[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12248.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

With,

[image-1][image_desc]The image contains the text "CCEAL" in a stylized font with a subtle shadow effect. The letters are light blue with a white outline and a darker blue shadow. The background is a gradient of white and light yellow.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12248.002.png[/image_path][/image-1]:

Number of CCE according to the aggregation level:

 1 CCE for AL1,

 2 CCEs for AL2,

 4 CCEs for AL4,

 8 CCEs for AL8,

 16 CCEs for AL16.

The parameters defining the AL allowed for the common search spaces are the followings:

 dciSiAggregationLevel: AL used for the System Information RNTI (SI-RNTI).

 dciPagingAggregationLevel: AL used for the Paging RNTI (P-RNTI).

 dciRaMsg2AggregationLevel: AL used to send the Random Access Message 2 (RA-Msg2).

 dciRaCompletionAggregationLevel: AL used to send the DCI until the completion of the Random Access procedure.

When the dynamic aggregation level is activated, this AL is used as the starting one until the dynamic AL algorithm selects another AL according to the PDCCH Block Error Rate (BLER) computed for the UE and the expected one.

 dciDedicatedAggregationLevel: AL used to send the DCIs after the contention resolution, when the dynamic AL is not activated.

 When the dynamic AL is activated, the gNB-DU computes the CCE start indexes according the number of candidates allowed in the type3 search space(s).

[image-2][image_desc]The image contains a blurry, close-up view of the letters "mm" followed by a small, blurry symbol that appears to be a lowercase "s" with a small square or box attached to its bottom right. The letters are rendered in a gradient of colors, with hints of yellow, orange, blue, and purple. The background is white.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12248.003.png[/image_path][/image-2]:

PDCCH candidate indexes, defined in a given search space, between 0 and [image-3][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is "M^(L)_(p,s,max)". The letter "M" is in the foreground, with a superscript "(L)" and a subscript "p,s,max". The text is in a dark color against a white background.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12248.004.png[/image_path][/image-3]-1.

[image-4][image_desc]The image contains the text "NccE,p" with a slight blur.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12248.005.png[/image_path][/image-4]:

Number of CCE available in the CORESET(p) computed as follows.

[image-5][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is: $N_{CCE,p} = \sum_{i=19}^{63} coresetFreqDomain_p(b_i) \times coresetDuration_p$[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12248.006.png[/image_path][/image-5]

With,

[image-6][image_desc]The image contains the text "coresetFreqDomain(b)". The text is in a light gray color and is slightly blurry. The text is written in a sans-serif font. The background of the image is white.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12248.007.png[/image_path][/image-6]:

Value of the bit index (i) in the coresetFreqDomain bitmap associated to the CORESET(p).

###### 3.25.2.3.2.1.0-4 Control Channel Element management PDCCH candidates for UE-Specific Search Spaces (ID: 11170944)

**3.25.2.3.2.1.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11171061`)

Control Channel Element management 11171061: Control Channel Element management For the DCI transmitted in a UE-Specific Search Space, the CCE start position depends on :

 CORESET identifier associated to the common search space(s).

 The CORESET size expressed in number of CCEs.

 The number of PDCCH candidates configured per AL.

 The congruence relation of the RNTI and constants linked to the CORESET identifier and the slot number in the radio frame.

The gNB-DU computes the CCE start indexes allowed according to the UE-Specific search space, the associated CORESET, the number of PDCCH candidates defined for the UE-Specific search space, the RNTI and the slot number, using the following formula.

When the dynamic AL is activated, the gNB-DU has to compute the CCE start index of all PDCCH candidates for all AL configured in the search spaces. When the static AL is selected, then the gNB-DU computes the data only for the AL declared in dciRaCompletionAggregationLevel and dciDedicatedAggregationLevel [CB008246-A]and dciDedicatedAggregationLevelHR[End CB008246-A] parameters.

[image-0][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is: $cceStart_m = CCE_{AL} \times \left( \left( Y_{p,n_{sf}^\mu} + \frac{m_s \times N_{CCE,p}}{CCE_{AL} \times M_{p,s,max}^{(AL)}} \right) \mod \left| \frac{N_{CCE,p}}{CCE_{AL}} \right| \right)$[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12251.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

 1 CCE for AL1,

 2 CCEs for AL2,

 4 CCEs for AL4,

 8 CCEs for AL8,

 16 CCEs for AL16.

The parameters defining the AL allowed for the UE-Specific search spaces are defined by the numOfPdcchCandidatesInALx (x = 1, 2, 4, 8 or 16) is not equal to (n0). When the static AL is configured only the number of PDCCH candidates associated to the dciRaCompletionAggregationLevel and dciDedicatedAggregationLevel [CB008246-A]and dciDedicatedAggregationLevelHR[End CB008246-A] have to be considered.

[image-10][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula presented as a system of equations. The formula defines a sequence $Y_{p,n_s,f}^{\mu}$ based on previous terms and constants. Here's a breakdown of the equations: 1\. $Y_{p,n_s,f}^{\mu} = (A_p \times Y_{p,n_s,f-1}^{\mu}) \mod D$ This is a recursive formula. The current term $Y_{p,n_s,f}^{\mu}$ is calculated by multiplying the previous term $Y_{p,n_s,f-1}^{\mu}$ by a factor $A_p$ and then taking the result modulo $D$. 2\. $Y_{p,-1} = n_{RNTI}$ This is the base case for the recursion. The term $Y_{p,-1}$ is initialized with the value $n_{RNTI}$. 3\. $D = 65537, A_p = \begin{cases} 39827, & p \mod 3 = 0 \ 39829, & p \mod 3 = 1 \ 39839, & p \mod 3 = 2 \end{cases}$ This defines the constants $D$ and $A_p$. * $D$ is a fixed value of 65537. * $A_p$ is a value that depends on the remainder of $p$ when divided by 3. * If $p \mod 3 = 0$, then $A_p = 39827$. * If $p \mod 3 = 1$, then $A_p = 39829$. * If $p \mod 3 = 2$, then $A_p = 39839$. The overall system describes a process that generates a sequence of values, where the generation rule changes based on the value of $p$.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12251.011.png[/image_path][/image-10]
