### 3.25.2.4 PDCCH least blocking algorithm

#### 3.25.2.4.0-1 PDCCH least blocking algorithm Overview (ID: 13361387)

**3.25.2.4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13361388`)

PDCCH least blocking algorithm The PDCCH least blocking algorithm consists of two parts:

  1. Truncation of the CS1 list: When the R&D parameter rdActCs1ListTruncationAndQuotaAllocation is true, gNB-DU shall truncate the non-GBR UEs in the CS1 list to a smaller list based on a threshold computed for each direction (DL: [13346611: CS1 list truncation considering the PDCCH capacity](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_VjDU5eVfEfCmxLW1M7HMrQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9), UL: [13347070: CS1 list truncation considering the PDCCH capacity](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_5qJa4eWLEfCmxLW1M7HMrQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) at the TD scheduler after the TD metric is computed for the UEs in the CS1 list and before the CS2 list is created,
  2. Detailed algorithm [13346612: CS1 list truncation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_VjDU4uVfEfCmxLW1M7HMrQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)
  3. UE sorting and least blocking algorithm: When the R&D parameter rdActUeSorting and rdActLeastBlocking are True, at the dynamic start CCE selection phase ([11171067: Start CCE selection](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuBFXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) where PDCCH resources are allocated to the UEs in the CS2 list, sort the non-GBR UEs in the CS2 list based on the AL computed after PDCCH link adaptation and number of candidates configured for the AL, Then use the PDCCH least blocking algorithm at the time of CCE allocation to the UEs in the CS2 list.
  4. Detailed algorithm: [13354860: UE sorting and PDCCH least blocking algorithm](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_YMc8pe--EfC3ocOh_n7w7A?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

---

#### 3.25.2.4.0-2 PDCCH least blocking algorithm CS1 list truncation (ID: 13346612)

**3.25.2.4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13346613`)

PDCCH least blocking algorithm 13346613: PDCCH least blocking algorithm Purpose: * For each PDCCH occasion i, gNB-DU shall select n-GBR UEs (prioritized in the TD metric order in the CS1 list) to a truncated CS1 list based on the available CCEs XLS_CAPi, where XLS_CAPi = CCE_XLi x rdPdcchAlpha and CCE_XLi is the maximum # of CCEs available in the PDCCH occasion for the scheduler in UE specific search space (for DL, X=D andfor UL, X=U). rdPdcchAlpha is an overbooking factor and it is an R&D parameter ([13347081: rdPdcchAlpha](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_oOM5seWREfCmxLW1M7HMrQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). * For each PDCCH occasion i, gNB-DU shall initiate a quota for the # of n-GBR UEs (for the ALs allowed in UESS) in the truncated CS1 list based on XLS_CAPi: _Qi,j= floor (XLS_CAPi /_ ALj) where**j** ∈**{All ALs configured to the UEs in UE SSS}_Qi,j: UE quota for_ ALjin PDCCH occasion i** * When a UE is added to the truncated CS1 list in PDCCH occasion i, sumCcesi of all the UEs in the truncated CS1 list and the UE quotas of all n-GBR UEs are updated. _Q_ i,j _= floor ((X_ LS_CAPi - sumCces _i_) / ALj) where**Qi,j: Adjusted UE quota for j** ∈ __{All ALs configured to the UEs in UE SSS} sumCcesi: sum of the CCEs requested by all the UEs in the truncated CS1 list. Algorithm: [image-0][image_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a process for managing UE (User Equipment) lists and their associated metrics. The flowchart begins with a "Start" oval, leading to an input step labeled "Input: CS1 list and TD metrics of all entries". Next, the UEs are arranged in decreasing order of their TD metric. A calculation step follows, "Compute XLS_CAP", with the formula "XLS_CAPI = CCE_XLi x rdPdcchAlpha". Then, the UE quota for each ALJ is initialized using the formula "Qi,j = floor (XLS_CAPi / ALj)". A decision diamond asks "All UEs in CS1 list visited?". If the answer is no, the process proceeds to "Take the next UE from the top of the list". After taking the next UE, a decision diamond checks "Is the UE quota exceeded for its AL?". If the quota is exceeded, the UE is removed from the CS1 list and added to the truncated CS1 list. If the quota is not exceeded, another decision diamond asks "UE is an n-GBR UE?". If the UE is an n-GBR UE, it is removed from the CS1 list and added to the truncated CS1 list. If the UE is not an n-GBR UE, the process updates "sumCces" with the formula "sumCcesi = sumCcesi + CCEs needed for this UE and update the UE quota of all ALs Qi,j = floor ((XLS_CAPi - sumCcesi)/ALj)". Following the update of sumCces, a decision diamond checks "XLS_CAPi <= sumCcesi". If this condition is true, the process moves to the output step. If this condition is false, the process loops back to "Take the next UE from the top of the list". If the initial decision "All UEs in CS1 list visited?" is yes, the process moves to the output step. The output step is labeled "Output: CS1 list and truncated CS1 list", followed by a "Stop" oval.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/img-01201820.png[/image_path][/image-0] Link: [truncationOfCs1ListInDls.vsdx](https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:u:/r/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/Drawings%20and%20diagrams%20for%205G/User%20Plane/5G%20UP%20Algorithms/3%20L2RT%20Algorithms/CB012732%20PDCCH%20least%20blocking%20algorithm/truncationOfCs1ListInDls.vsdx?d=wec8323dd3bd64a1e94e3445e73002940&csf=1&web=1&e=TRW6YV) Rational: * _rdPdcchAlpha > 1 is used to select enough RNTIs per AL so that PDCCH candidates in the PDCCH occasion are properly utilized._ * CS1 list is truncated based on the PDCCH capacity as the processing of additional UEs will provide limited gains. \+ A quota is given to each AL to improve the PDCCH resource utilization in the truncated CS1 list by preventing high AL UEs with high priorities blocking all the PDCCH resources at the beginning which can later be left unused by lower AL UEs due to truncation.

---

**3.25.2.4.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13361421`)

PDCCH least blocking algorithm CS1 list truncation for multiple BWPs

---

**3.25.2.4.0-2.0-1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13361423`)

PDCCH least blocking algorithm 13361423: PDCCH least blocking algorithm When small dedicated BWPs and/or PS BWP are configured in the cell, when adding an n-GBR UE to the truncated CS1 list, gNB-DU shall consider whether the UE belongs to a BWP satisfying the conditions of a nested BWP ([11169245: Definition of a nested BWP](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt2GQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

  1. When two BWPs satisfy the condition of a nested BWP (nBwp) and the CORESETs are overlapping in a PDCCH occasion, UEs are added to the truncated CS1 list using algorithm in [13346612: CS1 list truncation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_VjDU4uVfEfCmxLW1M7HMrQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) with following exceptions:
  2. the union of CCEs in the CORESETs configured in the UESS in a PDCCH occasion i in the nested BWP determine the total CCEs in the nested BWP (CCE_XLnBwp,i) for direction X (for DL, X=D andfor UL, X=U)​​​​: [image-0][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in black text. The equation is: $CCE_XL_{nBwp,i} = \bigcup_{k=1}^{y} Cces_{k}$.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/img-01181038.png[/image_path][/image-0] where y is the number of BWPs in the nested BWP and [image-1][image_desc]The image contains a blurry, grayscale rendering of the uppercase letter "U".[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/img-01181116.png[/image_path][/image-1] is the union operation.
     * XLS_CAPnBwp,i = CCE_XLnBwp,i x rdPdcchAlpha
  3. _sumCces_ nBwp,i _is updated for the nested BWP whenever a UE in BWP 1..y is added to the truncated CS1 list._
  4. For BWPs not satisfying the condition of a nested BWP or when two BWPs satisfy the conditions of a nested BWP but CORESETs are not overlapping in a given PDCCH occasion, 
  5. CCE allocation is separately per BWP using algorithm in [13346612: CS1 list truncation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_VjDU4uVfEfCmxLW1M7HMrQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) when a UE is added to the truncated CS1 list.
  6. When two BWPs satisfy the condition for a nested BWP, CCE split is activated in a slot and only one half of the CCE set of a CORESET of one BWP is overlaping with the CORESET of a smaller BWP without CCE split in a given PDCCH occasion , then above conditions in case 1 only applies to the direction that has the overlap. The direction having no overlap is treated as in case 2 in that PDCCH occasion.
  7. E.g. CCE split is enabled in symbol 0 in BWP1 only. Case 1 applies to symbol 0 UL direction and case 2 applies to symbol 0 DL direction and symbol 1 DL direction.  
[image-2][image_desc]The image displays a diagram illustrating two Bandwidth Parts (BWPs), BWP1 and BWP2, and their respective Control Resource Sets (CORESETs) within two symbols, Symb_0 and Symb_1. BWP1 is shown in Symb_0 and consists of a Downlink (DL) portion and two Uplink (UL) portions. The DL portion occupies the upper half of BWP1, while the two UL portions are side-by-side and occupy the lower half. The entire vertical extent of BWP1 in Symb_0 is labeled as "CORESET of BWP1". BWP2 is shown in Symb_1 and consists of a single Downlink (DL) portion. The vertical extent of BWP2 in Symb_1 is labeled as "CORESET of BWP2". Additionally, there is a label "CORESET of BWP2" associated with the vertical extent of BWP2 in Symb_0, indicating that BWP2's CORESET also spans across Symb_0, although no specific resource allocation for BWP2 is depicted in Symb_0. The diagram visually represents how different BWPs and their control resources can be allocated across symbols in a communication system.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/img-01231310.png[/image_path][/image-2]
  8. When two BWPs satisfy the condition for a nested BWP, CCE split is activated in a slot, CORESETs of both BWPs are having the CCE split, one CCE split set is fully overlapping and the other set is partially overlapping in a given PDCCH occasion, then both directions are treated as in case 1.
  9. E.g. CCE split is enabled in symbol 0 and 1 in both BWPs. Case 1 applies to symbol 0 in both directions and case 2 applies to symbol 1 in BWP2.  
[image-3][image_desc]The image displays two diagrams illustrating the concept of Bandwidth Part (BWP) in a communication system. Each diagram represents a symbol, labeled "Symb_0" and "Symb_1". The diagram for "Symb_0" shows two vertical bars, representing two different Bandwidth Parts (BWP1 and BWP2).
     * BWP1 is shown as a taller bar, divided into two sections: "DL" (Downlink) at the top and "UL" (Uplink) at the bottom. The entire height of BWP1 is labeled as "CORESET of BWP1".
     * BWP2 is shown as a shorter bar, also divided into "DL" at the top and "UL" at the bottom. The entire height of BWP2 is labeled as "CORESET of BWP2". The diagram for "Symb_1" shows a single vertical bar, representing BWP2.
     * This bar is divided into two sections: "DL" at the top and "UL" at the bottom. The entire height of this bar is labeled as "CORESET of BWP2". The diagrams visually represent how different parts of the bandwidth can be allocated for downlink and uplink transmissions within different Bandwidth Parts, and how these allocations can vary across different symbols.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/img-01231336.png[/image_path][/image-3]

---

#### 3.25.2.4.0-3 PDCCH least blocking algorithm UE sorting and PDCCH least blocking algorithm (ID: 13354860)

**3.25.2.4.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `13354992`)

PDCCH least blocking algorithm **UE sorting algorithm**

---

**3.25.2.4.0-3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13354993`)

PDCCH least blocking algorithm When NRCELL.actPdcchLeastBlockingAlg is enabled and rdActUeSorting ([13359785: rdActUeSorting](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_5Sb2JPIbEfC0Z6kKit-MzQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) is True, the UE sorting Algorithm shall be executed during the execution process of the the Least Blocking Algorithm and when modifications to the input Candidate Set 2 List (CS2 List) sequence necessitate reordering and may be bypassed when the CS2 list sequence contains zero or one non-GBR UE to reduce computational overhead.

The UE Sorting algorithm shall operate as follows:

  * The input CS2 List sequence shall be evaluated, and the UE Sorting Algorithm shall be executed only on a stable CS2 List, ensuring no overlap with data modification operations.

  * If the CS2 List sequence contains zero or one non-GBR UE, it shall be considered sorted and returned without modification.




\- Otherwise, the non-GBR UEs in the sequence shall be sorted based on the desired heuristic, such as sorting in ascending order of the number of PDCCH candidates valid for the slot. In case the number of candidates are not the same for a UE in the PDCCH occasions valid for the slot, the highest number of candidates shall be used.

\- In case at least two UEs share the same number of PDCCH candidates, those UEs are sorted in the descending order of the Aggregation Level (AL).

  * In case at least two UEs share the same AL, those UEs shall be sorted using alternative heuristic such as descending order of TD metric. 

  * If all non-GBR UEs in the CS2 List sequence have been sorted, then exit the function. Otherwise, repeat the function's execution.

---

**3.25.2.4.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `13354895`)

PDCCH least blocking algorithm **PDCCH least blocking algorithm**

---

**3.25.2.4.0-3.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `13361442`)

PDCCH least blocking algorithm **Blocking cost calculation**

---

**3.25.2.4.0-3.0-3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13361443`)

PDCCH least blocking algorithm The Blocking cost calculation shall be executed during the execution process of the the Least Blocking Algorithm and shall operate as follows:

For the given candidate UE, represented by the index i, the gNB-DU shall define the following values:

  * ALi shall be defined as the Aggregation Level (AL) associated to the UEi 
  * startCCEi shall be set as the starting Control Channel Element (CCE) for the PDCCH candidate associated with UEi 
  * cost(i, startCCEi) denote the value to be calculated and returned by the Blocking Cost Function, where i represents the index of the UE and startCCEi is the starting CCE value associated with UEi.



\- overlappingCCEs represent the overlapping CCEs with the current candidate. overlappingCCEs should be calculated after the 5G-L2-PS has generated all the lists of preempted CCEs as per the requirement CCE Pre-emption List Update ([11169911: CCE Pre-emption List Update](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6-s_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

The gNB-DU shall compute the following values:

  * maxAL, which represents the highest Aggregation Level (AL) configured to the UE in the PDCCH occasion.  
\- maxCCEsInCoreset, which represents the maximum number of Control Channel Elements (CCEs) in the specified PDCCH occasion.



For a selected UE, the Blocking Cost Function defined at the gNB-DU shall operate as follows:

If ALi = maxAL:

  * then the Blocking Cost Function returns cost (i, startCCEi) = 0 and exit the function.



Otherwise, proceed with the function's execution as follows:

  * Let currAL be an iteration variable defined over the sequence containing the elements: {maxAL, maxAL/2, …, max (1, ALi)}



In case ALi < currAL:

  * Then verify If all CCEs that fall within floor (startCCEi / currAL) × currAL to min (floor (startCCEi / currAL) × currAL + currAL - 1, maxCCEsInCoreset - 1) are unoccupied.
  * If the verification is satisfied, then:
  * size the CCEs as: CCESetSize = min (floor(startCCEi / currAL) × currAL + currAL, maxCCEsInCoreset) - floor (startCCEi / currAL) × currAL
  * And compute cost (i, startCCEi) as follow:
  * If the UE is in the large BWP, and there is an overlapping CORESET with the small BWP(s), then: cost (i, startCCEi) = cost (i, startCCEi) + overlappingCCEs
  * Else: cost (i, startCCEi) = min (currAL, CCESetSize)
  * And stop the function execution and the Blocking Cost Function returns the computed cost (i, startCCEi).
  * If the verification is not satisfied, then repeat the function's execution with the next value of currAL.



In case ALi >= currAL:

  * If the UE is in the large BWP, and there is an overlapping CORESET with the small BWP(s), then: cost (i, startCCEi) = overlappingCCEs
  * Else: cost (i, startCCEi) = 0 and exit the function.

---

**3.25.2.4.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `13368164`)

PDCCH least blocking algorithm **Restriction due to overload control**

---

**3.25.2.4.0-3.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `13368165`)

PDCCH least blocking algorithm If the real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric (See 5G_UP_ALG_31301_replaced([11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) value provided by the gNB-DU overload control handler is below the deactivation value set for rdPdcchLeastBlockingAlgPercent([13368142: rdPDCCHLeastBlockingAlgPerCent](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_srYPlvdsEfC0Z6kKit-MzQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) then, gNB-DU shall deactive UE sorting and PDCCH least blocking algorithm ([13354860: UE sorting and PDCCH least blocking algorithm](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_YMc8pe--EfC3ocOh_n7w7A?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

If the real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric (See 5G_UP_ALG_31301_replaced([11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) value provided by the gNB-DU overload control handler is greater than or equal to the activation value set for rdPdcchLeastBlockingAlgPercent([13368142: rdPDCCHLeastBlockingAlgPerCent](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_srYPlvdsEfC0Z6kKit-MzQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) then, gNB-DU shall activate UE sorting and PDCCH least blocking algorithm ([13354860: UE sorting and PDCCH least blocking algorithm](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_YMc8pe--EfC3ocOh_n7w7A?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

#### 3.25.2.5.0-2 PDCCH power boosting PDCCH Power Resource (ID: 11171220)

**3.25.2.5.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `13462888`)

PDCCH power boosting PDCCH power resources are tracked per PDCCH symbol for each DL and UL direction respectively.

On each slot to send DCI, gNB shall initialize the PDCCH power resource rrmPdcchPowerResource[i, x] for each PDCCH symbol as below.

 For asymmetric DSS (NRCELL.actAsymmetricDss=true) initialize the PDCCH power resources according to the [12708869: PDCCH Power Resource for Asymmetric DSS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ewELAGMeEfC3KtQ77je1xA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

 For without CCE split [Before CB012733-C-UPD001] , rrmPdcchPowerResource[i, x] = the number of PRBs of cell DL bandwidth.[CB012733-C-UPD001]

if (NRCELL.actThreeSymbolPdcch is not disabled with either NRCELL.actPowerSavingBwp is true or NRBTS.actMultipleDedicatedBWPs is true), then

rrmPdcchPowerResource[i, x] = the number of PRBs of cell DL bandwidth - the PRBs not covered by the union CORESETs

Else

rrmPdcchPowerResource[i, x] = the number of PRBs of cell DL bandwidth [End CB012733-C-UPD001]

 For CCE split, the initial values

o rrmPdcchPowerResource[i, DL] = Max DL PDCCH power resource (5G_UP_ALG_29310_replaced([11171229](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuCTgfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

o rrmPdcchPowerResource[i, UL] = Max UL PDCCH power resource (5G_UP_ALG_29310_replaced([11171229](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuCTgfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

 Where:

· i: PDCCH symbol index

· x: DL or UL

· the number of PRBs of cell DL bandwidth: 5G_UP_ALG_1795_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the blanked PRB shall be included.

· the PDCCH slot and PDCCH symbol are determined as 5G_UP_ALG_3958_replaced([11168909](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktzp8fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

PDCCH power resource update is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_29314_replaced([11171254](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuCThPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

#### 3.25.2.5.0-3 PDCCH power boosting PDCCH Power Resource of CCE split (ID: 11171229)

**3.25.2.5.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `13462881`)

PDCCH power boosting 13462881: PDCCH power boosting For asymmetric DSS (NRCELL.actAsymmetricDss=true) initialize the PDCCH power resources according to the [12708869: PDCCH Power Resource for Asymmetric DSS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ewELAGMeEfC3KtQ77je1xA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) For slot with CCE split, Max DL PDCCH power resource and Max UL PDCCH power resource are split based on DL/UL CCE split ratio. The granularity of DL PDCCH power resource is one CCE, while UL PDCCH power resource uses the remaining. maxPDCCHPowerResourceDL = max ( rounddown (nPRB_DL / Step * ratio_DL), nCCE_DL ) * Step maxPDCCHPowerResourceUL = nPRB_DL - MaxPDCCHPowerResourceDL Where: · [Before CB012733-C-UPD001] nPRB_DL: number of PRBs of the cell DL bandwidth as 5G_UP_ALG_1795_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).[CB012733-C-UPD001] if (NRCELL.actThreeSymbolPdcch is not disabled with either NRCELL.actPowerSavingBwp is true or NRBTS.actMultipleDedicatedBWPs is true), then nPRB_DL: the number of PRBs of cell DL bandwidth as [11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) \- the PRBs not covered by the union of CORESETs Else nPRB_DL: number of PRBs of the cell DL bandwidth as [11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) [End CB012733-C-UPD001] · ratio_DL = nCCE_DL / (nCCE_DL + nCCE_UL) · nCCE_DL, nCCE_UL: the number of CCEs for DL and UL of largest BWP from 5G_UP_ALG_3955_replaced([11169860](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6Xp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). **For tdLte config0 frame structure, in slots with 2 K2 and 1 K1 configured, refer 5G_UP_ALG_32469_replaced([11169885](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6XrPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the number of CCEs for DL and UL.** · Step: Granularity of PDCCH power resource, which is the number of PRBs of one CCE over each PDCCH symbol of reference CORESET = 6 PRBs / duration of target reference CORESET of the largest BWP as 5G_UP_ALG_11211_replaced([11168405](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktv_kfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Example: · Cell DL bandwidth is 106 PRBs. CORESET duration is 1 symbol. 4 CCEs for DL and 5 CCEs for UL. · Max DL PDCCH power resource: max(rounddown(106 / 6 * 4 / (4 + 5)) , 4) * 6 = 42 PRBs. · Max UL PDCCH power resource: 106 - 42 (Max DL PDCCH power resource) = 64 PRBs. [image-0][image_desc]The image displays a diagram illustrating the concept of "blanked PRBs" within a cell's downlink (DL) bandwidth. The diagram is divided into two main sections. The left section, which occupies the majority of the space, is labeled "Cell DL bandwidth = n PRBs". This indicates that the total downlink bandwidth of the cell is comprised of 'n' Physical Resource Blocks (PRBs). The right section of the diagram is further subdivided into three smaller rectangular areas. The top and bottom areas are shaded gray and are labeled "blanked PRBs". The middle area is white and is labeled "available PRBs". This visual representation suggests that within the total 'n' PRBs of the cell's DL bandwidth, some PRBs are designated as "blanked" and are not available for data transmission, while others are "available" for use. The arrangement implies that the blanked PRBs are located at the edges or specific portions of the total bandwidth, leaving a central portion as available for data.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12286.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] [image-1][image_desc]The image contains a table with two columns and three rows. The first column is labeled "CCE Split Case" and has two entries: "for UL DCI" and "for DL DCI". The second column is labeled "PDCCH symbols" and is further divided into three sub-columns labeled "i₀", "...", and "i<0xE2><0x82><0x96>". The table entries are as follows:

CCE Split Case | PDCCH symbols |  |   
---|---|---|---  
| i₀ | ... | i<0xE2><0x82><0x96>  
for UL DCI | n-m | n-m | n-m  
for DL DCI | m | m | m

#### 3.25.2.5.0-4 PDCCH power boosting PDCCH Power Resource for Asymmetric DSS (ID: 12708869)

**3.25.2.5.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12708871`)

PDCCH power boosting [CB007372-M]

For asymmetric DSS (NRCELL.actAsymmetricDss=true) the PDCCH power resources are tracked per PDCCH symbol for each DL and UL direction respectively. In symbol#2 the PDCCH power resources depend on DL resources assigned by the CRM.

On each slot to send DCI, gNB shall initialize the PDCCH power resource rrmPdcchPowerResource[i, x] for each PDCCH symbol as below.

 For symbols #0 and #1 (symbols without CCE split),  
rrmPdcchPowerResource[i, x] = nPRB_DL - nPRB_SharedArea

 For symbol #2 if no coreset overlaps the LTE shared area (no CCE split in symbol#2),  
if LTE shared area is not assigned to NR then:  
rrmPdcchPowerResource[2, x] = nPRB_DL - nPRB_SharedArea  
else: // LTE shared area is assigned to NR  
rrmPdcchPowerResource[2, x] = nPRB_DL - nPRB_LTE 

 For symbol #2 if any coreset overlaps the LTE shared area (CCE split in symbol#2),  
if LTE shared area is not assigned to NR then:  
allPowerResources = nPRB_DL - nPRB_SharedArea  
else: // LTE shared area is assigned to NR  
allPowerResources = nPRB_DL - nPRB_LTE 

If the first PDCCH occasion is allocated to DL then assign power resources in symbol#2 first to UL:  
rrmPdcchPowerResource[2, UL] = max (rounddown (allPowerResources/6 _ratio_UL), min(nCCE_UL, rounddown (allPowerResources/6)) )_ 6  
rrmPdcchPowerResource[2, DL] = allPowerResources - rrmPdcchPowerResource[2, UL] 

else if the first PDCCH occasion is allocated to UL then assign power resources in symbol#2 first to DL:  
rrmPdcchPowerResource[2, DL] = max (rounddown (allPowerResources/6 _ratio_DL), min(nCCE_DL, rounddown (allPowerResources/6)) )_ 6  
rrmPdcchPowerResource[2, UL] = allPowerResources - rrmPdcchPowerResource[2, DL]

Reasoning: the power resources should be allocated first to the direction which has more PRBs in the NR dedicated area, see [12658544: CCE split for asymmetric DSS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_vqrj8UqyEfC0Ye3M8ARUWQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). Other direction may have all CCEs not available if they are all in the LTE shared area.

 Where:

· i: PDCCH symbol index

· x: DL or UL

· nPRB_DL: PRBs available in DL ([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the blanked PRBs shall be included.

· nPRB_SharedArea: number of PRBs in LTE shared area ([12620260: Resource sharing in asymmetric DSS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_NsAEcDfZEfCYiuaHdt7wgQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))

· nPRB_LTE: PRBs assigned to LTE. When the DL PRB sharing in subframe 5/9 is enabled (rrmLteDLPrbSharing=TRUE, [11172097](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuJoPfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) then in subframes 5 and 9 some PRBs are assigned to LTE. [CB007372-G] CAT-M doesn't impact PDCCH power budget calculations because CAT-M doesn't use symbols 0,1 and 2 where PDCCH is located. [End CB007372-G]

· the PDCCH slot and PDCCH symbol are determined in [11168909: PDCCH Slot Pattern](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktzp8fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

· nCCE_DL, nCCE_UL: the number of CCEs for DL and UL of largest BWP are defined in [12658544: CCE split for asymmetric DSS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_vqrj8UqyEfC0Ye3M8ARUWQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_vqrj8uqyefc0ye3m8aruwq?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9")

· ratio_DL = nCCE_DL / (nCCE_DL + nCCE_UL)

· ratio_UL = nCCE_UL / (nCCE_DL + nCCE_UL)

PDCCH power resource update is defined in [11171254: Update PDCCH power resource](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuCThPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

[End CB007372-M]

---

#### 3.25.2.5.0-5 PDCCH power boosting Update PDCCH power resource (ID: 11171254)

**3.25.2.5.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `13415110`)

PDCCH power boosting PDCCH power resource is updated for PDCCH power resource allocation (5G_UP_ALG_29306_replaced([11171200](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuCTevvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_29346_replaced([11171327](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuC6lPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_29348_replaced([11171360](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuDhmPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

rrmPdcchPowerResource[i, x] = rrmPdcchPowerResource[i, x] - pdcchPowerPerCandidate[i, x]

Where:

· rrmPdcchPowerResource initial value is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_29308_replaced([11171220](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuCTf_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

· pdcchPowerPerCandidate[i, x]: PDCCH power resource used by a PDCCH candidate in 5G_UP_ALG_29316_replaced([11171274](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuC6g_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), pdcch_power_boost_factor is determined as follows,

 IF UE is scheduled from waiting list (5G_UP_ALG_29348_replaced([11171360](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuDhmPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), Then pdcch_power_boost_factor is 2,

 Else, If PDCCH power boosting due to AL not configured (item in candidate list as 5G_UP_ALG_29346_replaced([11171327](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuC6lPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), Then pdcch_power_boost_factor is 1,

 Else, If UE is scheduled as case1 [Before CB007372-M] in 5G_UP_ALG_2552_replaced([11118347](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqCkQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (AL2 power boosting when DSS with PRB blanking) or case2 in 5G_UP_ALG_2552_replaced([11118347](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqCkQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (AL2 power boosting when DSS with PDSCH in SSB slot) [CB007372-M] or case2 in [13415103: Conditions for PDCCH power control in symmetric DSS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_QRCaYBNOEfG3gf_qmG8Vww) [End CB007372-M] , Then pdcch_power_boost_factor is 2,

 Else, pdcch_power_boost_factor is 1.

Note1: For PDCCH power boosting due to AL not configured, it calls twice power update, one from normal PDCCH allocation (5G_UP_ALG_29306_replaced([11171200](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuCTevvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and another from 5G_UP_ALG_29346_replaced([11171327](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuC6lPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) which decides power boosting to compensate AL downgrade due to AL not configured.

Note2: For case1 and case2 in 5G_UP_ALG_2552_replaced([11118347](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqCkQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), rrmPdcchPowerResource[i, x] may down to negative value from legacy DSS implementation.

---

#### 3.25.2.5.0-6 PDCCH power boosting Check PDCCH power resource enough for a PDCCH candidate (ID: 11171263)

**3.25.2.5.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11171268`)

PDCCH power boosting PDCCH power resource checking is requested upon PDCCH allocation for 5G_UP_ALG_29348_replaced([11171360](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuDhmPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) / PDCCH power resource allocation for 5G_UP_ALG_29346_replaced([11171327](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuC6lPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 Checking passed if rrmPdcchPowerResource[i, x] >= pdcchPowerPerCandidate[i, x] over all PDCCH symbols on UL or DL direction.

 Checking failed if rrmPdcchPowerResource[i, x] < pdcchPowerPerCandidate[i, x] for any of PDCCH symbol on UL or DL direction.

Where:

· rrmPdcchPowerResource[i, x]: PDCCH power resource defined in 5G_UP_ALG_29308_replaced([11171220](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuCTf_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

· pdcchPowerPerCandidate[i, x]: PDCCH power resource used by a PDCCH candidate defined in 5G_UP_ALG_29316_replaced([11171274](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuC6g_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

o For UE scheduled in waiting list (5G_UP_ALG_29348_replaced([11171360](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuDhmPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), pdcch_power_boost_factor is 2, otherwise pdcch_power_boost_factor is 1.

---

#### 3.25.2.5.0-7 PDCCH power boosting PDCCH power resource by a PDCCH candidate (ID: 11171274)

**3.25.2.5.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11171281`)

PDCCH power boosting 11171281: PDCCH power boosting For each PDCCH symbol of the PDCCH candidate

pdcchPowerPerCandidate[i, x] = 6 / duration of PDCCH candidate CORESET * AL* pdcch_power_boost_factor

Where:

 AL: AL1 is 1, AL2 is 2, AL4 is 4 and so on.

 pdcch_power_boost_factor: refer 5G_UP_ALG_29314_replaced([11171254](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuCThPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_29350_replaced([11171263](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuC6gfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 i is PDCCH symbol index

 x is DL or UL

[image-0][image_desc]The image displays a table illustrating the power resource consumed by one CCE (Common Control Channel Element) for the Physical Downlink Control Channel (PDCCH). The table is divided into two main sections: the first section shows the power resource consumption without any boost, and the second section shows the consumption with a 3dB boost. The columns represent PDCCH Symbols determined by CORESET and SearchSpace, labeled as 'i', 'i+1', and 'i+2'. The rows represent the CORESET duration in symbols: '1 symbol', '2 symbols', and '3 symbols'. **Section 1: Without Boost** * **1 symbol CORESET duration:** Consumes 6 power resources for symbol 'i'. * **2 symbols CORESET duration:** Consumes 3 power resources for symbol 'i' and 3 for symbol 'i+1'. * **3 symbols CORESET duration:** Consumes 2 power resources for symbol 'i', 2 for symbol 'i+1', and 2 for symbol 'i+2'. **Section 2: With 3dB Boost** * **1 symbol CORESET duration:** Consumes 12 power resources for symbol 'i'. * **2 symbols CORESET duration:** Consumes 6 power resources for symbol 'i' and 6 for symbol 'i+1'. * **3 symbols CORESET duration:** Consumes 4 power resources for symbol 'i', 4 for symbol 'i+1', and 4 for symbol 'i+2'. The table highlights that a 3dB boost effectively doubles the power resource consumption for each symbol.

CORESET.durartion | i | i+1 | i+2  
---|---|---|---  
1 symbol | 6 |  |   
2 symbols | 3 | 3 |   
3 symbols | 2 | 2 | 2  
1 symbol | 12 |  |   
2 symbols | 6 | 6 |   
3 symbols | 4 | 4 | 4

---

#### 3.25.2.5.0-8 PDCCH power boosting Condition to skip PDCCH power boosting (ID: 11171287)

**3.25.2.5.0-8.0-3**  (ID: `13398578`)

PDCCH power boosting gNB-DU shall determine whether a slot skips PDCCH power boosting or not. If any one of following conditions is satisfied, then the slot skips PDCCH power boosting.

 If NRBTS/NRCELL/actPdcchSharingWithPdsch is set to TRUE and the last PDCCH symbol(s) is for DL and only 1 DL UE is allocated after 5G_UP_ALG_29306_replaced([11171200](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuCTevvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) step 2.

 [CB012733-C-UPD001]NRCELL.actThreeSymbolPdcch is disabled and[End CB012733-C-UPD001] PDCCH power boosting determination is for UL and multiple K2 mode (5G_UP_13617_replaced([11348263](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubTk3vvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_30394_replaced([11116305](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp2-FPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_30707_replaced([11169564](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt4icfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is being used.

Rationale: PDCCH Power boosting AND shared PDCCH and PDSCH allocations are not applied on a same slot. Shared PDCCH and PDSCH allocations takes precedence over PDCCH power boosting. Because PDCCH allocation is performed prior to PDSCH allocaiton, this condition checks a potential eligilble condition for shared PDCCH and PDSCH allocations (5G_UP_ALG_25285_replaced([11183087](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvH4l_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) during PDCCH allcation.

---

#### 3.25.2.5.0-9 PDCCH power boosting Candidate list for PDCCH power boosting (for AL not configured) (ID: 11171300)

**3.25.2.5.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `11171303`)

PDCCH power boosting According to 5G_UP_ALG_29306_replaced([11171200](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuCTevvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), gNB-DU shall maintain 2 candidate lists for PDCCH power boosting, one for DL and another one for UL.

gNB-DU shall reset DL candidate list and UL candidate list to empty before PDCCH scheduling on a slot to send DCI.

Refer 5G_UP_ALG_29324_replaced([11171308](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuC6kPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for condition to add item to a candidate list.

#### 3.25.2.5.0-10 PDCCH power boosting Condition for item in Candidate list for PDCCH power boosting (ID: 11171308)

**3.25.2.5.0-10.0-2**  (ID: `12707267`)

PDCCH power boosting The gNB shall add an item to candidate list for PDCCH power boosting only when all conditions are met:

· Not case1 in [Before CB007372-M] 5G_UP_ALG_2552_replaced([11118347](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqCkQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (AL2 power boosting when DSS with PRB blanking) [CB007372-M] [13415103: Conditions for PDCCH power control in symmetric DSS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_QRCaYBNOEfG3gf_qmG8Vww) [End CB007372-M] . 

· Not case2 in [Before CB007372-M] 5G_UP_ALG_2552_replaced([11118347](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqCkQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (AL2 power boosting when DSS with PDSCH in SSB slot) [CB007372-M] [13415103: Conditions for PDCCH power control in symmetric DSS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_QRCaYBNOEfG3gf_qmG8Vww) [End CB007372-M] .

· the PDCCH candidate must be allocated on the PDCCH symbol applicable for PDCCH power boosting as 5G_UP_ALG_29362_replaced([11171368](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuDhm_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

· The intended AL is not configured as 5G_UP_ALG_29330_replaced([11171320](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuC6kvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

· Final allocated AL from 5G_UP_ALG_13518_replaced([11173699](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuV1cPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) downgrades one level from the intended AL in 5G_UP_ALG_4071_replaced([11170399](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-pGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

o E.g. eligible condition (true): AL8 is the intended AL, and AL4 is allocated.

o E.g. not eligible condition (false): AL8 is the intended AL, and AL2 is allocated.

· The final allocated AL is allowed for PDCCH power boosting by at least one NRDRB-allowedPdcchPowerBoostALDueCfg of UE's bearer(s).

o Where allowedPdcchPowerBoostALDueCfg value: AL2_AL4 means both AL2 and AL4 are allowed. AL2 means AL2 is allowed. AL4 means AL4 is allowed. None means no AL is allowed.

o E.g. UE has two DRBs.

|  |   
---|---|---  
**NRDRB-allowedPdcchPowerBoostALDueCfg** |  | **ALs allowed for PDCCH power boosting due AL not configured**  
**DRB-1** | **DRB-2** |   
none | AL2 | AL2  
none | AL4 | AL4  
AL2 | AL4 | AL2 and AL4  
none | AL2_AL4 | AL2 and AL4  
AL2 | AL2_AL4 | AL2 and AL4

#### 3.25.2.5.0-11 PDCCH power boosting Conditions for PDCCH power control in symmetric DSS (ID: 13415103)

**3.25.2.5.0-11.0-1**  (ID: `13415104`)

PDCCH power boosting Case1 referred in [11171254](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuCThPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ), [11171308](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuC6kPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ). AL2 power boosting when DSS with PRB blanking.  
If cellBW is equal to 10MHz, 15MHz, 20MHz, On an FDD carrier shared with LTE [CB007372-M] and NRCELL.actAsymmetricDss is set to "false' [End CB007372-M] and the PRB blanking function is also enabled (NRBTS/NRCELL/actPRBBlanking set to true), the pdcchDciTransmitPower shall be added 3db after it calculated with the “pdcchDciTransmitPower” formula above if the aggregation level used (refactor to sync with implementation, tag will be removed after review)**for the relative PDCCH transmission is equal to 2, ie dciDedicatedAggregationLevel, dciRaMsg2AggregationLevel or dciRaCompletionAggregationLevel.**

o Case2 referred in [11171254](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuCThPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ), [11171308](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuC6kPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).AL2 power boosting when DSS with PDSCH in SSB slot.  
**For 10 MHz and 15 MHz and 20 Mhz FDD carrier shared with LTE [CB007372-M] and NRCELL.actAsymmetricDss is set to "false' [End CB007372-M], when the used aggregation level of the PDCCH is configured as 2: For PDCCH in SSB slot, the pdcchDciTransmitPower shall be added 3db after it calculated with the “pdcchDciTransmitPower” formula above. Note that the aggregation level of the PDCCH shall be dciDedicatedAggregationLevel when the Al selection mode is set to static, or PDCCH used one from aggregationLevelList when the Al selection mode is set to dynamic.**

#### 3.25.2.5.0-15 PDCCH power boosting Condition for item in waiting list for PDCCH power boosting (ID: 11171343)

**3.25.2.5.0-15.0-1**  (ID: `11171348`)

PDCCH power boosting The gNB shall add an item into waiting list when all conditions are met.

 The AL is selected by 5G_UP_ALG_4071_replaced([11170399](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-pGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) Dynamic AL selection procedure.

 No available PDCCH candidate from 5G_UP_ALG_11025_replaced([11171067](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuBFXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) Start CCE selection.

 The target AL is the AL downgraded one level from the AL selected by 5G_UP_ALG_4071_replaced([11170399](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-pGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The target AL is allowed for PDCCH power boosting by all NRDRB-allowedPdcchPowerBoostALDueCce of UE's bearer(s).

o E.g. AL8 downgrades one level is AL4, AL4 downgrades one level is AL2, and so on.

o E.g. AL8 is selected and AL4 is allowed per allowedPdcchPowerBoostALDueCce

o E.g. allowedPdcchPowerBoostALDueCce value: AL2_AL4 means both AL2 and AL4 are allowed.

 Not skip AL downgrade with PDCCH power boosting due DTX (5G_UP_ALG_29334_replaced([11171351](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuDhlfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 The condition of “Intended AL is not configured” of 5G_UP_ALG_29330_replaced([11171320](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuC6kvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is NOT satisfied.

 The item is for DL PDCCH request and the number of items in the DL waiting list does not reach to maxmium size specified by rdDlWaitingListForPDCCHPowerBoostingSize (5G_UP_ALG_29364_replaced([11171834](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuHzAfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) OR the item is for UL PDCCH request and the number of items in the UL waiting list does not reach to maxmium size specified by rdUlWaitingListForPDCCHPowerBoostingSize (5G_UP_ALG_29366_replaced([11171843](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuHzA_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

#### 3.25.2.5.0-16 PDCCH power boosting Skip AL downgrade with PDCCH power boosting due DTX (ID: 11171351)

**3.25.2.5.0-16.0-1**  (ID: `11171355`)

PDCCH power boosting If NRCELL-actPdcchPowerBoost is enabledNonDTX and PDCCH is allocated as 5G_UP_ALG_29352_replaced([11171181](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuCTcvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and the corresponding PDSCH HARQ/PUSCH reception result is DTX, then gNB shall skip PDCCH power boosting with downgraded AL for all retransmissions of this transmit block.

#### 3.25.2.5.0-17 PDCCH power boosting Handle item in waiting list for PDCCH power boosting (ID: 11171360)

**3.25.2.5.0-17.0-1**  (ID: `11171364`)

PDCCH power boosting gNB shall try to allocate PDCCH with downgrade AL with 3dB PDCCH power boosting for item in waiting list.

If the PDCCH power resource is enough as 5G_UP_ALG_29350_replaced([11171263](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuC6gfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), then,

 gNB-DU shall apply the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_29352_replaced([11171181](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuCTcvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with the requested AL to be one level downgraded from the original AL selected by 5G_UP_ALG_4071_replaced([11170399](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt-pGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the PDCCH request.

 If a PDCCH candidate is allocated, then update PDCCH power resource as 5G_UP_ALG_29314_replaced([11171254](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuCThPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and mark the PDCCH power boosting flag for the handled PDCCH candidate, else the RNTI of the PDCCH request is not scheduled.

Else,

 the RNTI of the PDCCH request is not scheduled.

---

#### 3.25.2.5.0-18 PDCCH power boosting PDCCH symbol for PDCCH power boosting (ID: 11171368)

**3.25.2.5.0-18.0-4**  (ID: `12733390`)

PDCCH power boosting **If the frame structure is not tdLte config0 or the frame structure is tdLte config0 and slots are configured with one K2 and one K1,**

  * if NRBTS/NRCELL-actDynPdcchTdMode is ‘perBWP’, PDCCH power boosting shall be only applicable to symbol 0.
  * [Before CB012733-C-UPD001][CB012733-C] if NRCELL.actThreeSymbolPdcch is not Disabled and multiple BWPs are configured, then there is no PDCCH power boosting. If multiple BWPs are not configured, then power boosting shall apply to all available PDCCH symbols.[End CB012733-C][CB012733-C-UPD001]if NRCELL.actThreeSymbolPdcch is not disabled, then power boosting shall apply to all available PDCCH symbols. [End CB012733-C-UPD001]



Else,

  * in slots configured with two K2s (with or without K1), PDCCH power boosting shall be applicable to all PDCCH symbols.



Rationale:

 When NRBTS/NRCELL-actDynPdcchTdMode is ‘perBWP’ (CB008367 is enabled), it is possible that both PDCCH and PDSCH on symbol 1. (5G_UP_ALG_17072_replaced([11178235](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku09rvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 PDCCH allocation and PDCCH power boosting are performed before PDSCH start symbol determination (5G_UP_ALG_17072_replaced([11178235](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku09rvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 Considering that new feature not degrade the legacy feature performance, we choose CB008367 takes precedence over PDCCH power boosting. So that there is no DL throughput downgrade when CB008367 is enabled. 

 When NRBTS/NRCELL-actDynPdcchTdMode is ‘perBWP’ (CB008367 is enabled), it is possible that one or more PDCCH symbols may be not applied on the largest BWP per 5G_UP_ALG_17022_replaced([11169603](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt4ievvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G_UP_ALG_17072_replaced([11178235](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku09rvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G_UP_ALG_19210_replaced([11178315](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku1kuvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The current solution can solve the interworking with this case also.

 This requirement avoids the PDCCH power boosting impact on PDSCH power control.

---

HARQ process number | 4 | 4 | 5G_UP_ALG_12737_replaced([11184145](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvQbevvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) | One TB for msg4. **[CNI-81991] The HARQ process number is between 0 and 7 until the UE has a dedicated configuration activated in it UE active BWP. Otherwise when the UE dedicated configuration is activated, the range of the HARQ is between 0 and 15.**[End CNI-81991].****  
Downlink assignment index | 2 | 2 | if it is for msg4, value is 0, else value as 5G_UP_ALG_4466_replaced([11178897](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2y0fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) |   
TPC command for scheduled PUCCH | 2 | 2 | 1 | Corresponds to 0dB, i.e. no power control  
PUCCH resource indicator | 3 | 3 | 5G_UP_ALG_18087_replaced([11187133](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvY-UvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) | Set to 0 for PUCCH resource determination for HARQ feedback for msg4.  
PDSCH to HARQ feedback timing | 3 | 3 | 5G_UP_ALG_4448_replaced([11178110](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku0WmfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) |

###### 3.25.3.1.3.1.0-3 DCI format 1_0 structure DCI Format 1_0 structure to be Used for PDCCH Order (ID: 13353948)

**3.25.3.1.3.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13353951`)

DCI format 1_0 structure DCI 1_0 for PDCCH order shall be scrambled by C-RNTI and will be monitored in UE-specific search space. The information provided in the field below is based on Clause 7.3.1.2.1 in TS 38.212. The DCI used for PDCCH order shall have an aggregation level determined by NRBTS.BWP_PROFILE.PDCCH.dciRaCompletionAggregationLevel.

|  |  |  |   
---|---|---|---|---  
Field Name | Number of Bits | Number of Supported Bits | Value | Comment  
Identifier for DCI format | 1 | 1 | 1 | Value "1" means it is a DL DCI.  
Frequency domain resource assignment |  | Least integer value that is greater than log2(NRBDL,BWP (NRBDL,BWP+1)/2), where NRBDL,BWP is the is the number PRBs in the active DL BWP | All ones. | As per Clause 7.3.1.2.1 of TS 38.212, If the CRC of the DCI format 1_0 is scrambled by C-RNTI and the "Frequency domain resource assignment" field are of all ones, the DCI format 1_0 is for random access procedure initiated by a PDCCH order. For the number of bits in the parameter, refer to the following sections in 38.212 v18.4 * Section 7.3.1.2.2 * Section 7.3.1.2.0 * Section 7.3.1.2.1  
Random Access Preamble index | 6 | 6 | Refer to [13345951](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_L9hUMOSSEfCmxLW1M7HMrQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) | Set according to ra-PreambleIndex in Clause 5.1.2 of TS 38.321  
UL/SUL indicator | 1 | 1 | Reserved field | If the value of the "Random Access Preamble index" is not all zeros and if the UE is configured with supplementaryUplink in ServingCellConfig in the cell, this field indicates which UL carrier in the cell to transmit the PRACH according to Table 7.3.1.1.1-1 in 38.212; otherwise, this field is reserved  
SS/PBCH index | 6 | 6 | Refer to [11111961](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpRvS_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) | If the value of the "Random Access Preamble index" is not all zeros, this field indicates the SS/PBCH that shall be used to determine the RACH occasion for the PRACH transmission; otherwise, this field is reserved.  
PRACH Mask index | 4 | 4 | Refer to [11111961](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpRvS_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) | If the value of the "Random Access Preamble index" is not all zeros, this field indicates the RACH occasion associated with the SS/PBCH indicated by "SS/PBCH index" for the PRACH transmission, according to Clause 5.1.1 of TS 38.321; otherwise, this field is reserved  
Reserved bits | 12 | 12 bits for DSS Scell, 10 for other Scells | Reserved bits | 12 bits for operation in a cell with shared spectrum channel access in frequency range 1 or when the DCI format is monitored in common search space for operation in a cell in frequency range 2-2; otherwise 10 bits  
  
The USS in which DCI 1_0 shall be monitored shall be an additional search space which will be used to monitor PDCCH order only and will be separate from the search space used to monitor DCI 1_1 and DCI 0_1. The USS for PDCCH order shall be monitored by the UE only in its SCell. The USS configuration is given in [SearchSpace for PDCCH Order](https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:f:/r/sites/ASCOP/AS%20Documents/FS1TAs-CFAMs/CB/CB015000%20-%20CB015499/CFAM/CB015279%20FR1%20UL%20CA%20with%20non-collocated%20SCell/SearchSpace%20for%20PDCCH%20Order?csf=1&web=1&e=GdPw95).

### 3.25.3.2 DCI Format Size Management during UE (re)configuration

#### 3.25.3.2.0-2 DCI Format Size Management during UE (re)configuration Flowchart - reference (ID: 11171588)

**3.25.3.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11171600`)

DCI Format Size Management during UE (re)configuration 11171600: DCI Format Size Management during UE (re)configuration The gNB controls the DCI Format 0_1 size at the UE (re)configuration as follow.

[image-0][image_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a process related to DCI 0_x size management, triggered by the C-Plane. The flowchart depicts various steps, decisions, and responses within a system, likely a telecommunications network. Here's a breakdown of the elements: **Start Points:** * "DCI 0_x size management" - This is the overall process being managed. * "Triggered by the C-Plane" - Indicates the external trigger for this process. **Main Paths and Decisions:** 1\. **Left Path (Initiated by PsCell_CellSetUpReq):** * `PsCell_CellSetUpReq` initiates the process. * "Initialize the common TDRA lists UL" is performed. * `PsCell_CellSetupResp` is sent, containing `puschTimeDomainAllocationList`. * The process ends. 2\. **Right Path (Initiated by PsUser_UserSetUpReq or PsUser_UserModifyReq):** * This path branches based on whether the request is `PsUser_UserSetUpReq` or `PsUser_UserModifyReq`. * **Decision:`ueAddCause: Initial Access (SA)?`** * **No:** Leads to `ueSssNotAdded(1)?` decision. * **Yes:** Leads to `ueSssNotAdded(1)?` decision. * **Decision:`ueSssNotAdded(1)?`** * **No:** Leads to "Transient phase activation (UL/DL)". * **Yes:** Leads to "Transient phase activation (UL/DL)". * **Decision:`DSS Transient phase activation?`** * **No:** Leads to `act TdraFallback?` decision. * **Yes:** Leads to "DL DSS transient phase Activation". * **Decision:`act TdraFallback?`** * **No:** Leads to `BWPDC 0_x conflict(2)?` decision. * **Yes:** Leads to "Transient phase maintained (UL/DL)". * **Decision:`BWPDC 0_x conflict(2)?`** * **No:** Leads to `PsUser_UserModifyResp (per BWP): - no puschTimeDomainAllocationList`. * **Yes:** Leads to `PsUser_UserSetupResp (perBWP): - puschTimeDomainAllocationList (according to current setting)`. * Following `PsUser_UserSetupResp (perBWP): - puschTimeDomainAllocationList (according to current setting)`, the process continues to `RRC Set up acknowledgement`. * After `RRC Set up acknowledgement`, it leads to "DSS Transient phase maintained (DL)" and then ends. 3\. **Path from`PsUser_UserModifyReq`:** * `PsUser_UserModifyReq` initiates this path. * **Decision:`ueSssNotAdded(1)?`** * **No:** Leads to "Transient phase activation?". * **Yes:** Leads to "Transient phase Activation". * **Decision:`Transient phase activation?`** * **No:** Leads to `act TdraFallback?` decision. * **Yes:** Leads to "Transient phase Activation". * **Decision:`act TdraFallback?`** * **No:** Leads to `BWPDC 0_x conflict(per BWP)?` decision. * **Yes:** Leads to "Transient phase maintained (UL/DL)". * **Decision:`BWPDC 0_x conflict(per BWP)?`** * **No:** Leads to `PsUser_UserModifyResp (per BWP): - no puschTimeDomainAllocationList`. * **Yes:** Leads to `PsUser_UserModifyResp (per BWP): - puschTimeDomainAllocationList(3)`. * Following `PsUser_UserModifyResp (per BWP): - puschTimeDomainAllocationList(3)`, it leads to `RRC reconfiguration acknowledgement`. * After `RRC reconfiguration acknowledgement`, it leads to "Transient phase deactivated (UL/DL)" and then ends. **Other elements:** * **Rectangular boxes with rounded corners:** Represent start/end points or specific states. * **Rectangular boxes:** Represent processes or actions. * **Diamonds:** Represent decision points. * **Arrows:** Indicate the flow of the process. * **Text labels:** Describe the actions, decisions, and parameters. * **Footnotes:** * `(1) ueSssNotAdded set to false is equivalent to flag not present` * `(2) DCI 0_x conflict needs 2 conditions: UE-Specific search space with CORESET (0), Parameters leading to have the same size for DCI 0_0 and 0_1` * `(3) Default puschTimeDomainAllocationList computed at the PsCell_CellSetUpResp` The flowchart details how the system handles different scenarios related to user setup and modification requests, particularly concerning transient phases and potential conflicts in bandwidth part (BWP) configurations.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12358.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

[image-1][image_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a process triggered by the U-Plane. The flowchart begins with a single starting point labeled "1". From this point, three parallel processes can be initiated: "SRS ports reconfiguration", "Transform precoder reconfiguration", and "Beam group reconfiguration". Following these initial steps, the process converges to a decision point: "Consider the UE-Specific search space are configured". If the condition is "True", the next step is "act TdraFallback". If it's "False", the process proceeds to a check for "BWP DCI 0_x conflict (per BWP)?". The "act TdraFallback" path leads to a decision point. If the answer is "No", it branches to "PsUser_ReconfigurationRequiredInd: - no pusch TimeDomainAllocationList". If the answer is "Yes", it leads to "PsUser_UserModifyReq". The "BWP DCI 0_x conflict (per BWP)?" decision point has two branches: \- If "Yes", it leads to "PsUser_ReconfigurationRequiredInd: - pusch TimeDomainAllocationList (per BWP) (according to new setting)". This is followed by "PsUser_UserModifyReq". \- If "No", it leads to "PsUser_ReconfigurationRequiredInd: - pusch TimeDomainAllocationList (per BWP)(3)". Both "PsUser_UserModifyReq" paths converge to a decision point: "Modification(s) accepted?". \- If "No", the process leads to "Previous pusch TimeDomainAllocationList (per BWP) are used" and then to "End". \- If "Yes", the process leads to "New pusch TimeDomainAllocationList (per BWP) are used". After the "New pusch TimeDomainAllocationList (per BWP) are used" step, the process enters a "Transient phase maintained or activated" state. From here, there's a check: "ueSssNotAdded(1)?". \- If "True", it leads to "RRC reconfiguration acknowledgement" and then to "Transient phase maintained", followed by "End". \- If "False", it leads to "RRC reconfiguration acknowledgement" and then to "Transient phase deactivated", followed by "End". The "Beam group reconfiguration" path directly leads to an "End" state.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_12358.002.png[/image_path][/image-1]

Figure:

Folder:
