#### 3.25.3.2.0-3 DCI Format Size Management during UE (re)configuration User setup (UE Configuration) (ID: 11171605)

**3.25.3.2.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `11171623`)

DCI Format Size Management during UE (re)configuration When the TDRA fallback mode enabled (5G_UP_5786_replaced([11362081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uc6HWvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): The gNB shall support the TDRA fallback mode for compatibility to handover to another gNB with old SW version (before 21B) and/or avoid UE bug on TDRA decoding) or UE-Specific search space is not added (5G_CP_ARC_ALG_4832_replaced([11308949](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TrFkVfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for Initial Access (5G_CP_OTH_1198_replaced([11612017](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Y5Sb1vwOEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_CP_OTH_1517_replaced([11615732](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Y544svwOEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) related procedures, the gNB does not fill the puschTimeDomainAllocationList to C-Plane for this UE. Otherwise, the puschTimeDomainAllocationList is always reported to the C-Plane.

When the puschTimeDomainAllocationList (for 10MHz [CB009355-A] and 15MHz [End CB009355-A] TDD without the TDRA potentially added to increase the RA-Msg2 candidate slots in TDD) is reported to the C-Plane (see above), the 5G-L2-PS checks the DCI Format 0_1 size expected per BWP configured in the UE and applies one of the following actions:

 If there is DCI conflict detected (5G_UP_ALG_7112_replaced([11171658](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuF96_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the gNB shall report modified puschTimeDomainAllocationList in order to remove the conflict (5G_UP_ALG_7112_replaced([11171658](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuF96_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for each configured BWP in the UE. In the UE context, the gNB saves the DCI TDRA size for each BWP configured in the UE (up to one larger and one power saving dedicated BWP with same TDRA list) according to the number of items in the common PUSCH TDRA list computed at the cell setup.

 If there is no DCI conflict detected (5G_UP_ALG_7112_replaced([11171658](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuF96_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the gNB shall fill the puschTimeDomainAllocationList using default TDRA list to the C-Plane. The default TDRA list corresponds to the one sent back to the C-Plane at the cell setup procedure (for 10MHz [CB009355-A] and 15MHz [End CB009355-A] TDD without the TDRA potentially added to increase the RA-Msg2 candidate slots in TDD).

For PUSCH Slot Aggregation: The behavior described above for reporting TDRA table to C-Plane also applies. The only difference is that L2 PS must decide between including pusch-TimeDomainAllocationList for a UE not eligible for Slot Aggregation and pusch-TimeDomainAllocationListDCI-0-1-r16 for a UE eligible for Slot Aggregation (see 5G_UP_ALG_19245_replaced([11204746](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwlRLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for definition of Slot Aggregation eligibility)

---

#### 3.25.3.2.0-4 DCI Format Size Management during UE (re)configuration Dynamic UE reconfiguration (ID: 11171627)

**3.25.3.2.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11171636`)

DCI Format Size Management during UE (re)configuration When the TDRA fallback mode enabled (5G_UP_5786_replaced([11362081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uc6HWvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): The gNB shall support the TDRA fallback mode for compatibility to handover to another gNB with old SW version (before 21B) and/or avoid UE bug on TDRA decoding) or UE-Specific search space is not added (5G_CP_ARC_ALG_4832_replaced([11308949](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TrFkVfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the gNB does not fill the pdschTimeDomainAllocationList to C-Plane. Otherwise, the pdschTimeDomainAllocationList is always reported to the C-Plane.

When the pdschTimeDomainAllocationList is reported to the C-Plane (see above), the 5G-L2-PS checks the DCI Format 0_1 size expected per BWP configured in the UE and applies one of the following actions:

 If there is DCI conflict detected (5G_UP_ALG_7112_replaced([11171658](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuF96_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the gNB shall report modified pdschTimeDomainAllocationList in order to remove the conflict (5G_UP_ALG_7112_replaced([11171658](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuF96_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for each configured BWP in the UE.

 If there is no DCI conflict detected (5G_UP_ALG_7112_replaced([11171658](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuF96_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the gNB shall fill the pdschTimeDomainAllocationList using default TDRA list to the C-Plane. The default TDRA list corresponds to the one sent back to the C-Plane at the cell setup procedure.

When the dynamic reconfiguration is required by the U-Plane reason (5G_UP_ALG_4816_replaced([11194889](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv4GhfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the TDRA field size update, in the UE context, must be done only when the reconfiguration is accepted.

When the dynamic reconfiguration is required by the C-Plane (not by U-Plane reason), the TDRA field size update, in the UE context, must be done after the computation of the puschTimeDomainAllocationList.

[CB008236-A] For PUSCH Slot Aggregation: The behavior described above for reporting TDRA table to C-Plane also applies. The only difference is that L2 PS must decide between including pusch-TimeDomainAllocationList for a UE not eligible for Slot Aggregation and pusch-TimeDomainAllocationListDCI-0-1-r16 for a UE eligible for Slot Aggregation (see 5G_UP_ALG_19245_replaced([11204746](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwlRLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for definition of Slot Aggregation eligibility) [End CB008236-A]

---

#### 3.25.3.2.0-5 DCI Format Size Management during UE (re)configuration Default uplink configuration used for the call setup and DCI Format 0_0 size for reference (ID: 11171641)

**3.25.3.2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11171646`)

DCI Format Size Management during UE (re)configuration The gNB shall identify the DCI Format 0_0 length according to the CORESET(0) size using default configuration:

 If the CORESET(0) is on 24 RBs, the DCI Format 0_0 has 37 bits.

 If the CORESET(0) is on 48 RBs, the DCI Format 0_0 has 39 bits.

 If the CORESET(0) is on 96 RBs, the DCI Format 0_0 has 41 bits.

The default configuration expected by the L2-PS for the SA call setup is:

 txConfig: codebook.

 Transform Precoder: disabled.

 PUSCH config: codebook.

 HARQ-Ack-Codebook: dynamic.

 Frequency Hopping: not set.

 Number of SRS ports: 1.

 maxRank: 1.

 maxMIMO-Layer: 1.

 codebookSubset: nonCoherent.

 Aperiodic CSI: not configured.

 Uplink PT-RS: not configured.

 betaOffsets: semiStatic.

---

#### 3.25.3.2.0-6 DCI Format Size Management during UE (re)configuration Size of DCI format 0_1 computation (ID: 11171650)

**3.25.3.2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11171654`)

DCI Format Size Management during UE (re)configuration To check the DCI size, the gNB computes each variable and optional fields as detailed in the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4937_replaced([11171437](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuEIqvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), with the following inputs for each BWP configured in the UE for BWP with UE-Specific search space associated to the CORESET(0):

 UE (re)configuration triggered by the C-Plane. In that case, the gNB shall use the parameters received in the PsUser_User[Setup,Modify]Req and in the UE context to compute the DCI format 0_1 size. The TDRA field size in the DCI 0_1 is the one based on the initialized TDRA list if there is none defined in the UE context. Otherwise, it is a reconfiguration, and the current DCI TDRA size is already saved in the UE context.

 UE reconfiguration triggered by the 5G-L2-PS (5G_UP_ALG_4816_replaced([11194889](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv4GhfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The gNB shall use the current UE configuration and updates the the parameters linked to the requested configuration to compute the DCI format 0_1 size. The DCI TDRA size is the one saved in the UE context.

---

#### 3.25.3.2.0-7 DCI Format Size Management during UE (re)configuration DCI Format 0_0 and 0_1 conflict detection and TDRA list modification (ID: 11171658)

**3.25.3.2.0-7.0-8**  (ID: `12656176`)

DCI Format Size Management during UE (re)configuration The gNB shall check the DCI Format sizes for each BWP configured when at least one of the following conditions is met:

 At least one UE-Specifc search space (with DCI Format 0_1 and 1_1) is using the CORESET(0).

In this BWP, the CORESET(0) handles at least one Common search space using the DCI Format 0_0 and 1_0 too. With both search space types, the UE is not able to differentiate the DCI Format type (x_0 or x_1), if they have the same size.

 At least one UE-Specific search space (with DCI Format 0_1 and 1_1) is using a CORESET with an identifer above 0 and without PDCCH DM-RS scrambling identifer (ueSssDmrsScramblingId equal or lower than 1007).

With this type of configuration it is possible that the UE is not able to differentiate the DCI Format (x_0 and x_1), because the DCI data scrambling applied is the same for both DCI format types and the CORESET ID is not broadcast on the radio interface.

The gNB shall compare the DCI Format 0_0 size and the DCI Format 0_1 length computed. If there is a conflict, the gNB shall apply the following rule to build the expected TDRA list (the activation of this TDRA list in the U-Plane is specified in 5G_UP_ALG_7080_replaced([11171605](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuFW1PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_7087_replaced([11171627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuF92vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

 If the current DCI TDRA field size is not the largest one, the gNB adds a dummy TDRA on top of the common TDRA list computed at the Cell setup in order to increase by 1 bit the DCI field, reports to the C-Plane this list and updates the DCI TDRA size in the UE context according to the source of the (re)configuration (triggered by the C-Plane or the U-Plane).

The dummy entry added has the following parameters:

 k2 is set to 12.

 PUSCH mapping type is same as the one defined in the PUSCH common TDRA list reported at the cell setup.

 Start and Length Indicator Value (SLIV) is set to 55.

 If the current DCI TDRA field size is already the largest one, the gNB removes TDRAs in the dedicated TDRA list computed at the Cell setup in order to decrease by 1 bit the DCI field, reports to the C-Plane this list and updates the DCI TDRA size in the UE context according to the source of the (re)configuration (triggered by the C-Plane or the U-Plane).

The priority applied to select the TDRA to remove is the following:

 Dummy entries added previously, if present.

 TDRA entries used to extend the candidate slots of the RA-Msg3 scheduled by a RAR (only one SLIV for a k2 value).

 TDRA entries with the largest number of PUSCH symbols configured for the the DCI 0_1 scheduling and from the highest k2 value.

For PUSCH Slot Aggregation:

 For no sharing with LTE: **If the default puschAllocationList-r16 table (see 5G_UP_ALG_26269_replaced([11204853](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwl4OPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is applied, **the DCI 0_1 TDRA field is 4 bits in length (14 entries) due to addition of 2x and 4x repetition options in pusch-TimeDomainAllocationListDCI-0-1-r16. In this case L2 PS adds 3 dummy entries (with k2/PUSCH mapping type/SLIV content as defined above, plus the Repetition entry set to n1) after the last row. This will increase the DCI 0_1 TDRA field size to 5 bits (supporting 17 table entries).****

 Note: For sharing with LTE: the DCI 0_1 TDRA field is 3 bits in length (8 **entries) due to addition of 2x and 4x repetition options in pusch-TimeDomainAllocationListDCI-0-1-r16. In this case no DCI size conflict is expected.**

 For TDD FR1: the DCI 0_1 TDRA field is 5 bits in length (6 entries) due to addition of 2x and 4x repetition options in pusch-TimeDomainAllocationListDCI-0-1-r16. In this case no DCI size conflict is expected.

 When PUSCH Slot Aggregation for VoNR is enabled in the cell and either the UE Add Cause = Reestablish in a modification request from CP-RT or on a PDU session setup: L2-PS shall wait, to decide upon modification of PUSCH TDRA table due to DCI size conflict, until it is known whether the UE can be classified as SAg Eligible (see 5G_UP_ALG_19245_replaced([11204746](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwlRLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Note:

 When there is PUSCH Slot aggregation scheduling, the MSG2 to MSG3 timing must be increased for all UEs to avoid MSG3 PRBs collision with PRBs for Slot Aggregation (see 5G_UP_ALG_4346_replaced([11177880](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuyhaPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). This is only needed for FDD. This requires additional K2 values in pusch-TimeDomainAllocationList (Rel-15 TDRA). This table is broadcast in SIB1 and is referenced by the MSG3 grant within MSG2. CP gets this table from L2 PS at cell setup and uses it for both PUSCH common configuration in SIB1 and for PUSCH dedicated configuration in RRC ReConfiguration. The interworking with Slot Aggregation increases the corresponding DCI field size from 2 to 3 bits (FDD with no LTE) and from 1 bit to 2 bits (FDD with LTE). The DCI size conflic avoidance described above for pusch-TimeDomainAllocationList will still apply.

For UL Tx switching UE with FDD PCell [CB010439-C] (not DSS cell) [End CB010439-C] and TDD UL SCell:

 If **NRCELL.actUlSlotAgg = "Disabled" on FDD PCell or the UE is not eligible for Slot Aggregation, FDD PCell DCI 0_1 dedicate TDRA field** is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_24789_replaced([11115992](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpz6yfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), gNB-DU shall add minimal number of dummy entry in order to increase DCI TDRA field bit size by 1 if conflict detected****.

 If the UE is eligible for Slot Aggregation, FDD PCell DCI 0_1 dedicate TDRA field is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_26270_replaced([11204898](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwl4PPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), gNB-DU shall add minimal number of dummy entry in order to increase DCI TDRA field bit size by 1 if conflict detected.

[CB010439-C] 

For UL Tx switching UE with FDD DSS PCell and TDD UL SCell:

 If the UE is not eligible for Slot Aggregation, FDD PCell dedicate TDRA field **is defined in** [11115957](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpz6wPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), gNB-DU shall remove the entry with k2min+1 in order to decrease DCI TDRA field bit size by 1 if conflict detected.

 If the UE is eligible for Slot Aggregation, FDD PCell DCI 0_1 dedicate TDRA field is defined in [11115957](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpz6wPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), gNB-DU shall add minimal number of dummy entry in order to increase DCI TDRA field bit size by 1 if conflict detected.

[End CB010439-C] 

[CB010439-A]

For UL CA UE with FDD DSS PCell and TDD UL SCell:

 If the UE is not eligible for Slot Aggregation, FDD PCell dedicate TDRA field **is defined in** [11115957](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpz6wPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), gNB-DU shall add minimal number of dummy entry in order to increase DCI TDRA field bit size by 1 if conflict detected.

 If the UE is eligible for Slot Aggregation, FDD PCell DCI 0_1 dedicate TDRA field is defined in [11115957](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpz6wPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), gNB-DU shall add minimal number of dummy entry in order to increase DCI TDRA field bit size by 1 if conflict detected.

[End CB010439-A]

Slot Aggregation eligibility is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_19245_replaced([11204746](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwlRLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For TDD FR1 + TDD FR1 intra-band contiguous UL CA UE:

 If TDD PCell adds the dedicated TDRA list specified in 5G_UP_ALG_29277_replaced([11116009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpz6zfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)):

 If TDD PCell DCI 0_1 dedicate TDRA field (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_29277_replaced([11116009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpz6zfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is 2 or 3 bits length, in this case gNB-DU adds dummy entries for puschMappingType=1:TypeB or dummy entries for puschMappingType=0:TypeA (with k2/PUSCH mapping type/SLIV content as defined above) after the last row, in order to increase the DCI 0_1 TDRA field size by 1 bit.

  * If TDD PCell DCI 0_1 dedicate TDRA field (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_29277_replaced([11116009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpz6zfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is 4 bits length, in this case gNB-DU only keeps the first 6 entries and removes other entries. This will decrease the DCI 0_1 TDRA field size to 3 bits.



The DCI Management is applicable to any configuration TDD or FDD.

For UL CA SCell, DCI Format 0_0 and 0_1 conflict detection and dedicate TDRA list modification is not needed because SCell does not configure CSS (DCI 0_0).

---

#### 3.25.3.2.0-8 DCI Format Size Management during UE (re)configuration DCI Format 1_0 and 1_1 size management (ID: 11171698)

**3.25.3.2.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11171701`)

DCI Format Size Management during UE (re)configuration When a UE-specific search space is associated to the CORESET(0), the 5G-L2-PS checks the configuration parameters to identify if additional entries must be added or not to differentiate the DCI Format 1_0 and 1_1 size.

When the following conditions are met, the 5G-L2-PS adds an additional entry (see hereafter) in the TDRA list to avoid the DCI size issue between the DCI Format 1_0 and 1_1:

 The Dedicated downlink BWP configured in the UE has a size of 52 or 106 RBs (PsCell_CellSetupReq and PsUser_User[Setup,Modify]Req)

 The CORESET(0) size is 48 RBs.

 The rbgSizePdsch parameter is set to config2 in the PsCell_CellSetupReq.

 The current TDRA list contains only 2 elements.

The TDRA added has the following parameters:

 The slot offset (K0) is set to 0.

 The PDSCH mapping is set to “typeA”.

 Start Symbol: 3 ; Length: 10 ; SLIV: 80

---

## 3.25.4 Downlink Control Information transmission

### 3.25.4.0-2 Downlink Control Information transmission PDCCH transmission settings (ID: 11171714)

**3.25.4.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11171723`)

Downlink Control Information transmission The gNB-DU shall send DL/UL DCI over PDCCH with following configurations:

  * CORESET allocation (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_4086_replaced([11170862](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuAeT_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

  * Serach Space (5G_UP_ALG_4036_replaced([11168496](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktwmofvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

  * CCE start index (5G_UP_ALG_4426_replaced([11170801](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuAeQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) from CCE candidates (5G_UP_ALG_3934_replaced([11169817](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt5wnfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

  * Aggregation Level (5G_UP_ALG_4055_replaced([11170246](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt9a9_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

  * PDCCH scrambling (5G_UP_ALG_7263_replaced([11095260](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kmkZhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

  * CCE interleaving (5G_CP_IF_RRC_2140_replaced([11333360](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wVAG3_vjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

  * PDCCH DMRS (5G_UP_ALG_141_replaced([11095662](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kmnc1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

  * PDCCH transmission scheme and precoding (5G_UP_ALG_7117_replaced([11171730](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuGk6fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))




When NRBTS/NRCELL-actDlPaWarmUp is set to 'true', 5G-L2-PS shall send dummy grant over PDCCH with following special configurations:

  * select DL slots for dummy PDCCH transmission in 5G_UP_ALG_15336_replaced([11171772](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuHL9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

  * define dummy grant in 5G_UP_ALG_15296_replaced([11171785](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuHL-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

  * Aggregation Level selection (5G_UP_ALG_4056_replaced([11170257](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt9a-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

  * calculate CCE capacity for dummy grant ( 5G_UP_ALG_15307_replaced([11170009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt7lxvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) )

  * start CCE selection for each dummy grant of DCI_1_1 configured with a dedicated C-RNTI ( 5G_UP_ALG_15302_replaced([11171115](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuBsZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ).




\- cceToRegMapping shall be "nonInterleaved" and interleaverSize shall be "none"

\- cRbStart shall be set with 0

  * regBundleSize shall be "n6"



\- coresetFreqDomainRbShift shall be 0

\- precoderGranularity shall be equal to 0(regBundleSize)

\- nShiftModNumOfRegBundles shall be 16

[CB008509-B]

When NRCELL.actConfDlInterferenceGen is set to "2" or "3", 5G-L2-PS shall send dummy grant over PDCCH with following special configurations:

  * select all DL and special slots for dummy PDCCH transmission

  * dedicated corset for dummy PDCCH is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_15299_replaced([11168360](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktvYk_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

  * define dummy grant in 5G_UP_ALG_15296_replaced([11171785](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuHL-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

  * Aggregation Level selection (5G_UP_ALG_4056_replaced([11170257](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt9a-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

  * calculate CCE capacity for dummy grant (5G_UP_ALG_15307_replaced([11170009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt7lxvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

  * start CCE selection for configured dummy PDCCH with a dedicated C-RNTI (5G_UP_ALG_15302_replaced([11171115](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuBsZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).




\- cceToRegMapping shall be "nonInterleaved" and interleaverSize shall be "none"

\- cRbStart shall be set with 0

  * regBundleSize shall be "n6"



\- coresetFreqDomainRbShift shall be 0

\- precoderGranularity shall be equal to 0(regBundleSize)

\- nShiftModNumOfRegBundles shall be 16

[End CB008509-B]

### 3.25.4.1 PDCCH precoding configuration

#### 3.25.4.1.0-1 PDCCH precoding configuration PDCCH precoding configuration w/o valid CSI ~~and beam reports~~ (ID: 11171730)

**3.25.4.1.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `12814019`)

PDCCH precoding configuration PDCCH scheduling for PDSCH with P-RNTI/SI-RNTI/RA-RNTI/Temporary C-RNTI , or PDSCH with C-RNTIs w/o valid CSI and beam reports:

  * Polarization Selection: over both polarizations (+45/-45 polarization on FR1, 0/90 on FR2) )



Precoding configuration:

1)For _NRCELL.actBeamforming is True, and_ NRCELL.numOfSubSectors is "0sub-sector":**

[CB008577-A] If NRCELL.cellTechnology is equal to 'TDD' [End CB008577-A] :

Precoding matrix generation method for 4 antenna ports transmission: One X Pol beam Repetition Precoding over first or second XPolBeam (refer 5G_UP_ALG_162_replaced([11095747](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kmoD7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[CB008577-A] If NRCELL.cellTechnology is equal to 'FDD': the same precoding as with valid CSI report, refers to [12806257: PDCCH precoding configuration with valid CSI reports](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_DEgo86AyEfCkxIKMlo4L6w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). [End CB008577-A] :

2)For TDD sub-sectorisation case with 2 subsectors:

If numOfSubSectors == 2 and rdNbXpolAntennasCommonChannel == 1 (two Xpol antennas used) no antenna port selection is applied. rdTwoXpolAntennasPdcchPrecodingOption (cf. 5G_L2_1227_replaced([11191943](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28gZnPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is used to select correct precoding matrix for PDCCH, therefore PdcchPrecodingOption4X4 IE in DlData_PdcchSendReq shall be equal to rdTwoXpolAntennasPdcchPrecodingOption.

Refer to 5G_UP_ALG_1924_replaced([11111609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpOsAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the mapping between Beam ID, Pattern ID and BeamIndex for sub-sectorisation;

3) If NIDD parameters configuration (_NRCELL.actEnhCtrlChannelTrans = True and_ NRCELL.enhCtrlChannelTransMode is not 0, 5G_UP_13733_replaced([11353784](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucB9oPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) , refers to 5G_UP_ALG_30890_replaced([11171749](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuGk7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**.** **

4)For other cases:

Precoding matrix generation method for 4 antenna ports transmission: SCDD Precoding (refer 5G_UP_ALG_162_replaced([11095747](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kmoD7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

eCPRI configurations:

Parameters setting for PDCCH eCPRI configurations based on pdcchPrecodingOption4x4, follow up the 5G_UP_ALG_4703_replaced([11193195](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvqrIfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: SIB1 and etc. common channel will not join Mu Mimo paired scheduling.

When _NRBTS/NRCELL-actDlPaWarmUp is set to 'true', in the_ initActivateDlSlot (see 5G_UP_ALG_15336_replaced([11171772](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuHL9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), for those dummy PDCCHs scheduling for the dedicated C-RNTI , the IEs in DlData_PdcchSendReq shall be:**

\- The parameter ” polarizationSelection” is set to “FIRSTPOLARIZATION”.

When NRCELL.actConfDlInterferenceGen is set to "2" or "3", in all the DL Slots, for those dummy PDCCHs scheduling for the dedicated C-RNTI, the precoding/power shall be set according to:

~~[CB008577-D] - If the cell has FDD beamforming enabled ([11111439](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) :~~

~~- - The same as not dummy PDCCH, refers to [12806257: PDCCH precoding configuration with valid CSI reports](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_DEgo86AyEfCkxIKMlo4L6w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).~~

~~- - Transmission power setting shall be the same as not dummy PDCCH ([11118347](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqCkQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).~~

~~- else: [End CB008577-D]~~

  * \- The parameter ” polarizationSelection” is set to “bothPolarizations”.

  * \- Transmission power setting for dummy PDCCH shall follow _staticPdcchPowerOffset which is defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2552_replaced([11118347](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqCkQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))._




~~[CB008577-D] - End precoding/power setting. [End CB008577-D]~~

For eCPRI configurations, the beam for dummy PDCCH transmission shall be fixedly configured as [CB008577-D] for TDD BF: [End CB008577-D] the SSB beam from beam set #1 with 90 degree ( see 5G_UP_ALG_1941_replaced([11111798](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpQhJPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). [CB008577-D] For FDD BF the full sector beam for DL. [End CB008577-D]

5G-L2-PS shall loop from high aggregation level to lower level to attempt filling un-used CCEs until dummy grant can be filled with a suitable level.

\-- if the UE support-LI (5G_UP_ALG_30852_replaced([11171756](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuHL8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ) and the valid CSI report contains LI,

When rank 1 is reported, gNB-DU shall assume LI =0. gNB-DU shall indicate the LI and PMI [PR824936] and rank from the report [End PR824936] as 5G_UP_ALG_30764_replaced([11095806](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kmoq9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). \-- if the UE support-LI (5G_UP_ALG_30852_replaced([11171756](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuHL8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ) and the valid CSI report contains LI,

Precoding is selected from PMI of UE report. When rank 1 is reported, gNB-DU shall assume LI =0. gNB-DU shall indicate the LI and PMI [PR824936] and rank from the report [End PR824936] as 5G_UP_ALG_30764_replaced([11095806](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kmoq9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Note here LI is from 3GPP's point of view.

\--else

gNB-DU shall indicate the transmission scheme and precoding as 5G_UP_ALG_30503_replaced([11095796](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kmoq8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**Note: gNB has flexibility on deciding precoding at the transient phase when CSI report is reconfigured and before CSI report based on new configuration is received or some abnormal UE failure and recovery procedure. Because it depends on whehter gNB reset the previous report to invalid or not when new CSI report configuration is received.**

#### 3.25.4.1.0-4 PDCCH precoding configuration Special handling for LI report when dlMimoMode is CL 4x MIMO (ID: 11171756)

**3.25.4.1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11171761`)

PDCCH precoding configuration If NIDD parameters configuration NRCELL.actEnhCtrlChannelTrans = True and (NRCELL.enhCtrlChannelTransMode = [Before CB013440-A-UPD002]2 or 3 [CB013440-A-UPD002] 5 or 6 [End CB013440-A-UPD002], 5G_UP_13733_replaced([11353784](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucB9oPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) ,

UE is marked as support-LI when receiving CSI report configuration with “reportQuantity” including LI.

For each valid CSI report for channel acquisition, if LI mismatch happens, gNB-DU shall mark the UE as not-support-LI and not use LI field for this UE.

Mismatched LI report is defined as: the indicated layer by LI is larger than rank indicated by RI.

#### 3.25.4.2-1.0-2 dummy PDCCH transmission [CB015769-A] This requirement shall only work when NRBTS/NRCELL/actPdcchSharingWithPdsch is TRUE and NRCELL.actCsiRsMuting is TRUE and NRCELL.actPdcchSharingAfterMuting is FALSE  [End CB015769-A] When NRBTS/NRCELL/actPdcchSharingWithPdsch is set to TRUE, 5G-L2-PS shall select initActvateDlSlotWoDummyOnPdcchSym where PDSCH shall not be multiplexing on the 1st PDCCH symbol: (The PDCCH symbol(s) can be shared with PDSCH in other PDCCH symbols, please see 5G_UP_ALG_25285_replaced( 11183087 )) 1) If  ( [Before CB015668-A] NRBTS.actTddCsiRsOpt is set to TRUE [CB015668-A] actTddCsiRsOpt is TRUE (note: actTddCsirsOpt is not get from NIDD but from L3 indicator) [End CB015668-A] and [Before CB015769-A] rdUseDAfterMutingForPdcchSharingTdd (5G_UP_ALG_31585_replaced( 11171869 )) [CB015769-A] NRCELL.actPdcchSharingAfterMuting [End CB015769-A] is set to FALSE - For the cells which are NOT previliged with ZAB (5G_UP_ALG_14549_replaced( 11213394 )), each first activate DL slot after cell specific CSR-RS slot of other cisRsPoolingGroupId as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_25819_replaced( 11116978 ) that is going to start trasmission shall be selected as initActvateDlSlotWoDummyOnPdcchSym. - For the cells which are previliged with ZAB (5G_UP_ALG_14549_replaced( 11213394 )) , each first activate DL slot after cell specific CSI-RS (5G_UP_ALG_25817_replaced( 11116933 )) that is going to start trasmission shall be selected as initActvateDlSlotWoDummyOnPdcchSym only if NRCELL.actCsiRsMuting is set to TRUE. (ID: 12816284)

#### 3.25.4.2.0-1 dummy PDCCH transmission Downlink slot selection for dummy PDCCH transmission (ID: 11171772)

**3.25.4.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11171779`)

dummy PDCCH transmission When NRBTS/NRCELL-actDlPaWarmUp is set to 'true', 5G-L2-PS shall select initActvateDlSlot where dummy PDCCH transmission shall be requested:

1) If actInfTddFrameMuting is set to false, according to the configured slot format pattern based on the tddFrameStructure(NRCELL.tddFrameStructure) in Cell Setup in 5G_UP_ALG_2313_replaced([11114697](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpnGefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

Each first activate DL slot after each Rx-to-Tx switching point shall be selected as initActvateDlSlot .

2) If actInfTddFrameMuting is set to true, according to the resultant slot format pattern which is determined in 5G_UP_ALG_2313_replaced([11114697](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpnGefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

Each first activate DL slot which is not muted and is going to start transmission after Rx-to-Tx switching point shall be selected as initActvateDlSlot.

If there is no real grant of DCI_1_1 for scheduling in the initActvateDlSlot , dummy PDCCH filling shall be skipped on this initActvateDlSlot .

[CB008370-CA]

when NRBTS/NRCELL-actDlPaWarmUp is set to TRUE and NRBTS/NRCELL/actPdcchSharingWithPdsch is set to TRUE,

If dummy PDCCH scheduled in the initActvateDlSlot,

then PDCCH symbol sharing with PDSCH is not possible in initActvateDlSlot.

(The PDCCH symbol(s) can be shared with PDSCH in other PDCCH symbols, please see 5G_UP_ALG_25285_replaced([11183087](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvH4l_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

else the PDCCH symbol(s) can be shared with PDSCH, please see 5G_UP_ALG_25285_replaced([11183087](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvH4l_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB008370-CA]

#### 3.25.4.2.0-2 dummy PDCCH transmission dummy grant setting (ID: 11171785)

**3.25.4.2.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11171801`)

dummy PDCCH transmission When NRBTS/NRCELL-actDlPaWarmUp is set to 'true', 5G-L2-PS shall define and create dummy grant used for dummy PDCCH allocation and transmission with following specified configurations:

  * dummy grant shall be defined for DCI_1_1 only

  * all dummy grant shall be configured with a common dedicated C-RNTI same to the reserved C-RNTI used for artificial PDSCH loading (see, 5G_UP_ALG_9012_replaced([11152046](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksdmKPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

  * dummy grants shall be transmitted in those initActivateDlSlot (see 5G_UP_ALG_15336_replaced([11171772](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuHL9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

  * dummy grants shall be transmitted in the DL primary subcell only

  * dmrsReferencePoint shall be 'POINT_A'

  * dmrsScramblingSequenceInt and dciScramblingSequenceInt shall be filled with any values (e.g. 9020) for dummy grant




[CB008509-B] When NRCELL.actConfDlInterferenceGen is set to "2" or "3", 5G-L2-PS shall define and create dummy grant used for dummy PDCCH allocation and transmission with following specified configurations:

  * dummy grant shall be defined for DCI_1_1 and DCI_0_1

  * all dummy grant shall be configured with a common dedicated C-RNTI same to the reserved C-RNTI used for artificial PDSCH loading (see, 5G_UP_ALG_9012_replaced([11152046](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksdmKPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

  * dummy grants shall be transmitted in all DL slots (see 5G_UP_ALG_17661_replaced([11183983](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvOmS_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

  * dmrsReferencePoint shall be 'POINT_A'

  * dmrsScramblingSequenceInt and dciScramblingSequenceInt shall be filled with any values (e.g. 9020) for dummy grant




[End CB008509-B]

**3.25.4.2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11171816`)

dummy PDCCH transmission When NRBTS/NRCELL-actDlPaWarmUp is set to 'true', [CB008509-B] or NRCELL.actConfDlInterferenceGen is set to "2" or "3" [End CB008509-B] for dummy grant transmission with a dedicated C-RNTI (see 5G_UP_ALG_15296_replaced([11171785](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuHL-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), 5G-L2-PS shall use following configuration

### 3.25.5.0-9 R&amp;D parameters rdHighPdcchLoadT20 (ID: 12729998)

### 3.25.5.0-17 R&amp;D parameters rdNumUesToActThreeSymbPdcch (ID: 13420217)

**3.25.5.0-17.0-1**  (ID: `13420218`)

R&D parameters Short description: When the number of UEs with 3 symbol PDCCH configured exceeds the value of this parameter, this activates the third PDCCH symbol in slots configured with three PDCCH symbols.

Value range: 0...100  
Default value: 1  
Step size: 1  
Unit:   
Online modifiable: Yes  
Type: Control   
Performance Impact: 

Used in: [12729897: CORESET duration pattern with 3 PDCCH symbols](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_SFUu8nKOEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)  
Trigger for deletion: Never   
Owner: sameera.palipana@nokia.com
